In the arena in the Immortal Skills Hall of the eastern Devilbirds, the bone cauldron thrummed loudly. It was surrounded by intense, raging, nine-colored fire. The magical symbols covering the cauldron were pulsing with dazzling light that caused the flames to rage even further. The refinement process... had officially begun!

Among the emissaries of the Imperial Sovereign mountains, there were three who had very grim expressions on their faces. The others seemed bewildered.

This turn of events was completely out of the blue. None of them could have predicted that the grand elder who had started this very ceremony would, in his moment of dominance, suddenly meet with failure. After all, the grand elder would never have invited the emissaries from the Imperial Sovereign mountains unless he was completely confident in succeeding.

Of course, in order to start this ceremony to begin with, he had to invite the emissaries. But regardless, he wouldn’t have done so unless he was certain nothing unexpected would happen. And yet... something unexpected had just happened.

No one knew how Yue Dong had fooled the grand elder and suddenly seized the upper hand. But there was no doubt that there was now a lot of suspense over who would ultimately become the grand immortal adept.

Obviously, the identity of the grand immortal adept would have different ramifications on the interests of different Imperial Sovereign mountains. Some of them would prefer that the grand elder succeed. Others were partial toward Yue Dong. Yet others were neutral.

Among those who supported the grand elder were the third and seventh Imperial Sovereign mountains. And thus, when the dramatic developments occurred, the emissaries from those mountains wanted to interfere. Before they could, the emissaries from the fourth and sixth mountains blocked their paths. Those emissaries glared at each other without saying a word. Their actions revealed all their intentions, and instantly, the atmosphere became very tense.

As those four faced off, a whistling sound entered the Immortal Skills Hall. Along with it came a group of black-robed cultivators along with some immortal adepts. Leading them was a young man in a fancy robe.

Pulsing with killing intent, the young man and the cultivators following him immediately started fighting with the immortal adepts who supported the grand elder.

As for the young man, he shot with incredible speed past the fighting and leaped up into the air over the cauldron. As the air rippled and distorted, three immortal adepts who were personal friends of the grand elder rushed forth to meet him.

These three immortal adepts were extraordinary cultivators, and didn’t hesitate to unleash a gruish immortal skill that caused three pitch-black fangs to shoot toward the young man in the fancy robe. The young man didn’t seem surprised at all, as if he had anticipated that these three would attack him. Quickly taking out a bell, he threw it viciously toward the pill cauldron.

A clang rang out as the bell expanded to a size of several hundred meters, making it so large it could settle down over the cauldron, completely covering it. Waves of energy rolled off it in every direction. All of this takes a bit of time to describe, but actually happened in the time it takes a spark to fly off a piece of flint.

After the bell landed, the three immortal adepts’ attacks landed on the young man in the fancy robe, and he tumbled backward with blood spraying out of his mouth. However, his voice was cold when he said, “That bell shows the attitude of the Yun Clan! Our clan backs Yue Dong as the grand immortal adept!”

The immortal adepts loyal to the grand elder glared grimly at the young man in the fancy robe. The emissaries from the Imperial Sovereign mountains also looked over at him.

“The Cloud Heaven Bell!”

The bell was quite famous among the eastern Devilbirds. It was a precious treasure of the Yun Clan, and that clan was just as powerful as the Lan Clan.[1]

As for this young man in the fancy robe, he was also quite famous. He was the young lord of the Yun Clan!

When the emissaries from the Imperial Sovereign mountains realized who he was, strange looks appeared on their faces. It was no secret among the eastern Devilbirds that Young Lord Yun had long been pursuing Yue Dong, and most intelligence reports indicated that he had helped her out recently at the Immortal Skills Hall. But everyone had assumed that he was acting on his own. After all, when Yue Dong was arrested, he had been driven out of the Immortal Skills Hall. But now... he arrived at precisely the right moment, and with the Yun Clan’s precious treasure in tow!

That was a totally different thing. He was now here representing the Yun Clan! And that gave an entirely different meaning to this conflict for the position of grand immortal adept.

In reality, it wasn’t the Yun Clan or the immortal adepts who were in control of this battle. It was... the ten Imperial Sovereign mountains. They were the ones with the true authority.

From the group of immortal adepts that supported the grand elder emerged a middle-aged man who clasped hands to the emissaries from the mountains. “Yue Dong betrayed the Immortal Skills Hall. Clearly, she hoodwinked Young Lord Yun into getting her the support of the Yun Clan. Unless Patriarch Yun himself shows up, the Immortal Skills Hall won’t acknowledge the wishes of the Yun Clan. Therefore, I would like to request that all of you emissaries help quell this chaos. Afterward, the Immortal Skills Hall will definitely repay you for your kindness!”

Upon hearing this, Young Lord Yun’s face turned grim. Clasping hands to the emissaries of the Imperial Sovereign mountains, he said, “This is an internal matter of the Immortal Skills Hall. Miss Yue Dong didn’t betray the Immortal Skills Hall in any way. She is the only apprentice of the former grand immortal adept, and she commands the Six Thieves Deceive Life immortal skill. She is the true successor.

“The grand elder has evil intentions. Instead of respecting the traditions of the Immortal Skills Hall, he plotted to become the new grand immortal adept. He couldn’t be more ruthless and malevolent! I sincerely hope that all of you can maintain your neutrality of years past, and not interfere in the internal affairs of the Immortal Skills Hall!”

Young Lord Yun clasped hands respectfully. Inside, he was very worried about how things would work out. When he went to get the precious treasure of his clan, things had gone very smoothly. That alone went to show what the patriarch of his clan was thinking.

If Young Lord Yun succeeded, then the support of the Yun Clan would turn into a reality. But if he failed, then the Yun Clan would say that he took the precious treasure without permission, and that they had never intended to interfere.

Thus, his gaze swept over the emissaries from the Imperial Sovereign mountains, especially those from the fourth and sixth mountains. He knew that both of them had secretly been in communication with Yue Dong, and actually supported her claim to the title.

The emissaries from the fourth and sixth mountains thought about it. They had already done everything they could by blocking the emissaries from the third and seventh mountains. If they actually spoke up now, it would be pushing things too far. As of now, an equilibrium had been reached. As everyone remained silent in thought, the emissary from the first Imperial Sovereign mountain spoke.

“Fellow Daoist Yun, at what point did the Yun Clan gain the right to speak for the Immortal Skills Hall?” The emissary from the first mountain was an old man. He currently sat on his throne with his eyes closed. When he spoke, his voice seemed to thrum as if overlapping with itself. “The ancient agreement states that the Imperial Sovereign mountains can jointly make decisions about the Immortal Skills Hall. We refrain from interfering in order to show respect. But that doesn’t mean we can’t interfere. We just wait until the right time to do so. And now is just such a time. Everyone, I suggest we open the cauldron and assist the grand elder. We should quell this chaos and end this entire affair.”

Young Lord Yun’s expression flickered. At the same time, the supporters of the grand elder looked excited. All of them knew that the opinion of the first Imperial Sovereign mountain carried a lot of weight.

The other emissaries looked thoughtful, and even those from the fourth and sixth mountain seemed like they were weighing their options. It looked like a decision was about to be made.

However, that was when Xu Qing spoke in a voice like a chill winter wind.

“I disagree!”

All eyes looked in his direction. The old man from the first mountain opened his eyes and did the same.

Sir Blood Dust’s opinion carried a lot of weight. And the tenth Imperial Sovereign’s opinion carried even more weight than that. Therefore, the fact that the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain disagreed caused the first emissary’s heart to start pounding.

As everyone looked at Xu Qing, his facial expression remained placid. He could see what was going on here, and now knew with certainty that everything had been planned out by his Eldest Brother. Given that, he couldn’t allow anyone to mess up his Eldest Brother’s plan.

“Before I came here, my Imperial Sovereign issued orders stating that the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain would not participate in any infighting in the Immortal Skills Hall. Our mountain... will support the winner, and no one else!”

With that, he looked over at the emissary from the first mountain, his gaze strong and unwavering.

The other emissaries said nothing. They were just waiting to see what would happen between Xu Qing and the old man.

The old man from the first mountain looked at Xu Qing for a moment, then spoke in a hoarse voice. “I find this very strange, Sir Blood Dust. You have a beef with Yue Dong. So why are you doing this?”

“If I have to pick between my Imperial Sovereign’s orders and my personal vendetta,” Xu Qing said calmly. “I’ll naturally choose the former.” Then his voice turned icy and sinister as he continued, “Besides, I would love for Yue Dong to become the grand immortal adept. That will just make it all the more satisfying when I kill her myself.”

The old man from the first mountain looked at him through narrowed eyes. “And what will you do if I ignore your wishes?”

Xu Qing’s facial expression didn’t change. “You can find out if you want.”

The atmosphere in the arena suddenly became much more tense. It was as if two violent tempests were building around Xu Qing and the first mountain emissary, and they were about to collide with one another.

However, Sir Blood Dust’s actions among the western Devilbirds were being talked about everywhere. And everyone was shocked by the fact that he had killed Sir Westdevil. Even the old man from the first mountain was feeling a bit leery of him.

***

Inside the cauldron, the grand elder’s heart was pounding. He had inspected Yue Dong thoroughly on several occasions. He had also gone so far as to shatter her meridians, drain most of her blood, and place warding spells all over her. How could he have ever guessed that, at the most critical of moments, she would use some gruish magic to teleport him to the interior of the cauldron and become part of the refining process?

He still had contingency plans. For one thing, he had long since reached out to the first Imperial Sovereign mountain and gained their support. As such, he was certain that all he had to do was wait for a bit, and help would come from outside of the cauldron. Of course, that would also mean that his relationship with his saviors would change forever.

There was another reason he was completely confident that he would be able to get out of his situation. That confidence came because of how much he understood the bone cauldron, and how well he could control it!

Although he couldn’t control the cauldron as well as the previous grand immortal adept, he was still confident that there was no way Yue Dong could possibly match up to him in understanding or control.

According to the rules of the Immortal Skills Hall, only the grand immortal adept and the grand elder had the right to use the cauldron. Since the grand immortal adept had perished, he as the grand elder was naturally a hundred percent confident in being able to use the cauldron as an asset.

“Yue Dong,” he said coolly, “you don’t understand this pill cauldron. From the moment you entered it, your fate was sealed. Therefore, this little plot of yours is completely pointless.”

He quickly performed an incantation gesture, causing the cauldron to tremble. Then he flew up, calling on his control over the cauldron to open it and escape. The cauldron trembled, and the lid blurred. It seemed like the grand elder was going to be free a moment later.

However, that was when Yue Dong, who had only her head left, suddenly laughed sarcastically.

“I don’t understand this cauldron?” Erniu said. “Fuse permanently!”

All of a sudden, the vortex above the pill cauldron vanished, and countless amounts of flesh and blood emerged from it. They spread out, covering the lid and body of the cauldron... and fused them together permanently! It was as if they all had the same origin, and were now inseparable.

No matter how the grand elder used his immortal skill, nothing happened. It was as if... his qualifications had become nothing but a show.

The grand elder was understandably bewildered. When he had been teleported into the pill cauldron, he had been taken aback. It was no exaggeration to say that he had been sucked into an extremely dangerous situation.

“This can’t be happening! You’re not Yue Dong! Yue Dong couldn’t do this. Who... who are you??”

Erniu laughed cruelly as his head floated there. “Anything can happen. This pill cauldron is made from my damn stuff! As for who the hell I am, let me freaking tell you. This cauldron was refined from me. So who do you think I am?”

Inside, Erniu was thinking fondly back to that time he, Master Seventh, and Xu Qing had visited that operations palace beneath Sea-Sealing County. There had been an Immortal Skills Hall there, and he had actually seen a statue of Grand Emperor Immortal Skill. [2]

Back then, the old man wanted me to bow to Grand Emperor Immortal Skill, but I said no. That bitch is the last person I would ever bow to. He was the same damned Grand Emperor who killed me in my third life and refined me into a cauldron.

That was only my third life! Back then, I was so pure, and didn’t understand the treachery of the heart. So what if I took a few treasures from some random species? And all I wanted to do was play around with Dark Serenity’s imperial crown! What’s the big deal about that? Dark Serenity didn’t even complain about it. It was that bitch Grand Emperor who took it upon himself to kill me.

And you know, I would have been fine with being killed, if that was all that happened. But no, he had to turn my corpse into a pill cauldron. How outrageous! And he even made my skull into the lid? Completely ridiculous! Thankfully I spotted the cauldron in Yue Dong’s memories. Otherwise, an entire lifetime of planning wouldn’t have been enough to track down the corpse of my pure and innocent third life.

1. Yun is a surname, but it also means cloud. So the ‘cloud’ from the Cloud Heaven Bell is the same as their clan surname. ☜

2. The time Erniu, Master Seventh, and Xu Qing visited the Immortal Skills Hall in Sea-Sealing County was in chapter 519. ☜

In the Immortal Skills Hall of the eastern Devilbirds, the unique properties of the bone cauldron made it impossible for anyone to know what was happening inside it. But they could see the cauldron vibrating. The nine-colored flames indicated that the refinement process had already started.

Previously, the grand elder had held the upper hand. But not now, and the immortal adepts who had sided with him were now very anxious as they cast glances at the emissary from the first mountain.

Young Lord Yun in his fancy robe was also nervous about how things would turn out. He knew about the conflict between Sir Blood Dust and Yue Dong, and was aware that the former was intent on killing the latter. That said, what Sir Blood Dust had said just now was good for Yue Dong. For now, all he could do was place all his hope in Sir Blood Dust.

The emissaries from the other mountains said nothing. They just looked at Xu Qing and the first emissary. Of the two of them, one had risen to prominence recently, and was about as famous as you could get, while the other was a very senior figure with a good reputation.

Of course, the Imperial Sovereigns who backed those two, the tenth and first, were much the same. In other words, whoever came out on top of this clash would make the final decision.

“Look, boy,” said the old man from the first mountain. “I admire you for what you did among the western Devilbirds. But you’re in the east now, and you’re pushing things a bit too far.”

Inside, he was sighing regretfully. He didn’t want to take any action right now, but he did represent an Imperial Sovereign, so doing nothing wouldn’t be appropriate. Unfortunately, if you ride a tiger, it's hard to get off, and thus, he slowly rose from his throne. Nine-world Smoldering God fluctuations rolled off him with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force as projections of worlds appeared around him.

He took a step forward and it caused the entire Immortal Skills Hall to tremble. Even the sky outside flashed with wild colors.

Xu Qing didn’t react at all to the display of force. Although he wasn’t confident that he could beat a nine-world Smoldering God in a fight, just as when dealing with Sir Westdevil, he could definitely inflict some nasty damage. That said, he didn’t need to win. He just needed to buy enough time.

Therefore, he also rose to his feet, his hair whipping about him, his blood-red robe flapping. Blood clouds rolled out and around, which turned into blood dragons that howled loudly. What was more, the godly authority of sound stirred within him, all while the godly authority of fate turned into a carving knife that glinted coldly. Black lotus flowers appeared around him as well, which formed a high level of defense.

All of this caused quite a reaction from the others present, and everyone was thinking about what Sir Blood Dust had recently done among the western Devilbirds.

“Grand Emperor Netherflame’s secret magic.”

“It provides amazing defenses, can shake nine-world Smoldering Gods, and basically makes you invincible to anything under an Imperial Sovereign!”

“Don’t forget that Sir Westdevil actually died, right? Although the exact details aren’t clear, we know that Sir Blood Dust has some incredibly astonishing trump cards.”

As everyone reeled, the old man from the first mountain vanished, then reappeared in midair.

Xu Qing also blurred and reappeared in midair. It looked like the two might begin fighting at any moment.

However, that was when laughter broke out from a spot between the two of them. Lin Kun, the fifth mountain representative Xu Qing had run into earlier, suddenly appeared in between them, his nine-world aura exploding out to create a barrier.

“Do the two of you mind taking some advice from me? The ancient agreement states that although the Imperial Sovereign mountains can interfere with the internal affairs of the Immortal Skills Hall, the reality is that throughout all history, the Imperial Sovereign mountains have never exercised that right.

“Brother Zhang, as the official representative of the first Imperial Sovereign mountain, are you really sure that at this exact moment, when the fires of war burn all around us, and Grand Emperor Netherflame’s secluded meditation facilities are about to be opened, that you want to respond to Sir Blood Dust’s formal dissent by forcefully interfering in the affairs of the Immortal Skills Hall?”

Lin Kun looked deeply at the old man from the first mountain. “Brother Zhang, there will be consequences for this. In fact, before I came here today, my venerable father ordered me to support any decisions made by the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain. As such, I highly suggest that you think thrice before taking action.”

The old man from the first mountain had a very grim look on his face. He looked at Lin Kun. He looked at Xu Qing again. Then, after a long moment of silence, he gave a cold harrumph.

“Since you put it that way, Fellow Daoist Lin, I suppose I’ll just drop the matter.” With that, he returned to his throne, sat down, and closed his eyes. Now that he had backed down, the conflict was over.

Xu Qing didn't care one way or another. He had been able to tell from the beginning that, though the old man from the first mountain had been acting aggressively, he hadn’t been interested in fighting. In other words, averting a fight was the best outcome.

It was really Lin Kun who had resolved the issue, so Xu Qing looked over at him and nodded.

Lin Kun grinned. He obviously had his own motives for doing what he did. For one thing, he had sensed that the old man from the first mountain had been looking for a way to get out of an open conflict. It hadn’t been hard for Lin Kun to provide that to him. Another reason was that he wanted to show some goodwill toward Sir Blood Dust.

His one action had resulted in two benefits. What was more, he had cleverly highlighted that the fifth Imperial Sovereign wanted to respect the Immortal Skills Hall’s right to select their own grand immortal adept. It was just like the saying killing three birds with one stone. Still smiling, he went back to his place along with Xu Qing.

The scene that had just played out caused all of the grand elder’s supporters among the immortal adepts to look a bit pale in the face. And though they weren’t exactly happy with this result, it was clear that the emissaries had made up their minds, and there was nothing to do about it. They could only grin and bear it.

Young Lord Yun breathed a sigh of relief and looked back at the cauldron in the middle of the arena. It was currently letting off some intense fluctuations.

***

Given what Yue Dong’s head had just said, and the fact that the cauldron had been fused shut, the grand elder was reeling in mind and heart. He almost couldn’t believe what was happening. There was no doubt about it; Yue Dong’s words surpassed anything he could have imagined.

“You’re saying... that this cauldron is made from your bones? You’re... the megavillain that Grand Emperor Immortal Skill killed? That's not possible!”

The grand elder struggled to control his breathing. His first reaction was to disbelieve. But there was no doubt that his control over the cauldron had disappeared. And it was also true that the words spoken by Yue Dong had caused the flesh and blood to fuse with the bone. It truly surpassed believability.

“It doesn’t matter if you’re lying or telling the truth. You’re not strong enough. That’s the most important thing. If you were strong enough, you wouldn’t have to resort to tricks like this.”

The grand elder’s eyes glittered coldly. He knew that the truth didn’t really matter. What mattered... was whether or not he could come out on top in the end. Therefore, the killing intent in his eyes and heart began to rage.

“I’ll put you to death! That’ll resolve everything!”

The grand elder burst into motion, heading right toward Yue Dong’s head. His nine-world cultivation base, combined with his gruish immortal skill, gave him astonishing speed. In the shortest of moments, he was right in front of her.

It didn’t matter how quickly that head fell back. Trying to evade was pointless. The grand elder pulled his hand back and then viciously slapped the head. A boom rang out, and Yue Dong’s head exploded.

And yet, the grand elder’s face just turned grimmer. That was because... as soon as the head exploded, all of the flesh and blood converged together... and the head formed anew!

But this time, it didn’t look like Yue Dong. It was Erniu. “You want to put me to death, you old codger? You couldn’t do it in an entire lifetime!”

Not offering a response, the grand elder attacked again, this time using an immortal skill. The only thing visible was a huge gray hand that appeared in front of Erniu. It instantly stabbed into him to drag out his soul. What flesh remained rotted into a black sludge that dripped down to the ground. However... it only took a moment for a blue worm to fly out from within that sludge. It exploded into a blood mist, which then shrank back down to reveal Erniu’s head.

This time, however, he looked quite pale. Despite that, he was still shouting arrogantly. “Bring it on, bitch! Let’s see what happens first, fool, you killing me, or me killing you! Let’s do it! Let’s have a little contest and see who’s tougher between the two of us!

“You’d better watch out for my immortal skill, and let me tell you, I want your immortal skill! And incidentally, I’m not interested in wasting my damn time studying immortal skills. I’m going to refine you and gobble down your immortal skill in one bite!”

The grand elder was really starting to get nervous, as the refinement process of the cauldron was already starting to affect him. Therefore, he didn’t hesitate to attack again. And yet, every time he blew up Erniu’s head, it would gruishly form again. The only upside was that it looked paler and paler each time. This enemy seemed like some sort of freak who couldn’t be wiped out of existence no matter how hard you tried.

Meanwhile, in the time that had been bought, Erniu crazily unleashed his trump card. “You have your wind, rain, thunder, lightning, and fire? Well I’ll use my damned metal, wood, water, fire, and earth! I hereby summon from my past life’s... eternal frigid water!”

He opened his mouth and spat out a stream of ice-cold water that filled the cauldron and made the refinement process become even more intense.

The grand elder took a deep breath. Looking more anxious than ever, he launched another attack.

After Erniu was resurrected again, he shouted, “I hereby summon my current life’s... undying life force fire!”

A pop rang out as Erniu exploded, then formed again. “I hereby summon the North Emperor’s corpse coffin of wood! I hereby summon from the immortal world the North Emperor’s burial earth!”

With every shout, he spat out something. Life force flame. A coffin’s wood. Burial earth. The refinement in the cauldron grew even more mighty.

After all, each of those four items was extraordinary. Collectively, they included his past and present life, as well as the personhood of the North Emperor’s coffin and burial soil. With that bolstering the refinement, it became heaven-shakingly, earth-shatteringly powerful.

Given how strong the grand elder was, he immediately ignited his fleshly body. His soul also burned. And in that critical moment, his killing intent reached an even higher level. He again attacked Erniu.

Erniu exploded, then formed again. His eyes were flashing with a crazy light. This was the pinnacle of life, and as such, he shouted, “And now, water, fire, earth, and wood are complete. The only piece missing is metal! I hereby summon the karmic bones of metal! I shall borrow the boundless power of karma to shatter your immortal skill!” freewebnovel.com

As Erniu howled deafeningly, he took out a finger-nail sized piece of bone. Astonishingly, it was the color gold! Dazzling golden light shone out along with an incomparably powerful karmic force.

The grand elder’s face fell.

Erniu was wrapped up in both craziness and weakness. But he was also feeling very pleased with himself.

“This is from my little Junior Brother, from when he self-detonated all those years ago in the imperial capital. Spirit energy burned, drawing on flesh and blood until the entire body shattered, bones included, to produce this little treasure! Back then, I managed to snatch it away secretly. And today... I’ll use it to take care of you!”[1]

1. Xu Qing self-detonated in chapter 966. ☜

Xu Qing sat in the arena in the Immortal Skills Hall, frowning slightly. After taking in his surroundings, he focused on the bone cauldron. A moment ago he had sensed something very peculiar, as if something that belonged to him had suddenly appeared. Unfortunately, when he focused on that sensation, it became vague. He justuldn’t pin down what was causing it.

What’s going on?

No amount of thought would clear up the matter, though, so he put it aside and kept looking at the cauldron.

Eldest Brother should be wrapping things up with a success shortly. I wonder how he managed to turn things around with the grand elder. I bet it has something to do with the cauldron. By the time this is over, it should be very close to when the empress opens Grand Emperor Netherflame’s secluded meditation facilities.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. He was fully aware that when it came to his cultivation base level, he was at a standstill thanks to his fleshly body. He had put a lot of thought into how to proceed, but currently only had two good ideas.

The first was to use that white dust and the Mask of Wishes. However, that was only the backup plan. The other option, which seemed more likely to succeed, was to find a destined opportunity in the secluded meditation facilities.

I hope that place has something that can help me achieve a breakthrough! But if not, then when I get out of the Devilbird holy land, I’ll go back to South Phoenix and go into seclusion. I’ll use the Mask of Wishes to make a clone, and then use the white dust to wipe out any karma from it.

Hentinued to think about those matters as time passed.

The immortal adepts were doing much the same thing. They were wrapped up in various thoughts as they watched the pill cauldron. Slowly but surely, the immortal adepts were starting to get really nervous. Some wanted the grand elder to succeed. Others were rooting for Yue Dong. Regardless of who came out on top in the end... the eastern Devilbirds’ Immortal Skills Hall was going to have a new grand immortal adept soon.

Ofurse, the atmosphere was a lot more intense inside of the cauldron. The grand elder was nervous as he struggled, shouted, andnstantly attacked Erniu. Erniu’s head exploded and formed again repeatedly, and he was just as nervous. And yet, even though he was nervous, he was also giving full reign to his craziness.

“You’re dead,” he said through gritted teeth. “Dead, dead, dead!”

The five items he had spat out thatnformed to metal, wood, water, fire, and earth were bolstering the refinement process. And thanks to the outworking of his will, the interior of the cauldron was burning with great intensity. The will of refinement was growing increasingly shocking.

As far as the grand elder wasncerned, that meant that death was looming. He was having more and more trouble standing strong. Ten hours passed.

Outside of the cauldron, Young Lord Yun and the immortal adepts were nervous and restless. A killing air was building up again.

Then, all of a sudden, a deafening booming rang out from the cauldron.

The Imperial Sovereign mountain emissaries, who had been sitting there with their eyes closed, all looked up. That included Xu Qing. His eyesntained anticipation. And as he looked at the cauldron... the booming grew louder.

The lid of the cauldron clanged open. Tenlored flame erupted from within, climbing high to the top of the arena, where it made a flame vortex that swirled out in all directions.

At the same time, a blurry figure floated up from the inside of the cauldron! Upon emerging fully into the open, the figure grew clear. It was Yue Dong, clad in a red gown. Her hair drifted around her beautiful face, and in the light of the flame, it looked like it was dancing.

The immortal adepts were all shaken to there, the reason being that there were people behind her! Astonishingly, the middle-aged, young man, and boy forms of the grand elder were there. As for his true form, it was nowhere to be seen. Apparently he had been devoured and replaced by Yue Dong!

Yue Dong’s eyes opened. The moment they did, the emotions of the crowd were stirred like the strings of an instrument.

It was the immortal skill of Six Thieves Deceive Life! As the emotions stirred, Yue Dongldly waved a hand, causing the cauldron below to rise up into the air. It grew smaller and smaller, until it was the size of a hand. Then it floated over to hover above her right palm, where it spun endlessly. Incredible pressure rolled out.

Xu Qing calmed himself. He was now certain that the cauldron must be related to one of his Eldest Brother’s past lives. He was about to look away from Yue Dong, when he suddenly frowned and looked more closely. At her forehead.

Though nothing looked out of the ordinary about that spot, Xu Qing got the feeling that there was something extremely familiar there. Something that came from him.

Young Lord Yun took a deep breath. His gaze softened as he faced Yue Dong, bowed, and loudly said, “Well met, Grand Immortal Adept!”

The immortal adepts who had backed Yue Dong were finally reacting. They were excitedly bowing. Yue Dong’s success meant that, going forward, they would be the driving force in the Immortal Skills Hall. The immortal adepts who had backed the grand elder looked bitter. They knew that they had lost and had no choice but to bow their heads and clasp hands.

The only people who qualified to not clasp hands and bow were the emissaries from the Imperial Sovereign mountains. However, out of respect for the new grand immortal adept, they stood and inclined their heads.

“Many thanks to all of you forming to the ceremony,” Yue Dong said calmly. “The formalities are over, so all of you can feel free to take your leave. However, I would like one of you to stay for a moment.” Her gaze shifted to Xu Qing, whereupon it turned veryld. “Sir Blood Dust, the time hasme to sort out our issues.”

Xu Qing looked calmly at her, focusing on her forehead. “That’s just what I was thinking.”

From this point onward in this chapter, there is A LOT of fancy-sounding stuff similar to this, in other words, bits and pieces of things taken from real life texts. At a certain point, I just stopped doing research on each one, because A) they don’t relate to their “real-life” applications and B) the point is not to understand what they mean; they are just supposed to soundol. ☜

A sound like singing immortals drifted over the horizon as a group of immortal adepts appeared, shouldering a massive palanquin. Inside of the palanquin was a woman. She had a very arrogant look on her face, but then....

“Come here,” the empress said.

Shivering, the woman flew over to the empress and stood obediently by her side. Meanwhile, Xu Qing also flew over, surrounded by a seething blood cloud. He stood at the empress’ other side.

Now there were six people in each group. The empress and Grand Emperor Devilbird were each leading a group of five others.

After glancing at Xu Qing and Erniu, Grand Emperor Devilbird said, “Grand Emperor Netherflame is the paramount entity of our Devilbird holy land. I originally didn’t approve of opening his secluded meditation facilities. But given that Lu Lingzi is his apprentice, and that his other apprentices gave their approval, then I had no reason to reject the proposal.

“However, I do have one demand. All of you must show respect! The primary objective in going inside is to perform an inspection. We cannot disturb the Grand Emperor’s meditation! If it turns out that the Grand Emperor truly has passed away... then all of you will kowtow three times, then do nothing more to disturb him.”

By the time Grand Emperor Devilbird finished speaking, his voice bordered on being aggressive. Everyone clasped hands and bowed in a respectful show of acknowledgment. Seeing that caused Grand Emperor Devilbird’s expression to soften. Then he turned to the enormous dao altar. Eyes glimmering with reminiscence, he sighed.

“Grand Emperor Netherflame’s secluded meditation facilities might seem like they’re in the dao altar. The reality is that they are a mysterious heaven beyond heaven. They were acquired from the starry sky by Grand Emperor Netherflame.

“If he has truly perished, then because the heaven beyond heaven is sealed, it will contain all of his memories incarnated as worlds.

“It’s also possible that the Grand Emperor’s legacy will be there. Before the Grand Emperor returned, no one had any clue about the details of his cultivation in the starry sky, or what he did out there. Nor does anyone know what else exists in his memories.

“Out of respect for the Grand Emperor, I hope that if any of you see such things, you not spread word about them later.”

Grand Emperor Devilbird shook his head and strode forward. Reaching the apex of the dao altar, he sat down and waved his hand. Instantly, the entire dao altar rumbled and changed from being dim into shining brilliantly.

“You may now do as you see fit. I will stand as dharma protector for all of you going forward.”

The dao altar shone brilliantly as Grand Emperor Devilbird’s words echoed through heaven and earth. The Imperial Sovereigns of the eastern Devilbirds were observing intently. So were the western Devilbirds. The same went for the rogue cultivators and the various clans. Everyone was watching.

Under the focus of countless gazes and streams of divine will, the empress strode toward the dao altar. There was no explosion of light. There was no complicated ceremony. The only thing that happened was that a third eye opened on the empress’ forehead.

One by one, drops of blood flew out. It was the blood of the Lan Clan, which had the same origin as the Grand Emperor’s blood. It pulsed with something mysterious, including natural and magical laws.

The blood converged in front of the empress, then landed on the dao altar. Under the gaze of the third eye, they became a blood-red vortex that rumbled loudly as it revealed a pathway.

Without any hesitation, the empress stepped inside. Xu Qing and Erniu similarly showed no hesitation as they flew after the empress.

Next came Young Lord Yun, Lin Kun, and the young man from the ninth Imperial Sovereign mountain. The group from the western Devilbirds followed. After they were inside, the vortex of blood became a mist that spread out and vanished. The vortex was gone.

Atop the dao altar, Grand Emperor Devilbird closed his eyes. A big show packed with secret agendas....

***

Xu Qing wasn’t sure how everyone else was reacting upon entering Grand Emperor Netherflame’s secluded meditation facilities. But he was frowning.

Upon entering the vortex, his vision swam. When things became clear again, he heard music, smelled rouge, and saw dancing....

He was standing in a luxurious palace constructed from elegantly carved jade. Also inside the palace were no less than a thousand young women wearing flowing gowns that were nearly transparent. The skin beneath the fabric would stir the heart of anyone. The women were either singing, dancing, or conversing intimately, making the entire palace seem like a place of luxury.

The women came from all species, but there was one thing about them that was the same. They were all extremely beautiful. All of them were looking at him with either caution or desire. It was as if fire burned in their eyes.

Xu Qing was already on guard. Looking around, he realized that the palace was surrounded by some unknown land mass. After scanning his surroundings with divine will, he was shocked to realize that... he was the only male present. This seemed to be a nation made up entirely of women.

What was more, his own physical appearance had changed. He was now a young man, and he was seated on a throne at the head of the hall. It was almost as if he was an emperor of some sort. Spread out in front of him was a meal of the finest delicacies, including food and alcohol fit for immortals and spirits.

Is this one of the memories of Grand Emperor Netherflame, transformed into a world?

***

Erniu was thinking the same thing. However, Erniu was currently located on a barren planet a great distance away.

Erniu was visibly taken aback. As he looked around, he saw that this planet was completely empty. It had a gray sky, blackened lands, and no plants whatsoever. He saw rotting flesh and bones. He saw piles of excrement. And there were even huge maggots that were now crawling toward him. The noxious smell that filled the area made him want to vomit.

This place was like hell. As for himself, he was a rotting corpse.

Is this... a world made from the memories of Grand Emperor Netherflame? How could he remember something like this? Did everyone else come here also?

Alarmed, he looked at the maggots, wondering if little Ah Qing was inside one of them.

On the barren wasteland planet, Erniu sighed regretfully. He had not found little Ah Qing in any of the maggots....

Next, his attention turned to the corpses, and he begrudgingly continued his search.

***

A full-scale war had broken out in another of Netherflame’s memory worlds, a world that consisted of a starry sky.

Leading a massive army was Netherflame himself, clad in a pitch-black suit of armor that made it look like he had climbed out of death itself. He was waging war against a host of nonhumans, unleashing mad and brutal slaughter. The sound of magical techniques mixed with terrifying screams to echo out nonstop.

Eventually, a figure appeared off in the distance, pulsing with astonishing godly might. Seemingly unconcerned with either side of the conflict, that figure shot directly toward Netherflame. A moment later, that individual's finger stabbed into Netherflame’s forehead, shattering his body, shattering the starry sky, and shattering the memory world.

As the fragments scattered, the figure became clear. It was the empress. Unlike Xu Qing and Erniu, who had appeared in the memory worlds in Netherflame’s place, the empress had come in true form.

Did you really perish, causing your memories to scatter and become worlds? Or did you use scattered memories to create an outer layer of defense? Which is it, Netherflame? Are you actually dead, or are you really alive?

The empress continued onward.

***

The others who had entered the secluded meditation facilities were in various locations. Some were searching their surroundings, some were ignoring them, some were immersing themselves in the worlds they had entered. Each were doing different things based on their own different goals.

For example, on a sprawling pitch-black plain was the old man from the western Devilbirds. The ground seemed to contract beneath him with each step he took. Though he looked like he was strolling along casually, his every step took him a shocking distance. As he walked, he was accompanied by a clanking sound, as if there were iron chains wrapped around him beneath his black cloak.

Eventually, he reached a section of broken land that turned out to be a massive ravine. Upon reaching the edge of the ravine, he looked down into its depths. He chuckled hoarsely.

So this is where it is.

***

As I recall, Grand Emperor Devilbird said that if we encounter memory worlds, it indicates that Grand Emperor Netherflame perished. freewebnovel.com

Xu Qing looked around at all the women in the grand hall. He definitely wasn’t going to take action before analyzing the situation fully.

That said, I can’t just blindly trust what Grand Emperor Devilbird says. Regardless, this seems to be one of Grand Emperor Netherflame’s memory worlds. In that case... what’s the significance of this particular memory? Is it a legacy? Or are the worlds like some sort of maze that I need to navigate?

As Xu Qing pondered these things, his gaze suddenly shifted to the right and turned cold.

On that side of him was a bewitchingly charming young woman, clad in a sheer garment that hardly covered half her body. Her cheeks were flush, and her eyes flashed seductively as she crawled toward him on all fours. Her manner of crawling only accentuated her alluring curves.

Xu Qing said nothing. His eyes grew colder.

The coldness of his gaze caused the crawling woman to shiver. Her expression became one of terror, and she slowly backed away from him.

He looked away, only to frown a moment later. A ripping sensation appeared, filling the world, the hall, and him. It was as if this world was rejecting him. Along with it came a sense of great danger, as if his action just now had attracted the attention of the world he occupied.

What was even more noteworthy to Xu Qing was that he felt an immense pressure, as if an entire mountain was weighing down on him. The upside was that the ripping sensation wasn’t very strong, as if it was only a warning.

“How interesting...” he murmured. Eyes narrowing, he stood, walked off the dais, across the hall, and toward the doors.

Along the way, the women in the hall noticed him, and looks of terror and confusion appeared on their faces.

Xu Qing ignored them. He wanted to find out what was causing the ripping sensation. As he neared the doors, the women in the hall seemed to become more agitated, all while their voices faded, becoming softer and softer. By the time Xu Qing was only one step away from the doors... the hall was completely silent.

The music stopped. The lascivious sounds ceased. There wasn’t even the sound of breathing. And every single woman present was looking directly at Xu Qing, their gazes cold and full of death. The ripping sensation appeared again.

Xu Qing stopped in place and looked back at the women. Now he understood where the ripping sensation was coming from.

This world is indeed one of Grand Emperor Netherflame’s memory fragments. And I’m standing in for him in this memory. Therefore, I’m supposed to do the same things he did back when this event actually played out.

If I don’t, then I’ll be viewed as an enemy invader, and the ripping sensation will appear. The entire world will view me with hostility, and terrifying pressure will build up. In other words, if I want things to go smoothly, I need to do what Grand Emperor Netherflame did.

After some thought, he walked back across the hall and back to the throne.

As he did, the music came back. The women’s expressions returned to normal. The licentious sounds started up again. Many of the women neared Xu Qing, bowing their heads flirtatiously, undulating their bodies, their expressions those of desire.

And yet, Xu Qing continued to frown. It was because he could still sense the ripping sensation. Returning to the throne hadn’t caused it to go away.

Leaving isn’t the right thing to do. But neither is staying. So what did Netherflame do back then?

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered as he made a decision. Turning to one of the approaching women, he clenched his hand into a fist and punched her. There was a boom, and the ripping sensation vanished. Xu Qing realized at that moment that when this event occurred in the past, Netherflame had also chosen to launch an attack.

A moment later, the doors of the hall opened, and Xu Qing walked out. The wind carried the aroma of flowers, and as it lifted Xu Qing’s hair, it caused the doors to swing open. As it blew into the hall, it became clear... that though there were no corpses inside, there also weren’t any living women. There were only a host of withered flower pistils.

Everything was an illusion.

As soon as Xu Qing walked out of the hall, the nation of women transformed dramatically.

The earth quaked. The sky went dark. The wind and clouds seethed. Buildings crumbled as huge vines spread out, covering everything. And at the ends of the vine were hosts of branches, with flowers and flower pistils. Each flower pistil was a woman.

The nation of women was crumbling as the massive vines spread, each of which split dozens of times to create dozens of pistils. Licentious sounds built up, growing louder and louder as it surrounded Xu Qing.

And then, as the ground in the middle of the nation of women collapsed, a 30,000-meter flower rose up. This was the main flower, and in the middle of all the petals was a single flower pistil, which was the queen.

It’s a euphoria iris!

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. He recognized this flower. He had seen one back in Daybreak Prefecture, and had rescued Ningyan from it.... The main difference was that the version he had seen all those years ago was very small compared to this one, which was gargantuan.[1]

The moment Xu Qing looked at it, all of the countless pistil-women looked at him, laughed, then raced toward him.

Face completely expressionless, Xu Qing shot up into the air to avoid the vines. Then he thrust his right hand out and pushed down. The power of taboo poison created a black miasma that shot toward the vines. Wherever it passed, the laughter of the pistil-women turned into shrieks of agony as they melted.

The ripping sensation came back, stronger than ever, filling him with a ripple of fear. It was as if some terrifying entity was coming, something that he couldn’t possibly fight. The more he attacked, the stronger the sensation got.

“Hold on,” he murmured. He retracted the taboo poison and backed up, all while analyzing the situation. As the vines whistled toward him, the queen pointed at him.

Instantly, a host of innumerable flowers popped into being around Xu Qing, and their pistils exploded toward him. Xu Qing evaded all but one of the pistils, which hit him and left behind a deep wound. Put precisely, it slashed through Netherflame’s body within this memory world. But Xu Qing could feel the pain it inflicted.

The memory itself is attacking me!

As he experienced the pain, he realized that the ripping sensation was ebbing again. Apparently, the combination of being wounded, and the arrival of that terrifying entity, was causing the ripping to go away.

This all seems to indicate one thing. I can’t fight back! This flower is going to kill me! Does that mean that Netherflame was killed by this flower?

Xu Qing refused to believe it. Unfortunately, the ripping sensation seemed to indicate that something even more terrifying was about to happen.

There’s still something else I can try!

Eyes flashing, he summoned the carving knife made of the godly authority of fate. But then, even as his sea of consciousness surged, cracking sounds suddenly rang out from his bag of holding.

Xu Qing backed up, a puzzled expression appearing on his face.

The golden rat egg in his bag of holding was starting to hatch. It seemed like it could be because of the carving knife, although he couldn’t be sure. A stream of golden light shot out, swirled around the egg, devoured the egg, then emerged from the bag of holding without him doing a thing.

A small golden rat landed on his palm. With some struggle, it opened its eyes, looked at Xu Qing, and squeaked. Then it nuzzled his palm and pulsed with emotional fluctuations of familiarity.

All of a sudden, the memory world began to change. The sound vanished. The flower pistils stopped moving. The queen froze in place, as did her facial expression.

Everything seemed to go still.

Xu Qing was stunned. This definitely was not something he had predicted would happen.

He had been aware that these golden rats were extraordinary. After all, the old man from the Fifth Star Ring had one, and it was intelligent enough to flee through time from him. Because of that, Xu Qing had been looking forward to seeing what his rat would be like. But regardless of that, he could never have predicted that the moment the rat emerged, it would do something like this.

***

Meanwhile, in a much deeper memory world in Grand Emperor Netherflame’s secluded meditation facilities, there was a very strange heaven and earth.

In this place, heaven was made of flesh, and it was covered with countless downy hairs. Every single strand of that hair was a memory world. As for the earth, it was made up of a transparent sea. On top of the sea was a conglomeration of flesh that looked like a huge tumor.

Inside of the tumor was a middle-aged cultivator, seated cross-legged. He looked threatening without being angry, and pulsed with an extremely ancient and terrifying aura. His eyes were currently closed. All of a sudden, they snapped open, and he looked out into the memory world.

“So, a chronoflitter? Who would have guessed that an animal like that would appear now?”[2]

1. Xu Qing rescued Ningyan from the euphoria iris in chapter 491. There are some slight differences in the description of the flowers between that chapter and this one. What’s more, the author actually didn’t use the same name in this chapter, although it’s very close (he just changed one character). My guess is that he didn’t take time to go back and double-check what he called it before. I’m going with the original version of the name to maintain continuity. Another confusing element is pistil/stamen. In Chinese, there is one word that can mean both things. Essentially, that word means “floral reproductive organ.” You can get more specific in Chinese by adding the word male or female to clarify if it’s a stamen or pistil. I feel like it would be weird to use “floral reproductive organs,” and would rather use pistil or stamen depending on how it’s described. In chapter 491, the way it described those flower parts corresponds to what we would call the stamen in English. In this chapter, the way it describes a single thing in the middle of the flowers seems to correspond to a pistil. I don’t think the author is concerned with the difference between pistils and stamens. In Chinese, the term is much less scientific-sounding. ☜

2. I’ve coined the term ‘chronoflitter’ after consulting with the author. In Chinese, the name of the animal is made up of two characters. One is the character for “leave/depart” and the other is “the present.” It’s a fairly obvious meaning when you read it in Chinese. It means “to leave the present.” That said, it’s also not necessarily so clear what it means, because each character can have multiple meanings. After struggling for a while without much context, I finally reached out to the author for clarification. For the English version, I’m combining the prefix “chrono” which relates to time, and “flit” as in “to flit away.” ☜

The golden rat that belonged to the old man from the Fifth Star Ring was so quick it could move faster than time. It left no traces of its passage, and could also hide within time itself. Only a truly almighty expert could ever detect it. That just went to show how terrifying it was.

Of course, to reach the same level as that rat from the Fifth Star Ring, this new rat would have to mature. And that would involve going through a host of tribulations, the type that were so difficult that only one out of a hundred individuals could survive. Accomplishing that would require paying a huge cost.

It wasn’t just that mysterious middle-aged cultivator who noticed what happened with the Chronoflitter.

Outside of the Devilbird holy land, in the Revered Ancient mainland, in the cave in Fardark territory, Sir Nightcrusher suddenly opened his eyes. They shone with bright golden light as hē looked up in the direction of the Devilbird holy land. Hīs blood was telling hīm that a descendant of hīs had just been born.[1]

A complicated look appeared in those eyes. Years ago, when Master Righteous Veil captured hīm and extinguished hīs godfire, hē did not have any descendants. Those two eggs were really hīs last hope to gain freedom. Using an innate ability, hē had extracted some of his bloodline power, then used time itself to conceal it from karma, and thus prevent Master Righteous Veil from noticing. And in the end... Xu Qing and Erniu took the eggs away. [2]

Although it seemed like that entire event was random, the truth was that only hē knew how much of it played out according to hīs own plan. Sir Nightcrusher eventually closed hīs eyes, whereupon hīs life force began to seep away. The only thing left behind was a faint murmur.

“Chronoflitter. Chronoflitter. The Chronoflitter Dynasty. Burrow through time. Pierce myriad spaces. Flee without a trace....”

***

In the nation of women in Grand Emperor Netherflame’s secluded meditation facilities, Xu Qing was feeling deeply shaken. He looked at the little golden rat in his palm, then at the huge euphoria iris. The moment the golden rat had been born, the latter went completely still and quiet. It wasn’t just the flower. Everything around him reacted the same. It went silent.

Only Xu Qing and the golden rat weren’t affected. The little rat squeaked and nuzzled Xu Qing’s finger. Then it seemed to pulse with incredible hunger. Flashing with golden light, it flew off Xu Qing’s palm, opened its mouth, and took a big bite out of space itself.

A rift appeared as space was torn open, and the rat swallowed the portion it had bitten. Unfortunately, it was still a juvenile, so doing this sort of thing was a bit difficult for it. The action had weakened it. However, it was still hungry, so it ravenously took another bite.

Space split open, and that disturbed the stillness. An instant later, everything went back to normal. The euphoria iris started flailing about again.

Astonishingly to Xu Qing, as everything went back to normal, a terrifying will approached through the void, heading toward the euphoria iris. Just barely sensing this will caused Xu Qing to shiver in fear, as if he were sinking into a sea of death.

There was no time for thinking or planning. Without the slightest hesitation, he grabbed the little golden rat, who seemed intent on taking a third bite. Then Xu Qing blurred into motion, becoming a stream of light that shot through the gap in space. As the terrifying will closed in at top speed, Xu Qing vanished.

Once through, he caught sight of a dazzling starry sky. He had no idea if there was a real starry sky outside of the memory world. But he knew that, regardless, he was in danger. Therefore, he didn’t slow down a bit.

A moment later, the sense of danger from that terrifying will vanished. Yet he didn’t let his guard down. That was because this boundless and indescribably beautiful starry sky also contained danger.

There was a tempest churning there. It swept everywhere, shattering heavenly bodies as it turned into something like a black hole that could devour anything and everything.

Xu Qing was on the edge of the tempest. Given the critical nature of the moment, he didn’t spend time thinking. He waved his hand to summon the Sageheaven Pagoda, and stepped inside. Without a moment of hesitation, he sent the pagoda racing away from the tempest.

This was the best thing Xu Qing could think to do. After all, the mysterious pagoda was designed to traverse starry skies. And the sageheaven god vine, which was part of the pagoda, was a mutant entity from the starry sky.

After about an hour, the speeding pagoda had left the outer border of the tempest. Seeing that, Xu Qing breathed a sigh of relief. At the same time, he could sense longing from the sageheaven god vine.

It was a longing directed toward the starry sky itself. It deeply wished that Xu Qing would let it leave the pagoda and roam wildly. After a bit of thought, Xu Qing cast his senses out to confirm that the tempest was a great distance away. Then he sent a message of approval to the vine.

The vine let loose a sound like a cheer. Unwrapping from the pagoda, it swelled in size, reaching a length of 30,000 meters. Then, it wrapped one end of itself around the pagoda, while the other end swayed back and forth.

Seeing that, Xu Qing stepped out of the pagoda. The vine swirled around, letting loose more cheering. The free end then stretched forward so he could step onto it. A tremor passed through it, and then a mysterious will spread out, and it started speeding through the starry sky like a fish through water.

If an ordinary cultivator could see what was happening, they would be shaken to the core. There was Xu Qing, his long robe whipping about him as he sat atop the god vine. The vine was 30,000 meters long, and looked completely glorious. It glittered with starlight, and its leaves pulsated as the starry sky seemed to part, making a path for it to fly along like a dragon.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. From the sense of joy coming from the vine, and its speed, he could tell that the starry sky truly was its domain.

As they sped through the starry sky, they passed countless fragments that shone like heavenly bodies. There were images in the fragments. They were memory worlds!

However, after what he had just experienced in the world of the euphoria irises, Xu Qing knew how dangerous the memory worlds could be. He wouldn’t go into one casually, and thus, instructed the god vine to skirt them.

At the same time, he started searching for whatever worlds contained the empress and his Eldest Brother.

This place is where a Grand Emperor went into secluded meditation. There is danger everywhere. Finding the empress as quickly as possible is definitely the right thing to do.

Eyes narrowing, Xu Qing had the vine speed up.

***

In the blood-red world, in the transparent tumor of flesh atop the huge sea, the middle-aged cultivator who had sensed the chronoflitter suddenly looked up again. He looked up at the fine hair covering the flesh that was the dome of heaven, and then his pupils constricted, as if he had just caught sight of something completely unbelievable.

An instant later, he struggled to control his breathing as he closed his eyes to think.

His eyes opened a moment later, and they glowed with a strange light as he raised his hand and pointed to the dome of heaven. The fine hair above stopped moving briefly, then started intertwining as if arranging into a specific pattern.

***

Xu Qing was far away in the starry sky, in a place where there were seven or eight memory worlds. However, those worlds were slowly blurring until they disappeared, to be replaced by a far larger memory world. What was more, that memory world was moving forward slowly, almost as if it were making a path for Xu Qing to follow.

Sometime later, the god vine shot through the starry sky, bringing Xu Qing close to the memory fragment ahead, which was larger than any other he had seen up to this point. The image within that memory fragment was a necropolis. After some thought, he instructed the god vine to go around it.

But then, golden light flared in his bag of holding, and the little golden rat shot out, pulsing with a sensation of longing. It became a beam of golden light that shot with astonishing speed toward the memory world.

Xu Qing’s face fell. He had no time to stop it, and thus, could only frown and send the god vine flying toward the memory fragment.

A moment later, he entered it. His vision blurred, he felt like he was piercing through something. He felt the exact same sensation as when he’d entered the world of euphoria irises.

When his vision cleared, he saw a sprawling necropolis in front of him. At the entrance of the necropolis was a blue pool of water, the fragrant aroma of which filled the first level of the necropolis.

The little golden rat had jumped into the pool, and was excitedly drinking, which caused its aura to grow stronger.

There were no other entities present.

Xu Qing checked himself and found that, yet again, he looked like Netherflame. But this time, he was covered with wounds and splattered with blood. He felt incredibly weak. He had clearly just fought a brutal battle.

Just as he was gaining his bearings, an emotionless stream of divine will emerged from the depths of the necropolis.

“Master Netherflame, you are the first person in the past 30,000 years to pass the 931st assessment of our Heavenmaker species. As stipulated, you may now cleanse your fleshly body once, for the time it takes an incense stick to burn.”

Xu Qing looked more closely at the pool of water. A moment later, he walked up to it and looked at the golden rat.

This memory world is strange. There was no test. Nothing difficult happened. It just directly led to the acquisition of a destined opportunity.

Eyes narrowing, he sent his divine will out to check the pool. The moment his divine will touched it, his expression flickered, and his eyes shone.

He had no idea what the ‘water’ in the pond was made of. But... just now, when his divine will touched it, something that Xu Qing didn’t understand happened, which resulted in his fleshly body and soul being deeply nourished. In fact, he could tell that the soul injuries he had sustained in his fight with Sir Westdevil had recovered by more than half.

But of even greater significance was what happened with his fleshly body! He got the clear sensation... that his fleshly body was being replenished. Put precisely, it was being filled with life force. Though his fleshly body had seemed fine before, the reality was that it had a huge deficit. Now, strength was pouring into it.

What kind of water is this that can cause a sensation like this in a fleshly body made from Eminent Desolation’s flesh and blood?

Xu Qing took a deep breath. After a bit of thought, as well as some observation, including a look at the little golden rat, he decided that the water was safe. Eyes shining with determination, he knelt down and dipped his right hand into the water.

The moment he made contact, he felt massive amounts of life force pouring into him. His mind reeled as his cultivation base and aura erupted. And most important, his fleshly body surged with strength. He was becoming increasingly flawless!

***

In another memory world, Grand Emperor Netherflame had just fought a fierce battle with a clone of himself. He now stood amidst sprawling ruins, clad in a long violet robe, his hand clenched around the neck of a second version of himself.

Out of the captives’ eyes, ears, nose, and mouth flowed streams of white energy.

The version in the violet robe absorbed the energy, while the captive version trembled and howled in agony. Eventually, the captive version’s shape began to change. Instead of looking like Netherflame, the captive looked like a woman. It was one of the two women who had come from the western Devilbirds. The absorption process continued. Sometime later, the woman’s external form collapsed, revealing that she was actually an old hag!

If Xu Qing had been there, he would have recognized her. That old woman... was actually the seventh Imperial Sovereign from the western Devilbirds’ seventh Imperial Sovereign mountain! Her eyes shone with despair and venom.

“Who... are you...?”

The violet-clad Netherflame said nothing, and his facial expression didn’t change. Eventually, the seventh Imperial Sovereign collapsed into dust. Netherflame licked his lips, turned, and walked off.

As he did, Netherflame’s outer form changed. It faded away, turning into a tall figure with long black hair and a young face.

He was none other than Yue Dong’s pursuer, Young Lord Yun!

However, though his physical appearance was that of Young Lord Yun, his eyes seemed profoundly ancient. The truth was that he wasn’t Young Lord Yun, he was actually the patriarch of the Yun Clan. He was Patriarch Yun![3]

Ascending to the highest point in that world, he clasped hands to the dome of heaven.“Your humble servant has complied with your orders from years ago, Grand Emperor, and come here for an audience. Everything you predicted would happen over the past years has indeed come true. The sons rebelled. The Lan Clan plotted evil. And as they fought, both in the open and in the shadows, they sought to open the way to the grotto-heaven.”

The dome of heaven swirled. Winds shifted. A pair of cold eyes appeared and looked down.

A moment later, Young Lord Yun clasped hands and bowed. “Your orders shall be followed!”

1. Sir Nightcrusher appeared last in chapter 927. ☜

2. Master Righteous Veil was mentioned in chapter 927, 961, and 1040. I originally rendered his name as Master Deluo, but eventually consulted the author about it, after which I settled on Righteous Veil. For more information about that, check the footnote in chapter 927. ☜

3. The line elaborating on the identity of this person isn’t actually in the original text. I added it. The reason is that a few chapters from now, it becomes clear that this character is not the young lord but the patriarch, except that there is no explanation other than the line in this chapter about his eyes looking ancient. I was initially confused and thought the author had made a mistake. However, it’s clear based on later events and references that this character is the patriarch. There is never any explanation about when the switch happened. Was he always the patriarch? Or did he switch roles after going offscreen a while back? We don’t know for sure, although there are vague clues in previous and subsequent chapters. Regardless, I feel it makes slightly more sense to just outright explain who he is, rather than assume the audience will realize from this seemingly throwaway line of text that he’s actually the patriarch of the clan. ☜

In the world made of Grand Emperor Netherflame’s memories of the Heavenmaker species, the massive necropolis was wreathed in shadows. The walls were carved with complex designs, but looking closely at them would reveal only a blur. It was impossible to make out any details about them. It was only possible to sense that the designs were like liquid, constantly flowing to form a host of ever-changing images.

The necropolis was completely empty. The only beings inside were Xu Qing and the golden rat, both of whom were at the blue pool. freewebnovel.com

There were no bystanders. There was no sound. There was only time, slowly passing. So far, enough time had passed for an incense stick to burn.

Xu Qing looked down at the pool and sensed the terrifying life force flowing constantly into him, healing his injuries and nourishing his fleshly body. The sense of strength within him was growing increasingly intense, as was the feeling of flawlessness.

The Heavenmaker species....

Xu Qing had never heard of such a species before. However, given how astounding this pool of water was, he could tell that they were incredibly powerful. All in all, this was the first time Xu Qing had encountered anything that could bolster this fleshly body of his. Furthermore, from the moment he started the absorption process, he could tell with certainty that the pond was not harmful.

Too bad everything just happened so fast.

His eyes flashed as he looked at the little golden rat splashing in the water. The rat was continuing to madly absorb the water. Apparently, the unusual water was so important to it that it didn’t want to waste even a fraction of a moment.

Xu Qing thought about the situation for a moment, and in the end, decided not to do as the rat was doing and immerse himself in the pool. Although the water was obviously beneficial to him, he was also slightly suspicious about this good fortune coming out of nowhere.

Therefore, he stopped after putting only his hand in the water.

As Xu Qing carefully controlled how much he was absorbing, the rat’s belly began to swell up. Eventually, it reached its limit and reluctantly returned to his side.

Looking hesitant, Xu Qing finally pulled his hand away to end the destined opportunity. However, he did take out a bottle from this bag of holding, in the hopes that he could fill it with water and take it away.

Intentionally speaking out loud, he said, “I need to think more about where this destined opportunity came from. Only then can I decide whether or not to bathe in the water. Even if I can’t take it away, I'm not going to risk immersing myself. Hopefully this works.”

He had been acting very cautiously so far, including what he was doing right now. Some time passed, and then he shook his head and sighed. It wasn’t possible to extract the water and take it away.

“What a pity,” he murmured. “What a real pity....”

But he wasn’t ready to give up just yet, so he spent some time thinking of other possible ways to take the water. Unfortunately, all attempts failed. Although the water would enter the bottle, it would subsequently disappear.

Xu Qing sighed again, then stood to leave. At the same time, he gestured to the little golden rat to bite open a rift in space.

The rat burped. Then, looking very happy, it opened its mouth wide and bit down onto the air. A loud crunch rang out, and the same thing happened which had happened in the world of euphoria irises. A spatial rift opened up.

This time, however, the little golden rat didn’t seem interested in the spatial shard that resulted. Instead of eating it, it ignored it and lazily lay down on Xu Qing’s shoulder.

Xu Qing took a deep breath, then turned into a stream of light that shot toward the rift. He vanished inside.

Everything looked normal.

After enough time passed for an incense stick to burn, Xu Qing came back out. When he emerged, his eyes were sparkling. He was not as hesitant as before.

I was very careful in everything I did. I wanted to make it seem like I was suspicious of the destined opportunity, and in the end, I chose to just leave. As it turns out, I really could leave if I wanted to. There are a few possible explanations.

First, it’s possible there was never anybody manipulating things from behind the scenes. Everything was a big coincidence, and I was just overthinking things. After all, if there is someone manipulating things, it would make sense for them to let me take the water out of the pool to get me to let my guard down. Except, I failed to take the water away. What’s more, nothing prevented me from leaving the place.

A second possibility is that there really is somebody manipulating things, and they didn’t want me to take the water away. But they did let me leave, which begs the question of what their purpose is....

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered brightly. If the second option is the correct one, then maybe the person is simply putting a game piece into play randomly in the hopes of it paying off later. Either way, if there’s somebody trying to manipulate me, then it makes no difference if I take the destined opportunity or not. Ultimately, they could make a move on me either way.

Xu Qing’s eyes shone with determination, but at the same time, he still had suspicions. However, the good fortune in front of him was just too amazing, and considering he had already done some tests, he finally gritted his teeth.

Blurring into motion, he entered the pool of water, settled down cross-legged, and began to absorb it. The water seethed and a vortex formed.

Xu Qing absorbed it, causing it to pour into him. The sensation of nourishment was a hundred times that of before. It was the same with the feeling of life force.

After the time it takes an incense stick to burn, Xu Qing opened his eyes. He had reached his limit. As it turned out, the water in the pool couldn’t provide unlimited bolstering to a fleshly body made from Eminent Desolation’s flesh and blood.

At the same time, Xu Qing found that the world around him was starting to blur and fade away.

Then the emotionless divine will that had spoken to him earlier returned.

“An incense stick of time has passed. Your good fortune is over.”

The world vanished, and Xu Qing found himself in the starry sky again. The sageheaven god vine flew over to him. Xu Qing looked around and thought back to everything that happened in the Heavenmaker necropolis. Making sure to keep his guard up, he had the god vine fly off into the distance.

Time slipped by slowly but surely.

A few days later, as Xu Qing was continuing to check memory worlds, his heart leaped. It was because the sageheaven god vine had suddenly transmitted emotional fluctuations that indicated it had recognized something with a similar origin as itself.

The only explanation was that it had found Erniu.

Xu Qing immediately sent instructions to the vine with divine will, and it rushed in that direction. It didn’t take long to arrive. Xu Qing found himself looking at a very small memory fragment that depicted a barren planet full of filth and decay.

Erniu... was there.

When Xu Qing saw what was going on, a strange expression appeared on his face. Without the slightest hesitation, he sent the god vine forward to enter the place.

At the last moment, though, he backed up, his eyes shining. He couldn’t enter the world!

Don’t tell me that if somebody else is inside a memory world, others are prohibited from entering? Is it because the memory worlds only contain one Netherflame, which prevents others from coming inside...?

After some more thought, he looked at Erniu’s memory world again, then waved his hand and sent the golden rat flying out.

“Bite it open!”

On the barren planet, Erniu was hopping vigorously on one leg. That was because he only had one leg. As he hopped, he cursed constantly.

What the hell kind of place is this? It’s bad enough there’s no spirit energy and the place has massive pressure weighing down. And of course there’s the terrifying sealing in place. I can’t even use one damn bit of my cultivation base!

To make it even worse, I'm incarnated as a weak and dying version of Netherflame! And I'm even missing body parts....

He had been hopping around for quite a while trying to find a way to leave, or at least determine what Netherflame had done. But no matter what Erniu did, he found himself in error. Looking at the maggots surrounding him, his eyes began to shine with madness.

Despite the fact that Erniu prided himself on not being a picky eater, he couldn’t stomach the idea of eating maggots. Unfortunately, he was truly out of options. Shouting, he prepared to go all out.

However, that was when an intense rumbling sound filled the sky, like thunder. As it spread out, the canopy of heaven sank down. It looked as if some enormous entity were attacking the sky from the other side.

Then everything went back to normal.

The moment the words left his mouth, another sound filled the sky. This time it wasn’t rumbling, but rather, a cracking sound. The canopy of heaven, which had just repaired itself, looked like it was being bitten. And then a small rift opened up. Then, a loud tearing sound could be heard as the rift turned into a large opening.

Erniu’s heart pounded. Then his eyes went wide with disbelief as he realized he could see a starry sky on the other side of the rift.

And within that starry sky was a huge god vine. The vine’s leaves were spread wide, and the vine itself was shining brightly. Looking almost like a dragon, it swept through the opening and screamed through the sky.

Most astonishing of all was that there was someone standing on the vine. He had long flowing hair and a blood-red robe. He was none other than Xu Qing in the form of Sir Blood Dust. The god vine served as a foil, and starlight as the backdrop as his terrifying energy crushed down on everything.

Because of the opening in the canopy of heaven, the sealing power was vanishing. And with Xu Qing’s energy crushing down on everything, the countless maggots were being blasted away.

Erniu looked completely bedraggled as he stood there on one leg looking blankly at Xu Qing. Finally, he took a deep breath. Puffing his chest out, he proudly said, “You’re too late, little Junior Brother. Your Eldest Brother already conquered this planet!”

I didn’t get a damned thing from this stupid place. What a waste of effort and suffering!

As the Eldest Brother, I'm not going to bicker with you over particulars. Just enjoy the show as your Eldest Brother rises to prominence!”
