Unfortunately, I have no such treasures.... But now that you’re here, I have an option that comes very close to option two....”

After seeing his Eldest Brother’s fierce determination, Xu Qing thought briefly, then tapped into his own Six Thieves authority. His own threads of seven emotions and six sensory pleasures appeared, and linked with Erniu’s. As the threads overlapped and connected, an intense sensation of greed and madness flowed out from Erniu’s threads. Along with them came a strong desire for victory.

“Are you sure?” Xu Qing asked.

“Absolutely,” Erniu replied. “Don’t worry. My desire to stay alive might not be the strongest. But I have plenty of greed. As long as I'm greedy enough, everything else will be a breeze.”

Erniu took a deep breath, gritted his teeth, then winked.

Xu Qing could sense that the threads really could tap into Erniu’s deepest emotions of greed. Most importantly, he noticed that wink. And thus, he sat down cross-legged without any sign that anything was amiss.

Erniu also sat down, then lifted his hand and slammed it down onto the top of his head. A boom rang out, and he crumpled to the ground.

However, he wasn’t dead. Gasping for breath, he weakly said, “Help me, little Ah Qing. I can’t actually kill myself....”

Xu Qing’s gaze hardened as he realized that the connected threads were extracting his life force.

Time passed slowly but surely.

Erniu, who was standing in for Netherflame, had almost no life force left. Xu Qing’s authority glittered as he finally yanked Erniu back from the brink. Erniu shivered, and his greed surged. Life force was thus stimulated, and he breathed in raggedly. Then his eyes snapped open. At first, they seemed blank, but as he recovered, they filled with excitement.

“I sensed the power of death.... I was right! The destined opportunity here can only be acquired by dying! Okay, let’s do it again, little Ah Qing. This time, wait a bit longer before saving me.”

Erniu looked at Xu Qing with great anticipation.

Erniu toppled.

This time, as his life force faded away, Xu Qing held back from saving him. Eventually, when the threads of the seven emotions and six sensory pleasures grew dim, as did the greed, Xu Qing knew he couldn't wait any longer. His authority surged, and he began to yank Erniu back again. His carving knife of fate shone brightly.

Without a moment of hesitation, he used his carving knife to slash viciously at the gray mist.

At the same time, the fading greed suddenly seemed to shed its disguise and become incredibly strong. Greed towered to heaven, seemingly turning into a heavenly dog that howled noiselessly and then started gobbling up the mist.

All of a sudden, wild colors flashed in heaven and earth. Intense rumbling sounds rose into the dome of heaven. All of the corpses on the barren planet opened their eyes. Countless maggots screamed, trembled, then exploded one after another.

Xu Qing observed as the gray mist inside Erniu rapidly returned to the planet. However, there was a bit of it that was snagged and eaten by Erniu’s greed.

What was more, Xu Qing could also see that the carving knife of fate he had already retracted also had some gray mist on it, which it had absorbed in the moment of impact. Xu Qing’s eyes gleamed.

An aura of death erupted within Erniu, causing him to rise up into the air. As he hovered in midair, all of the corpses on the planet kowtowed to him. The living maggots shrank back and pulsed with a will of allegiance.

Erniu slowly opened his eyes. They were gray. A moment later, the gray color vanished, replaced by pure greed. Erniu laughed maniacally.

“I’ve conquered this planet!”

Xu Qing felt a bit relieved, and was about to open his mouth and speak when something dramatic happened.

Rain began to pour down. It was much heavier than before, forming streams and then thick sheets. Within the sheets of water, a world was visible. It was a dark world filled with countless grave mounds....

It was raining outside and inside.

At that moment, the rain became a medium that could fuse everything, including the laughing Erniu and the grim-faced Xu Qing. Everything was being devoured.

The head opened its mouth and inhaled deeply. That inhalation unleashed a terrifying gravitational force in the area. Unending soil rose up into the air. Innumerable rain drops flew toward the mouth.

It was as if it were eating.

The earth rose up, revealing coffins, and they also started flying into the mouth. Great crunching sounds rang out as the gruish head snapped them up. Strangely, no matter how much the head put into its mouth, it all vanished, as if the interior of the head was a bottomless pit.

The trembling Xu Qing and Erniu could do little more than fight back against the gravitational force. It took all their strength just to remain in one spot. Gradually, they lost the ability to hold firm.

As the crisis built, Xu Qing looked at Erniu. Erniu knew exactly what that look meant. Without any hesitation, he shouted, “Awaken, my warriors!”

A gray mist erupted from Erniu, causing the power of death to arrive. The grave mounds that had been thrown into chaos by the gravitational force suddenly trembled, and corpses started crawling out of the coffins. There were a lot of them. Because of the gravitational force, the corpses didn’t need any orders from Erniu. They immediately shot toward the huge mouth of that head.

In a very short period of time, the head devoured over 10,000 of them. Apparently, the head had gotten enough, as it started chewing. The gravitational force disappeared and the head blurred and vanished.

Xu Qing breathed a sigh of relief and looked at Erniu. Erniu’s eyes gleamed with lingering fear as he looked back. Both could see how the other was shaken.

It had truly been a moment of danger. They had only just arrived in this world and had already encountered an extremely gruish and terrifying entity. They could only imagine what other dangers lurked in the rain.

“On the one hand, the more dangerous a place is, the more good stuff will be there. However... Little Ah Qing, I feel like the best thing to do is find the empress as quickly as possible.”

As crazy as his Eldest Brother was, even he was thinking the same thing as Xu Qing. Xu Qing didn’t need any convincing. He nodded, and the two of them prepared to start moving. Unfortunately, that was when the terrifying pressure suddenly returned.

The head was back. It was floating right above the two of them. This time, it was closer than before. And it was staring at the two of them.

Before either of them could do a thing, the head inhaled. This time, the gravitational force didn’t spread out widely. Instead, it was focused directly on the two of them.

In the blink of an eye, and before Xu Qing and Erniu could fight back, they were sucked up. However, the head didn’t devour them. Instead, it just brought Xu Qing and Erniu up to it, bound them so they couldn’t move, and then flew off with them in tow. The land screamed past below. The rain did nothing to block the path of the head.

Xu Qing and Erniu couldn't move at all. They could only exchange terrified glances and try to think of ways to escape. Unfortunately, the head was just too powerful, so nothing they did could affect it.

As their anxiety mounted, the head reached another graveyard, where it suddenly stopped moving. Then it exhaled.

Xu Qing and Erniu were thrown down into the graveyard.

Next, the head opened its mouth. The widespread gravitational force appeared again, and the head looked down coldly at them.

Apparently, it was telling them it was ready to start eating.

Xu Qing and Erniu were completely and utterly incapable of fighting back or defending against this terrifying head. Along the way, they had been bound so thoroughly that nothing they had attempted had given any hint that they could free themselves. All their efforts had failed.

Upon being freed, and checking to see the head’s facial expression, Erniu inhaled sharply.

“Uh... does it want us to cook for it or something?”

Xu Qing was getting a sense of what the head wanted. Presumably, it had taken note of how his Eldest Brother summoned all of those corpses, which had saved it a lot of effort. In one fell swoop, it had acquired all the food it had been after there. That was what had led to it taking them captive. The reason he had been included probably had something to do with how he lent the power of his carving knife with its gray mist to the effort.

Xu Qing looked at Erniu. That’s most likely what’s going on here....

Meanwhile, the huge head was looking at them like two servants who were loafing around instead of getting to work. Therefore, it intensified the gravitational force coming out of its mouth, which swept over Xu Qing and Erniu like a warning.

The two of them were shaken. Without any hesitation, Xu Qing unleashed the gray mist from his carving knife of fate.

At the same time, Erniu held nothing back as he shouted, “Awaken!”

The graveyard trembled, and the burial mounds began to collapse. Corpses started crawling out in response to the summons. An instant later, the gravitational force pulled them up into the air and into the head’s mouth. It lasted for the time it takes an incense stick to burn, during which time Xu Qing and Erniu kept working hard to facilitate the process. After that, the gravitational force faded away, and an expression of contentment appeared on the head’s face.

Apparently, it had been a long time since it was able to feed until it was full. After all, in the past, it had been forced to eat a lot of dirt along with the food. Now it had someone to extract and clean the food for it.[1]

Seeing the head looking so content actually caused Erniu to scowl on the verge of tears. Xu Qing was also frowning. The reality was that they were in a very passive position in which they couldn’t take the initiative at all. Before they could even start formulating a plan, the gravitational force sprang up again, and they shot uncontrollably back up to the head. And then they started moving again....

The head screamed along to the next big restaurant. As a result, Xu Qing and Erniu were able to travel a huge distance in a very short time. They soon appeared in a mountainous region. Just like before, the lands were pitch black. Rain was falling. And as Xu Qing and Erniu looked around, they were shocked to realize that the so-called mountains... were actually enormous burial mounds.

In the previous locations they had visited, the burial mounds were ordinary in size. But here, they were the size of mountains. The place was also dotted with smaller gravestones and tombs.

Upon stopping in midair, the huge head opened its mouth, but this time there was no gravitational force. Instead, the head howled. The sound was like thunder as it echoed through the rain.

Next, Xu Qing and Erniu bore witness to something completely shocking.

There was a howl of response. And then another. In fact, there were many of them, all coming from different directions. And then... a head appeared that was only slightly smaller than the head which had captured them, moving with stupefying speed in their direction. From the look of things, this head was female, and from the fluctuations coming off of it, it was also in the Imperial Sovereign level.

Meanwhile, seven or eight smaller heads rushed from other directions. They looked almost like children. They were much weaker, being only in Void Returning.

Xu Qing’s heart sank. Erniu was trembling.

“It’s a whole family?” Erniu murmured.

It was indeed a family. Upon reuniting, they all noticed Xu Qing and Erniu. As they edged closer to them, they opened their mouths as if to devour them. However, that was when the biggest head of them all, the one that had captured the two of them, let loose a howl. It seemed to be warning its mate and children. Next... the eyes of the other heads opened wide and began sparkling.

Seeing that, Xu Qing and Erniu had no choice but to sigh. They were completely helpless, and were captives of this family. Thus, they had no choice but to work hard getting them food.

And the restaurant was this huge area of burial mounds. With the two of them working together, it wasn’t long before corpses appeared. Unfortunately, they failed to summon anything out of the massive burial mounds.

As for the family... at first, they unleashed their own gravitational forces to devour the corpses. As a result, some of the burial soil still ended up getting mixed in with the corpses. But eventually, the floating heads stopped using their gravitational force. They would just wait for the corpses to climb out into the open, and then gobble them up one by one. They would occasionally howl, which seemed to be their family method of chatting during a meal.

Xu Qing and Erniu were quickly becoming exhausted. After all, doing this constant summoning work was very draining. Unfortunately, the family had a huge appetite.

Erniu sighed inwardly. They’ve eaten a few mountains each? How could they not be full?

Then he gave Xu Qing a look. Xu Qing could tell what he meant. The two of them sent the gray mist into one of the mountainous burial mounds. Although it didn’t summon anything out, their previous work had brought them to the realization that they could stimulate whatever was inside.

And there was always the possibility that such stimulation could lead to an awakening. As for what would happen after that, they couldn’t do much about it. After some hard work, they got the burial mound to start rumbling. The mountain shook, and then a huge hand stretched out from inside.

The instant it appeared, the biggest head’s eyes glittered. The expression on the face was enigmatic, as if it completely understood what Xu Qing and Erniu were trying to do. It didn’t seem surprised at all that this huge corpse had shown up. Without any hesitation, it and its mate shot forward and slammed into the huge hand.

The hand trembled as if in fear, and then began to retract. The two heads, however, were very fierce. They continued to slam into the mountain, sending dirt spraying everywhere.

Without any hesitation, Xu Qing and Erniu fled in the opposite direction.

The little heads wanted to stop them, but weren’t fast enough. Before long, Xu Qing and Erniu had disappeared over the horizon. They hardly took a breath for the time it takes an incense stick to burn, nor did they slow down or exchange words. They just fled.

Unfortunately, it didn’t take long for a familiar pressure to appear. The huge head appeared in front of them. First it looked at the surrounding grave mounds, then it looked at the two of them with that same enigmatic smile from before.

Xu Qing and Erniu lurched to a halt, their scalps tingling. At the same time, the rest of the family of heads raced into the vicinity and surrounded them.

Heart pounding in the face of disaster, Xu Qing solemnly said, “This area has a higher concentration of corpses.”

Erniu nodded fervently. Putting a fawning expression onto his face, he said, “That’s right! Exactly! We weren’t running away. We were scouting for areas with more corpses. This area is perfect.”

With a moment of hesitation, he and Xu Qing started the summoning work again. Before long, rumbling sounds echoed out, and burial mounds started collapsing. Corpses crawled out, turning into food that the family made short work of.

Xu Qing and Erniu felt more helpless than ever. Not daring to harbor any further thoughts of escape for the time being, they focused on summoning. Occasionally, slip-ups would occur, and their summoning wouldn’t succeed. However, accidents sometimes led to unexpected successes. As their summoning work yielded fewer and fewer corpses in the area, and they were just about to give up, an enraged howl erupted from under the ground.

“Who’s interrupting my cultivation??”

The ground shook violently and dirt sprayed in all directions as a huge vortex appeared. An old man emerged from the vortex, a frown on his face, his eyes sinister and cold. He was actually one of the western Devilbirds. Given the energy that surged around him, it was clear that he was actually an Imperial Sovereign. His authority related to death, which was why he had been delighted to sense the death aura in this rain world. As far as he was concerned, this was the ideal place to practice cultivation. As such, he had chosen to just settle down cross-legged in a subterranean cavern and absorb the death aura. But then the gravitational force appeared, and sensing the disturbance, he had emerged with a cold expression on his face.

When Xu Qing and Erniu saw him, strange expressions appeared on their faces.

Even as the old man’s words echoed out, he stopped in place and looked up to see Xu Qing and Erniu. He recognized who they were, yet didn’t reveal that via his facial expression. And that was because of the terrifying heads. In fact, his heart was already pounding. Moments ago, he hadn’t sensed any terrifying entities outside. He had only noticed Xu Qing and Erniu. Otherwise, he would never have shown his face.

But now... he was nearly shivering with fear. And it was all because the family of heads were all looking directly at him.

Seeing that, Erniu’s eyes lit up, and he suddenly realized that he wasn’t in that bad of a position after all. Sticking his chin up, he coolly said, “Did I hear someone bitching just now?”

The old man suppressed the fury that flared in his heart. Keeping his eyes on the two huge heads, he took a cautious step backward.

But Erniu wasn’t going to let an opportunity like this pass, so he looked down arrogantly at the Imperial Sovereign below and continued, “And what was he bitching about?”

The old man choked down his humiliation. Never in his life had someone talked to him like this. But all he could do was grit his teeth helplessly and keep trying to back up.

That was when Xu Qing narrowed his eyes and said, “Drop your bag of holding!”

The old man’s face fell. However, that was when the huge head let loose a wave of pressure.

Shaken, the old man had no choice but to suppress his feelings, throw down his bag of holding, and turn to flee.

Erniu licked his lips. “Drop that bracelet too. And your hairpin. And the belt too. It’s obviously a treasure. Oh, don’t forget that jade pendant as well. Drop it too. That’s a nice robe! Take it off!”

The old man let loose a bellow of rage. But that only caused the pressure from the huge head to increase. Trembling in fear, the old man gnashed his teeth and threw down his bracelet, hair pin, belt, pendant, as well as his outer robe.... Then he fled at top speed.

The huge head glanced at him but didn’t give chase. As for the things he had left behind, the head wasn’t interested in them. It just looked around for more food.

Xu Qing and Erniu were a bit disappointed. That said, at least they got some loot. They quickly collected all the things the old man had thrown onto the ground. Then they exchanged a look, and could tell that they were both thinking the same thing.

What a wonderful family.

***

In the depths of the rain-soaked world of graveyards, there was a towering mountain that was actually a tomb. The mountain was completely still. The only motion to be seen was the empress, strolling through the mausoleum in the middle of the mountain.

There were countless corpses around hēr, but they were all turning into dust. It was the same with the huge coffin in the middle of the mausoleum. The terrifying entity in the coffin never woke up. It just faded away for all eternity.

No expression could be seen on the empress’ face as shē strode to the far end of the mausoleum.

There was a stone door there. The empress stood in front of the door, hēr vision piercing through to the other side. There was a majestic crypt inside. It was full of skeletons. There were so many piled together they formed something like a sea of bones.

In the middle of them was an altar. Atop the altar was a corpse, glittering with silver light. It also pulsed with immortal energy and the mightiness of a Grand Emperor. Sadly, this individual had long since perished.

Floating around it in the air were a host of multi-colored legacy seals. Each pulsed with extraordinary fluctuations, indicating that they were fantastic in nature. There were also dao lineaments visible. They were made from authority, and contained terrifying mightiness. Also present were various Grand Emperor treasures, dormant, but shining brightly. If even one of these things appeared in the outside world, they would drive Imperial Sovereigns mad with desire.

Especially noteworthy was that the cross-legged corpse held a black crystal in its hands. Within it was a swirling mist that contained the face of Grand Emperor Devilbird! freewebnovel.com

Astonishingly, there were eight doors leading into the crypt, all of them sealed tightly. The empress was only standing in front of one of those doors. Shē didn’t open the door. Shē just looked at it thoughtfully.

The legacy seals are real. The dao lineaments of authority are real. The Grand Emperor treasures are also real. As for the corpse of that immortal, it certainly seems to have the aura of Netherflame. The skeletons were likely used as a source of life force. This is how you would expect to find Netherflame in his state of seclusion.

The empress’ gaze came to focus on the black crystal in the gnarled hands of the corpse.

That’s the fate-soul of Grand Emperor Devilbird, which was taken away by Netherflame when he was at the peak of his power. Whoever controls that will control the fate of Grand Emperor Devilbird. And that’s what Grand Emperor Devilbird wants back!

1. In Chinese the verbiage is a bit different. It uses the word that translates as “to peel” (as opposed to clean), and is the verb usually used when talking about peeling shellfish. In the context it makes sense in Chinese, but I think using the verb “peel” is confusing in English, thus my translation choice. ☜

After looking through the stone door at the immortal’s corpse, the empress sighed and retracted hēr vision. Next, shē sent hēr vision to the other seven doors. One by one shē examined them. Upon reaching the third door, hēr eyes narrowed before closing. Then shē sat down cross-legged to wait quietly.

Standing in front of that third door was the very same figure who had been furtively making his way through the secluded meditation facilities. He was the black-robed man wrapped in chains.... He stood in front of the stone door, his vision piercing through it to examine the crypt beyond, and specifically, the black crystal in the hands of the immortal’s corpse. He didn’t do anything rash. Expression turning grim, he chose to sit cross-legged and wait.

***

In the world of rain, other people were using their own special knowledge and abilities to close in on the crypt. All of them were looking for stone doors. Different people had different advantages. Some had intelligence reports that gave them a deeper understanding of Grand Emperor Netherflame’s secluded meditation facilities. Some had more acute senses thanks to their cultivation base.

Other than Xu Qing and Erniu, everyone who came to the secluded meditation facilities were powerful experts who were pursuing their own hidden agendas. In contrast, Xu Qing and Erniu were like headless flies buzzing around in the rain, with absolutely no idea that there were stone doors somewhere leading into a crypt.

Fate was a fickle thing. After driving away the Imperial Sovereign, the two of them summoned corpses from a few dozen graveyards. Only then did the family of heads finally get full.

Xu Qing and Erniu had been kept so busy that they had no time to look through the bag of holding. Both of them were exhausted to the bone. However, there were some upsides. In the beginning, they had been unfamiliar with the gray mist and how to use it. But now that they had so much practice, they were nothing short of skilled. That was especially true of Erniu. Given that he had taken the lead, his level of skill had reached the point of perfection.

As for earning their freedom... that hadn’t happened yet. After eating to their fill, the family of heads took the two of them back to their lair.

The lair was actually a massive necropolis! In fact, the necropolis was so big it was basically a mountain.

During their entire journey so far, Xu Qing and Erniu had not seen any mountains as majestic as this. It was so big it seemed to touch the sky, and covered such a large area it seemed like it was the biggest thing in this world. The necropolis was filled with all sorts of catacombs, as well as a host of warding spells. That said, when the family returned, the warding spells seemed little more than facades.

Once inside, the family scattered. The two main heads went to the main palace, where they immediately went to sleep. The smaller heads went to their own subsidiary palaces, where they also went to sleep. The truth was that they really had eaten to their fill, and now they needed time to digest. Before long, thunderous snoring had filled the necropolis.

Xu Qing and Erniu finally had their freedom back.

“Only a necropolis this big could fit a family like this,” Erniu said. “Looks to me like each member of this family used to be a corpse in the past. For whatever reason, they became intelligent and somehow woke up.”

The two of them exchanged a glance, waited for a bit to make sure the family was really asleep, and then started looking for a way out. Before long, they sighed in disappointment. Their freedom was obviously very limited. There wasn’t much special about the necropolis, but sadly, it wasn’t possible to leave it.

It wasn’t that they couldn’t get past the warding spell. Rather, after they got a certain distance from the mountain, a feeling of fear began to build up within them. The thunderous snoring would stop, making it seem like the huge heads were about to wake up. freewebnovel.com

“Dammit!” Erniu snapped angrily. “They’re not going to let us go! They’ve probably never eaten this well before, and now they’re addicted!”

Finally, Erniu decided to look through the loot from the Imperial Sovereign in the hopes that it would help him calm down.

Xu Qing, on the other hand, looked thoughtful. He wasn’t interested in checking the loot. Instead, he looked around at the various catacombs. Finally, he said, “Eldest Brother, remember your idea back on that barren planet? You theorized that Netherflame must have had some destined opportunity. And thus, the worse things got for you there, the more likely it was that you would get some good fortune. So... what about this place?”

Xu Qing’s eyes shone. “I just counted the catacombs here, and they match up perfectly to the number of family members. And though the warding spells were all intact, they did nothing to prevent the family from entering.

“In that case, it seems very likely to me that this necropolis was made for this family. And if that’s the case, then why did they wake up? Could it be because of whatever destined opportunity or good fortune is here? Maybe that’s what provoked the transformation to their corpses!”

Xu Qing looked at Erniu.

Erniu thought about it for a bit, whereupon his eyes lit up. “Good thinking, little Ah Qing! Your analysis conforms exactly to what I was thinking! In fact, I was just going to say that we should search this whole place thoroughly.”

Erniu rubbed his hands together and looked around.

Xu Qing didn’t feel the need to bicker with Erniu. Since his Eldest Brother agreed with him, he didn’t hesitate to get to work. And thus, they split up and started searching. In that matter, time slipped by slowly but surely.

Soon, seven days passed. The family slept the whole time. Clearly they weren’t planning to wake up of their own accord. During that time, Xu Qing and Erniu performed a thorough search of the place. They even managed to study the smaller palaces of the small heads. Unfortunately, they did not find any sort of destined opportunity. The necropolis seemed completely devoid of anything useful. Whatever things they did find were decaying and unusable.

Finally, the two of them appeared outside of the main palace where the two big heads were sleeping. This was the last place they could think of that might have some destined opportunity inside.

“Don’t tell me it’s in there,” Erniu said, struggling to control his breathing.

Xu Qing’s eyes sparkled.

Going into the sleeping chambers of the two main heads was going to be dangerous. But given that they had reached this point, it seemed likely that they would face danger no matter what they did.

After exchanging a glance, they gritted their teeth and went inside. They were met with thunderous snoring sounds. The two heads were leaning up against each other, asleep.

This area was much like every other place they had searched. It was empty. However... there was a stone door on the far end of the room. It seemed very ancient, and was carved with complex symbols that were reminiscent of antiquity. Clearly, the door had been there for a very long time.

Upon seeing that door, both Xu Qing and Erniu felt their heart rate increasing. They had searched this entire place, and this door was the only thing that seemed unusual. They exchanged another glance, then looked at the two heads to make sure they were really asleep. Then they carefully proceeded toward the door.

Upon reaching it, their pupils constricted. Being up close caused the sensation of ancientness to increase. There was also a strong aura of death coming from the other side of the door.

“The precious treasure is in there!!” Erniu murmured. His nose twitched, and his eyes shone with a very crazy look. “Based on my extensive experience hunting for treasure, little Ah Qing, I have a premonition that we’ve found the treasure we’re looking for!!”

Gnawing his lip in excitement, Erniu hurried forward and put his hand on the surface of the door. Heart racing, he pushed. The door didn’t move at all.

Xu Qing reached out, and the two of them pushed together. The door shifted slightly but didn’t open.

Erniu was starting to get anxious. Eyes shining with blue light, he shot a look to Xu Qing, who turned to the two sleeping heads.

Focusing on the one who had captured them, he clasped hands and bowed. “Senior, thank you for taking care of us on our journey. Considering that you brought the two of us here, I find it hard to believe that you don’t want us to open this door. Therefore, I hope you can help us out.”

During their time together, the huge head had never spoken to them. It seemed to act based on instinct. However, Xu Qing had never forgotten the enigmatic smile it gave. And it seemed to tacitly approve of how they had extorted that Imperial Sovereign....

As a result, Xu Qing refused to believe that it wasn’t intelligent. In fact, he was convinced that it had brought them here for the express purpose... of having them open this door. Erniu was clearly thinking the same thing, because as Xu Qing turned and bowed, so did he.

The snoring stopped. The two heads opened their eyes and looked at Xu Qing and Erniu. Then their gazes shifted to the stone door, and their expressions became various serious. They even looked a little bit fearful.

However, in the end... either Xu Qing and Erniu were right, or there was some other explanation that wasn’t forthcoming. Either way, the two heads exchanged a glance, then exhaled sharply.

Their two exhalations hit the stone door. The stone door rumbled, and Xu Qing and Erniu took advantage of the moment to shove it. A rumbling boom echoed out as the door opened by a crack. Instantly, an aura of death poured out, and they sensed dao lineament fluctuations.

Both were shaken. Through the small crack that had opened, both of them had seen... a mind-blowing scene. It was a majestic crypt. There were countless bones piled around an altar. An immortal corpse was seated cross-legged on the altar, surrounded by legacy seals and dao lineaments of authority. And floating everywhere... were Grand Emperor treasures!

Both Xu Qing and Erniu were now thinking exactly the same thing. This is Grand Emperor Netherflame’s secluded meditation chamber!

At the same time, they noticed that there were other stone doors leading into the chamber. Some were sealed shut. Others... had been opened. The opened doors all had figures seated cross-legged on the other side. There were a total of three. All of them... were western Devilbird cultivators who had been with them on the dao altar!

The moment that Xu Qing and Erniu saw them, the three figures looked up. All of them saw Xu Qing and Erniu through the opening in their door. Their gazes met.

Of the three people at the other doors, one was a teenager. He looked to be no more than fourteen or fifteen years old. His facial features were delicate, even pretty. He had long hair bound with a ribbon, and when he looked at Xu Qing and Erniu, he smiled, revealing pearly white teeth. He seemed pure and innocent, without a trace of malice or evil in him.

Next to him was a huge black silkworm that was larger than he was. It was covered with waving tentacles that made it look unusually malevolent. Coming out of the silkworm’s mouth was a strand of black silk that was connected to one of the Grand Emperor treasures by the immortal’s corpse. It looked like a jade bottle. The silk was pulled taut. Apparently, the treasure was resisting the silk, and yet, was slowly being pulled away.

In another direction, seated beyond another of the open doors, was a young woman. She was exquisitely beautiful, with eyebrows like crescent moons, a long straight nose, and cherry-red lips. However, there was something very cold about her, including her gaze. She wore palace attire, a voluminous gown with wide sleeves that made her seem aloof and out of touch with reality.[1]

The arrival of Xu Qing and Erniu on the scene caused her to frown slightly. However, she quickly looked away from them and focused on an octagonal mirror floating in front of her. The mirror was currently facing the crypt and pulling everything there inside of it as a reflection. That included the immortal’s corpse, as well as all the legacies, authorities, and treasures surrounding it. The woman was currently inserting her hand into the mirror to take something. Unfortunately, it was a difficult task that she had not yet succeeded at.

The third party was a young man. He wore a green scholar’s robe, and had his hair bound atop his head with a simple hairpin. He seemed calm and collected, with an erudite air about him. He was very thin, like a bamboo stalk, and had attractive facial features and sparkling eyes. Of the three, he paid the least attention to Xu Qing and Erniu. His gaze flitted over them briefly, no more.

He was fully focused on a burning stick of incense in front of him. The incense was about as thick as a finger, and it was bright red. As it burned, it sent out puffs of smoke. The scholar would then blow on the smoke, sending it into the crypt toward the legacy seals.

It was a very strange smoke. As it continued to blow into the crypt, some of the legacy seals flickered with increasing intensity, as if they were becoming alive. They even seemed to be growing tiny limbs. And then they began to form ranks and slowly start walking toward the young man.

When Xu Qing and Erniu saw all of this, various thoughts ran through their heads. After extorting that Imperial Sovereign earlier, they had begun to speculate about the identities of the others who had come into Netherflame’s secluded meditation facilities.

After laying eyes on these people, Xu Qing realized that their speculations were correct. They’re all Imperial Sovereigns in disguise! As for this crypt, it’s full of danger and the unknown. The Imperial Sovereigns from the western Devilbirds are obviously being very careful. What’s more, you can tell... that none of them want to actually go inside the crypt. That’s why they’re using different ways of extracting the good fortune!

Furthermore... the fact that they’re all here goes to show that they all knew about this crypt and were ready to come here!

Erniu came to the same conclusion as Xu Qing. The two of them exchanged a glance and could see the serious look in the other’s eyes. After all, there was no denying the fact that they were the weakest people in the group. If even one of these people chose to attack them, they would have to take the situation very seriously.

Thankfully, we have a wonderful family backing us up.... Erniu looked over his shoulder with a fawning look, then gritted his teeth. “Little Junior Brother, we can’t worry about blowing our cover now. Our disguises are already gone. They’ve probably already guessed who we really are. And therefore, we—”

“We need to go for broke!” Xu Qing finished, speaking in a voice so decisive it could sever nails and chop iron.

Erniu’s eyes burned with a crazy look. At the same time, both of them shoved hard on the stone door. They held nothing back. Rumbling sounds echoed out as the stone door slowly opened.

Not even Imperial Sovereigns were willing to enter this crypt. And though Xu Qing and Erniu were both a bit crazy, there was a big difference between acting crazy and acting suicidal. At the very least... things hadn’t reached the point where they would need to act suicidal. Therefore, after opening the door, they looked around the crypt and all the skeletons. At that point, they made a joint decision.

Gray mist appeared in Erniu’s eyes. Mist also began to pour off Xu Qing’s carving knife of fate. Their power merged, and they sent it into the crypt.

In the blink of an eye, the eyes of one particular skeleton began to glow. And then, it shakily lurched onto all fours and started crawling toward the altar and the immortal’s corpse. At first, it moved in a rather wobbly fashion. But soon enough, it was moving more smoothly and with greater speed.

If Xu Qing and Erniu had tried this back when they first got this power of death, they would never have been able to exercise such control. It would have been too difficult. But after all of their work gathering food for the family of heads, they had so much practice that their level of control had reached the point of perfection.

Before long, the skeleton reached the altar and managed to hop up onto it. There, it slammed into one of the Grand Emperor treasures that resembled a shield. It slammed into it in a way that would hopefully send it flying toward Xu Qing and Erniu. Instead, the moment it made impact, the treasure sent out a force of rejection that ripped the skeleton into shreds.

The treasure didn’t budge an inch. The other three people at the other doors didn’t bother looking at what was happening.

Xu Qing and Erniu looked on with glittering eyes. Next... about eight skeletons rushed toward the altar, where they slammed into the shield. Some popping sounds rang out as the skeletons turned into ashes. Next, a few dozen skeletons rose up. Then came over a hundred.

In the end, several hundred skeletons charged forth, each trying to outdo the other as they slammed into the shield. At long last, the shield moved. As the process went on like that, the shield slowly but surely inched toward Xu Qing and Erniu at the stone door. The progress was slow, but that was only considering the process on its own. freewebnovel.com

If you compared it to how things were going with the other three parties, it was actually moving quite quickly. As a result, the three Imperial Sovereigns took notice and looked over.

Meanwhile, something else was happening at two of the other doors. The black-robed figure on the other side of one of the stone doors was watching things play out, and he was frowning.

At another door was the empress. Shē had an odd expression on hēr face as shē watched the skeletons slamming into the shield. Then shē saw the look of anticipation on the faces of Xu Qing and Erniu, and shē sighed.

In that matter, time slipped by slowly but surely. Two hours went by.

Two more individuals arrived. The first was the son of the fifth Imperial Sovereign, Lin Kun.

Of course... it wasn’t really Lin Kun. It was a person disguised as Lin Kun. He was actually the fifth Imperial Sovereign of the eastern Devilbirds, who was one of Grand Emperor Netherflame’s apprentices! Upon arriving, he showed no interest in any of the treasures. Instead, he focused on the dao lineaments of authority, which caused his eyes to gleam in anticipation. His method of acquisition was unique. He just sat down cross-legged and exuded fluctuations of the same origin as one of the lineaments. As a result, the dao lineament started inching toward him.

The last to arrive was someone familiar to Xu Qing and Erniu. It was the old man they had clashed with earlier.

Upon arriving, he looked around at the crypt, at all the parties present, and of course, he saw Xu Qing and Erniu. The moment he caught sight of those two, his killing intent raged inside of him. However, after scanning the crypt and noting the stone door where Xu Qing and Erniu stood, he suppressed his killing intent.

There’s no rush. If they somehow manage to make it out of this alive, I’ll definitely track them down and wipe them out of existence!

With a cold snort, he sat down and unleashed his aura of death, which he used like a fishing hook to snag one of the dao lineaments of authority.

This time, another incense stick’s worth of time passed.

Everyone continued on with their differing methods of acquiring their targets. Everyone was making progress, especially Xu Qing and Erniu. The shield was only about 30 meters away from them at this point. The only downside as far as they were concerned was that the huge heads seemed scared of the crypt, and weren’t helping them with gravitational force.

“It doesn’t matter,” said Erniu, licking his lips. “As long as things go on like this, it will only take an incense stick of time before the treasure is ours.”

Unfortunately, whoever had set up this entire situation obviously wanted people to go into the crypt, because that was when something unexpected happened.

Just when everyone was about to succeed in getting what they wanted, one of the previously sealed stone doors suddenly slammed open. Unexpectedly, someone shot out of the door. To the shock of everyone, this newcomer moved with incredible speed as they entered the crypt.

It was an old woman! It was very clearly the same old woman that Patriarch Yun had killed. But here she was.

With the wave of her hand, she sent Imperial Sovereign fluctuations raging out into a tempest. The silk thread snapped. The mirror wobbled out of control. The death aura was severed. The awakening legacies were blocked. The connections to the authority were cut. And it caused Xu Qing and Erniu’s shield to shoot back in the opposite direction. It all happened before anyone could react.

As everyone looked on with glittering eyes, the woman walked up to the immortal’s corpse and sat down cross-legged.

Voice cold, she said, “Since all of you are afraid of taking risks, don’t come in here.”

The old woman closed her eyes and performed a double-handed incantation gesture. Opening her mouth in the direction of the immortal’s corpse, she inhaled deeply. That action caused an intangible connection to spring up between her and the corpse. It was impossible to tell what shocking technique the woman was using. But regardless, the corpse started crumbling. And as the old woman absorbed it, her own aura began to rise dramatically.

She got stronger and stronger. Apparently, she was absorbing Grand Emperor Netherflame’s personhood. And as she inhaled, all of the legacies and authorities trembled and began to shoot toward her, as if she were their master and they wanted to fuse with her.

All of a sudden, all of the Grand Emperor treasures seemed to have spirit automatons that were on the verge of waking up. This dramatic turn of events upset the balance of power!

This was a conspiracy! It didn’t matter who could or couldn’t see what was really going on with the old woman. Everyone knew that if they didn’t do something, the old woman would succeed. And if she got everything in the crypt, then the rest of them would be in great, unpredictable danger. Most importantly, the old woman... was also absorbing the black crystal with Grand Emperor Devilbird’s fate-soul in it!

It was a critical moment, and everyone had grim looks on their faces. As for Lin Kun, a cold look gleamed in his eyes as he shot forward to prevent the old woman from absorbing everything around her. Booms rang out as the two started fighting.

The other Imperial Sovereigns hesitated.

As for Xu Qing and Erniu, they exchanged a glance, then gritted their teeth and unleashed as much gray mist as they could. Countless skeletons in the crypts shivered and woke up. After crawling to their feet, they shot toward the legacies, authorities, and Grand Emperor treasures.

The aura darkened the sky of the world outside. Before, it had been dusky, but now, it became deep and pitch black. The rainwater was also affected, as a resonance came into being. Now it seemed that their master had returned and called out to them. As a result, they were also coming back. Howls and roars filled heaven and earth.

And some people even believed that he had an extraordinary shackle-breaking magic hidden on him.

Regardless, there was definitely some karmic relationship between his meteoric success and ultimate decline. Because of that, all Devilbird Imperial Sovereigns wanted to reveal the secrets and seize the destined opportunity as a means of breaking through their own cultivation base shackles.

Maybe it would lead to similar meteoric successes and ultimate declines. But cultivators had long since ceased practicing cultivation for the mere purpose of living forever. The best way to live without regrets was really to reach the highest heights.

Unfortunately, the most dangerous situation they could possibly imagine was now playing out right in front of them. Netherflame wasn’t really dead!

The moment he appeared, Grand Emperor fluctuations exploded out, and his actual body began to form. Grand Emperor treasures appeared all around him. Dao lineaments rose up from him, and concentric halos of black mist could be seen at his back. The might of a Grand Emperor was incredibly strong.

As he stared at the hand, his gaze was astonishingly aggressive, like lightning.

“So, you finally showed your face!” Grand Emperor Devilbird said.

Meanwhile, the black-robed man howled in anguish as he was dragged into the vortex by the blood-red hand. An instant later, he was gone. Everyone looking on was stunned.

Then Grand Emperor Devilbird spoke again. “I knew all along you weren’t dead, Netherflame. You were struggling at death’s door. The memory worlds from before were simply there to confuse anyone who came this way. In fact, this whole crypt is also nothing more than a smokescreen.

“That said, one thing that did surprise me, Netherflame, is how daring you are. In order to lure me in here, you actually put your fate-soul in this place. You wanted me to personally witness the fate-soul about to be assimilated, all to give me no choice but to intervene.”

Grand Emperor Devilbird looked coldly at the blood-red vortex, his eyes burning with killing intent.

The vortex spun, emitting loud rumbling sounds, but no words of response.

“But of course, how could I come here unprepared?” Next, Grand Emperor Devilbird looked, not at any of the people present, but at the final remaining stone door that hadn’t been opened. “You’re here, empress of humankind. So why haven’t you shown yourself yet?”

Every single Imperial Sovereign present was visibly surprised as they turned to look in the same direction as Grand Emperor Devilbird. After all, there was only one person who could be referred to as the empress of humankind. And that was Empress Summer Departure, who had reached godly ascension!

As everyone looked over, the empress appeared. At first, everyone saw Lu Lingzi standing there. But that form faded away, revealing the empress’ true form! Destiny aura went wild in the area, taking the shape of countless humans. At the same time, an imperial robe and crown appeared on the empress.

As of that moment, all human lands outside of the Devilbird holy land, plus the will of all humans, seethed, causing destiny aura to surge forth to bolster the empress. A terrifying aura and momentum began to build up on the empress.

It caused all of the Imperial Sovereigns to tremble and struggle to breathe. That was especially true of those who had previously considered stirring up trouble with Lu Lingzi.

All of this was both expected and unexpected. Unexpected things often happened in circumstances like this. And after Xu Qing and Erniu appeared, the arrival of the empress fell into the realm of being expected. Either way, the Imperial Sovereigns present were all taking the situation very seriously.

The empress’ expression was the same as ever as shē took a step forward and then appeared right in front of Xu Qing and Erniu. There, shē blocked the tempest and negated the pressure.

Xu Qing breathed an inner sigh of relief, as did Erniu. Both of them didn’t hesitate for a moment to clasp hands in greeting.

The empress didn’t turn to look at them. Instead, shē looked at Grand Emperor Devilbird up in midair. Clearly, shē had expected that shē would be called out by him at some point.

“The Devilbird holy land will leave human skies,” she said coolly. “And Netherflame’s soul will be given to me.”

Grand Emperor Devilbird smiled. He knew that it would be difficult to please the empress considering he had revealed hēr true identity. What was more, he knew that though he and the empress were at war, there was something far more important to him personally than victory.

And that was the life or death of Netherflame. He wanted Netherflame to die so that he could get his fate-soul. There was no conflict between him and the empress in that regard.

Back when had suspected that Lu Lingzi wasn’t really Lu Lingzi, he hadn’t interfered. He had allowed Lu Lingzi to return, and had even opened the secluded meditation facilities. In the final analysis, he had actually hoped that the empress would test him out and ultimately choose to join forces with him when things reached a critical point. What was more, the empress’ demands came as no surprise to him.

“My fate-soul has two parts. I already took the first part. But the second part is still down there.” Grand Emperor Devilbird’s eyes shone with determination. “Join forces with me. You can take Netherflame, and I’ll take my own fate-soul. When we both get what we want, the Devilbird holy land will leave human skies!”

“Deal!” the empress replied.

With that, Devilbird moved over to the vortex, stopped, and looked back at the empress.

The empress looked around at the Imperial Sovereigns, especially the old man who commanded that death energy. When the empress looked at him, he shivered and then bowed his head respectfully.

They might be enemies, but this was an Altar God he was dealing with, and not even he was brave enough to look someone like that in the eyes. That was especially true considering... he could tell that look had been a warning.

The empress looked away, then joined Devilbird by the vortex. The two of them then stepped inside and vanished.

Everyone else hesitated about whether to follow. Before any of them could decide, a will of extermination filled the crypt. Everything started withering up. It was vanishing.

Seeing that, the Imperial Sovereigns gritted their teeth and flew over to the vortex. One by one, they entered. The old man who had clashed with Xu Qing and Erniu was apparently worried about a misunderstanding. Not daring to be the last to enter, he jostled with the fifth Imperial Sovereign to beat him into the vortex. It didn’t take long for all the Imperial Sovereigns to be gone.

Xu Qing and Erniu looked at each other. They could see the determination in each other’s eyes. Both took deep breaths and burst into motion. They also entered the vortex, and rumbling sounds echoed out as they vanished.

When they reappeared, they were in a blood-red world. In this place, heaven was made of flesh, and it was covered with countless downy hairs. The lands below were covered with a transparent sea. On top of the sea was a conglomeration of flesh that looked like a huge tumor.

Inside of the tumor was a middle-aged cultivator, seated cross-legged. He pulsed with an extremely ancient and terrifying aura as he slowly opened his eyes and looked up at the group above.

“Everyone’s here. Welcome. The time has come for all of you to witness my rebirth.”

Atop the huge sea, inside the horrifying magenta tumor, a voice spoke, and an aura spread out.... A storm sprang up on the transparent sea, giving birth to a tsunami. A screaming sound shook everything, and huge waves swept back and forth that seemed capable of overturning heaven and earth. The sky of flesh quivered. Countless fleshy tentacles swayed back and forth. And the opening the group had just come through was already closing. The area had become a deadly danger zone.

The mocking voice that had just spoken echoed within the danger zone, reaching the ears of the Imperial Sovereigns, causing grim expressions to reach their faces and filling their hearts with regret. They should not have come here.

Sometimes, though, the advancement of the cultivation base did not reduce one’s capacity for greed. It all came down to how much something was worth. Powerful experts like Imperial Sovereigns were not people who lacked the capacity to fight hard for what they wanted. And they were not cowards. Otherwise, they would not have been able to tread their path to the current position. Therefore, it made sense that they would take a chance by coming to a place like this.

Right now, all of them were instinctively backing up and activating their most powerful defenses. At the same time, they were trying to come up with ways of dealing with the situation, while simultaneously putting most of their hope in Grand Emperor Devilbird. All of them, with the exception of the fifth Imperial Sovereign, had come here, not because it was their idea, but because Grand Emperor Devilbird had persuaded them and even sworn dao oaths to convince them.

The way things played out wasn’t set in stone. That was especially true about the empress joining forces with Devilbird. In other words, it was still possible that they could get their hands on authority legacies or Grand Emperor treasures.

As for Xu Qing and Erniu.... They each had their own unique objectives.

Xu Qing’s goal was relatively simple. He wanted a way to break through the shackles confining his cultivation base. And the power emanating off this transparent sea, though neither spirit power nor god power, did contain a life force that gave him a bit of hope. This is the perfect place for cultivation base advancement!

Erniu, meanwhile, was looking at that huge tumor. Specifically, he was licking his lips as he looked at the figure inside. His original goal in coming to this place had been to gain control of a Grand Emperor’s corpse.

Of course, a goal like that was not going to be easy to accomplish. So he had a second goal as well, and that was to activate the bone cauldron made from his past life to find the memories of his third life. The reality was that he was missing memories from his first, second, and third lives. And he had the feeling that the only way to start finding the memories from the first and second lives was to start by getting control of his third life memories.

Therefore, he had multiple objectives in mind as he slowly backed up.

At exactly the same moment that the empress and Grand Emperor Devilbird were already shooting toward the tumor...

As Grand Emperor Netherflame sat within the huge tumor on the transparent sea, he lifted his right hand. The dome of heaven trembled and then sank downward.

The sight of it struck everyone to the core. This was a case of heaven destroying earth! Everything was being crushed.

The air vibrated as if it were turning solid, and then began to converge inward. It was the same with the sea below, which began to rise up to connect with the sky and the air. The entire world was contracted as if to form a powerful sealing mark.

All Xu Qing could sense was that heaven and earth were blurring, and seemingly infinite pressure was building up. And yet, after he got over his shock and looked around, everything looked normal. reewebnovel.com

The sky was still made of flesh. The earth was still covered by the transparent sea. There were no other dramatic transformations anywhere else.

The only difference was that... the empress and Grand Emperor Devilbird were now surrounded by a sphere-like magenta tumor. It was formed from the sky, the sea, and the air. That was because the event which just occurred had been focused on the empress and Grand Emperor Devilbird!

Xu Qing realized that he would have a hard time describing exactly how it played out. All he knew was that he had a feeling inside him that this entire world was like a fruit. They were currently in the core of that fruit, and just now, Grand Emperor Netherflame had used an unimaginable power to carve a sphere out in the middle of that fruit. The empress and Grand Emperor Devilbird were now sealed within that sphere.

Before Xu Qing’s senses could process it, heaven and earth rumbled, and the same thing happened again. In fact, it happened twenty-three times in a row before it stopped.

Everything was back to normal. However, everything seemed... flimsier than before. Everyone was stunned.

And Netherflame’s voice then echoed out again from within the tumor. “I’ve been planning this for a thousand years. I just needed Devilbird to show up at the right moment. Then I could possess him and use him as a body in which to be reborn. And you are the nutrients I need for that rebirth. Granted, I didn’t expect an Altar God to show up. To be honest, it was... a pleasant surprise.”

Netherflame’s gaze came to rest on the empress and Grand Emperor Devilbird in the tumor. Then he looked at the rest of the surprised cultivators present. “I have thirty-three worlds. I already peeled away twenty-three of them to perform this sealing. That means there are ten left for the rest of you.”

Netherflame lifted his hand and then gently lowered it. It didn’t matter how people struggled, fought back, or tried to evade. Nothing helped. Instantly... heaven and earth filled with rumbling sounds. One world became a mass of flesh that surrounded the young woman in palace attire. Another world became a cage that sealed the fifth Imperial Sovereign. As for the scholar, the teenager, and the old man with the grudge against Xu Qing and Erniu, none of them were able to escape the fate of being surrounded by one of the worlds peeled away by Netherflame. All of them became tumors floating in midair. Another tumor contained Xu Qing and Erniu.

Having accomplished that, Netherflame closed his eyes. Then his chest heaved as he started performing breathing exercises. When he inhaled, the floating balls of flesh quivered and began to contract. When he exhaled, the fleshy tumors shivered again and expanded. Because of his breathing, the people caught in the tumors felt their life force and cultivation bases weakening. A sensation of crisis was starting to grow strong.

However, at that critical moment, the tumor of twenty-three worlds that held the empress and Grand Emperor Devilbird began to tremble. And then the tumor started to act in exactly the opposite way as everything else. When Netherflame inhaled, the interior of the tumor expanded. And when he exhaled, the opposite happened. It was using Netherflame’s strength to create a conflicting force that sent cracks spreading out through the tumor.

Netherflame frowned slightly.

As the cracks proliferated, streams of godlight began to seep out, along with the power of Devilbird’s authority. It took only three breaths of time. At that point, the sealing tumor of twenty-three worlds emitted a loud bang as it exploded.

The empress flew out and shot toward the tumor containing Netherflame. The mere passage of the empress caused heaven and earth to shatter. Grand Emperor Devilbird was next to the empress, his killing intent surging. They were unstoppable.

In the blink of an eye, the two of them smashed into the tumor containing Netherflame, and began to fight. The tumor swelled and became nothing but a chaotic blur. No one could see what was happening inside.

That said, no one was keen on trying to find out. The Imperial Sovereigns were taking advantage of the moment to unleash various trump cards to break free from their own sealing tumors.

Some used secret magics, others used Grand Emperor treasures they had kept in reserve. No one held anything back.

Xu Qing and Erniu were also going all out to break free, using the empress’s medallion and Xu Qing’s carving knife. Unfortunately, the tumors were fantastically gruish. It was as if they took advantage of cracks between fate to create layer after layer. It was never-ending. Erniu opened his mouth and took a bite, but that didn’t do anything.

It was the same everywhere. No matter what anyone did, it was pointless.... Even if they broke through a layer of the sealing, there was always another sealing beyond that. People started wondering if they were seeing things.

Erniu inhaled sharply. “Are these sealing marks really made from only one world each? If we couldn’t break out of them, that would make sense. But look at all the Imperial Sovereigns! They’re using all sorts of trump cards. Even Grand Emperor treasures! And not even that is doing anything.”

His eyes glittered. “Wait a second,” he continued suspiciously. “Why would Netherflame say that to begin with? Maybe... these sealing marks aren’t made from worlds at all! And if that’s the case, why would Netherflame do all of this? What would be the point of tricking us? Wouldn’t it make more sense to put a bunch of sealing marks on the empress and Devilbird? After all, they’re a much bigger threat than us.”

Clearly, Xu Qing and Erniu weren’t the only ones pursuing this train of thought. The Imperial Sovereigns were starting to come to the same conclusion.

And then, just as Erniu gave voice to that concept, something dramatic happened!

Almost all of the tumors started twitching violently and at the same time, contracting and expanding rapidly. And that caused immense pressure to weigh down on the Imperial Sovereigns. In fact, it was a pressure that surpassed what Imperial Sovereigns could sustain.

An instant later, howls of anguish rang out of their mouths. Their bodies then began to collapse and be assimilated. Their life force was being forcefully sucked out. The pressure also caused their cultivation bases to be brutally stripped away. The same thing happened with their souls and authority. Even their magical treasures were unable to escape the effects. The pressure caused them to collapse and be sucked up. It was almost as if they were turning into spirit stones!

This was a consummate level of power, something they couldn’t fight against. They could only writhe in helpless agony and despair.

Of course, that was happening to almost all of the tumors. The reason for the word almost... was that it wasn’t happening to the tumor that contained Xu Qing and Erniu! Their tumor wasn’t contracting. It was only expanding. And that was because something dramatic was happening inside....

That development caused Erniu to inhale sharply, and it filled Xu Qing with a sense of unbounded danger. A boundless life force swept toward them from all directions, and it... directly entered the tumor that contained them!

Astonishingly, it was the life force that was being stripped away from the Imperial Sovereigns. Unseen hands were manipulating things to send all of it to Xu Qing and Erniu. The previous expansion was clearly intended to make room for it all.

In the blink of an eye, the life force quintessence of all of the Imperial Sovereigns had become a liquid that pooled all the way up to Xu Qing’s ankles. And as it coursed into his flesh and blood, it provided incredible nourishment. And the focus of that nourishment was his fleshly body.

When Erniu saw that, he gasped.

As for Xu Qing, he was shaken to his core as he suddenly recalled something. It was something that happened in the world of the Heavenmakers.

Someone is catalyzing my fleshly body into maturity!

His heart was racing as he thought back to that experience. He suddenly got the sensation that being cleansed by the Heavenmakers' might have seemed like good fortune in and of itself. But the reality was that it was like... cleaning vegetables!

Before you eat something, you need to clean it thoroughly.

Xu Qing had already begun picking up on the clues back in that memory world of the Heavenmakers. After a lot of testing and probing, he had ultimately decided to absorb some of the water in the pool. However, he had come to the conclusion that the good fortune was likely a case of someone randomly putting a game piece on the board in the hopes of using it later. And right now, he was scowling deeply.

It wasn’t a case of randomly playing a game piece. It was a case of someone setting me up! And they were doing it for a specific reason....

Xu Qing didn’t need to put a lot of thought into it. He now realized that, given what happened before, Grand Emperor Netherflame’s first objective was Devilbird. And the entire purpose of his secluded meditation facilities was to lure Devilbird inside at the right time. But then Xu Qing also came... which forced Netherflame to change his plan.

The only question is whether I’ve become Plan A or Plan B. After all, there’s some major karma at play because of me having a body made from Eminent Desolation’s flesh and blood. Will he be willing to ignore that future karma just to seize this body?

As Xu Qing’s mind raced, the howls of agony continued to echo out from the surrounding tumors.

The woman in palace attire, the teenager, the scholar, and the old man, and even the fifth Imperial Sovereign were all trembling as they slowly withered up. Their life force, cultivation base, and even their essence, was all being sucked away. They had no way to stop it from becoming liquid that poured into the tumor with Xu Qing.

By now, it had gone past his ankles and up to his knees. The liquid seemed to have a will of its own as it rushed madly inside Xu Qing, swirling through his fleshly body. Not only was it nourishing his fleshly body, but also, it was causing certain transformations. The pain was intense and all-encompassing. Xu Qing fought against it instinctively.

The will within the liquid, upon sensing Xu Qing fighting back, became even more aggressive, and began trying to wipe out Xu Qing’s soul.

Xu Qing was beginning to lose consciousness as the union between his soul and fleshly body began to break down. There was nothing he could do to reverse the situation. All he could do was use his carving knife of fate to protect his soul. He felt like a rowboat in a tempest, struggling to hold on. At the same time, he was trying various methods of breaking free. But nothing worked.

“In that case...” he murmured. Eyes glittering with cold light and heart filling with determination, he settled down cross-legged. And with that, he stopped preventing his fleshly body from absorbing the liquid. Because of that, the will of the liquid stopped working so hard to wipe out his soul. His body trembled as massive amounts of quintessence poured into his body, nourishing it and making it stronger.

Erniu could sense that something wasn’t quite right. He took a deep breath and prepared to help, but realized how unbelievably powerful the liquid was. He blinked a few times. That was when he realized Xu Qing was working hard to absorb it.

Eyes glittering, he loudly said, “Let me help you, little Junior Brother!”

With that, he suddenly sat down cross-legged, settling himself as if to help Xu Qing out by doing his own deep breathing. Unfortunately, an action like that wouldn’t be permitted. The moment he started breathing, an incredible force of expulsion erupted within the tumor. Rumbling sounds filled the tumor as the force of expulsion ejected Erniu from inside.

Xu Qing’s eyes snapped open and he burst into motion. As he did, a gravitational force appeared, wrapping around him and dragging him back so he couldn’t leave.

In that manner, Erniu became the third person after the empress and Grand Emperor Devilbird who escaped one of the tumors. After the expulsion came a wave of killing intent.

It rumbled loudly as it swept over Erniu from head to toe. Cracking sounds rang out, accompanied by Erniu’s howls of pain. All of the bones in his body were shattered, his flesh was crushed, and he began to fall apart. Masses of shredded flesh began to fall down into the transparent sea below. They sank down to the bottom.

Xu Qing heard Erniu screaming and saw his body collapsing. Unfortunately, he had no attention to spare. Besides, Xu Qing was confident that killing Erniu wouldn’t be an easy task for anyone.

What was more, Xu Qing knew that he was currently facing the most deadly crisis he had faced in his entire life. It was a situation in which it was going to be difficult to find help from any external source. If he wanted to break free, he would have to rely on himself.

Xu Qing gritted his teeth, and his eyes flashed with cold light. Even as he continued to focus on absorbing the surrounding liquid, the liquid continued to build up around him.

The life force liquid from the Imperial Sovereigns had currently gone past his chest and was up to his neck. And the level was still rising. Before long, it went past his head. He was fully immersed.

Things weren’t over yet. The Imperial Sovereigns howled as they grew weaker and weaker, all while the tumor Xu Qing was in reached the point of being more than eighty percent full. The astonishing amount of life force quintessence that was nourishing Xu Qing’s fleshly body had reached an unfathomable level.

His body was made from the broken face’s flesh and blood, and though it seemed like a unified whole, it actually wasn’t. Over the past few years, Xu Qing had been working hard to fuse all the pieces together, and even more importantly, improve the level of his soul. He needed to achieve a state of balance to be in the safest position. Whether it was the immortal mercury from the very beginning or the dao lineament of authority, his ultimate goal had always been the same. Unfortunately, progress had been very slow.

Eventually, he came to Netherflame’s secluded meditation facilities, where he found the pool in the Heavenmaker world. And now he was absorbing the life force, cultivation bases, souls, and quintessence liquid of numerous Imperial Sovereigns. As a result, his fleshly body was being pushed toward a state of completion. His aura was climbing higher, pushing against the shackles of the Smoldering God and climbing toward the level of an Imperial Sovereign.

The ideal outcome would be for his soul to follow along to a similar result. Unfortunately, his soul was not growing. Only his fleshly body was being catalyzed. And that made him like a child donning a thousand-pound suit of armor. In the end, either his soul would be crushed, or the fleshly body would be rejected. If he tried to stop the process, the will of the liquid would explosively crush his soul. If he didn’t stop it, then the stronger his fleshly body got, the harder it would be for his soul to stay inside. It was a lose-lose situation.

Xu Qing’s decision was to just keep focusing on absorbing the liquid. His soul filled with pain, and felt like it might be forcefully ejected from his body, but he didn’t hesitate. He just kept absorbing the liquid, his eyes glinting coldly the entire time.

He was waiting. He was waiting for the force of rejection against his soul to reach the highest level possible.

And thus, time slipped by.

The howls from the Imperial Sovereigns grew weaker. The chunks of Erniu’s flesh sank deeper into the transparent sea.

And then another dramatic event unfolded. A heaven-shaking, earth-shattering rumbling sound emerged from the tumor where the empress and Grand Emperor Devilbird had disappeared. Then the tumor began to expand rapidly, getting bigger and bigger. The fighting inside seemed to have reached a climax. Ultimately, the tumor couldn’t hold itself together. It exploded violently. Massive amounts of flesh and blood rained down onto the transparent sea.

The empress and Grand Emperor Devilbird flew out and hovered in midair. Their eyes were both grim as they looked at the flesh and blood raining down. They also took note of what had been playing out while they were gone. They saw the Imperial Sovereigns withering up, and they saw Xu Qing’s aura rising explosively.

The empress frowned. Grand Emperor Devilbird looked at the tumor that contained Xu Qing, and his eyes narrowed.

At the same time, now that the tumor had exploded, allowing the empress and Grand Emperor Devilbird to emerge, Grand Emperor Netherflame finally appeared. A meaningful smile played out on his face as he looked at the empress.

“You didn’t come here just for my soul. You probably want my sealed grotto-heaven, don’t you? Let me guess, you want to resurrect someone.”[1]

The empress’ expression was the same as ever as shē coldly replied, “You’re not a complete version of Netherflame.”

Netherflame smiled but didn’t respond. Turning, he looked down into the transparent sea. The entire sea then turned into a vortex. Loud rumbling sounds echoed out, and a terrifying aura spread out. Sky-obscuring, sun-blocking winds sprang up.

Then a gruish figure rose out of the vortex. The left side had a humanoid shape, and had clearly been reborn. But the right side had not been fully reborn. It had no skin, only a network of blood vessels. It looked shocking and ghastly. The sense of incompleteness in it was clear.

Seeing this emerging figure caused Grand Emperor Devilbird to breathe heavily, all while his pupils constricted. Along with the gruish figure came a host of dancing lightning bolts. The dome of heaven trembled, the sea water seethed, and an aura that was immeasurably close to a Summer Immortal erupted out.

“So, it’s an omniscient god,” the figure growled as it looked at the empress with a gaze that seemed to contain magical laws. “You’re right. He’s an incomplete version of me. Put precisely, he’s one of my two clones. And he has some karma connecting him to those two human chosen of yours. That’s because, before changing appearances, he had a different identity in the Devilbird holy land. He was the grand immortal adept of the eastern Devilbirds.

“In order to welcome you, I didn’t just prepare that immortal puppet in the crypt, I also sent this clone out to die under the pretense of seeking the legacy of the Six Thieves Deceive Life. And now, as a show of respect, I’ve come out with my true form.”

The half-complete half-blood-vessel-filled Netherflame smiled. “And therefore, this ceremony is now ready to be completed. Devilbird, have you thought about what I said to you?”

Netherflame looked at Devilbird. Devilbird’s expression darkened. Turning to look at Xu Qing in the tumor, his eyes filled with a decisive look. Spinning in place, he shot toward the empress. At the same time, the clone of Netherflame that they had been fighting erupted with killing intent and also flew toward the empress. The three of them started fighting.

Heaven and earth rocked back and forth. The air crumbled. The entire world began to break apart like a shattering mirror.

Only Netherflame’s true form didn’t seem affected. He simply began to walk toward a shard of the world that contained Xu Qing in the tumor. At the same time, he said, “Devilbird, I swear a dao oath that, after this is over, your fate-soul will be returned to you unharmed, and forever after, you and I will have no conflict. Clone, I promise that, after this is over, you can have the freedom you so desire. As for you, empress... after this is over, you can have the grotto-heaven. Go ahead and resurrect the person you want to resurrect. All I want is for the lot of you to leave me alone while I’m reborn.”

As Netherflame spoke, his eyes locked onto Xu Qing with the same greed and admiration one would expect of someone staring at a precious treasure.

His original plan had been to possess Devilbird. Using the body of a Grand Emperor as the second half of his reborn self would help him rise to the level of a Summer Immortal. Although there would be side-effects, he was confident that, over time, he would be able to recover from them.

But then he had seen Xu Qing! It had stunned him deeply, and as a result, he had changed his plan. He had abandoned any thoughts of possessing Devilbird, and had instead secretly reached out to communicate with him. And then he had manipulated things perfectly to reach this current situation.

Netherflame strode up to the tumor with Xu Qing in it. Looking inside, he licked his lips. A fleshly body like that is simply unimaginable. So what if I have to devour some of its karma....

At this point, his greed had reached the level where he couldn’t control it.

“That body of yours... is mine.”

With that, he extended his right hand, pushing it into the tumor to rest on the top of Xu Qing’s head.

The sky of flesh was like a shattered mirror. Innumerable rifts split the world into numerous fragments. And within every single one of those fragments was a unique heaven and earth.

Within one of those worlds was the empress, Grand Emperor Devilbird, and Netherflame’s clone, who was the grand immortal adept from the eastern Devilbirds.

The other Imperial Sovereigns, who were now hardly more than desiccated corpses, were gasping for breath in their own fragments.

In the very middle of them all was the fragment with Xu Qing and Netherflame’s true self. Xu Qing sat cross-legged, his eyes closed, seemingly unaware of anything happening on the outside. He wasn’t even moving.

Netherflame’s gruish form was half a complete person, with the other half a mass of blood vessels. A malevolent look of greed and anticipation filled his face. He had plunged his right hand into the tumor and placed it on Xu Qing’s head, and was sending terrifying energy directly through that hand and into Xu Qing.

When he spoke, his voice was raspy, but grew louder and louder as he went along. “I have two clones. One is that grand immortal adept of the eastern Devilbirds.
