As his energy poured in through the top of Xu Qing’s head, innumerable strands of the seven emotions and six sensory pleasures spread out, covering Xu Qing and boring into him through his every pore. Xu Qing’s seven emotions were stirred. And along with the six sensory pleasures, which had the same origin, they made him ripe for growth. Next....

“Immortal skill: Five Dogs Cleave Immortals!”

The stingy dog cleaves to a place and loses treasure; the greedy dog cleaves to a place and is bound; the foolish dog cleaves to a place and falls into death; the depraved dog cleaves to a place and falls into hell; the austere dog cleaves to a place and forever loses the body.

This art had been passed down over many years, and had eventually come to be regarded as a gruish magical technique designed to kill. But the truth was that, when it was originally created, it was intended for... possession! [1]

Therefore, in this case, Netherflame’s memories became the stingy dog that would enter Xu Qing’s ‘place’ and cleave to it. It would forcefully cover over Xu Qing’s memories, creating countless white hairs that would make a door of entrance. [2]

That door of entrance was what would allow the possession to take place! When the door opened up inside Xu Qing, it would also form inside Netherflame. The opening of the door would also connect them. Netherflame’s soul would become a gruish white eye. And when the door opened inside him, it would charge into Xu Qing through the door.

Outside evil would invade, spinning to create a vortex.

Having insatiable desire. That is called greed. The greedy dog cleaves to a place and is bound. Renouncing the rules of life. That is called foolishness. The foolish dog cleaves to a place and falls into death.

A power of separation exploded out. Netherflame’s terrifying soul would cleave to him, and would forcibly rip his soul away from his fleshly body. As a result, Xu Qing’s body and soul would be completely unrelated to each other.

When the vortex formed, a white mouth appeared.

Arguing without understanding the facts. That is called depravity. The depraved dog cleaves to a place and falls into hell.

The mouth viciously bit down. It took a bite of his soul!

At that moment of crisis, the eyes of Xu Qing’s soul suddenly opened, and they brimmed with determination and craziness. From the moment Xu Qing realized he was in a deadly situation, he had known that he wasn’t possibly strong enough to fight back against Netherflame’s malicious possession attempt. Any type of resistance would be pointless.

Since he didn’t have the option of fighting back, he decided to intentionally absorb quintessence liquid to nourish his fleshly body and push his body into a state of being increasingly whole. The process itself would cause his fleshly body to reject his soul with increasing intensity.

That was actually what he wanted!

Of course, the process would involve immensely painful pressure on his soul.

The protection provided by his carving knife would be key. Right now, the Five Dogs immortal skill was just increasing the rejection from his fleshly body to his soul, and was actually pushing it toward a crescendo. It was essentially driving his soul away.

As far as Xu Qing was concerned, this was actually his best shot at survival! And thus....

“Five Dogs Cleave Immortals!”

The immortal skill also exploded within Xu Qing’s sea of consciousness. He wasn’t trying to stop Netherflame from carrying out his possession. He wasn’t resisting at all. It was as if his fleshly body didn’t even belong to him! He just... abandoned it without hesitation!

At the same time, he took advantage of the possession of Five Dogs Cleave Immortals, and he also took advantage of the force of expulsion from his fleshly body toward his soul.

The former was a pulling force, the latter was a pushing force. With those two forces working together, Xu Qing’s soul shot out just before it was devoured. It went through the door Netherflame had opened. And left the body!

In the moment that the other soul possessed him, he burned his own soul, used his tattoo of fate, and tapped into the warding spells his Master had put in place. He did not hold anything back. Just when his own soul was about to collapse, he stepped through the door of possession within Netherflame. It took one step for him to leave his fleshly body behind.

Once he was through that door... he entered the fleshly body that Netherflame had abandoned! He stepped right through the door Netherflame himself had opened! He became the greedy dog from Five Dogs Cleave Immortals.

He entered the place and became an external evil! He became the white eye in the opened door inside Netherflame. He was switching bodies with Netherflame!

At any other time, this would have been impossible for Xu Qing. But right now, possessing his enemy was the best path to walk. And it was all because his enemy was trying to possess him.

Xu Qing’s Five Dogs became the pulling force. The expulsion of his fleshly body became the pushing force. And thus, something which normally would have been very difficult to pull off... became a reality.

Most importantly was that, just before leaving, Xu Qing put certain things in place! For the first time, Netherflame was caught by surprise by Xu Qing’s actions. However, he was still confident in being able to stop him.

But then the fleshly body warding spells activated. At the same time, a malicious will erupted from the back of the fleshly body. That was when the first instability surfaced in the possession attempt, and it forced Netherflame to consider the situation.

Killing Xu Qing wasn’t the point. Netherflame wanted to push Five Dogs Cleave Immortals to the point of completion and gain complete control over this fleshly body. That was what he had chosen to do. Compared to that, everything else was secondary.

As for abandoning his old body....

That body isn’t even complete. It’s missing the Devilbird part. It was only my soul that managed to force it into a state of balance. Now that my soul is gone from it, it’s like a candle flickering in the wind. It won’t be long before it just crumbles.

Laughing coldly, Netherflame ignored what was happening there. Going all out with his own soul, he focused on the fifth will of Five Dogs Cleave Immortals.

It was a white face. With it, the Five Dogs immortal skill was complete, and it formed a complete face. White hair fluttered, and it grinned enigmatically, as if it were crying and laughing at the same time. It was very gruish. Its might became a restrictive warding spell, and its power covered the back of the fleshly body. It formed a balance.

Within the tumor, the ‘Xu Qing’ seated cross-legged started chanting, “Renouncing the three paths of hell before attaining lifelessness. That is called austerity. The austere dog cleaves to a place and forever loses the body.”

Smiling faintly, he opened his eyes. Though he still looked like Xu Qing on the outside, his eyes were profoundly ancient, and he contained a terrifying energy that made him seem completely and utterly different compared to before. And his fleshly body power was rising.

The might of an Imperial Sovereign pulsed out, and it was getting closer to the level of a Grand Emperor. The sense of perfection caused Netherflame’s eyes to gleam with praise.

“This body was wasted on you, boy. Your soul couldn’t sustain the full majesty of its mightiness.”

Outside of the tumor, his abandoned body suddenly shivered and staggered backward a few paces. All the while, it was withering, with chunks of flesh falling off it. It was as if the force inside couldn’t sustain a balance with the body itself. The eyes struggled to open, and it was Xu Qing’s gaze that appeared. But that was all.

Netherflame shook his head as if he was looking at an ant. He prepared to lift his right hand. But then, all of a sudden....

Within the body he had just possessed, the warding spell power that he had suppressed with Five Dogs Cleave Immortals suddenly erupted as the fleshly body power reached a tipping point thanks to the new soul.

The balance was broken. There was another explosion!

Master Seventh had actually put two warding spells in place. One was a limitation on the Imperial Sovereign level. The other was a limitation on the Grand Emperor level.

The former had been in balance because of Netherflame’s Five Dogs Cleave Immortals. But now... the second warding spell seal had been removed. In the blink of an eye, a host of silver threads appeared on the fleshly body, which turned into innumerable sealing marks. They were so densely packed they were like flowing water that swept back and forth. It took only a moment for it to create a huge net that covered the entire body, flickering with silver light that surpassed natural laws.

As soon as it appeared, it suppressed the rising power of the fleshly body. It had been put in place by Master Seventh to protect Xu Qing.

Seeing that, Netherflame’s eyes flickered with mysterious light, and he frowned slightly. However, he wasn’t very surprised. After all, there was no way this fleshly body had been prepared by some member of the Junior generation. It was obviously the work of some almighty being. Therefore, it made perfect sense that he would leave some contingency plans in place on it.

Whoever left behind this warding spell is no simpleton.

Netherflame’s eyes narrowed. Reaching up, he placed his right hand atop his head. Next, the black lotus beneath him began spinning, allowing him to suck up all the remaining quintessence in the tumor. The black lotus bloomed, and chains like stamens whipped about. Under his control, they wrapped around the body. They became a suppressing force.

“Although the warding spell can’t be wiped out right away,” Netherflame said coolly, “I can at least force a state of balance. That will work. In the future, I’ll just need some time, and I can wipe it out! So, boy, what else did you leave behind in this body? The candle on the back?”

Rumbling sounds echoed out from behind him as the fire of the candle erupted, illuminating the world around Netherflame.

“I studied that candle for a lot longer than you ever did.” Netherflame waved his hand, severing a portion of his own soul and sending it over to the candle tattoo to create a lampshade. “Look, that’s all it takes to control it. And then you can tap into some of its power. So, boy, what else did you leave behind?”

Netherflame smiled faintly. However, even as his words were still ringing out, and before Xu Qing could even answer, a heaven-shaking, earth-shattering roar of rage echoed out from the depths of the transparent sea below.

“You want to hurt my little Junior Brother, you old codger? You’d better check in with me first!”

The transparent sea started seething. A huge tsunami wave rolled out in all directions. And then the sea started changing color. It was turning blue! Innumerable blue worms could be seen in the huge tsunami wave. As they converged, they turned into a gigantic blue hand holding a bone cauldron. And it was heading straight toward Netherflame!

The bone cauldron was made from Erniu’s third life by Grand Emperor Immortal Skill from that time. It was terrifyingly mighty and could use a will of greed to refine the dome of heaven. As the huge hand made of blue worms broke out of the sea, spraying water everywhere, it closed in on the tumor that contained Netherflame.

Netherflame sat cross-legged within it looking calm. However, the truth was that he knew how amazing this body was, and also how difficult it was going to be to fully control it.

The source of difficulty was the karma, but also... Master Seventh’s warding spells! Although he had suppressed the warding spells, the truth was that all he had done was barely manage to reach a level of balance. At the moment, he could not fully control the body.

All he could do was look on with a cold gleam in his eyes as the huge bone cauldron raced toward him. The cauldron’s top then opened, scooped the tumor inside, then slammed shut.

“Be refined!!” countless blue worms howled simultaneously.

The huge hand collapsed, turning into a writhing sea of worms that started swarming around the cauldron. Their momentum increased exponentially, causing heaven and earth to shake violently, and turning the sky into a blue vortex. As it spun madly, the blue worms spat out intense frigid energy. The frigid energy poured into the cauldron, but it didn’t turn into ice. Instead, it became a blue fire that started refining the tumor inside of it. Intense rumbling sounds grew louder and louder.

Erniu didn’t dare to get careless. He poured all of his effort into controlling and bolstering the bone cauldron. He held nothing back to refine the tumor. In the end, he knew that he didn’t even have a good shot of succeeding. This was Grand Emperor Netherflame he was dealing with, after all.

However, this was a critical moment, and time was of the essence, so this was the best option. He needed to buy as much time as possible for the empress and Xu Qing.

Hopefully that would enable the empress to come help as quickly as possible, and also give Xu Qing the opportunity to do whatever else he had planned. And thus, Erniu was going all out. Rumbling sounds echoed out constantly as the vortex of blue worms spun faster and faster. freewebnovel.com

Off in the distance, the empress could see what was happening, and had a grim expression on hēr face. Then golden light flickered around hēr, blurring everything; apparently, shē was trying to break free.

Hēr opponent, Grand Emperor Devilbird, looked surprised. Seeing that the empress was tapping into godly might, he had no choice but to back away. However, on the other side of the empress was Netherflame’s clone. His eyes shone with determination as he shot forward and turned into a black lotus. Black fire surged, sweeping out everywhere, and completely sealing the fragment of space. Everything in that area blurred, making it impossible to see inside. However, the rumbling from inside quickly formed a resonance with the rumbling from the bone cauldron.

Meanwhile, Xu Qing took advantage of the moment to finish possessing the Grand Emperor’s fleshly body. The world around him was being slowly refined inside of Erniu’s cauldron. The tumor was on fire, and the Imperial Sovereigns’ quintessence was bubbling and boiling.

As for Netherflame, he remained seated in a cross-legged position as he opened his eyes. They glittered grimly.

Erniu was his first slip-up. He had previously overlooked this seemingly inconsequential cultivator, only for that cultivator to pull off a completely unexpected move at a critical moment.

It’s a bit of a surprise that I failed to predict this person’s interference or even existence. How could I not tell what sort of reserve powers he had in place, nor sense the existence of this bone cauldron...? Either someone is interfering, or... there is something seriously suspicious about this person. Very interesting. Both the Elder and Junior Brother are very unusual. In that case, what about their Master...?

Grand Emperor Netherflame’s eyes narrowed as he gave a cold harrumph. Although there had been some unexpected twists, he was still confident that he could come out on top.

I’ve been preparing for this rebirth for a long time. And that’s especially true of my secluded meditation facilities, this grotto-heaven that isn’t part of Revered Ancient. As long as this grotto-heaven exists, then no one from the outside can interfere with me. Though I did change my plans upon seeing this particular fleshly body, in the end... everything is under control. My control.

Netherflame remained calm in the face of the refining power. He took a deep breath, which immediately resulted in him absorbing more than thirty percent of the liquid.

A second black lotus appeared over his head. It pulsed with terrifying black flames, and it sent out a host of chains that connected it with the flower beneath his feet. As they spun, the chain pierced out of the tumor and rocketed toward the bone cauldron. And the boundless black fire suppressed the other fire within the cauldron.

The two lotuses caused Netherflame’s aura to surge, and as the refining fires were suppressed, he fought Master Seventh’s warding spells and also began to extinguish the candle on his back. The balance that had been lost was now regained.

There are some upsides to being in this cauldron. It’s helping to screen me away from the outside. And that buys me time to get control over this fleshly body. I’d say it’ll be an hour at the most before I’m strong enough to exercise control. And when that happens....

Netherflame opened his eyes, and deep inside there was a gleam of violet. His pupils suddenly constricted.

My eyes have violet light in them?

For an almighty individual like Netherflame, the unknown was always a surprise, and was an indication of many possible variables. The violet light in his eyes was the second unexpected twist. Even as Netherflame trembled inside, more violet light erupted. He couldn’t control it. And as it filled him head to toe, he realized where it was coming from.

It was coming from the flesh in his chest. Right there in the chest was some object that Grand Emperor Netherflame hadn’t noticed up to this point. It was a violet-colored crystal! [1]

Upon noticing it, his face flickered with dramatic emotion, the reason being that this object existed outside of his perception! None of his previous deductions had revealed its existence. And even after the possession was complete, he had been completely unaware of it until it emitted violet light. It was almost as if it had an unimaginably high personhood. If it didn’t want him to sense it, then he would never possibly notice it.

This was an unexpected twist that shook him far deeper than what just happened with Erniu.

What was more, within the depths of the violet crystal was a figure with no facial features, seated cross-legged. It looked like little more than a shadow. At almost exactly the same moment that he looked at the shadow, it opened its eyes. Then, it was almost as if the violet crystal had been activated. It erupted with dazzling brightness, like a sea of light that enveloped the entire fleshly body, as well as Netherflame’s soul.

In the thousand years that Netherflame had been in seclusion, he had never felt like he had lost control. But right now, that was how he felt, and it filled him with an intense sensation of deadly crisis. He was actually struggling to control his breathing.

This thing is completely beyond me! What is it??

A deep sense of unease erupted within Netherflame. However, it was a critical moment, so he didn’t hesitate at all to try to seal the crystal with every ounce of strength he possessed. But the spread of the violet light had a widespread influence. It also affected... Master Seventh’s warding spells. Netherflame’s control over the warding spells collapsed. And then the candle on his back erupted into flame.

Thanks to the violet light, Erniu’s bone cauldron erupted with greater force.

Astonished, Netherflame opened his mouth and inhaled as deeply as possible. All of the remaining seventy percent of the quintessence in the tumor surged into him, and he borrowed its power to fight back. He gritted his teeth, and fluctuations rolled out of his soul, revealing something that had been concealed within, something that he considered as valuable as his own life.

This item was his greatest secret. Golden light glittered in his soul. It was a drop of water. A drop of golden water. Put most precisely, it was a golden drop of river water.

The moment the water drop appeared, a majestic golden river materialized in Netherflame’s soul.

“Mother River...” called Netherflame.

Deep rumbling sounds echoed out as a boundless golden river flowed, not in the Devilbird holy land, not in the Revered Ancient mainland, but in the north of the Ninth Star Ring in the boundless starry sky.... Within that river were countless heavenly bodies as well as innumerable living things. And there were lotuses.

Seated cross-legged on the lotuses were innumerable figures, including humans, nonhumans, cultivators, and gods.... On one lotus was a cultivator who looked like a human. Suddenly, his eyes opened, and they shone sharply as he looked out into the starry sky. Rising to his feet, he clasped hands and bowed to the river.

“Mother River, a game piece deployed to Eminent Desolation’s location has sent a distress signal.”

The river water rippled. A moment passed, and a tiny fragment of a terrifying, indescribable will awoke.

It was only a fragment, but it was enough to affect millions upon millions of heavenly bodies in the river. The hearts of countless living beings trembled.

“It’s not time yet....”

Upon hearing that, the cultivator bowed his head and sat back down. “In that case, he will either live or die based on that single drop of Mother River water.”

No one in the secluded meditation facilities had any idea what was happening inside the cauldron.

No one but Xu Qing, that is. When the violet crystal erupted, his connection with it allowed him to sense what was happening. And that was exactly how Xu Qing had planned it! He had left his body to activate Master Seventh’s first warding spell. He had also unsealed the candle to ensure that, when the warding spell activated, the candle would ignite. He knew that it would affect Netherflame.

At the same time, he had left the violet crystal behind! He had left it in his fleshly body. What was more, he had left Little Shadow inside of it, with instructions to unleash the power of the violet crystal when the critical moment arrived. He wasn’t really sure how it would turn out.

But over the years, he had come to realize something. And that was... that no one knew about the violet crystal except him. Not Master Seventh. Not the empress. Not even that old man from the Fifth Star Ring he had encountered in the outer sea had noticed it. Therefore, in this most desperate of situations, he had chosen a path of no return.

To be honest, he didn’t care what the violet crystal did. The reason was that the eruption of the violet crystal was just a cover for the last part of his overarching plan.

If Netherflame noticed what he was really doing, he would stop him. And Xu Qing couldn’t afford to be interrupted.

That was the real purpose of the violet crystal eruption. It was to be a delay and a distraction to Netherflame.

Xu Qing took a moment to check his current fleshly body. Based on what he could sense, this body contained a terrifying essence. Unfortunately, he was currently like a child trapped in a thousand-pound suit of armor. He couldn’t control it. There was something wrong with this body, as if it had previously existed in a state of balance, which had since been broken....

It wasn’t going to last for much longer. It was already crumbling and withering.

But this is enough....

Eyes shining with determination, he spoke in a raspy voice. “I wish for....”

A gruish mask appeared out of nowhere. It pierced through all obstacles, even the void itself, and even space-time, to appear in front of Xu Qing. It was as if it had been waiting. It looked at Xu Qing.

He looked back. “I wish that I could use this body as nutrients to reconstruct my original body!”

At almost the exact same instant that Xu Qing’s mask appeared.... In another spatial fragment, Grand Emperor Devilbird was working with Netherflame’s clone to keep the empress under control. Apparently, Grand Emperor Devilbird sensed what had just happened, as his expression flickered, and he turned to look in the direction of Xu Qing. All of a sudden, rumbling sounds seemed to fill his heart and mind.

He knew exactly what that mask was! He had searched the Devilbird holy land for years looking for it. However, just as that black-robed man had said, the mask... didn’t want to be found. In fact, the more you looked for it, the less likely you would be to find it.

“I can’t believe he has it!” Grand Emperor Devilbird said, inhaling sharply. He turned, planning to break free from the fighting to go after the mask.

But then... the empress’ eyes glittered coldly despite being locked down by the Grand Emperor and Netherflame’s clone. Shē took a step forward, breaking free from all obstacles and bindings.

Grand Emperor Devilbird could not possibly break free.

The moment Xu Qing gave voice to his wish, the mask smiled broadly and gruishly. At the same time, a voice drifted out to fill the surrounding world.

“Granted. As for the price—”

The masks’ smile grew even more gruish as it spoke, but before the words were completely spoken, it crumbled into ashes.

As it disappeared, Xu Qing’s fleshly body rumbled loudly, and a force filled him, so powerful it was difficult to put into words. It surpassed the power of gods or cultivators or heavenly bodies or even the universe. It became a stream of energy that swept over Xu Qing’s current fleshly body. The void crumbled, separating from all things. Nothing could stop this force. Nothing could block it.

Xu Qing shivered from head to toe as his fleshly body started crumbling to pieces. It started with the face. Then the flesh seemed to lose its capacity to stick to the body and began peeling off. As it did, it turned into crystalline light.

Next, the half of the body covered with veins also collapsed, and also turned into crystalline light. Ultimately, both halves of the body crumbled because of the unimaginable wish power.....

The incredible life force within the body scattered. All elements that could sustain life were extracted. The flesh couldn’t remain as a whole, and the shocking power reverted it to its most primitive state.

The crystalline light actually came from countless transparent crystals that normally weren’t visible, which bound the flesh together. freewebnovel.com

Those crystals had no color. They simply reflected the color of the world around them. Because all impurities had been removed from them, any consciousness that had remained in them was wiped out. And as that happened, they became the ultimate origin of life force. They became primeval essence!

Xu Qing’s soul hovered within the light. And as his divine will spread out, the countless crystals began to swirl around and collide with each other....

As they absorbed Xu Qing’s color, and as they sucked in his energy, they began to form life force sparks that belonged to Xu Qing. They contained Xu Qing’s memories. They contained reversals of time and transpositions of space. They contained the intersections of daoist magics. In other words... they relied on Xu Qing’s soul to pulse with the soul essence of Xu Qing’s life force.

It was like a guidepost. Xu Qing’s soul essence guided the crystals to reverse engineer his body. It was a process that would normally take a long time, as it was essentially creating something from nothing.

Xu Qing opened his eyes in soul form. He looked at the huge cauldron and everything around it, including the countless blue worms.

“Eldest Brother, give me my remains.”

The moment he spoke via divine will, the blue worms started shining with blue light, and from within the forehead of each flew a gray light. The light converged to form a golden bone fragment. That fragment was what had been left behind when Xu Qing self-detonated. It was a physical manifestation of his essence!

It merged into Xu Qing’s soul, and the power of the wish began making his body anew. And this time, it was more perfect.

In an instant, the guidance of his soul caused the innumerable crystals to rush to the golden bone fragment. They became nutrients. They became the power of life force essence that caused the bone... to start growing! Gradually, it turned into a complete bone.

More bones began to grow. Then veins spread out, along with flesh. Then skin.... And then, as Erniu watched on excitedly, and as the surrounding world bore witness... Xu Qing’s familiar old body formed!

He was tall, with flowing violet hair, and a perfect face that could only be described as incomparably perfect. His aura was not that of an immortal. It was not that of a god. It was that of a mortal! He was back in his original mortal form! He was like a newborn infant. A sense of purity filled him. A sense of cleanliness inundated him.

Xu Qing’s soul was perfectly fused, and it was telling him... that this really was his own body. His soul was telling him... that this was the most suitable form for him.

Xu Qing opened his eyes. He felt as if he had been reborn. It was as if he had gone back to the very beginning.

“This is my true self,” he murmured. “The fleshly body made from Eminent Desolation is now a god clone of mine.”

He looked up. He wasn’t looking at the refinement going on in the cauldron. He didn’t look at the empress. Instead, he fixed his gaze on the crystalline light. Remolding his own body had only taken part of the life force essence from Netherflame’s body. And his new fleshly body didn’t even have a cultivation base. Now, an idea that had been percolating in the back of his mind for years was suddenly a real possibility.

I’ve walked the path of gods, and the limitations I faced made progress slow. Every step involved breaking through powerful shackles. In the end, I don’t think it’s the right path for me to walk. Maybe my god clone could walk it. I need to get that clone back... and let it walk the pure path of the gods. As for my true self, I need to walk... the pure way of immortals! That is the appropriate path for me!

Eyes shining with determination, he unhesitatingly inhaled. Instantly, the essence crystals shot toward him, entered his body, and turned into pure spirit energy. It flowed through his meridians, instantly giving a cultivation base to his mortal body.

First level of Qi Condensation! In the blink of an eye, the essence poured into him, causing his cultivation base to advance at freakishly indescribable speed. He went right to the tenth level of Qi Condensation. For most cultivators, the tenth level was the limit of Qi Condensation. But Xu Qing’s fleshly body had been made anew with primeval essence. Because of that, his limitations were beyond ordinary. He quickly jumped to the nineteenth level of Qi Condensation!

Only then did he break through to Foundation Establishment. 121 dharma apertures opened in an instant. But then, an additional 26 hidden apertures were blown open by the essence power. This was absolutely unprecedented! Rumbling sounds echoed out as 147 dharma apertures shone dazzlingly as they turned into life flames.

They didn’t become five flames. They became nine! And then, Xu Qing’s life lamps appeared beneath the nine flames. Life lamps were made from one’s blood. And Xu Qing’s life lamps looked like sundials. As they appeared one by one, his life lamps raged high.

Watching this happen left Erniu feeling deeply shaken. He had lived many lives, yet had never seen anything like this before.

However, I do remember hearing about... the legendary path of the extreme immortal in the Deep Earth star ring....

Meanwhile, Xu Qing’s cultivation base continued to climb. Nine flames erupted, giving rise to heavenly palaces.

Legend had it that in Deep Earth, there were a total of thirty-three heavens. That legend was now becoming a reality in Xu Qing’s sea of consciousness. Thirty-three heavenly palaces rumbled into being, becoming completely true and real. And within each of the heavenly palaces was a nascent soul, seated cross-legged and glittering with silvery light.

Each looked like an immortal. Every step Xu Qing took reached an extreme ultimate limit. This was the pure path of the immortal that Xu Qing wanted to walk. It was also the ‘extreme path of the immortal’ that Erniu had mentioned.

After Nascent Soul was Spirit Trove, and thanks to the stimulation of the primeval essence crystals, he reached the peak of that level as well. Nine huge troves erupted like nine staggering volcanoes. Rumbling sounds echoed out from within Xu Qing, spreading far and wide. If you looked closely, you would see that the nine secret troves were like erupting furnaces. However, they were empty inside. They had no divine abilities or daoist magics.

Xu Qing thought about all his divine abilities. And then, astonishingly, a dandelion seed appeared in one of his secret troves. That dandelion seed contained an imprint of the original divine ability that Xu Qing had fully mastered.

It was... Fishing the Moon in the Well!

Fishing the Moon in the Well’s substructure... is formed from the void. It’s about creating something from nothing. It is a dao related to space. And now, I make it one of my Spirit Trove secret magics. As for the second....

Xu Qing stared at the dandelion seed with Fishing the Moon in the Well in it, all while putting more thought into the subject. Suddenly, the dandelion seed superimposed on itself. Then, it split, becoming a host of dandelion seeds that spread through his sea of consciousness. Xu Qing’s heart sank at the sight of it.

At the same time, the profoundly ancient voice of a woman spoke by means of the dandelion seeds, her voice echoing in his sea of consciousness.

“There’s no need for such confusion. I’m using a secret magic to transmit my divine will to you. You’ve finally stepped onto the extreme path of immortals in Deep Earth. Last time, I gave you ten breaths of time to gain enlightenment of the immortal essence of Deep Earth. Today, based on the ancient agreement, you step onto the extreme path of immortals as a mortal, and therefore I’m giving you thirty breaths of time.[1]

“Deep Earth has a daoist magic called the Eight Extreme Daos. If you are connected to this daoist magic by destiny, you can obtain it. I have nothing more to say.” [2]

The voice faded away.

***

Outside of the Devilbird holy land, in the imperial capital of humankind in the Revered Ancient mainland, there was a bustling area within which was an ancient temple. Despite being in such a busy location, no passersby realized it was there. It was almost as if it didn’t exist within reality.

An old man was just on his way out of the temple. He looked bleak.

The very same palace lord that Xu Qing had met in the Summer Immortal Palace years ago was seated there cross-legged, looking sorrowfully at the departing figure.

Next to the palace lord was a little butterfly, who said, “Master, who was that old fellow? And why are you helping that other guy I hate? And also, why do you look so sad?”

The palace lord of the Summer Immortal Palace sighed softly. “He’s an old friend of mine. Unfortunately, a storm is coming, and I’m not sure if his umbrella can hold up to it.”[3]

1. Reference for “ten breaths of time” is chapter 808. ☜

2. Most readers in Chinese seemed to agree that these Eight Extreme Daos are the same as the Celestial Ancestor’s Eight Extreme Dao(s) that were first mentioned in Renegade Immortal chapter 1917, and were elaborated on in chapter 1957 and subsequent chapters of that novel. ☜

3. The ‘storm is coming’ here is literally a ‘transformation to sky/heaven’ and is also a common metaphor referring to a change in rulership, regime, or the general situation of a land/nation. I’m opting for the ‘storm is coming’ translation because of the way it flows here and in other places. The vast majority of readers in the comments section in Chinese seemed to take the umbrella to be a metaphor, although there were a couple comments mentioning actual umbrellas or parasols that existed in other novels in the Er Gen universe. ☜

A sigh echoed through the lonely time within the Summer Immortal Palace. Only the butterfly in the temple could hear it. And yet, she didn’t actually understand what the sigh meant. She was still obsessed with finding out why her Master called her naive, and why her Master was helping that annoying guy she hated. Because of that, she didn’t notice the gleam of determination in her Master’s eyes.

***

Of course, Xu Qing did not hear that sigh. He was still in Netherflame’s secluded meditation facilities, looking at the dandelion seeds. A few breaths of time passed.

“Eight Extreme Daos...” he murmured. With that, he sent his divine will into the dandelion seeds.

Rumbling sounds filled Xu Qing’s mind, like the explosive sound that echoed out upon the creation of heaven and earth. The sound shattered time, becoming a force of attraction that dragged Xu Qing into the location that held the immortal essence of Deep Earth.

The ground was made of flesh and blood that seemed to go on forever. Growing out of that sludge was the same gigantic dandelion he had seen before. The stalk of the dandelion was covered with innumerable symbols, each of which emanated terrifying might. All of it combined to make the dandelion miraculous and one-of-a-kind.

As for the ground, it was actually formed from the corpses of countless gods. Thēy had been turned into a dandelion that provided eternal power. The god souls of these gods were trapped, forced to bow, with no choice but to howl in terror and agony. Thēir godly voices just helped the dandelion to grow.

This was the land of the immortal essence. Nine Summer Immortals had buried a god world to create it.

Immortal essence!

Xu Qing had been here once, which meant that this was his second time. Yet it was still just as shocking to behold the dandelion. It was in full flower, sending countless wispy seeds out into the distance. At the same time, some seeds returned from afar, to be absorbed by the dandelion before being sent out again. It was an endless cycle.

Xu Qing sent out his divine will, which split into millions, tens of millions, or even hundreds of millions of strands that swept after the seeds, filling the void, filling the starry sky, and filling all the legacies.

Countless daoist magics appeared in front of him. Countless blurry figures stepped into his senses. They were training. They were practicing cultivation. Time seemed to lose purpose. Space seemed to lose meaning. The only thing in existence were the never-ending legacies. It was like being in a majestic library.

As Xu Qing studied such things, he was repeating ‘Eight Extreme Daos’ in his soul. Even as he did, within the boundless legacies within the immortal essence, three seeds became clear and floated toward him.

At the same moment that Xu Qing noticed the three seeds, the palace lord’s ancient voice echoed within the land of the immortal essence. “Those are three of the Eight Extreme Daos that make up the legacy. You only have time to gain enlightenment of two. Make your decision. I can’t help.”

Xu Qing looked quietly at the three seeds.

Within the first he saw a figure seated in meditation, seeking enlightenment.

In the second, he saw two figures looking at each other. He couldn’t make out their facial features.

Within the third, he saw three figures, apparently in the middle of passing on a legacy.

He would have two chances. What would he choose?

Xu Qing looked them over before focusing on the second. His eyes shone with determination. The reason he decided to pick the second was that he got the vague sense that the two figures inside actually had the same origin.

A clone and a true self?

He sent his divine will into the second of the dandelion seeds. Heaven and earth trembled.

At the same time, a scene from the history of Deep Earth played out for Xu Qing to see. He saw an unfamiliar continent that couldn’t possibly compare to Revered Ancient. But there was something special about it. There were a lot of fierce beasts in it. Apparently, those beasts provided the operational force of the continent. [1]

But what caught Xu Qing’s attention was a palace atop the continent. The canopy of heaven was over it, which seemed to have been ripped out to be an independent entity. Night and day were currently switching!

As Xu Qing looked down at it all, a sigh drifted out from the palace. The sigh was extraordinary. It ripped apart heaven and earth, causing a host of magical symbols to be born. Upon looking at the magical symbols, Xu Qing determined that they contained essence power.

They’re warding spells.

Things were starting to get interesting. He wanted to look at the person practicing cultivation in the palace, but something was preventing him. It wasn’t the person inside, but rather, the power of the dandelion.

After some thought, Xu Qing came to the conclusion that he could only act as an observer. He could only see what was happening, not interfere or participate. Time passed. More and more warding spells appeared in the sky above the palace. However, they seemed blurry as if they were beginning to scatter.

But then a shocking whistling sound emerged from the palace as five beams of light appeared. Though Xu Qing couldn’t see them clearly, there were clearly five people inside of them. And Xu Qing could also sense... the power of the five elements.

Metal. Wood. Water. Fire. Earth. Xu Qing looked closely at them. He watched as the five beams of light pulsed with the sensation of the five elements, until... they combined to create a five elements body.

The body stood tall amidst heaven and earth, a giant that was fully 3,000 meters tall! The presence of the body also started to stabilize the vanishing warding spells created by the magical symbols of essence.

But then, a ragged howl echoed out from the depths of the lands below. A fierce soul body appeared along with the howl. It was a sphere of flesh with a huge, brutal, insane eye in the middle of it. [2]

The moment the beast appeared, Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. It actually reminded Xu Qing a lot of Hellfei. And the biggest similarity between the two was the raging ferocity they both had.[3]

The fierce soul looked at the five elements true body in the sky above the palace, and its lone eye glittered with greed. It charged forward. As it neared, it shrieked piercingly. Before it could arrive, though, a tranquil voice echoed through heaven and earth.

“Calm.”

That word caused everything to go still. The howling soul went completely still, and even the ferocity in its lone eye seemed frozen.

Xu Qing looked on with curiosity glittering in his eyes.

When the fierce soul froze in place, the surrounding magical symbols seemed to pulse with a hunger that had been building for countless years. And then, upon seeing some food, they madly rushed toward the soul. One after another, they burrowed into it. The soul shivered, and as it was devoured, it began shining with a mysterious light.

The ferocity in the eye disappeared, to be replaced by an illusory figure. That figure stepped out from within the eye to stand in the open, emanating a majestic power of an essence warding spell.

Xu Qing was shaken. This is the true body formed by the essence warding spells? The five elements true body drew out the fierce soul, and then the fierce soul was used as nutrients to complete the creation process!

Xu Qing continued to watch as the scene played out to the end.

As night and day shifted in the sky, the daylight became a rising sun, and the flowing light entered into the still body of the soul. The fierce soul trembled and shrank down again as a second figure emerged from its eye. The figure shone with bright light that made it seem like a sun. And as it emerged from the eye of the beast, it stood next to the true body made from the warding spell essence.

Next, the remaining darkness of night also entered the body of the soul. The soul shivered, and then its eye collapsed as a third true body emerged. When this figure emerged, the ultimate killing intent exploded out along with it. Everything trembled.

Xu Qing stared at the third essence body, and his heart raced. Next, the five elements true body began to absorb the power of the fierce soul. Xu Qing was now starting to understand what was going on.

When the soul was ripped apart, the parts instinctively wanted to come together again. That instinct became a guiding force that surpassed the fierce soul. It became a medium by which the true bodies could bridge together and fuse!

As Xu Qing came to those conclusions, a black bolt of lightning exploded from within the palace. Along with it came a very cold voice.

“Combine!”

At almost the same time that the voice echoed out, a majestic divine will enveloped heaven and earth.

The bodies combined! They turned into a fiendish figure with black hair! An extreme aura erupted from the figure, something that wished to destroy all living things, to eradicate heaven and earth. It was an essence power that represented slaughter!

A sonorous voice echoed out from the palace. “From now on, you will replace me in hunting down my enemies! You will spread my destructive intent and kill those that seek to harm me! Your name is Slaughter and you dao name is Punishment!”

The scene ended there. [4]

The world in front of Xu Qing’s eyes collapsed, and as it did, his divine will returned to the lands of the immortal essence. The second of the dandelion seeds dissipated.

Then the palace lord’s voice echoed out again. “You just witnessed the integration and unification, one of the precious aspects of the Eight Extreme Daos. Whether or not you master it will be up to your own good fortune.”

Xu Qing thought back to what he had just witnessed. A moment passed. “Senior... who was that person?”

The palace lord didn’t answer the question. After remaining silent for a moment, she said, “Perhaps you’ll encounter him in the timescape. The two of you are the same type of person.”

Xu Qing looked at the spot where the second dandelion seed had been moments ago. Then he looked at the first dandelion seed and sent his divine will inside. An instant later, an ancient scene played out for him.

He saw a person that appeared to be a middle-aged cultivator in an imperial robe. He seemed to be the ancestor of a species, as countless people were offering him worship and calling him ‘Celestial Ancestor.’ He was currently bowing to a broken stone, upon which was carved a symbol that was difficult to make out clearly. [5]

The symbol depicted a crystal that had been broken into ten irregularly shaped parts. Among them, five represented metal, wood, water, fire, and earth. One of them contained space, while another contained time. It was impossible to say what the other three were. The crystal was surrounded by the images of infants and stars. It seemed to depict the creation of worlds.

As the Celestial Ancestor bowed, he seemed to gain enlightenment of a technique from within the broken crystal. Then the symbol blurred away and didn’t return.

Xu Qing was shaken. He wasn’t sure what the Celestial Ancestor had seen, but it seemed like he had been looking at the birth of a star ring. As for the ten shattered pieces of the crystal, the power within was clearly that of... the Eight Extreme Daos.

“Origin...” he murmured.

He was back in the land of immortal essence. After a moment, he closed his eyes to analyze and seek enlightenment of everything he had seen.

Time passed. It was hard to say how much time went by within the dandelion. It might have seemed to be thousands of years, but in reality, it was only thirty breaths of time.

“Time’s up,” said the palace lord.

Xu Qing opened his eyes. Within them were the five elements. He stood and bowed.

1. Many Chinese readers seemed to think that this place is a version (perhaps an early version) of the Immortal Astral Continent from Renegade Immortal, which was described initially in chapter 1617 of that novel, although it was mentioned a few times before that. ☜

2. Chinese readers came to the conclusion that this beast was the same beast (or type of beast?) that the translator of Renegade Immortal rendered as “Luo Hou” in chapter 2046. ☜

3. Hellfei first appeared in chapter 888 of this novel. ☜

4. The scene in this chapter is obviously a reflection of what happened in chapter 2046 of Renegade Immortal. Many lines were exact copies, but many lines were not exact copies, although obviously intended to carry a similar meaning. The character Slaughter also appeared a number of times in I Shall Seal the Heavens, the first time being in chapter 1122. ☜

5. The term ‘Celestial Ancestor’ comes up a lot in Renegade Immortal. I think the first true explanation or mention comes in chapter 1800. In chapter 1825 there is a mistranslation in English, or at least a lack of continuity. The chapter is titled “Eight Signs” where in reality it’s the “Eight Extreme(s)” that are the same characters from the “Eight Extreme Daos.” The chapter title of 1825 should really be “The Celestial Ancestor’s Eight Extremes” or perhaps “The Celestial Ancestor’s Eight Extreme Daos.” Incidentally, the Chinese character being rendered as celestial here could also be rendered as immortal. If ever one day I did a master edit of all of Er Gen’s works to try to create continuity between everything, I would probably change Celestial Ancestor to Immortal Ancestor. It is what it is. There are many instances in my past translations of Er Gen works where I used celestial instead of immortal for that character. ☜

It was a bow to offer thanks for the guidance given. The moment he formed the immortal body, the guidance given had provided incredible help to Xu Qing in walking the path of the pure immortal. It aided him in walking a more correct way.

After bowing, the immortal essence faded away, becoming a dandelion seed. The dandelion seed then faded away, disappearing completely from Xu Qing’s sea of consciousness.

The nine secret trove furnaces continued to erupt, and in one of them, Fishing the Moon in the Well swirled, emanating the power of the void and the will of space.

Xu Qing’s soul was waking up. When he opened his eyes, the five elements erupted from within them. He knew how to walk the path going forward.

The so-called Eight Extreme Daos.... That is the earliest natural law required for the birth of a star ring. The first five extremes are rather simple. The latter three... well, that cultivator called the Celestial Ancestor lacked the perception and ability to go back through space and time, and thus, had to fill in the empty spots after the first five. That was what got passed down.

The end result was a different version of the Eight Extreme Daos. The reality is that the true Eight Extreme Daos include metal, wood, water, fire, and earth... and after that... time and space.

Those are the seven in total. But there are still three more extremes....

Xu Qing thought back to the symbol of the crystal broken into ten parts. The last three of them had been blurry.

Is it possible that the complete technique should have a different name? Is it the Ten Extreme Daos?

The irregularly shaped pieces of broken crystal were the strongest evidence to support that conclusion as far as he was concerned.

If you put them all together, they would form a complete crystal.

Xu Qing’s soul shivered as he realized something. That completed shape was completely and utterly the same as his own violet crystal! That being said, Xu Qing was well aware that now wasn’t the time to sit around pondering his violet crystal.

What was most important right now was to complete the formation of his fleshly body. He had no time to waste. Though it had seemed like he spent a lot of time gaining enlightenment from ancient times, the reality was that he had only spent thirty breaths of time with the immortal essence. And in the real world, only an instant had passed.

Xu Qing’s soul surged, and his divine will became a voice that spoke, drifting out through his nostrils like a command that could not be ignored.

“Metal!”

This place was not the Revered Ancient mainland. Netherflame’s secluded meditation facilities were isolated from the outside world. They were a standalone location, and they were completely sealed. Therefore, the five elements affected acted a bit differently here than they would outside.

If he used the energy of heaven and earth in this specific location to complete his five elements body to perfection, without any flaws, if he achieved his dao in this grotto-heaven... then he would be restrained here.

That was not what he wanted. He wanted to use his own five yin organs as the five elements!

If his five yin organs became the source of the five elements, then it didn’t matter if he was in this grotto-heaven or in Revered Ancient, or in the starry sky. It wouldn’t matter where he was. It wouldn’t matter what heaven he was in. He would not be bound. By cultivating his own body, he would be free. That was the pure path of the immortal. That was the dao of the extreme immortal.

Metal corresponded to the lungs, and the lungs related to the qualities of purification and restraint. It was a perfect complement to metal. Lungs related primarily to air, and they regulated breathing. They were also associated with the emotion of grief, and they opened into the nose.[1]

All of a sudden, his seven emotions and six sensory pleasures stirred, becoming an attracting force. Then, the lungs in his fleshly body emanated the pure power of metal, which merged into one of the secret trove furnaces. It melted within him, and in the blink of an eye, it made the dao of metal! The secret trove raged.

Next, Xu Qing felt the emotion of rage within him. Intentionally unleashing the anger, he used it as a bridge, and used his divine will to speak again.

“Wood!”

Wood corresponded to the liver, and the liver related to the qualities of growth, development, order, and happiness. It was a perfect complement to wood. The liver related primarily to unclogging and deflating, as well as the regulation of energy fluctuations. It was also associated with the emotion of rage.[2]

His liver vibrated as a sensation of growth surged out and returned to the secret trove furnace. It became the dao of wood. After that....

“Water!”

Water corresponded to the kidneys, and the kidneys related to the qualities of nourishment, descension, freezing, and obstruction. It was a perfect complement to water. The kidneys related primarily to fluid metabolism and the storage of vital essence. It was also associated with the emotion of fear, and opened into the ears.[3]

All of a sudden, a deafening sound erupted within his secret trove as the dao of water formed. At the moment, three of the five elements had been completed. Eyes shining, Xu Qing gave voice to the fourth of the five.

“Fire!”

Xu Qing’s tongue touched the roof of his mouth as he uttered the word. His heart suddenly thumped with thunderous loudness.

Fire corresponded to the heart, and the heart related to the qualities of actuation, warmth, and ascension. It was a perfect complement to fire. The heart was like the monarch governing the other organs. It was also associated with the emotion of joy, and opened into the tongue.[4]

Inside his secret trove, the dao of fire formed.

“Earth!”

Earth corresponded to the spleen, and the spleen related to the qualities of transformation, sustainment, and acceptance. It was a perfect complement to earth. The spleen was the source of all transportation and transformation in a body, could move and alter grain and liquid throughout the body. It was also associated with the emotion of thoughtfulness, and opened into the mouth.[5]

The dao of earth was complete. As of this moment, all of the five elements were there. Correspondingly, the five apertures of Xu Qing’s nose, eyes, ears, tongue, and mouth opened in unison. They were like five immortals standing guard to prevent any outside evils from invading.

Those five immortals had names. Grief. Rage. Fear. Joy. Thoughtfulness. But right now, there were only five elements. And that could not be described as extreme!

Xu Qing took a deep breath.

And then, all of the essence crystals that the wish had caused to form from the fleshly body of the Grand Emperor’s fleshly body turned into the highest quality nutrients possible. Sweeping together, they entered Xu Qing’s body and began to nourish his five yin organs.

As a result, the power of the five organs began to climb higher. So did the five elements, which began to burn with great intensity in the secret troves. In an instant, the crystals on the outside declined in number. They poured into Xu Qing, becoming boundless nutrients that made the five elements stronger, and at the same time, more extreme. Finally, that powerful refinement within the secret troves caused... An explosion of heavenly lightning!

Metal became extreme metal. Wood became extreme wood. Water became extreme water. Fire became extreme fire. Earth became extreme earth! Five elements. Five extremes. The dao was complete!

An astonishing aura surged from within Xu Qing, causing winds to scream around him as the world trembled. Inside his sea of consciousness, six of the nine secret troves were burning.

Metal, wood, water, fire, earth. They are five extremes. And then, in the space formed from Fishing the Moon in the Well comes the sixth extreme. The dao of extreme space. As for the seventh extreme....

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered brightly as the gnomons on his sundial life lamps began to spin. In an instant, all nine gnomons unified, spinning in time within the seventh secret trove. They became time itself! This was the dao of extreme time!

That makes seven extremes!

His soul form rose in his sea of consciousness, standing above the secret troves. As of now, there were still two secret troves that were empty.

I’ll complete them sometime in the future. For now, it’s enough to have seven extremes burning. That will be enough to break through from Spirit Trove into Void Returning.

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. Not bothering to worry about the two empty secret troves, he focused his attention on the second dandelion seed from the immortal essence. It was the one that had an image of a true body being unified.

The true body part won’t be hard. But the unification part. Well, that person’s technique was ingenious. It required a fierce soul. And though I have access to fierce souls, none of them are inside this current body. That said, with my five yin organs as the five elements, my organs and my body are the same. So why would I need outside souls to attract the power?

Xu Qing looked up.

“In that case... unify!”

The moment the words left his mouth, all of his secret troves burned with the greatest intensity imaginable. Unprecedented rumbling sounds echoed out as they erupted like volcanoes.

They turned into trove gates. And the trove gates were all open!

What came out wasn’t pure fire. Rather, it was five elements power, time power, and space power. Seven extremes, unified!

They became a single beam of silver light that, backed by the secret troves, smashed out of Xu Qing’s sea of consciousness, stirring his fleshly body and causing his mind and soul to rumble.

Ultimately, the same scene played out that Xu Qing had witnessed in the first dandelion seed. It was a scene of world creation. It was the formation of a star ring.

It was... opening heaven and establishing earth! The returning heaven was opened, and the spirit void land was established! The illusory was turned into a void! It was as if mortal remains which had been buried in a grand necropolis were smoldering as they slowly turned into an immortal! The silver light made of seven extremes streaked through this Void Returning. Will surged, and they turned into immeasurable magical and natural laws as they swept through all of the levels of Void Returning.

It all happened very naturally. It was like the idiom: where water flows, a canal is formed. When walking the correct path, it seemed only logical that things would play out like this.

Finally... Xu Qing decisively tapped into the remaining essence crystals to start his final breakthrough. Heaven had been opened within him. The earth had been established.

The mortal remains in the necropolis were smoldering as they turned into an immortal. That meant that next... he needed to blast apart the earth within him, and shatter the heaven, all to break through the shackles of life. All smoldering aspects of an immortal needed to be awakened and turned into major worlds!

The necropolis erupted. The void soil surged. And they turned into a blast of force that caused the heaven within him to tremble.

Heaven... collapsed! Rumbling sounds filled him as the area that corresponded to lungs filled with a vortex that contained a majestic major world.

He was finally reaching Smoldering God! Put most precisely, the level Xu Qing was actually entering was called Smoldering Immortal!

As for this first major world, it was an extreme world. It was the most extreme form of metal. In fact, it could be called an extreme metal world!

After that first major world appeared, Xu Qing’s breakthrough continued. A world centered around an extreme world appeared in the location of his liver. It was an extreme wood world!

Things weren’t over yet. Next came the extreme water world, extreme fire world, and extreme earth world....

Five worlds had been established in the locations of his five yin organs!

As for the sixth world, the extreme space world, it was on his left shoulder! The seventh world, the extreme time world, rested on his right shoulder!

Seven worlds all rumbled loudly as a powerful aura erupted from them, filling Xu Qing’s body and stirring his will.

Atop the transparent sea, Xu Qing’s eyes snapped open! Immortal energy surged within him, and combined with his astoundingly good looks, it really was a perfect representation of the word ‘immortal.’ As he looked around, he felt like an entire lifetime had just passed.

He sensed his body. He sensed his cultivation base. And though he felt dazed for a moment, an instant later, his eyes gleamed with a desire to do battle.

He had just experienced a truly dangerous situation. He had lost his god clone, but as often happens, a great danger will often bring with it a destined opportunity. And if you grasp it, you can fly to the highest heights.

He had grasped the opportunity. He has stepped past the limitations of his god body and begun to walk his own path. He had taken the seven extremes and pushed them to an unheard-of peak level.

There were still some essence crystals around him, so he waved his hand and sent them flying toward the countless worms that surrounded the bone cauldron.

“Eldest Brother,” Xu Qing said calmly.

The innumerable worms seemed to all start laughing as they brashly absorbed all of the crystals.

Meanwhile, it seemed that the fight between the empress and the others was about to conclude.

At the same time, inside the bone cauldron, Netherflame could sense that things were happening outside. The cauldron started rumbling, and then a monstrous voice rang out from within.

“Manywonders smolderlife grotto-heaven! Activate!”

Land-shaking, mountain-rocking force shook all of the worlds in the secluded meditation facilities. At the same time, something even more dramatic was happening at the dao altar in the lands of the eastern Devilbirds. As countless Devilbird cultivators looked on, the dao altar filled with more and more cracks, before ultimately crumbling into ash.

Then a massive withered tree branch shot up from the rubble. As everyone looked on in shock, a withered fruit appeared at the end of the huge branch. It pulsed with a majestic sense of an accumulated dao. Inside of the fruit were blurry images of Xu Qing and everyone else. That fruit was the grotto-heaven where Netherflame had been waiting in seclusion!

1. In traditional Chinese medicine, lungs and metal are indeed connected. For more info, you can check out the wikipedia pages for the Five Elements and the Lungs in TCM. Subsequent organs have their own TCM reference link, but all of them are mentioned in the Five Elements article as well. ☜

2. TCM liver reference. ☜

3. TCM kidneys reference. ☜

4. TCM heart reference. ☜

5. TCM spleen reference. ☜

Deathblade's Thoughts

This was one of those chapters that was excruciating to translate. I think I spent three times as much time on it as an average chapter.

Many thanks to Whiskas, wuyxi, Lassey, SweGhostie, Tangedenor, spols, AzureZeph, Onideus, and Nukemega for the reviews. Wow, a lot of reviews came in during the past week!

In the spot where the eastern Devilbirds’ dao altar had once stood, there was now pure pandemonium. To countless Devilbird cultivators, that dao altar was something of immense significance. And now it had collapsed as a huge branch snaked up, with a fruit on its end. All onlookers were shaken to the core.

That was especially true when... Grand Emperor Devilbird, who had been seated atop the dao altar, suddenly blurred away into nothing. As it turned out, he had been nothing but an illusory projection. And because of its Grand Emperor personhood, no one in the crowd had picked up on any clues otherwise. It was only when the dao altar collapsed and the aura of a dao fruit erupted into the open that people could see the truth.

An illusory tempest spun into being, and everyone in the area felt a sensation of extreme uneasiness, something instinctive that came from within their life force itself. One reason for the uneasiness was the dramatic turn of events. The other reason... was the sound of tolling bells that filled the Devilbird holy land.

It was an ancient sound that shook heaven and earth. They were bells of war. The collapse of the dao altar was apparently some sort of signal. At that moment, the humans and the Firemoon Darkheavens rose up from the Revered Ancient mainland and unleashed the full fury of war onto the two holy lands that floated above them.

In an instant, heaven and earth devolved into great chaos. As chaos reigned outside, disorder was also raging inside of the dao fruit.

As Netherflame howled from within the bone cauldron, a deafening rumbling sound echoed out, resulting in intense vibrations. Erniu, incarnated in countless worms, was hit by the force coming from the cauldron. One by one, the worms started exploding.

Inside the cauldron, Netherflame seemed to react to the might of the dao fruit, and once again reached a state of balance. Power began to rise explosively within him. The rumbling got so intense that it seemed like the lid of the cauldron was about to be blasted open. The cauldron lid vibrated, then cracks started to appear in it. Golden light shone out from within the cracks. Grand Emperor Netherflame was just about to break free.

At that critical moment, the world fragment that contained the empress surged with force.

Simultaneously, the remaining blue worms outside the cauldron madly absorbed the rest of the crystals Xu Qing had sent over. Then, they shouted, “I’m not afraid of you, bitch! Third life!”

The transparent sea below seethed. The boundless water was covered with huge waves as the entire sea turned into a whirlpool. An ancient aura then began to rise up from within the whirlpool.

Before, his body had exploded and dropped down into the water. But the reality was that Erniu had just been looking for pieces of his third-life body there. The downsides had been that he had very limited time, and also wasn’t actually strong enough at the moment. Because of that, he couldn’t quickly put all the pieces together.

But then Xu Qing gave him the last of the essence crystals.... Xu Qing was able to use that essence to craft an immortal body. But it was something equally precious to Erniu. It could nourish him and help him to release more of his sealing marks, and it enabled him to rapidly absorb memories from his third life. As he absorbed the essence, he gained the power to make the initial call to his third life.

An instant later, frigid flames erupted from the whirlpool of the transparent sea. Then, a huge black hand suddenly reached out from the whirlpool. It was not true and real. Rather, it was illusory. But it emanated an aura that was extremely ancient, and at the same time, pulsed with unparalleled ferocity.

It looked extremely gruish. It resembled a hand, except that the middle finger had a head on it. The ring and index fingers were bent like arms, while the pinky and thumb were like legs. In the palm was a gaping, blood-red mouth. What was more, the hand was actually covered with innumerable black hairs. It looked incredibly fierce, even horrendous.

This was a projection of Erniu’s third life. It was the very same megavillain that Grand Emperor Immortal Skill had refined. In response to Erniu’s summons, it rose up into the sky. In the blink of an eye, it reached the bone cauldron and made contact with it.

“Be refined!” Erniu howled.

The cauldron trembled, then went still. Then, before Erniu even had a chance to start preening, an intense force burst out from the interior of the cauldron. Deafening rumbling rocked the surroundings.

Erniu’s third-life projection blurred as if it might collapse. After all, this wasn’t truly his third life, but just a projection of it. Using it to suppress the power of the terrifying Netherflame wasn’t going to be easy.

Just when it looked like Erniu’s third-life projection was going to collapse.... Xu Qing finished fusing with all seven of his major worlds. Without any hesitation, he burst into motion. He appeared right next to Erniu’s third-life projection, his eyes gleaming. Extending his right hand, he pushed down onto the trembling bone cauldron.

Then he spoke in a booming voice. “Extreme metal. Extreme wood. Extreme water. Extreme fire. Extreme earth!”

Five of the seven worlds hovering behind him erupted, and it looked as if five crystal fragments suddenly let loose the power of the five elements, which crushed down onto the cauldron. Next, the remaining two worlds were unleashed. Extreme space. Extreme time!

A piercing cry echoed out from inside the cauldron. But then, Xu Qing and Erniu both reacted with surprise as a supremely terrifying force erupted from within the cauldron. It was a force that seemed capable of smashing through anything and everything. It was as if all obstacles were meaningless compared to it.

The lid of the cauldron blasted open, and Xu Qing and Erniu were sent tumbling backward. Then, Netherflame floated up inside as he prepared to emerge. No matter how strong the two of them were, it was insignificant compared to Netherflame.

Voice hoarse, he said, “All of you—”

But right then, the world fragment containing the empress exploded. It pulsed with the explosive aura of a god. It turned into a massive shockwave that swept through the world. At the same time, the empress stepped out, reaching the cauldron in an instant and shoving it down with great force.

Ripples and distortions spread. Peak Altar God power was released without any restraint.

Xu Qing and Erniu didn’t hesitate to shoot backward to get away from the field of battle. They knew that the forces which were about to be unleashed surpassed them by far.

The empress’ action caused Netherflame’s eyes to become bloodshot as he waved his hand in response, dispelling the attack power.

An instant later, a shocking, ancient planet appeared behind the empress. The planet’s mere presence caused wild winds to scream, and filled the area with a sky-obfuscating, land-enshrouding will.

Five figures were seated cross-legged on the surface of the planet. Those five figures were gods, as well as past emperors of humankind.

Eastglory. Sageheaven. Mirrorcloud. Dao Life. Dark War.

Thēy unleashed the full force of thēir god power into the ancient planet beneath.

Meanwhile, the shattered world fragment in the distance was no longer blurry. It was now possible to see how damaged it had become during the fighting. Also visible was the beheaded corpse of Netherflame’s clone.

Also present was Grand Emperor Devilbird, coughing up blood and badly injured. Devilbird looked at the empress, then at the surrounding world. His face was as pale as death.

This grotto-heaven is actually made from a manywonders smolderlife dao fruit! Manywonders smolderlife dao fruits are able to resurrect anything under the level of a True God. One such dao fruit can be used three times. However, it can only be used once in a lifetime by any given person.

Considering how withered the fruit looks, Netherflame must have already used it. It looks like after being used another time, it will disappear forever. So that’s how Netherflame managed to come back to life! And that’s also what the empress is here for!

Blood sprayed out of Devilbird’s mouth as he staggered backward. Meanwhile, the empress hovered above the bone cauldron, looking down at Netherflame. Netherflame’s body was currently fifty percent violet, thirty percent gold, and twenty percent green.

Shē couldn’t tell where the violet was coming from. But the gold was from a drop of water, and the green... came from a dao fruit. The empress’ gaze hardened. Shē had been holding back this entire time. Shē had not gone all out.

One reason was that hēr opponent had a spectacularly powerful cultivation base. The other reason was that shē knew shē would only have one chance to achieve hēr true objective here. And shē would not accept failure.

Her original plan had not accounted for the variables presented by Xu Qing and Erniu. Originally, Netherflame was supposed to try to possess Devilbird, whereupon shē would join forces with Devilbird to achieve hēr objective. Although Netherflame was strong, shē knew shē could handle him.

But things didn’t go according to plan. Xu Qing and Erniu did present new variables, and then circumstances shifted. Netherflame changed his mind, and instead of trying to possess Devilbird, had decided to cooperate with him. And he had decided to try to possess Xu Qing.

Therefore, the empress had just waited and watched for the opportunity to come. The empress didn’t believe the new variables to be negatives. Whether it was Erniu’s third life or Xu Qing’s strange fleshly body, they actually just made hēr more confident that hēr plan would succeed. That was why shē had just waited patiently.

It was only when Netherflame broke free and revealed the power of the manywonders smolderlife dao fruit... that the opportunity the empress had been waiting for finally arrived.

Shē actually wanted Netherflame to take this action. To reveal the dao fruit. Thus, the empress’ action just now was actually hēr unhesitatingly revealing the contingency measures she’d had in place the entire time.

Hēr contingency plan was humankind’s Planet Ancient Emperor. In terms of personhood, it was the most precious treasure humankind possessed. And with the blessing of the five human gods, the precious treasure was unleashing astonishing power. Rumbling sounds echoed out as Planet Ancient Emperor exerted crushing force.

Netherflame’s howl echoed back and forth. He wanted to break free, but before he could, the empress bit down on the tip of hēr tongue and spat out some god blood. Shē also unhesitatingly unleashed all the power of hēr god altar to prevent Netherflame from breaking free.

Next, a vortex appeared within Planet Ancient Emperor. The power of the planet, as well as the power of the five human emperors, along with the might of the empress’ god altar, caused Netherflame to be devoured by the planet!

Netherflame was sealed.

Having accomplished that, a gleam of human nature appeared in the empress’s eyes.

Shē had become she. For this entire time, hēr goal had not been to go all out to kill Netherflame. Nor had hēr goal been Netherflame’s soul. Shē had been waiting for hēr opponent to take out the dao fruit. And then, by means of Planet Ancient Emperor, shē would isolate him from the outside world. And that, in turn, would cut away his connection to the manywonders smolderlife dao fruit. At least temporarily, the dao fruit would have no karmic connections to anything.

In that way, shē would finally have the chance to reach her true goal.

“Grand Emperor...” she murmured. She waved her hand, and a majestic statue flew out from inside her body. It grew larger and larger above the surface of the sea. The sea water seethed. It was a statue of Grand Emperor Swordsage!

Xu Qing looked at it, his heart pounding with both anxiety and excitement. He could now guess what the empress was trying to do.

Ever since the empress reached godly ascension, hēr eyes had been calm and placid. Now, those eyes looked at the statue with longing like that of a child to a parent.

“Come back...” she said softly. She was attempting to resurrect Grand Emperor Swordsage!

She had started out as a mortal, without even the ability to practice cultivation. However, it was her strengths and talents that allowed humankind to finally complete their Dawning Suns project, which gave them the precious treasure they needed to stand tall as a species. That alone made her an outstanding person.

But she was relatively unknown among humankind. Few people were aware of her existence, and all of the glory for the Dawning Suns went to her husband.

After becoming the empress, she had two sons. She lived for her husband, sharing his worries and supporting him through his woes. She didn’t think twice about living solely for her husband and sons. But in the end, she was ripped away from her sons and brutally killed by her own husband. Her husband had mercilessly done whatever he could to try to reach godly ascension.

She didn’t realize where she had gone wrong. Nor did she understand why things ended up that way for her. And the grief and helplessness she felt about her life up to that point became a part of her soul.

In the past, she had knelt and prayed to the holy lands. The holy lands had never answered. She had prostrated to the nobility to beg for help. The nobility had ignored her.

She had wept. She had gnashed her teeth. She wallowed in sorrow. She had remained silent.

Eventually, on the evening when she reached the end of her life in the imperial palace, she had collapsed in front of the statue of Grand Emperor Swordsage, and there she shed her last tear. The tear rolled down her cheek and landed on the ground. She heard the sound of it splashing. And then she heard a sigh that echoed with fate.

“Humankind shouldn’t be like this.... Child, humanity has let you down....”

Then she saw someone walking toward her. It was someone she would never be able to forget.

Behind her, the source of her sorrow was cut down by a sword. It was a sword that could sever fate, and a sword that could change everything.

“The Grand Emperor,” she murmured. “Like a father.”

At the darkest moment in her life, Grand Emperor Swordsage saved her. In the most sorrowful time in her life, Grand Emperor Swordsage gave her hope. When she seemed most confused about the meaning of life, it was Grand Emperor Swordsage who gave her a cultivation base. He gave humankind to her.

That was when she became Dark War. She led humankind to prominence. And then, with the Grand Emperor backing her up, she removed her mask and became a god, and the only empress to ever reign over humankind.

It was not my desire to safeguard humankind. That was your wish, Grand Emperor. But it became my desire.

As the empress looked at the statue, the longing in her heart grew stronger. And along with it came determination. She wanted to resurrect the Grand Emperor who had been like a father to her!

It was you, sir, who brought me out of despair. Today, I will help you return from death.

The empress’ eyes shone with bright light. As Devilbird trembled, as Planet Ancient Emperor rumbled, as Erniu looked on incredulously, and as Xu Qing watched excitedly.... She took a step forward and hovered in midair.
