“I am the empress of humankind! I have gathered the destiny of all humans in Revered Ancient. And today....”

The empress’ gaze seemed to pass out of the world and into Revered Ancient to look at all humankind.

“I hereby call to all humans to remember Grand Emperor Swordsage, and turn those memories into his human spiritual soul!”

The words cracked like thunder, spreading to all human lands to enter the minds of all humans.

That included the Imperial Region and everything around it. All humans felt their memories stirring wildly as thoughts of Grand Emperor Swordsage rose within them. As long as people remembered him, it was possible that he could return.

And who could possibly forget about Grand Emperor Swordsage...? After Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity left, he chose to stay behind to safeguard humankind. He was the one who spared humanity from being devoured by nonhumans. He was the one who had protected humankind countless times in battle. His true form eventually fell in battle, but his clone remained behind. And even it had beheaded gods to keep humanity in peace.

Stories of his countless deadly battles spread far and wide. Even in his last days, he had used the power of his sword to strike fear into the hearts of nonhumans. There was no doubt about it. Without him, humankind would have been destroyed.

His life had been soaked in blood, but at the same time, he was the history of humankind after the departure of Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity.

Who could forget this Grand Emperor? And thus, memories of him became shimmering motes of light that rose from within all humans. The motes flew up to the Devilbird holy land and began to gather at the dao fruit. Motes of light even emerged from Xu Qing’s mind as he remembered Grand Emperor Swordsage. And those countless motes of light began to form into the human spiritual soul of Grand Emperor Swordsage, which entered the statue.

“The Grand Emperor spent his life protecting our species and our lands,” the empress said. “And today, I call on the spirits in all human lands to become the earthly spiritual soul of the Grand Emperor!”

The empress’s voice rang with a note of command, causing human lands throughout Revered Ancient to react. Mountains, rivers, soil, and buildings all began to tremble.

Heaven had spirits. Naturally speaking, so did earth. The spirits responded to the call, becoming motes of light that shot up in marvelous fashion from Revered Ancient. As countless cultivators in the Devilbird holy land looked on in shock, and as innumerable human cultivators trembled excitedly, they entered the dao fruit and the statue of the Grand Emperor.

“The spiritual soul is made of three parts. Heavenly. Earthly. Human. I hereby summon the destiny aura of humankind that has struggled defiantly from the time of Eastglory onward. And it will be the heavenly spiritual soul of the Grand Emperor!”

Heaven and earth in human lands throughout Revered Ancient trembled as the destiny aura of humankind rose up into the clouds. Ignoring any attempts of Devilbird cultivators to stop it, it bypassed all obstacles in decisive and domineering fashion....

And it entered the dao fruit and the statue of Grand Emperor Swordsage. The statue trembled.

As of now, the memories of the species had formed the human spiritual soul. The lands and rivers and mountains had formed the earthly spiritual soul. And the boundless destiny aura had formed the heavenly spiritual soul. Three spiritual souls had combined. This act of resurrection was meaningful to the empress, but it was also meaningful to humankind as a whole!

Beyond that, it was also meaningful to the human emperors!

“There are three spiritual souls. There are seven physical souls!”

The empress turned to look at Planet Ancient Emperor, and the five past emperors seated cross-legged there. The moment she did so, the five emperors opened their eyes and looked back at her.

“Ordinarily, it would be difficult to find a physical soul for the Grand Emperor. He lived his life for humankind. Therefore, since the memories, land, and destiny aura of humankind formed the three spiritual souls, then the successive emperors will make the physical souls! The first physical soul is the heavenly hub. Let my past become the first physical soul!”

The empress lifted her right hand and viciously chopped it down on herself. That action resulted in her body becoming somewhat illusory. She was severing her past to make the first physical soul, which then entered the statue of the Grand Emperor.

“The second physical soul provides rationality and intelligence. Emperor Mirrorcloud!”

On Planet Ancient Emperor, Emperor Mirrorcloud flew up, becoming a mysterious glow that entered the statue.

“The third physical soul acts as energy. Emperor Dao Life!”

Dao Life rose, took a step forward, and entered the statue.

“The fourth physical gives power. Emperor Eastglory!”

Eastglory shot up into the sky and turned into a physical soul.

“The fifth physical soul is the backbone. Let it be formed by my future!”

Looking more decisive than ever, the empress severed her future to form the backbone of the Grand Emperor’s physical souls.

“The sixth physical soul makes the quintessence. Emperor Sageheaven!”

Sageheaven closed his eyes and turned into a white beam of light that made the Grand Emperor’s physical soul origin.

“The seventh physical soul stands for heroism. Emperor Dark War!”

Dark War looked up, his eyes glimmering with shame and guilt. He stood. He was willing to become the seventh physical soul.

As of this moment, the three spiritual souls had united, and the seven physical souls were complete. The Grand Emperor’s statue trembled, the surrounding world shook, and the Devilbird holy land quaked.

Some distance away, Grand Emperor Devilbird could guess what was coming next. His expression flickered, revealing sorrow. But in the end, he chose to retreat. He would leave the world of the dao fruit. Once outside, he sighed deeply. He knew that he was powerless to turn things around, and thus, his best option was to get away as quickly as possible and take as many of his direct bloodline as possible away from the holy land.

As he left, the empress within the world of the dao fruit turned a cold expression to the outside. Taking in the entire Devilbird holy land, she lifted her right hand.

“I will not allow myself to fail. This dao fruit is already withered, therefore... I hereby sacrifice all living beings in the Devilbird holy land! Let them become nutrients for the manywonders smolderlife dao fruit!”

The empress’ words echoed from within the world of the dao fruit to the entirety of the Devilbird holy land. They spread out, reaching even the tenth Imperial Sovereign mountain that the empress had once occupied.

And that caused some concealment magics she had left behind on the mountain to vanish. At that point, it turned into a god mountain, and a god magic that the empress had left in the works there was suddenly activated!

It was a god magic that could strip away the concept of night and replace it with light. It was as if a sun were dawning over the Devilbird holy land. Wherever the light passed, the air rippled and distorted. Howls of anguish echoed out. Everything was being turned into a god domain.

With Grand Emperor Devilbird on the run, there was nothing the inhabitants of the Devilbird holy land could do to stop the impending catastrophe. In the face of an Altar God, anyone under the Grand Emperor level was like an ant.

The light shining in the Devilbird holy land made it almost like a new star that caught the attention of everyone in Revered Ancient.

The empress was not holding back any of her peak Altar God power. It poured into the dao fruit, filling its veins, filling its natural cycles, and creating a force of attraction that exploded out to cover the Devilbird holy land.

All life force would be sucked in. All souls. All flesh and blood.

Numerous Devilbird cultivators that Grand Emperor Devilbird had left behind were hit by the light and the force of attraction. They were instantly killed in body and soul, transformed into a bloody paste that was sucked into the dao fruit. As more flesh and blood converged, and as catastrophe filled the Devilbird holy land, the previously withered dao fruit began to become plump and glistening once again.

This made it clearer than ever that the empress had veins of steel! Without even the slightest hesitation, she waved her finger to connect the dao fruit to the Grand Emperor.

Then she spoke in a low voice.

“Manywonders smolderlife!”

The dao fruit, which has absorbed countless bits of flesh and blood, shivered. Then magical symbols became visible on its surface, and they began spinning. The gate of reincarnation was being opened. It was as if a path of life were being forged.

Wild colors flashed in heaven and earth. The void rumbled loudly.

Then, the dao fruit once again withered visibly as all of the nutrients inside were swept into the statue of the Grand Emperor.

The statue now had three spiritual souls and seven physical souls. It had life force brewing in it. And when the nutrients reached a certain level, it would undergo a mysterious transformation. The clay that made the statue was now glittering brightly as if it was about to turn into flesh and blood. A sense of reanimation erupted within it, and Grand Emperor Swordsage’s familiar aura... became manifest! The aura grew stronger and stronger!

It burst out of the world of the dao fruit, piercing into the Devilbird holy land, and shaking the entire Revered Ancient mainland. It attracted the attention of countless eyes.

The empress looked very excited, as did Xu Qing.

However... even as everyone looked on, the statue trembled, and that seemingly indomitable aura suddenly destabilized and started collapsing.

“NO!!” screamed the empress, her eyes turning red.

Many times in life, it can be difficult to give up on something just because it’s hard. That refusal to give up could even be called obsession. That was especially true of matters of life or death. That of others. That of oneself. Obsession with life or death. The inability to let it go. In such instances, there is always hope.

However... there are many times in which there is no hope. Only despair. Sadly, in many instances, despair becomes the main theme. The world is a cold place. Heaven and earth are indifferent.

For example, just as the flame of his life force flickered within the statue of Grand Emperor Swordsage, the statue started crumbling. It was like a lamp that had run out of oil. There just wasn’t a way to light it. It didn’t matter that the Devilbird holy land had been sacrificed. It didn’t matter that the manywonders smolderlife dao fruit had been awoken. Those things changed nothing.

And yet, the empress’ pure obsession could be heard in the words echoing in heaven and earth, turning into a reverberation of defiance like that cry of a thousand mountains. The empress was a god. But gods... were clearly not omnipotent. She even bit her tongue, causing god blood to spray out and soak her body. God blood became life force. An incantation gesture ignited it, and it poured into the statue of the Grand Emperor.

Xu Qing didn’t hesitate for an instant to do the same. He sent out his own life force, contained in his blood. He used his strength, his dao, and everything about himself to help the Grand Emperor.

Even Erniu sighed and lent his strength as well.

Unfortunately... none of that made much of a difference in the end. It was as if there was a massive ravine separating life and death.

The statue’s aura continued to collapse. As of this moment, there was no way to stop the resurrection ceremony from failing. Pain and bitterness filled the world.

How can this be happening...

The empress, however, was not ready to give up. It didn’t matter that all signs pointed to impending failure. She still unleashed the full power of her god altar. She did everything she possibly could to turn things around. At almost the exact same instant that she was about to harm herself by tapping too deeply into her own strength, an ancient voice echoed within the world of the dao fruit.

“Silly child.”

The familiar voice caused a tremor to pass through Xu Qing. Countless memories flashed through his mind. At the same time, the empress struggled to control her breathing. That voice was the source of her human nature. Xu Qing and the Empress looked at the statue simultaneously.

As the statue’s energy crumbled, the three spiritual souls and seven physical souls ceased moving for a moment. Then their momentum surged again.

This time, there was no obstacle. They returned to their peak, and Swordsage’s aura erupted into the world, an aura that belonged to a peak Grand Emperor.

Wild colors flashed in heaven and earth. Winds screamed. The world trembled. The holy land shook. The full Revered Ancient mainland was affected.

Even to the naked eye it was possible to see the statue transforming into flesh and blood, until a figure was visible. He opened his eyes.

Grand Emperor Swordsage. He stood on the surface of the transparent sea looking very, very old. An aura of death surrounded him, but he stood tall and straight. His gaze was soft as he looked at the world around him. Then he looked out of the Devilbird holy land and toward... humankind.

He saw all of the places where humans lived. He saw the people standing there. He gazed at the mountains and rivers, at the destiny aura. At everything. Everything that had happened in Revered Ancient since he perished was now pouring into his mind by means of the heavenly daos and all the living beings. He came to know that the holy lands had arrived after his death. He came to know that war had broken out. He came to know it all. Something fierce arose within him as he came to understand everything. It swirled out of him, affecting all heaven and earth.

And yet... off in the distance, Xu Qing and Empress Summer Departure simply couldn’t control the grief in their hearts as they looked at the Grand Emperor. That was because... the Grand Emperor was inundated with an intense aura of death.

Tears flowed down the empress’ face. She knew... that in the end, she was still going to fail. The Grand Emperor had not been fully resurrected. The power of the manywonders smolderlife dao fruit, and the strength of the three spiritual souls and seven physical souls, was only enough to bring him back to life temporarily.

Xu Qing felt like someone was squeezing down on his heart. Indescribable emotions filled him, including bitterness and emptiness.

“Oh, you two...” the Grand Emperor said with a sigh as he looked away from the outside world and focused tenderly on Xu Qing and the empress. “My Summer.” [1]

The empress looked up. At that moment, she wasn’t a god. She wasn’t an empress. She was the fragile young woman of years past that had just been rescued by the Grand Emperor. The tears flowing down her face made it difficult to see the fatherly figure in front of her.

“You’ve done very well,” the Grand Emperor said hoarsely. “You’ve done more than enough.” He strode over to the empress and tousled her hair, his eyes full of warmth, as if she were his own daughter. “It’s just that... your omniscience can’t tell you everything about me.

“The history books only talk about how my true form perished and my clone toiled to safeguard humankind. The truth about why it all happened was erased. By me.

“The reality is that back when I waged war against the god species from the central part of Revered Ancient, I did succeed in preventing humankind from being enslaved. But the price to pay was immense. It wasn’t just my true form that perished. My clone... also died in the fighting.

“After I perished, an old friend of mine used the manywonders smolderlife to resurrect me after the battle was over. That act of resurrection both failed and succeeded. It failed because the dao fruit only gives a chance at a resurrection. It can’t guarantee it. And thus, my true form did not return.

“You can say it succeeded, though, because my perished clone was resurrected. The point is that my clone already used the manywonders smolderlife dao fruit to come back to life. I can’t use it a second time. The failure of this resurrection attempt is no fault of yours, my Summer.”

The Grand Emperor spoke slowly and softly as he attempted to soothe Summer Departure’s emotions. He didn’t want the child whose life he had saved to end up regretting a failure for the rest of her days. He needed her to understand that the failure wasn’t due to her or her lack of effort.

The empress bit her lip as she listened to the explanation.

Finally, the Grand Emperor sighed and tousled her hair again. Then he looked at Xu Qing, whose face was tinged with bitterness.

“Xu Qing, you haven’t disappointed me.”

Xu Qing bowed his head. Heart filled with grief, he clasped hands and bowed deeply.

The Grand Emperor smiled as he looked at the empress and Xu Qing. They were his successors. One had inherited his cultivation base, while the other had inherited The Emperor’s Sword. He was very pleased with both of them, and didn’t feel an ounce of regret in picking them.

And yet... he still had some concerns about humankind. He was concerned about the people he had spent his life protecting.

“I understand everything now. The dao fruit can’t fully resurrect me. But it has brought me back temporarily. And the body I’ve returned in is not limited by the shackles of the star ring. I’ve returned to my peak. And that will do very nicely.”

The Grand Emperor smiled. It had been a very, very long time since he had felt this free. In fact, it was a sensation that he didn’t remember experiencing since the time his true form had been alive. In his waning years, he had always been struggling with lingering injuries, and had spent most of his time in slumber.

And even when he did wake up to do something, he felt exhaustion deep in his soul. Because of that he could never wield his sword to his heart’s content. He always had to be careful and maintain absolute control, always holding back his final sword move. It had all been extremely exhausting. Even in his final battle when he had longed to hold nothing back, he had been unable to.

The responsibility of safeguarding humankind was a weight like that of a mountain, and he had borne it for a lifetime. He had always wanted to let everything go and fight like he had when he was young.

“I suppose I don’t have much time left....”

The Grand Emperor grinned and reached his right hand toward Planet Ancient Emperor up above. He waved his finger, and the planet started rumbling and shaking. Then it began to spin, causing the sealed bone cauldron to appear.

The lid of the cauldron opened. A distorted figure shot out. It was none other than Netherflame.

His expression was ferocious as he opened his mouth. But then his face fell as he spotted Grand Emperor Swordsage. His pupils constricted, and all the hair on his body stood on end. Given the current state of his battle prowess, he could sense that Grand Emperor Swordsage was an extremely dangerous threat to him.

This clearly isn’t a Summer Immortal. But the sense I’m getting... is that this person is incredibly terrifying!

Scalp tingling, Netherflame shot backward to flee. He was too slow.

The Grand Emperor’s gaze fell upon him. A screaming sound filled the world as the most spectacular stream of sword energy imaginable erupted from within Netherflame’s fleshly body. Netherflame couldn’t stop it. Sword energy towered into the sky, shattering the clouds.

It was... The Emperor’s Sword!

The sword glittered with might that stunned Netherflame to the core. It did not slice through him. It hovered above the top of his head before lowering to touch him.

Netherflame shivered from head to toe. A terrifying power surged out of the sword like a wave. It smashed into his fleshly body with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force, slamming right into his soul.

This is as strong as a Summer Immortal!

That was the last thing Netherflame thought before his soul shattered. His soul did not form anew. Swordsage grabbed it, and Netherflame’s senses turned dark. The Grand Emperor waved a hand to send the soul flying toward the empress.

“It’s a good soul. It absorbed a lot of the karma from Xu Qing’s fleshly body. You can sacrifice it in the future.” The Grand Emperor smiled as he flicked his sleeve, sending the fleshly body to Xu Qing. “Xu Qing, your current body has immortal troves. This body has god troves. Going forward, you can advance on both the path of gods and the path of immortals. Though I never walked that path myself, from what I can tell, it is infinite.

“But that’s a good thing. There are two different paths, one of the extreme immortal, the other of the extreme god. In the case of the latter, as long as you successfully gain enlightenment of godly authority, then you can ignite godfire and become a god. And most likely, a very powerful god.”

Xu Qing took hold of his god body. He looked at the Grand Emperor, his heart full of sorrow. He owed too much to the Grand Emperor.

The Grand Emperor smiled. “Don’t look like that, you two. I’m very happy. My Summer. Xu Qing. Are the two of you willing to help an old man wield his sword one last time?”

The empress took a deep breath and then forced a nod. Xu Qing steeled his gaze and bowed.

“We’re willing, Senior!”

Laughing heartily, the Grand Emperor waved his hand. The sky opened and the Devilbird holy land trembled.

And then he took his two successors away with him. He left the Devilbird holy land, piercing through the air with astonishing speed as he went into the direction of the three holy lands hovering above the Firemoon Darkheaven people.

“I have a sword that can sever heaven and break open the earth!”

The Grand Emperor’s proud words echoed in Revered Ancient. In different parts of the Revered Ancient mainland, various ancient gods opened their eyes from slumber and looked at the figure in the sky that was familiar to all of thēm. That included Yu Liuchen. For a brief moment, all of thēm felt like thēy were tens of thousands of years in the past, when a young man with a sword in his hand had traveled the world fighting the gods.

“Swordsage....”

1. Swordsage actually takes one of the characters of her name and adds ‘er’ to it, which creates a sort of cute, tender, and intimate form of address. But since her imperial name is translated, adding the ‘er’ doesn’t really work. Summer’er or Departure’er would be ridiculous. So I’m going to have him address her as ‘my Summer’ in order to convey that intimacy that the Chinese has. I know it’s not perfect, but I feel that leaving out that little touch would be a shame. ☜

Few people can easily predict how long they will live. That’s especially true when life is brutal. One slipup or one deadly fight can end everything. Even powerful gods could perish. Even Grand Emperor Swordsage had eventually reached the end of the line.

However... the length of one’s life wasn’t the most important factor in determining how amazing that life was. As was said, the world is a tavern for living beings, and the timescape is an old guest.[1]

The most important thing was to examine what one had experienced in life. Each person had their own path to walk. It was the only freedom that all living beings controlled.

Grand Emperor Swordsage had safeguarded humankind for ages and ages. Though he couldn’t change how things would end for him, his life experience was something that all humans would remember.

That was glory. That was greatness.

Today, as the flame of his life force flickered one last time, he let go of everything. It was like a rebirth in which he felt completely unrestrained and unfettered. The spark of life force within him glittered even more brightly. It was now possible to catch a glimpse of how high-spirited and full of mettle he had been years ago.

“My Summer. Xu Qing. I don’t want your futures to be like this.... But given that I’ve lived this way, I want to share with you something that I’ve learned.” As Grand Emperor Swordsage led the way through the Revered Ancient mainland with Xu Qing and the empress in tow, he softly said, “No remorse. No guilt. No regrets.

“Work as hard as you possibly can in life. If you do, then no matter how things end, you will have no remorse about your obsessions.

“Listen to your heart. If you do, then no matter how you advance on your path, you will have light in your life. And that means you’ll have no guilt.

“If you succeed in those two things, then regardless of the people you encounter or the decisions you make, you’ll have no regrets. If you can live by those six words, then your life will be meaningful. You will not have lived in vain.”

As Grand Emperor Swordsage’s words echoed out into heaven and earth, the Empress and Xu Qing heard them and were deeply affected. freewebnovel.com

The Grand Emperor really had lived by those six words. He had safeguarded humankind for years on end. He had worked hard. And he had no regrets, no matter what happened. He had listened to his heart, and the light within him had never been tarnished. It spilled onto the path forward, becoming radiance free of any guilt. That was how had chosen to live, and he was now explaining it to Xu Qing and the empress. He had no regrets.

He laughed, and the sound echoed through heaven and earth, even reaching the three holy lands that were fighting the countless members of the Firemoon Darkheaven people and their three gods.

A total of sixteen celestial-level holy lands had come to Revered Ancient. And they had split up into four groups of four, which aligned with the four cardinal directions.

As for the east of Revered Ancient, one of the four holy lands had gone to deal with humankind, while the other three... went to the Firemoon Darkheavens. At the moment, those three holy lands were trembling.

The three gods of the Firemoons were visibly moved. Without any hesitation, they led their people into retreat, opening a path that led directly to the three holy lands.

The Grand Emperors of the three holy lands were shaking inside, and their expressions were unprecedentedly grave. All of them looked out and saw the same thing.... They saw Empress Summer Departure. They saw Xu Qing. And they saw the person in front of those two. He held a long sword and wore a voluminous robe, and despite being old, he stood tall and straight. The old man pulsed with a strong aura of death, but his soul emanated radiance that the death aura couldn’t cover up. In fact, it illuminated the entire sky over Revered Ancient.

Summer Immortal!!

That was what all of the Grand Emperors in the three holy lands were thinking. It caused their hearts to pound and their faces to turn ashen.

They weren’t the only ones who were astonished. The holy lands actually shook. Countless holy lands cultivators felt like their minds would explode as Grand Emperor Swordsage hefted his sword.

When he had been young, Swordsage’s dream had been to simply travel the world and expunge it of evil. He had still been a young man when he became a Grand Emperor. And thus, he had traveled far and wide cutting down gods and exterminating wickedness. He and his sword had left a lasting mark on heaven and earth. In his later years, when he thought back on his life, he spent most of his time thinking about those days. Right now, such concepts seemed to overlap with his current self, as if his memories and the present had become fused into one.

And therefore, he hefted his sword in a way that looked comfortable, carefree, and at ease. His sword shone with sword light that illuminated the dome of heaven. It filled the void and became like the will of heaven. It brought an incomparably domineering momentum that could shatter the sky, crush the earth, and devastate all enemies!

It landed on the nearest holy land.

That particular holy land looked like a planet. A deafening rumbling sound echoed out, as if an unstoppable tempest had arrived. The three gods looked on, as well as all of the Firemoon Darkheaven people, along with Xu Qing and the empress..... The holy land that resembled a planet rumbled as a huge rift opened up in it. The rift sank down, and within the space of a few breaths of time, the entire planet was cut through.

It started falling apart! It had been cut in half! The sword light wiped out all life in that holy land! An entire holy land had perished!

Countless streams of life force were swept up by the will of the sword, and rushed toward Grand Emperor Swordsage, to be absorbed by him.... He didn’t use it to stamp out the aura of death, but rather, to bolster his battle prowess.

Without the shackles of the star ring holding him back, Grand Emperor Swordsage wasn’t just back at his peak level of battle prowess. He was actually rising explosively to an even higher level. It didn’t matter that his rise to strength would only last for a short time. After all, there is a saying... once enlightened, one can die happy.[2]

Everyone gasped. All sound seemed to cease. The three Grand Emperors, looking as pale as death, didn’t hesitate to flee. They dropped everything and ran. They might be Grand Emperors, but there was absolutely no way that they could fight back against mightiness akin to that of a Summer Immortal.

Swordsage didn’t even look at them. He just calmly said, “My Summer. Xu Qing. You are my successors, and I gave you my cultivation base and sword. But I never passed on my most powerful sword techniques. Today, I’ll pass them on to both of you.

“My dao is that of the sword. During different parts of my life, I created different sword techniques. There are a total of five.

“The first stance is called... Earth Treasury.”[3]

Grand Emperor Swordsage pushed his right hand in the direction of the remaining two holy lands. Those holy lands trembled and started shaking. The sky dimmed, and the lands quaked, emitting muffled rumbling sounds. They were rumbling sounds that could shake the mind and heart.

Then Swordsage’s voice again echoed through the lands.

“I used Earth Treasury years ago to cut down a vicious killer who was proficient in the dao of earth. The sword move focused on the releasing of earth energy to replace the will of the earth with the will of the sword. It takes earth energy and turns it into sword energy. Then it converges to make an earth sword!”

As he explained, and as Xu Qing and the empress watched, the two holy lands trembled so violently that something like streams of smoke rose up from them. Those streams of smoke were the earth energy that Swordsage had just mentioned. More and more came out. In the shortest of moments, the lands of the two holy lands cracked as if all the nutrients were being sucked out of them. It turned into smoke, which rose up, converged... and turned into an astonishing sword! The sword didn’t just cause the holy lands to shake. The lands of the Firemoon Darkheavens were rippling as if they were the surface of the sea.

And then... the huge sword of earth energy chopped down!

Nothing could stop it! Everyone watched as the two holy lands crumbled into ashes. None of the people in the holy lands could escape or do anything to stop it from happening. They were killed in body and soul. The physical structures of the holy lands were similarly wiped out of existence.

Countless streams of life force swept into Swordsage, causing his aura to rise again. He waved a finger, and Earth Treasury was once again unleashed. Countless streams of fierce sword energy sucked in the aura of the surrounding lands and shot toward the three fleeing Grand Emperors.

It didn’t matter how they fought back. It did no good. The massive disparity made their deaths a foregone conclusion. As the sword energy passed, the three Grand Emperors shattered! Everything about them became nutrients for Swordsage, to be absorbed by him, causing his battle prowess to erupt.

Winds screamed, and the clouds roiled. The Firemoons said nothing. The three gods' heads were bowed. Seeing Grand Emperor Swordsage like this made thēm think about the past. The time period when the broken face came and Dark Serenity left was the most blood-soaked, most brutal, and most dark period of time imaginable. The common state of affairs was for gods to walk the lands either enslaving or slaughtering the populace. It didn’t matter what the species was. They either bent the knee or were wiped out.

Back then, Grand Emperor Swordsage was the only Grand Emperor among humans. And back then, humans were still the number one species. Because of that, they attracted the attention of more gods than most. During that time, Grand Emperor Swordsage fought many gods who wanted to enslave humankind. As a result, he was the focus of attention of many species.

It culminated in the battle in the central region of Revered Ancient. That was when his true form perished, and his clone was left behind. That said, all the battles he had fought dispelled any notions in the central part of Revered Ancient that humans could be enslaved. The gods there abandoned such plans. As long as the Grand Emperor was around, they would never again think to do that.

That was how humankind got through that period of darkness and gloom. It was after that time that the three gods took control of the Firemoon Darkheaven people. By then, Grand Emperor Swordsage’s true form had perished, leaving behind only a clone to safeguard humankind with the threat of his sword.

Seeing Grand Emperor Swordsage right now caused complex thoughts to fill the three gods.

They weren’t the only ones. All of the gods in Revered Ancient looked at Swordsage in action and thought back to that period of darkness. That was especially true in the central part of Revered Ancient. That was the only place where no holy lands had gone, and right now, a gaze from there was focused on the east.
