In the outer sea, Yu Liuchen sat on a boat looking off into the distance. He seemed to be deeply moved.

Though it’s not common knowledge, based on what I know from my stories, this guy almost certainly stayed behind in Revered Ancient because he’s always loved to show off. He’s a freaking showboater! He was like that back then, and now that he’s about to die, he just can’t resist the urge to showboat more than he ever did!

Yu Liuchen felt angry and jealous. And then... he sighed softly.

1. The “world is a tavern” saying came up previously in the following chapters: 29, 205, 546.1, 558.2. ☜

2. The line “once enlightened, one can die happy” also appears in I Shall Seal the Heavens in chapter 516 during the explanation for the Dao Seeking stage of that novel. And thanks to our proofreader UnifiedDivide for pointing out the other Xu Qing (the female one) is mentioned in that chapter. Lol. ☜

3. The Chinese characters for Earth Treasury are the same characters as the bodhisattva Kṣitigarbha. Those of you who read I Shall Seal the Heavens might remember that there’s a supporting character in the novel with that name. As is made obvious in the text of this chapter, the interpretation of the characters doesn’t relate to the bodhisattva as a person, or the person from ISSTH, but rather, the literal meaning of the two Chinese characters as rendered in my translation choice. ☜

Yu Liuchen’s sigh contained a mixture of regret, sorrow, and envy. However, it took only a moment for hīm to notice that there was something off about his thinking. After all... this was an old enemy. There was no way he could feel envious about an enemy.

People should stay dead when they die. Who goes out and dies twice? Snorting coldly, Yu Liuchen looked away from the horizon. That said, True Gods are rare nowadays, and the God Lords are sleeping. Your story is about to end, but my story... is just starting.

***

The sky over the east of Revered Ancient was empty. Four celestial-level holy lands had been floating there before, but Grand Emperor Swordsage’s sword had destroyed three of them. Only the Devilbird holy land was left. Swordsage waved his hand to bring its downfall, and then he gave it to the empress. Grand Emperor Devilbird had escaped, and there was no sign of him.

Next, Swordsage looked to the south and started moving. The empress and Xu Qing followed. It was a distance almost too vast to cross, but with Swordsage’s towering aura, that distance seemed to contract. In the time it takes an incense stick to burn, he took Xu Qing and the empress across many regions, all the way to the south of Revered Ancient.

Soon, it was possible to see three holy lands glittering in the distance. The battlefield in the south did not look like that in the east, where spell formations had kept the lands safe.

The south belonged to the Redland Nobleplexuses, and the lands resembled a sea of flames. Fire was the most suitable environment for them. When the flames became a sea, the Redland Nobleplexuses could release the full battle prowess of their species. The fighting between them and the holy lands had been growing in intensity.

From high in the sky, Xu Qing could see that the sea of flames was full of charred corpses, collapsed buildings, and shattered magical treasures. Some belonged to the various local species, but others... belonged to one of the holy lands that had collapsed.

The south had destroyed one of the holy lands and killed one of the Grand Emperors. There had been four holy lands here, but now there were only three.

Swordsage’s arrival attracted the attention of both sides. The cultivators of the Redland Nobleplexuses looked on in shock, and then their gods ordered them to retreat. They fell back. The holy lands had their defensive spell formations activated, and their three Grand Emperors didn’t dare to come out. They had already sensed what happened in the east.

It was clear that in the face of someone with battle prowess akin to that of a Summer Immortal, both the holy lands and the Redland Nobleplexus were on guard.

Swordsage wasn’t concerned about the reaction of the Redland Nobleplexuses. His goal here was to pass on his sword techniques. And thus, he looked at the three holy lands and then spoke directly into the minds of Xu Qing and the empress.

“The second sword stance in my enlightenment of the sword is called... Rending the Void!”

Grand Emperor Swordsage lifted his right hand and pushed it toward the three holy lands with their defenses raised. The Redland Nobleplexuses reeled, the sky went dark, and the sea of flames went out.... The three holy lands floating in the air, as well as everything surrounding them, suddenly blurred.

A terrifying power seemed to come out of nowhere, filling the area and cutting it off from the outside. Then, that power erupted, as if it had extracted all the energy from that area!

Grand Emperor Swordsage succinctly explained the sword move.

“I created this sword move back when I was working with the Ancient Emperor to wage war on the other species of Revered Ancient. It’s designed to kill all enemies within a certain area. In order to maintain lethality within a large area... it’s designed to extract all of the energy within range. It turns that area into a true void.

“The force of contraction created by the void shatters everything within that range. The shattered remnants are actually sword lineaments. The infinite sword lineaments then converge into a sword that creates the sword move Rending the Void!”

As the Grand Emperor spoke, the three holy lands and everything surrounding them began to tremble. As the energy was sucked out, pressure mounted. When combined with the blessing provided by Grand Emperor Swordsage’s will, all living beings in the area were visibly astonished.

The first place where rifts appeared were in the defensive spell formations of the three holy lands. The pressure of the void caused the spell formations to shake harder and harder. More cracks appeared, until the spell formations finally couldn’t take it, and they shattered. Then the pressure of the void erupted inside the holy lands. In an instant, howls of agony rang out.

However, they couldn’t pass outside of that specific area.

Only the strongest experts in the holy lands, for instance the Grand Emperors and Imperial Sovereigns, were able to stand firm, their eyes bloodshot as they tapped into their trump cards. Unfortunately for them... there was no point.

The crumbling continued, and the rifts proliferated. Soon, those rifts started to look like sword lineaments. In the end, countless sword lineaments combined, turning into an astonishing sword. Then, in that area of true void, sword light shone, sword energy proliferated, and a sword will crushed heaven and earth.

Sometime later, the barriers dissipated, and the rubble that remained of the holy lands fell to the ground. There was no flesh and blood. The only thing that remained of the living things was dust. All life force had been taken as nutrients by Grand Emperor Swordsage, causing his battle prowess to rise again. His energy swept the area, causing the gods of the Redland Nobleplexus to back away. They weren’t willing to get into a fight.

Only after Grand Emperor Swordsage had taken Xu Qing and the empress away did a calm voice drift within the lands of the Redland Nobleplexuses. “Without a True God... it would be difficult for us to deal with a Summer Immortal.”

In a brief moment, multiple holy lands had been destroyed, and multiple Grand Emperors had perished. It was a monumental story that was already shaking Revered Ancient. Countless species were reeling in shock, and numerous gods sank into silence. The past glory of humankind was now something innumerable species were thinking about.

The tempestuous news had already reached the celestial-level holy lands that had come to the west and north of Revered Ancient. They were both terrified and astonished. The holy lands there quickly joined forces, both to activate their defenses and also issued calls for help into the starry sky beyond Revered Ancient.

At the same time, they didn’t hesitate to leave the spots they had previously occupied and group together. Having come to Revered Ancient, they couldn’t leave it. Therefore, the best path forward seemed to be to join forces. They were going to rely on their joint strength to hold fast until the earthly-level holy lands and the one and only heavenly-level holy land arrived from the starry sky.

Sadly, there was no way their plan would work without a hitch. The west of Revered Ancient was controlled by the Netherworld Chasmcorpses. The north was in the hands of the Northfate Kings. And those two species would naturally do everything possible to take advantage of the situation.

As a result, the fighting in the west and north instantly became more intense. The cultivators of the two major species held nothing back as they tried to prevent the holy lands from retreating.

As chaos reigned and the sound of slaughter grew loud, Grand Emperor Swordsage appeared in the sky in the west.

“The third sword stance I gained enlightenment of... is called Heavenly Palaces. I created this stance in the war against the other species, before Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity managed to conquer Revered Ancient. However, the slaughter it can unleash is too brutal. It can only be used to target cultivators, and damages the heavenly balance.... After the gods came, I never used it.”

Grand Emperor Swordsage looked at the holy lands up ahead. He waved his hand.

The resulting scene caused Xu Qing’s pupils to constrict. It had been shocking to see the holy lands in the east and south collapse. But that was nothing like this.

The truth was that... the Heavenly Palaces sword technique was exactly as Grand Emperor Swordsage had said. It only targeted cultivators, and it damaged the heavenly balance. And that was because... the heavenly palaces mentioned in the name of the technique were not actual palaces that existed in the heavens. Rather, they were the heavenly palaces that Core Formation cultivators created inside their own cultivation base.

Their heavenly palaces all collapsed, as if something on the outside had taken control of them. They turned into illusory swords which then blasted out from inside their bodies. It was a brutal scene. There were unending howls of agony. Fatalities occurred nonstop. Seas of swords screamed through heaven and earth, filling the holy lands in the west. It was a pure catastrophe for all cultivators who were in the Core Formation level or higher.

Those under Core Formation had no hope of surviving either, as the sea of swords wiped them all out. The holy lands themselves were also devastated by the swords. Everything was suffering destruction and extermination.

In the quiet that resulted afterward, Grand Emperor Swordsage again spoke to Xu Qing and the empress.

“It turns the enemy’s heavenly palaces into swords. Thus the name of the technique. Next comes the fourth sword technique.... Its name is Star Splendor.”

As the words left his mouth, the dome of heaven rumbled, as if heaven were being opened. The light of day then vanished and was replaced by the darkness of night. Within that darkness were innumerable twinkling stars. It was an infinitude of starlight that filled heaven and earth, becoming beam after beam of sword light.

As swords filled the world, Grand Emperor Swordsage stepped forward onto a beam of starlight. Taking Xu Qing and the empress with him, he used that starlight to go to the frozen plains in the north of Revered Ancient. In that land of pure white, starlight radiated, reflecting on the snow to create brilliance that covered all of the holy lands. From a distance, it looked like a vortex of starlight consuming everything.

Everyone in Revered Ancient was struck speechless. Countless species sank into silence. The gods simply looked on.

Grand Emperor Swordsage was the most brightly shining star there was in Revered Ancient, and he was growing stronger thanks to the vortex of starlight. Endless life force streamed into him, causing his aura to climb higher, and pushing his battle prowess toward the peak level of that of a Summer Immortal. Heaven trembled. The earth shook.

And yet, his aura of death was stronger than ever. When he spoke, his voice was hoarse. “As for the last sword stance... I’m going to use it there.”

He looked up, his gaze piercing through the canopy of heaven and into the starry sky. In the starry sky outside of the Revered Ancient mainland, five holy lands had appeared.

Four were in the lead. It didn’t matter their size or speed. They were all beyond the celestial level. They were earthly-level holy lands.

Behind them... was something that resembled an enormous heart, pulsing and emanating an incomparably terrible mightiness. That was... the sole heavenly-level holy land!

There was a tower on that heavenly-level holy land, and standing atop it was an old man in a black robe. His hands were clasped behind his back, and his face was full of wrinkles. His expression itself seemed ancient, as if he was someone who had stepped through countless years of time and had witnessed all history play out.

He was looking at Revered Ancient. Despite the great distance between the two of them, he had locked gazes with Swordsage.

High in the sky was an ancient Summer Immortal. He had existed at the apex of Deep Earth and had walked his own path. He was a hero to Deep Earth, as he had led the cultivators from there to open up new horizons in Revered Ancient. He had crushed the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk, given rise to heavenly daos in Revered Ancient, and ensured that countless Deep Earth cultivators also had the chance to reach the apex.

For the purpose of protecting Deep Earth, of advancing the path of immortals, and of advancing the limits of the cultivation system, he and his companions had ventured out into the unfamiliar starry sky. They had sought enlightenment and destined opportunities. It had been a journey that lasted untold years. Now, one of them had returned.

Underneath that same sky was a new Summer Immortal. Though he could not quite compare to the Summer Immortals of the past, he had walked his own path, and was also a hero to humankind. After Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity left, he had killed gods, he had conquered other species, and he had waged war for the sake of keeping humankind safe. He had sacrificed everything for the sake of humans. To him, Deep Earth wasn’t important. The countless other species weren’t important. The only thing that mattered to him was humankind!

As of this moment, an old Summer Immortal and a new Summer Immortal locked eyes. When they did...

Heaven collapsed. Intense rumbling sounds echoed out as ripples filled the sky, making it look like undulated fish scales. They rippled so dramatically that spots started to appear. Then, accompanied by deafening booms, the spots shattered. The entire sky was affected. It almost looked as if a host of enormous devil’s trumpet flowers were blooming.[1]

As those flowers bloomed, an ancient voice spoke from beyond the heavens, a voice that filled Revered Ancient. The sea of Revered Ancient seethed. Countless species trembled. Every god that was under the level of a True God, including countless Godfire Gods and even Altar Gods, were all shaking. Even the extremely rare True Gods in their resting places... shivered inwardly.

That was because... the pressure in this voice surpassed the level of a peak Summer Immortal, and was infinitesimally close to that level which was equivalent to a God Lord. An Immortal Lord.

“It’s not impossible for you to be resurrected.”

Xu Qing inhaled sharply. The empress looked up, her heart, which had been full of desolation, suddenly stirring with hope.

“Submit to me. Take me into Revered Ancient to acquire what I seek. Once I dispel the fog in front of me and seize Immortal Lord personhood, then I can truly resurrect you.”

Silence reigned for a short time.

Then Swordsage spoke in a soft voice. “I grew up hearing stories about the nine of you Seniors. Your names are etched deeply in my memory. Your deeds brought light to my heart. I have great respect for all of you, even right now, oh exalted Ji Zun.”[2]

Swordsage bowed deeply. When he straightened up, his eyes glinted sharply. And when he spoke, his voice was more aggressive than before.

“But... are you really the exalted Ji Zun’s true form? I find it hard to believe that the nine Seniors who left Deep Earth, conquered the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk, and founded Revered Ancient, they with such pure emotions, would end up falling into this level of disgrace. I find it hard to believe that they would raise the butcher knife over their own descendants, all for personal gain. In fact, I refuse to believe it.”

Grand Emperor Swordsage spoke with decisiveness that could sever nails and chop iron.

Up in the sky, the black-robed old man on the high tower in the heavenly-level holy land looked down expressionlessly at Revered Ancient. With eyes locked onto Grand Emperor Swordsage, he coolly said, “Considering how difficult it must have been for you to push your cultivation to this level, I’m going to explain a few things to you.

“When it comes to Revered Ancient and Deep Earth, you could say that the entire cultivation system was created specifically for me to attain Immortal Lord personhood. It’s a profoundly meaningful thing. And all of the hard work that led to this point is for the purpose of creating a bright future.

“And thus, Junior, you are being too narrow-minded in your heart, mind, and will. Great daos are emotionless. If you want to continue making advancement, you need to keep your eyes fixed on what’s ahead.”

His voice boomed like thunder in Revered Ancient. Everyone heard him. Everyone understood what he meant. Some people agreed with what he said, others didn’t. But in the final analysis... everyone now knew why this holy land had suddenly shown up.

Unfortunately, it was easy to guess what this Summer Immortal sought, and the reason why the war had played out as it did. What he needed... was not some physical object. It seemed most likely that he needed life force. A blood sacrifice. Death.... It was hard to say the specifics. But everyone knew that it had nothing to do with the gods.

And this person was not planning to settle down in Revered Ancient. The broken face was not something he could fight against. Therefore... the arrival of this holy land, as well as the actions taken by the terrestrial- and celestial-level holy lands, just made things more obvious.

Swordsage shook his head. He looked away from the sky and to the surrounding lands. Gazing at humankind, he softly said, “I’m too narrow-minded in heart because all I care about is humankind.”

He lifted his hand and pointed The Emperor’s Sword toward the sky. “I’m too simplistic in mind because all I care about is humankind.”

Winds screamed across the lands, creating a tempest with Grand Emperor Swordsage in the middle. It spread dramatically. “I’m too immature in will because, yet again, all I care about is humankind.”

Grand Emperor Swordsage’s eyes gleamed with mysterious light that was a mixture of determination and decisiveness. His hand tightened on The Emperor’s Sword. And his aura was rising explosively. Wild colors flashed in heaven and earth. Thunderous rumbling sounds filled Revered Ancient.

“Great daos might be emotionless. But that doesn’t mean emotions don’t exist. As we tread onward, we don’t just keep our eyes fixed on the path ahead of us... we also enjoy the scenery around us, as well as the company of our loved ones. If walking this path means trampling on the corpses of my own people and drinking their blood... well... I’m not willing to do that!”

As those last words left Grand Emperor Swordsage’s mouth, his eyes blazed with brilliant light, and he looked up, his gaze passing into what lay beyond the heavens. His aura raged to the highest heights. The power and life force he had absorbed from all of his enemies, including the Grand Emperors, burned with great intensity, all despite the increasing strength of his aura of death.

All of a sudden, the vortex surrounding Swordsage swelled, filling region after region. At the same time, Swordsage himself grew dramatically taller until he was an enormous giant. The Emperor’s Sword in his hand became massive. Hefting it, he said, “My sword skills evolved during different stages of my life. In total, I created five techniques. The first four are Earth Treasury, Rending the Void, Heavenly Palaces, and Star Splendor....

“In the battle in which I defended my Summer, my life force was clearly sputtering out, so I had no opportunity to use the fifth one. But today, that sword will finally make its appearance in Revered Ancient.

“It’s called... The Human World!”

As Swordsage murmured those words, ancient memories welled up in his mind. Within those memories, he saw a glorious world. There was no war. There were no gods. Countless species rose to great heights under the leadership of the Ancient Emperor.

This was the flourishing human world before the broken face came.

Sighing, Swordsage hefted his sword and then slashed it toward the sky. A sword that contained all of the majesty and life of the human world shot upward. Next, Swordsage envisioned what happened after the broken face arrived and Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity left. It was a dark age. Corpses littered the earth, and howls of grief and anguish filled the sky everywhere. The sky went dark, and humankind descended into despair.

That was... the anguish of the human world.

Swordsage bitterly swept his sword out again, sending forth a sword move that contained the despair of all living beings. It shot toward the sky!

Next came the difficulties of the human world after Emperor Eastglory was defeated.

Then the struggles of the human world in the era of Sageheaven.

After that, the revival of the human world under Mirrorcloud’s control.

And then the tenacity of the human world when Dao Life reigned.

It was followed by the struggles of the human world for the thousands of years that Dark War ruled.

As the memories of the different time periods of the human world flitted through Grand Emperor Swordsage’s mind, they caused glittering swords to appear in the canopy of heaven.[3]

Finally, the image of Empress Summer Departure appeared in Swordsage’s memories. After she ascended the throne, the human world rose to prominence!

Swordsage smiled. “This is the human world that I have safeguarded.”

His body blurred as the aura of death covered him completely. As that happened, a sword shot forth that was filled with the glory of the human world, risen to prominence.

Up in the dome of heaven was the history of humankind that Swordsage had experienced. It was embodied in a host of swords that merged together into one massive sword that was The Human World. As Grand Emperor Swordsage called on all of his remaining strength, he slashed that sword at the dome of heaven, at the area beyond the heavens, at... the holy lands!

The sword split the sky, crushing everything in its path with impunity. Spectacular force glittered, the likes of which couldn’t be surpassed.

If that ancient immortal represented the will of heaven, then this sword represented the will of humankind, ready to battle with heaven! In the blink of an eye, it broke out from Revered Ancient and smashed into the four earthly-level holy lands that posed the first obstacle.

Outside of Revered Ancient, sound was consumed by the void. But all living beings could see what was happening, and it was a sight that shook them to the core and created an unforgettable memory. Four earthly-level holy lands... trembled violently. The momentum of their descent was halted, and they were sent tumbling away. They had been defeated with one attack!

Regret appeared in the eyes of the ancient immortal.

“That’s an outstanding sword move. If you weren’t in your current state, and were an actual Summer Immortal, then that sword would strike fear into my heart. But right now....”

The ancient immortal extended his hand toward the sword. He was going to destroy it. But then, his gaze hardened as his hand closed onto nothing. It was because....

The sword wasn’t actually targeting him! Instead, it was targeting the sealing mark up above that prevented all living beings from leaving Revered Ancient!

Sword light glittered, carrying with it the will of the human world and the will of Swordsage, which pierced into the sealing mark. Then it shifted to point toward the broken face of Eminent Desolation, the eyes of which were closed. If the sword shot forth, then the broken face would be struck, and the eyes would definitely open. As for what would happen after that, nobody knew. Whatever happened, nobody would be able to control or stop it.

The immortal’s face fell. He could see that The Human World had been set up with him in mind. It wouldn’t do much to anyone else, but if he got close to the sword, it would explode. His eyes shifted from the sealing mark to Grand Emperor Swordsage.

“Well done, youngster. There was still a chance you could have been truly resurrected, but you gave that up to delay my arrival. Well, that’s fine. The will of your sword will only last for half of a sixty-year-cycle.... I don’t mind letting you wait that much longer. I’ll be waiting out here for the sword will to vanish.”

The immortal slowly faded from sight. The heavenly-level holy land and the four earthly-level holy lands retreated.

1. The flower mentioned here is Datura stramonium, a poisonous flowering plant. The flowers sort of look like trumpets. Here’s the wiki page for the flower, which includes a picture. In Chinese, the name of the flower is a transliteration of a sanskrit word, so the specific characters aren’t really important per se. ☜

2. Ji Zun: This is an odd name. Ji is a surname which also means “to draw/suck up water.” Since there is another surname Ji that’s important in I Shall Seal the Heavens (that clan was even mentioned in the ISSTH reference I linked to a few chapters ago), I should probably point out that this is NOT the same Ji from that novel. It’s a different Ji entirely. Zun is a complicated character that is often used as a title. In other words, this name could be interpreted as a daoist name. In the comments in Chinese, the top comment was someone speculating that the name means “a respected person who sucks the life out of all people.” There were many other comments that were essentially making jokes about the “sucking” aspect of this character. Madam Deathblade had the same reaction. Given how unusual this name is, there’s a possibility it’s a daoist name. Similar to how I’ve handled other names, I am going to put a mental bookmark here and reserve the right to come back and change it to a translated daoist name later on if that makes sense. At the moment, there isn’t enough evidence to say definitively how it should be handled, and I don’t want to bother the author about it. ☜

3. The stories of the various emperors were first recounted in chapter 401. They were all mentioned in many contexts in other chapters, but probably the most important were the revelations in chapters 950 and 951. ☜

Something hazy filled the dome of heaven over Revered Ancient. It was haze from the human world. The human world of humankind. It was the will of Grand Emperor Swordsage’s sword, which had been added to the world. All living beings in Revered Ancient now had half of a sixty-year-cycle of time added to them.

Of course, it only applied to the mortal living beings and cultivators. As far as the gods were concerned, this was a conflict between cultivators, and it had nothing to do with thēm.

The only reason some would consider interfering was that it could theoretically reduce the joss flame they had access to. The three gods of the Firemoons fell into that camp. There were no other gods similar to the empress. Shē was the only one.

And taking in Revered Ancient as a whole, the gods who accepted the joss flame of local species were actually in the minority. Most of the gods there were just sleeping. None of them made a single move. In the final analysis, this war between cultivators was like a game to the gods. Ultimately, it didn’t really matter to thēm how it played out.

As for Grand Emperor Swordsage, he didn’t care what the gods thought. His entire will was focused on that one sword. At the moment, a rain of blood was falling from heaven. It was the rain that fell when a Summer Immortal perished.

Within that rain, hovered Grand Emperor Swordsage. Looking over his shoulder at the human world... he smiled.

“It’s hard to let go of the obsession to live. The willingness to let go leads to true rebirth.” [1]

His smile would last for all eternity. He was now completely inundated with an aura of death. His flesh and blood were now shrinking into nothing, and he was turning back into stone.

His three spiritual souls emerged from eyes, ears, nose, and mouth. The human soul returned to the memories of humankind. The earthly soul returned to the lands of humankind. The heavenly soul returned to the destiny aura.

Then came the seven physical souls. The physical souls made from the five emperors retreated, slowly regaining consciousness in the process. The past and future the empress had offered returned through Grand Emperor Swordsage’s smile.

Then there was The Emperor’s Sword he held. He loosened his grip, and the sword became a glinting arc that flashed in front of Xu Qing’s eyes.

The rain fell harder.

Xu Qing and the empress hovered in the rain, their hearts filled with grief at the sight of it. It was a grief that would not soon fade away. The wind blew, sweeping through the countless mountains, mixing with the rain of blood, and becoming something unforgettable that echoed in their hearts. Ultimately, it turned into a sigh.

Xu Qing bowed his head. Looking at the statue of the Grand Emperor, he clasped hands and bowed deeply. The empress bid farewell in her own silent way.

The image was something burned into the hearts of all cultivators.

***

A month passed.

After all the celestial-level holy lands collapsed, the war in the Revered Ancient mainland ended. The ancient Summer Immortal could not come down into Revered Ancient. And he didn’t demand that the four earthly-level holy lands do so in his stead. There was no point in that.

As for the terrestrial-level holy lands that were left behind in Revered Ancient, they were ignored, just as their own ancestors had ignored those they left behind on the mainland all those years ago.

And when the local people rose up, the terrestrial-level holy lands didn’t even have the option of surrendering. The only thing that awaited them was death. Fighting back only delayed the inevitable. And no matter how they delayed things, they couldn’t do anything about the deadline of half of a sixty-year-cycle.

As for humans... they rose to complete prominence. Whether it was the empress’ actions or Grand Emperor Swordsage’s heroic feats, the result was that humankind was once again at the peak of glory among the countless species in Revered Ancient. They had become a light in the darkness.

***

At the end of that month, as the rain continued to fall, the doors of an ancient temple opened in the Imperial Region of humankind.

Two figures strode out from within. One of them was Xu Qing. The other was Erniu.

Xu Qing’s eyes shone with confusion. Erniu’s face was clouded, and he seemed anxious.

A sigh echoed out in the temple behind them. Then the palace lord of the Summer Immortal Palace spoke. “I’ve explained everything to you. Going forward, all of the Summer Immortal Palace locations in the Revered Ancient mainland will be closed.

“Whenever Revered Ancient faces an impending catastrophe, the Summer Immortal Palace takes precautions. And we invite various powerful experts and chosen to slumber with us in the immortal essence. freewebnovel.com

“Those powerful experts and chosen are the seeds of civilization for the countless species. After the catastrophe is over, they’ll be woken up. If the world has changed, then their mission will be to establish a new civilization of cultivators. This is how things played out in previous catastrophes.

“The others have already been sent on their way. Xu Qing. Chen Erniu. Your choice is yours to make. Please, inform me of your decisions as quickly as possible.”

The door of the temple slowly closed, and then the temple slowly began to fade from sight within the rain. When it disappeared, it would indicate that the period of slumber had begun. There wasn’t much time left.

Xu Qing and Erniu stood silently in the rain. Half a month ago, when the war in the east wound to an end, they had been summoned by the palace lord of the Summer Immortal Palace. In the half month that followed, the palace lord gave both of them destined opportunities and good fortune.

Xu Qing’s immortal body had been stabilized even further. And with the help of the palace lord, his consciousness had been inserted into his god body, making it a completely functioning clone.

As for Erniu, his good fortune had involved awakening the memories from the bones of his third life. And by the means of various unknown techniques employed by the palace lord, Erniu had awakened even more memories. Unfortunately, that process had left him confused and somewhat blank.

That was why they had such strange expressions on their faces. That, and all of the information the palace lord had imparted to them over the past few days.

“Xu Qing, the reason I chose to help you walk the path of the extreme immortal and form your immortal body is that... your Master visited me. He paid handsomely to gain my assistance. I summoned you, helped you stabilize your immortal body and revive your god clone, because your Master... your Master... paid a very heavy price.

“It’s the same with you, Erniu. You have a very mysterious background. When your Master came to the Summer Immortal Palace, he paid a similarly high price to look into all the histories. Unfortunately, the records of the Summer Immortal Palace only contained information from after your third life. As for your second life, and your first life, we simply don’t have any information in our records. Perhaps you are the only one who can know the details. As for your third life, we don’t know much about it. It seems that some powerful force erased all of that information, and the Summer Immortal Palace is incapable of releasing it.

“But your Master gave up some of his essence. He sacrificed some of his own power to drag out an opportunity for you from within the immortal essence. He wanted to absorb the histories of the Summer Immortal Palace, and he wanted you to have more memories about... who you are.

“The two of you have a really good Master.”

***

Xu Qing looked up, peering into the rain in the direction of the continent of South Phoenix.

“Eldest Brother,” he murmured, “it seems like Master... is making arrangements for when he’s no longer with us.”

Erniu was quiet for a long moment. “Let’s go back. We can just ask the old man to explain what’s going on.”

Erniu headed in the direction of the teleportation portals in the imperial capital. Xu Qing nodded and followed him.

For now, they weren’t thinking about any other matters. The most important thing on both of their minds was to get back to South Phoenix to see their Master. They wanted an explanation for everything.

Not long after, a teleportation portal rumbled to life in the capital, and Xu Qing and Erniu vanished.

A few days later, a pagoda could be seen screaming at top speed through the air above the Forbidden Sea between Emperor-Receiving Prefecture and South Phoenix. Around evening, it arrived at Seven Blood Eyes. The pagoda vanished, and then Xu Qing and Erniu appeared on the summit of the Seventh Peak, outside the closed door of Master Seventh’s mansion grotto. Both of them kowtowed.

Time passed. Finally, a sigh echoed from within the mansion grotto.

“The two of you didn’t go into slumber in the immortal essence along with the Summer Immortal Palace, huh. What are you doing here?”

“Master,” they said.

Xu Qing looked up at the mansion grotto, his heart filled with conflicted concerns and worries.

Erniu’s face had remained grim these past few days. Looking up, he said, “What’s going on here, old man??”

The mansion grotto’s door slammed open and Master Seventh walked out and glared at Erniu. “You’re really asking for it, aren’t you??”

Upon seeing Master Seventh act like he normally did, Erniu breathed a visible sigh of relief. Putting a fawning expression onto his face, he chuckled.

Master Seventh snorted coldly. Then he looked at Xu Qing and gave a slight nod.

“You did well working on that immortal body.” Looking up at the dome of heaven, he started talking before Xu Qing or Erniu could ask any questions. “I know what the two of you want to ask about. You want to know what to do after I’m gone.”

Xu Qing and Erniu were both shaken to the core.

“It’s true the Summer Immortal Palace helped the two of you because of the price I paid. However, I’m your Master. So I was just doing what I ought to do. It wasn’t just the two of you. There are others from Seven Blood Eyes that I sent to slumber, including that good-for-nothing Third Sib. Second Sib can make her own decisions, and I won’t do anything to interfere.

“The reason I did this is to play things safe. There’s karma between me and that ancient immortal from the heavenly-level holy land. Of course, it’s not like I lack confidence. Swordsage used that final sword move to buy time for me. Therefore, you two can kindly get the hell out of here and stop interrupting my cultivation!”

Master Seventh glared at Erniu, then turned and gave Xu Qing another nod. Before the two of them could say anything, Master Seventh flicked his sleeve to send the two of them flying away. Then he stalked back into his mansion grotto and slammed the door.

On the inside, he stood for a long moment in silence. Then he sighed.

A storm is coming. Can my umbrella... offer enough protection?[2]

Master Seventh sat down and closed his eyes. It didn’t matter if it could or not. He would fight to make sure his umbrella could protect his apprentices from the coming tempest.

***

Outside of Seven Blood Eyes, the wind blew loudly in the spot where Xu Qing and Erniu had been ejected to. Neither of them spoke. They just struggled to stabilize their hearts. Although Master Seventh had seemed calm and relaxed, the truth was that Xu Qing and Erniu weren’t children. They could guess at what was really going on.

“The old man... is really getting old. And yet even in his old age, he’s still willing to put everything on the line....” Erniu looked at Xu Qing. “Little Ah Qing, I think you should go slumber with the Summer Immortal Palace. You don’t need to worry about what’s going on out here. I can deal with the old man.

“I mean, he’s just an immortal, right? Like I have any reason to be scared of a wimp like that. Thanks to my third-life memories, I now have some clues about my second life. And I know it has something to do with the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk.

“That’s why I’m planning to take a trip to where the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk are sealed. I should be able to find my second life there. And then... as the Eldest Brother, I will personally save the world!”

Erniu proudly clasped Xu Qing’s shoulder. “Things would be too dangerous for you there. After all, if you die, you’ll actually end up dead. Really dead. Not like me. That’s why you won’t be coming with me. Be a good boy now, little Ah Qing. Go to the Summer Immortal Palace. Believe me, in thirty years, your Eldest Brother and your Master will wake you up together.”

Erniu looked Xu Qing in the eyes and earnestly said, “If you don’t go, I won’t be able to rest at ease.”

Xu Qing thought for a moment and then nodded. “Let me at least send you on your way. After all, we’re going in the same direction, right?”

Erniu thought for a moment. Not wanting to give Xu Qing any spare time to think about things, he hauled him over to the teleportation portal, and activated it, sending both of them back to the imperial capital. After all, the entrance leading to the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk was beneath the imperial capital.

Xu Qing said nothing as Erniu escorted him all the way to the Summer Immortal Palace. After they bowed in greeting, the door opened, and the palace lord appeared. Erniu cleared his throat.

“I’m not going, Senior. But my Junior Brother will be going.”

With that, he pushed Xu Qing forward.

Xu Qing looked back at him through the door.

Erniu laughed heartily. “Alright, little Junior Brother. See you in thirty years!”

With that, Erniu vanished without a trace. The door closed quietly, and the temple disappeared.

A few days later, after the temple was definitely gone, Erniu stepped out of the concealment of invisibility. He finally felt very calm.

“He finally did as told. And I can rest at ease.”

Erniu took a deep breath. Eyes flashing with a crazy look, he shot toward the entrance leading to the sealed resting place of the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk. He had a way to get inside.

***

After Erniu was on his way, the temple appeared again in the rain. However, it was very blurry, as if it would disappear only a moment later.

The door opened and Xu Qing stepped out.

Behind him, the palace lord said, “Are you sure you aren’t going to slumber in the immortal essence?”

“I’m not,” Xu Qing whispered.

The palace lord declined to try to persuade him otherwise. The door closed and the temple vanished.

Xu Qing was left standing alone in the rain. He knew that everyone would be making preparations in the half-sixty-year-cycle that Grand Emperor Swordsage had bought for them.

His Master was currently in secluded cultivation. His Eldest Brother was going to go all out with the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk. A month after getting back to the capital, the empress had gone to the ghast hollow in Emperor-Receiving Prefecture.

It wasn’t just humans who were getting ready. Other species were doing the same. Everyone with a bit of skill or strength was preparing.

“Half a sixty-year-cycle....” Xu Qing looked off in the direction of the outer sea. His eyes gleamed with decisiveness and determination.

1. Grand Emperor Swordsage’s words combine the chapter titles of chapter 1081 and 1083. ☜

2. As I mentioned in the footnote of chapter 1078, this ‘storm is coming’ is usually a metaphor describing dramatic changes. ☜

Grand Emperor Swordsage had perished. His Master was in seclusion. The empress was working on cultivation. Erniu had gone away. It was almost like the spinning of a gnomon on a gigantic sundial. In half of a sixty-year-cycle, a huge storm would hit.

The ancient immortal waiting outside of Revered Ancient was now a sharp blade hanging over the heads of all living beings. He was a mortal threat. It was easy to imagine how intense the sensation of danger would become as time passed.

Even to mortals, half of a sixty-year-cycle wasn’t very long. And that was even more the case with cultivators. If one went into secluded meditation, that time could pass very quickly.

The sense of danger would turn into pressure that would weigh down on the world. All species were going to be making their final preparations. In fact, it seemed like the only option they had was to beg for protection from the gods. And thus, some places became even more peaceful than before. Others, in contrast, descended into chaos.

Meanwhile, the apathetic gods just watched everything play out. To thēm, this delay was just an amusing twist in all the drama.

As for the misery of the people.... The Revered Ancient mainland had been a place of misery ever since the broken face arrived. The main difference was that in the past, the misery had mostly affected mortals. Now, it affected everyone.

In the desert in the Moonrite Region, Nethersprite was boiling water in the Green Spirit Pharmacy.

The Heir Apparent took a sip of tea then put the cup down. “It’s actually fair when you think about it.”

Princess Brightblossom shook her head slightly as she looked at Xu Qing as he refilled the Heir Apparent’s cup.

“Did you think things through yet?” she asked.

Xu Qing put the teapot down, sat down in front of the two of them, and nodded.

After leaving the Imperial Region, his first stop had been here, the Moonrite Region. Before departing, he wanted to see Ling’er as well as the Heir Apparent and his siblings. Unfortunately, Ling’er was still in seclusion, with Grandpa Ninth standing guard. Xu Qing chose not to disturb them. And thus, he was here saying his farewells to the Heir Apparent and Princess Brightblossom.

“It’s good for kids to go out and get some practical experience,” the Heir Apparent said. “But the outer sea is a very chaotic place. Given your current cultivation base and battle prowess, you shouldn’t run into too much trouble. Just remember... don’t go in too deep.”

He put his tea down, looked at Xu Qing, and thought for a moment. Then he suddenly lifted his right hand. An instant later, a dao lineament swirled out, forming a sealing mark in front of him.

“This is a manifestation of my perception-altering authority. You can use it three times. Take it to defend yourself.”

Xu Qing had not told the Heir Apparent what his true destination was. But the sealing mark made it clear that the Heir Apparent was concerned for his safety. Xu Qing accepted it.

Princess Brightblossom looked at him deeply, then sighed. Waving her hand, she sent out an illusory river into a jade bottle. She gave the bottle to Xu Qing.

“That’s a bit of the River of Time that I assimilated.”

Xu Qing took it. Then he stood and bowed very deeply to the two of them. “I’ll take my leave now, Seniors. Grandpa Heir Apparent. Grandma Brightblossom. Please... take care of yourselves.”

He turned and walked away. He left the Green Spirit Pharmacy. He left the mountains. He vanished from the desert.

After he was gone, Princess Brightblossom sighed. “The kid isn’t going to the outer sea.”

The Heir Apparent said nothing for a moment. Then he also sighed. “It’s been many years since I first heard the legends about the outer sea. Those legends also mention the place he’s going.

“Thirty years.... Father is already on his way back. Based on my calculations, he isn’t very far away. I hope that by the time he gets back, he’s still our father. I guess it’s good that the kid is going away.”

Princess Brightblossom looked up into the sky and out into what lay beyond. She said nothing.

***

Xu Qing was making his way quietly through the Moonrite Region. Before departing, he wanted to go to Sea-Sealing County to see Plumdark. After that, he needed to remove all hindrances before starting on the journey of his own choosing.

Thirty years.... As he sped through the sky, ripples suddenly spread through the sky, and a huge mirror appeared.

In the middle of the mirror was a huge mountain covered with temples. An old woman appeared on the summit of the mountain. Next to her was an old man with a huge white beard covering his face.

Upon seeing the two of them, Xu Qing stopped in place and bowed respectfully.

“Grandma Fifth. Grandpa Eighth.”

Looking kindly at Xu Qing, Grandma Fifth nodded. Without saying a word she extended her hand, giving him a flower petal made from her own authority. When the flower petal formed, Grandma Fifth looked visibly older.

“Take it. As long as you have even one breath of life within you, that flower petal can restore you.”

Xu Qing knew that Grandma Fifth’s authority took away some of her life force every time she used it. He hesitated.

“She’s giving it to you. Take it!” said Grandpa Eighth, glaring. Then he waved his hand, and sent out a sealing mark made of his own authority of rage. “That can boost your battle prowess. Just remember that you’ll be temporarily weakened after the boost ends.”

These gifts from his elders filled Xu Qing’s heart with warmth. He accepted them and was about to say something when a beam of sword light suddenly shot toward him from above. Wild colors flashed in heaven and earth as five streams of sword energy turned into a sealing mark in front of him.

Then Grandpa Ninth’s voice echoed out in heaven and earth.

“That’s the will of my sword. If you use it all at once, it can slaughter an Imperial Sovereign!”

Xu Qing was visibly moved. After accepting everything, he took a deep breath and bowed to Grandma Fifth, Grandpa Eight, and in the direction the sword light had come from.

As the three venerable siblings looked on, he left the Moonrite Region.

***

A day later, a pagoda that glittered with starlight appeared in the clouds over Sea-Sealing County. Xu Qing stepped out of it. A moment later he was deep underground.

This had once been a palace of operations of an Ancient Emperor. And now, Xu Qing was standing outside of a hall in Plumdark’s phoenix palace. Everything was quiet. There were no signs that anyone had disturbed this place.

It had been years since Xu Qing ordered this place to be sealed tight. There was a spell formation constantly active to ensure that Plumdark wasn’t disturbed.

When Patriarch Golden Vajra Warrior sensed Xu Qing’s arrival, he appeared outside the grand hall. He bowed excitedly.

“Greetings, milord!” he said in a loud voice. “Milord, I’ve missed you so much! Don’t worry. Little Freespirit has been cautious and conscientious this entire time. I’ve been standing guard and can tell you that no slip-ups have occurred. With me on guard here, not even a speck of dust has dared to show up!” freewebnovel.com

He was attempting to convey how useful he was. Though he had been a bit bored in this place, he was more than happy to be here. After all, the outside was a dangerous place, and following Xu Qing around made things even more dangerous. He was still constantly worried about being turned into cannon fodder....

Considering how strong he had become, he knew that if he left this place, he would probably be put to use in nine battles out of ten.... As far as Patriarch Golden Vajra Warrior was concerned, that was just too dangerous.

In all of the novels he had read, being the bodyguard of the protagonist’s love interest always brought big rewards as long as you didn’t mess up. That was why he was working so hard to paint himself as being very useful.

Xu Qing nodded and then looked at the phoenix temple. Plumdark had been seeking enlightenment for a lot longer than Xu Qing had expected.

Eventually he looked away and studied the surroundings. As Patriarch Golden Vajra Warrior cautiously looked on, Xu Qing suddenly waved his hand.

The will of a god erupted out. Ripples spread to fill a 30-meter area, making everything within it distorted and difficult to see. However, it was possible to see a figure forming. It was a figure that settled cross-legged and then sank down into the ground.

Given that Patriarch Golden Vajra Warrior wasn’t up to date on everything that had happened, his eyes went wide. He was almost certain he had just seen another version of Xu Qing.... And that version of Xu Qing seemed cold, apathetic, and incredibly terrifying.

Shivering, the patriarch said, “Milord, was that...?”

“My god clone,” Xu Qing replied calmly.

Considering that Ling’er was in the care of the Heir Apparent and his siblings, Xu Qing wasn’t worried about her being kept safe in the thirty years to come. But he was worried about Plumdark. Therefore, he was going to leave his god clone behind, both to seek enlightenment of godly authority, and also, to stand guard over Plumdark. He had no intention of bringing his god clone with him on his journey. That was because in the place he was going... gods were not welcome.

Unfortunately, even though he was leaving his god clone behind in Revered Ancient, his immortal true self couldn’t use his godly authority magics. That included his authority of sound, the carving knife formed from his godly authority of fate, and his taboo poison. All of those could only be used by his god clone.

That said, given I have my extreme immortal cultivation base, my battle prowess isn’t any lower because of that.

Xu Qing reached up and rubbed his chest. The violet crystal was there. When he got his god clone back earlier, he had moved the violet crystal into his immortal body.

Looking one last time at the phoenix hall, he took a deep breath. As Patriarch Golden Vajra Warrior offered respectful farewells, Xu Qing took a step forward and vanished. When he reappeared, he was outside the Sageheaven Pagoda high in the sky. The god vine swirled. The golden rat bowed its head. As Xu Qing landed on the pagoda, he looked down at Sea-Sealing County....

A few breaths of time passed. Eyes flashing with decisiveness, he stepped into the pagoda. It rumbled loudly then turned into a beam of light that shot over the horizon and toward... the outer sea!

“Back when we met that old man in the outer sea, he said that the place had a name. The Primeval Sea. It’s a fantastic thing. Any location where it exists is a strategic spot and a prosperous place. And that’s because the Primeval Sea connects all of the star rings in the universe.

“In other words, the outer sea is actually a passageway leading to other star rings. The part of the Primeval Sea in which the Ninth Star Ring lays is special. It’s been sealed. And you can only get out of it through special rifts. He also said that you need the cultivation base of a Summer Immortal to make the journey.”

As the pagoda sped toward the outer sea, Xu Qing sat cross-legged inside. He pulled out a white scale. It was actually a command medallion. Back when he left the Summer Immortal Palace, he had given up his spot in exchange for this travel medallion, which would allow him to travel the Primeval Sea. With it, he could go to other star rings even though he wasn’t a Summer Immortal. The process would still be very dangerous. It was a very special medallion. It was so special, in fact, that the palace lord only had three of them.

Xu Qing looked at it, then looked up. In his mind’s eye, he could see that old man, and could hear the last words he had spoken.

“That’s a world controlled by humans, and it’s also a world of immortals.”

It was the Fifth Star Ring, and it was also called... the Immortal Capital. Xu Qing took a deep breath. Putting the medallion away, he closed his eyes and started meditating.

In that manner, time passed.

Four hours later, the Sageheaven pagoda sped through the sky over the Forbidden Sea. The border between the inner sea and the outer sea... was getting closer and closer. Even as the pagoda sped along at top speed, a flirtatious peal of laughter reached his ears from outside.

“So, your primal yang is back, you naughty little boy.”

In a location not very far from the border of the inner sea, the Sageheaven Pagoda had lurched to a halt as it flew through the sky.

Huge waves were surging out from one specific point, like a tsunami, as a statue that seemed as tall as the sky itself rose up from the water. The statue shone with dazzling golden light.

This was an actual god. The god towered over the ocean with such immense height that Xu Qing’s pagoda looked like a tiny toy in comparison. Astonishingly, the statue looked like a fox. It was not made of clay, but rather, hard stone that was as red as flame. The fox actually looked very realistic. What was more, shē didn’t pulse with the godfire of a Flawless God like before. No, this was the power of... an Altar God!!

It was an unknown star ring. An unknown world.

The lands were yellow and dry, covered with a spider web of crevices in all directions. The sky was pitch black. However, there were three eyeballs up above, staring down malevolently at the lands below.

There wasn’t much light in the world. There were just the three eyeballs like moons, sending out faint light. The place was hazy and deathly silent.

Xu Qing looked away from the frescoes and the legends. It seemed to him that the legend of the world could very well just be an excuse to make it easier to harvest life force.

That said, at least I have some clues to work with now.

He vanished from the shrine hall and appeared atop the mountain. Expression placid, he sat down cross-legged to continue working on his injuries. At the same time, he waited for the ninth eyeball to appear. He was quite certain that once the ninth eyeball was there, he would be able to see this world much more clearly.

1. The situation with the human nature, godly nature, and animal nature started in chapter 619. ☜

2. The lifespan flower as the anchor was in chapter 622. ☜

3. The Chinese characters I’m rendering as ‘eyeballs’ are actually the common ones normally translated as simply ‘eye.’ However, I want to differentiate them from Seven Blood Eyes. In reality, Seven Blood ‘Eyes’ would most accurately be rendered Seven Blood ‘Pupils.’ In the end, I went with ‘eyes’ as my translation choice because A) it sounds better, B) the sect was described as having seven literal eyes on the mountains (not just pupils), and C) I had no idea that something like 1,000 chapters later in a chapter the author hadn’t written at that point, there would be another situation with a specific number of blood-colored eyes. There is not supposed to be an obvious linguistic connection between them. Incidentally, the text does not make it clear what exactly they look like. Do they look like literal spherical eyeballs, or do they look like an eye drawn on a piece of paper? We don’t know. It could go either way, and the text never makes it clear. And in the end, there is not supposed to be a connection between Seven Blood Eyes and the eyeballs in this chapter. ☜

4. Another linguistic note here. There are different words that can be translated as hero. For example, the “xia” character from wuxia/xianxia is sometimes rendered as hero, and that “xia’ character is sometimes used as a form of address in wuxia/xianxia. The term in this chapter, however, is not ‘xia.’ It’s the most literal and common word for hero, the very same one that is used in the term “superhero” in Chinese. This isn’t particularly relevant, but since many of you are familiar with how ‘xia’ and ‘hero’ are used in these novels, I figured I would elaborate a bit. If I was reading a translation, I would be wondering which version was being used.... ☜

Looking up at the eight eyeballs and the blood-red light they emitted, Xu Qing thought, Based on what I’ve seen over the past few days, I can tell that days on this world are thirty-four hours long. That’s a bit longer than Revered Ancient. And that means that it’ll be another eight hours before the ninth eyeball appears. While I’m waiting....

Xu Qing closed his eyes to assess his current cultivation base and battle prowess. He had been very familiar with his god clone, including its godly authority and other assets.

When going into battle like that, I could turn into a real killing machine. As for this immortal body....

Truth be told, he had not yet had a chance to have a real fight with this body.

When he fought Grand Emperor Netherflame, he had been working with his Eldest Brother to simply contain the enemy, and he had not used any divine abilities or magical techniques. Therefore, Xu Qing felt that his priority as he waited was to make sure all his magical techniques were in order and ready to use.

This immortal body cultivates the Ten Extreme Daos. However, because I’ve only reached the level of nine in both Spirit Trove and Void Returning, my current limit is nine extreme daos.

They start with the five elements of metal, wood, water, fire, and earth. Those serve as the foundation, and are also natural laws that govern the operation of heaven and earth. By using my five yin organs as the basis, I can use my own body to perform the cycles, as opposed to using heaven and earth as the origin. Because of that... my battle prowess is not limited by any specific location or world. In other words, I can use the power of the five elements anywhere I go.

Xu Qing lifted his hand and then stretched his fingers out and looked at them. A metal-type power gathered in his palm. When it reached an extreme level, Xu Qing’s eyes gleamed.

The dao of extreme metal will allow me to control any type of metal in heaven and earth. It’s not a specific magical technique, but rather, will rely on quick thinking to be beneficial. The same thing applies to wood, water, fire, and earth.

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. With the dao of the five elements, all bits of wood around him could be pieced together based on his thoughts.

Theoretically speaking, the only limit to this five elements power is my own imagination. In other words, if I want divine abilities for the dao of five elements, I need to seek enlightenment about how to create them. Most importantly... any individual element can make a divine ability. Or, they can all be combined into a divine ability.

After experimenting briefly with each of the five elements, a thoughtful look appeared on his face.

Now, let’s deal with Little Shadow. Little Shadow does not suffer from any limitations because of the switch between god clone and immortal body.

Xu Qing waved his hand, and his shadow stretched out in all directions, ultimately covering the entire mountain. At that point, Xu Qing was able to see Little Shadow’s true form. It was a huge tree with a coffin hanging down from it, covered with numerous eyes. It pulsed with ingratiating emotional fluctuations.

And then there’s The Emperor’s Sword.

The Emperor’s Sword was part of immortal cultivation, so naturally speaking, it couldn’t stay inside a god clone long-term. Therefore, Xu Qing had extracted it and put it into his immortal body. Upon sensing the sword within him, he recalled the various sword stances Grand Emperor Swordsage had demonstrated.

Earth Treasury. Rending the Void. Heavenly Palaces. Star Splendor... The Human World.

Xu Qing spent some time mentally reviewing the five sword techniques before moving on.

Beyond all that, my magical techniques include Golden Crow Assimilates Myriad Spirits as well as my immortal skills.

A black spark appeared on Xu Qing’s forehead, which turned into a golden crow. Black fire spread all around him, which he could control and bolster with the dao of extreme fire. As the golden crow’s many tails spread, Xu Qing sensed something like a cheer coming from it.

After some contemplation, Xu Qing went on to the immortal skills. Immortal skills were a type of forbidden magic, and Xu Qing’s control was limited. He had Six Thieves Deceive Life and Five Dogs Cleave Immortals. The former had two dao lineaments, while the latter would require some personal enlightenment.

I can still use them.

His eyes shone with mysterious light as his authority of erasure formed.

Then I have my magical treasures....

He waved his hand, and three beams of light shot out. Three magical treasures. The first was a needle that could stitch karma. The second was a pair of shears that could sever perception. The third was a shield that could be used for defense. The first two came from the Vivifiends, while the last was something he had acquired in the Devilbird holy land. [1]

As for trump cards....

His eyes glittered

Fishing the Moon in the Well represents the dao of extreme space. That’s the first. My life essence sundials can influence the timescape, and they represent the dao of extreme time. That’s the second. And I have one more, assuming I can assemble it with the five elements. And that’s the God Decapitation Altar! Or I guess the most accurate way to say it would be a five elements God Decapitation Altar![2]

And finally...

He took a deep breath, and his expression became more serious.

The dao of extreme space and the dao of extreme time both have individual transformations.

He thought back to what he had seen when he opened his eyes in the vortex passageway.

Space was infinitely big and infinitely small. Time was infinitely long and infinitely short.

Xu Qing’s brow tightened into a frown, but soon relaxed. He knew that he needed enlightenment of additional factors before he could do anything like that with his immortal body. In fact, study and training was why he had chosen to travel to the Immortal Capital in the Fifth Star Ring to begin with.

There’s no reason to get anxious.

Calming his heart and mind, he closed his eyes to seek enlightenment. And thus, eight hours ticked by. At that point, ripples flowed through the dome of heaven, accompanied by thunderous rumblings.

All living beings were shaken to the core and instinctively looked up. High in the sky... a ninth eyeball had appeared. The moment it was there, the entire sky turned crimson! The gloomy world was stained with red, until everything... was the color of blood. A terrifying aura descended from above, becoming a dreadful tempest that covered anything and everything.

Along with it came the sound of murmuring, which were the voices of the heavenly daos speaking into the ears of all living beings. It became like thunder.

Then, all people in the world, be they mortals or cultivators, regardless of whether they were in villages or cities, or even out in the wilderness... all prostrated toward the dome of heaven. Regardless of what their facial expressions had been before, the murmuring caused them to look fanatical. And regardless of how emaciated they were or how withered their life force was, they didn’t hesitate to sacrifice some of themselves.

It was the same with children and the elderly. Everyone participated. Because of the willing sacrifice, the life force became streams of white smoke that rose up into the air toward the nine blood-colored eyeballs.

The eyeballs absorbed it!

As Xu Qing coldly observed things play out, he circulated his cultivation base, tapped into his five yin organs, and activated his seven major worlds. Spirit power flowed into his eyes.

That was when he could see that he wasn’t looking at nine eyeballs! Astonishingly, there were nine spell formations. And within each spell formation was a skeletal corpse seated cross-legged.

They still have life force. They’re not dead.

Xu Qing studied the nine corpses; he could tell from their facial features that they weren’t species from this world. They were human!

They’re all wearing the same clothes, too. Are they from the same organization? How were they injured?

As Xu Qing watched, the life force from the world converged on the nine corpses. However, after that, it came out of the tops of their heads and drifted off to a distant location that Xu Qing couldn’t see....

They’re not injured. They’re actually filtering out impurities!

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. Around then, a faint aura of awakening appeared on Xu Qing’s shoulder. Next, Starfire slowly transformed from a clay fox statue back into a flesh-and-blood form.

When shē opened hēr eyes, shē grumbled, “Where the hell are we, boy? Which star ring did we end up in? Why does this place suppress gods so strongly? It’s terrifying.... In fact, it rejects all forms of godly power! I could barely wake myself up.”

When Xu Qing didn’t answer, shē opened hēr eyes and looked at the lands below. Hēr pupils constricted.

“There’s a Flawless God sealed underground!” Shē studied the surrounding world, then noticed the nine eyeballs in the dome of heaven. Shē gasped. “It’s a god-assimilating spell formation!”

“Senior,” Xu Qing said, “I did make it clear that I was going to a place that doesn’t welcome gods.”

Starfire shrank in on hērself and weakly said, “The force of suppression on me is too strong. This isn’t a matter of ‘not welcoming’ gods.... This is a minor world set up specifically to assimilate a god. It’s extracting power from the god below to nourish the living beings here. But that’s only the first level of filtration. Next, the living beings send their life force to those nine cultivators. That’s the second level of filtration.

“After those two levels, an incomparably pure power is sent out for someone else to absorb. Very ruthless. In fact, this is even more ruthless than your Revered Ancient. I wonder who set this up. And how many formations like this are there....”

Starfire was clearly afraid of this place. After some thought, shē transformed into an earring on Xu Qing’s ear.

“This should be safer,” shē whispered. Then a tongue emerged from the earring and licked Xu Qing’s ear. Shē could sense the energy of his primal yang. That seemed to placate hēr a bit.

It felt a bit unsettling to Xu Qing, but considering the state Starfire was in, he didn’t stop hēr. He looked back up at the nine eyeballs in the dome of heaven.

“I don’t think they’ve sensed you,” Starfire said dully. “Are you just going to leave this place?”

Xu Qing shook his head. “It would be simple to break free. But there are likely more levels of defense outside. I’m still not fully recovered. What’s more, considering I don’t know the full story, I don’t want to do anything until I’m back at my peak.”

He had always been the type of person who remained unflustered. And he was extremely patient. He had been like that as a child, and that hadn’t changed after he joined Seven Blood Eyes. He was in an unfamiliar place, and therefore his best options were either to do nothing, or to wait until he was confident about what would happen if he did do something.

“Fine,” Starfire said. “I won’t do anything to help you for now. The pressure is too immense. I need to sleep a bit to get used to it.”

Starfire seemed very listless, and at the same time, helpless. All shē could do was grumble to hērself about the risk shē had taken to come to a hellish place like this for some primal yang.

Xu Qing just nodded and continued to observe what was happening.

And thus, the night passed.

The living beings in this world made this same sacrifice whenever the nine eyeballs came out. When the day dawned, the sacrifice was over, and all of them were in an extremely weak state. That said, the nine eyeballs didn’t absorb too much life force. They left some behind. That ensured that there was always some hope in the world, and people didn’t descend into true despair.

Up above, eight of the eyeballs were no longer visible. There was only one there.

In the following days, Xu Qing remained seated cross-legged atop the mountain. By the time a fourth eyeball was visible above, the injuries he had sustained in the Primeval Sea vortex were fully recovered. He was back at his peak.

He didn’t waste any time. For the next few days, he sought enlightenment about how to combine the dao of the five elements with the God Decapitation Altar. He also spent some time thinking about his experiences with space and time in the vortex passageway. He was becoming increasingly convinced that what he had experienced with space and time in the vortex were going to be crucial in confirming the dao he was personally searching for.

Time passed.

The world grew increasingly crimson as the ninth day came. The ninth terrifying eyeball slowly appeared in the canopy of heaven. Blood-colored light spread as the living beings began to offer their sacrifice.

Xu Qing stood.

“It’s time to leave,” he said calmly, and he stepped up into the sky!

The sky trembled. Lightning snaked out beneath his feet in all directions. Each step he took seemed to shake the entire world, and the brilliance of the spreading lightning vied with heaven itself!

The nine eyeballs suddenly stopped absorbing the life force energy. And then, as they sensed Xu Qing, they swiveled to face him!

The pupils of the nine enormous blood-colored eyeballs constricted. Inside the eyeballs were the nine corpses seated cross-legged, who were absorbing the spirit energy from the living beings below. All of them trembled.

Clearly, Xu Qing’s arrival was a complete shock. He had not been noticed before the moment he revealed himself. That was a very significant fact, and it was clearly shocking to the nine corpse-like cultivators.

“Excuse me,” Xu Qing said calmly. “I’d like to leave this place. Do you mind letting me through?”

Obviously, the ideal outcome would be to leave without having to make a scene.

Unfortunately, his words had a very different result than intended. The nine blood-red eyeballs emanated intense hostility. The nine cultivators within them didn’t know where this person came from or how he had entered this minor world controlled by their clan. But it didn’t matter. They simply couldn’t permit mishaps in this place. Killing intent surged within them, and they immediately sent messages to the outside.

Sadly for them... Xu Qing had prepared well before revealing himself, and it was a given he was ready in all respects. He knew that these nine eyeballs were strange, but getting past them wouldn’t be difficult. What was more, defeating the nine cultivators wouldn’t pose a challenge.

The main concern would be to make sure no one from the outside interfered when he was killing them. Xu Qing was confident that, given how this minor world was set up, there was likely some sort of guardian on the outside. If someone like that interfered when he was trying to leave, it could lead to a tricky situation. Therefore, the best option was to try to get out quickly and smoothly to ensure that the outside guardian didn’t notice what was happening.

As he strode up into the sky, he waved his right hand, causing a huge pair of shears to appear high in heaven above the nine eyeballs. The shears were so massive they filled the sky, and their arrival caused the aura of a Grand Emperor’s treasure to rage like a tempest. These were the shears that could sever all dao lineaments and karma.

They snapped shut.

They made no sound. And yet, all living beings, including the nine cultivators in the eyeballs, heard a cracking sound deep in their souls. At that moment, all information the cultivators were transmitting to the outside world was severed!

But things weren’t over yet. Next, the Grand Emperor’s needle glittered as it stitched the karma that had just been severed so that everything looked just as it had looked to Xu Qing nine days before.

Because of that... no information could leave this place. No fluctuations would emerge from it. In most respects, it was now completely invisible and independent. The Grand Emperor’s needle improved the concealment effect. Unless an outside force sent divine will into this world, then they would have no way of knowing that anything unusual was happening.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered with cold light. “Since you refuse to talk, then I guess....”

He took a final step, which caused the dome of heaven to tremble. Lightning converged beneath his feet, becoming like countless red snakes that shot toward the nine eyeballs.

The eyeballs shivered and glowed with red light. Within them, the nine cultivators quickly lifted their hands, their expressions very serious. They could sense that they were dealing with two extraordinary Grand Emperor treasures, and they also knew they were now cut off from the outside. Starting to feel despondent, they performed incantation gestures.

The nine eyeballs glowed with even more intense red light, and they pulsed with an astonishing defensive spell formation power. At the same time, the bodies of the nine cultivators began to transform from their withered state. Using the life force power they had absorbed, they began to recover from their previous state. They knew that they had to fight in the face of this sudden threat, or else they would end up dead.

Xu Qing’s face was completely expressionless. He didn’t care what cultivation base these people had. As long as they weren’t Imperial Sovereigns, it didn’t matter if they woke up completely.

I suppose this is the perfect opportunity to test out this immortal body.

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. Lifting his right hand, he pointed at the first eyeball.

The power of metal built within his lungs. He inhaled, then exhaled sharply, causing his breath to fill the entire minor world. It affected all metal in the world, including all weapons. In the blink of an eye, the world started trembling.... An instant later, all five elements metals in the world were replaced!

Xu Qing’s extreme metal power became a dao of this world! He could sense that, with a mere thought, he could control every metallic thing in the world. His eyes glittered....

All of the five elements metals in the world erupted, gathering together in the sky in a flowing stream. It turned into a gigantic finger made of metal.

The finger hit the first eyeball. The moment it did, the spell formation went wild, sending out incredible power to defend the eyeball. But the formation ended up being completely useless. It shattered, and the awakening cultivator inside the eyeball... had no chance of escaping. Rumbling sounds echoed out as the eyeball collapsed and fell out of the sky. The cultivator within it screamed as the power of metal killed him in body and soul!

The cultivators in the other eight eyeballs were visibly astonished, but quickly went all out to try to get back to their peak level.

So, this is the power of an extreme immortal?

At the moment in which Xu Qing had taken over the dao of metal in this world, he felt like he had become the embodiment of a heavenly dao.

Next, he said one thing.

“Wood.”

The power of wood from his liver swept out and filled the world. All vegetation in the world shivered, as did all wood-type cultivators and anything else related to wood. The world lost one of its daos!

A majestic finger made from the power of the dao of extreme wood formed in the air. It pulsed with intense life force and a boundless terror as it shot toward the second eyeball. All living beings shook at the sight of it. Another of the nine eyeballs fell.

Wild colors flashed in heaven and earth. Winds screamed. And then Xu Qing’s voice spoke like the flowing of the tide.

“Water.”

Water from Xu Qing’s kidneys replaced all five elements water in the world. It rose up into the sky and became rain, rivers, and seas. The foundation of all living beings. The world really was too small, and so, after taking the role of heavenly dao, Xu Qing could control all living beings.

“Fire.”

The sound of a heartbeat became like heavenly thunder. Fire raged, flickering in the eyes of all living beings. And finally...

“Earth.”

The lands of the minor world trembled, seemingly possessed of a will of their own as they shot toward the eyeballs in heaven backed by countless years of pent-up rage.

Three fingers rose into the sky. Three eyeballs collapsed! Three cultivators perished!

All the five elements power was under Xu Qing’s control, allowing him to take over and become a heavenly dao.

Meanwhile, the cultivators in the surviving four eyeballs had recovered, and were rising to their feet one after another. Under their control, the eyeballs shrank down and entered their foreheads, bolstering them. Instantly, their auras surged.

These were seven-world Smoldering Gods! Grim looks appeared in their eyes, all while fear simmered in their hearts. One of them then stepped forward.

“Sire, it matters not where you come from. There is only one way to leave this place. And that is to wait for us to leave. Once outside, we can open the way for you to leave this world.
