If you don’t trust us, then we can just send a single person. Considering the level of our cultivation, what’s the need for all this fighting and killing? What do you think, sire?”

The other three cultivators didn’t react with surprise to his words. Though none of them knew what this person was doing here, they could all tell that he had an astonishing background. Otherwise... he would have died just trying to get into their clan’s secret location. What was more, they weren’t confident at all in being able to overcome him, and didn’t want to throw their lives away. That was why they needed to get out as quickly as possible and contact the elder who controlled the secret location.

If the elder stepped in, this interloper would be killed beyond the shadow of a doubt. Thus, the three other cultivators nodded.

“Everything from before was a misunderstanding.”

“We reacted impulsively.”

Maintaining vigilance, the three of them slowly backed up.

Xu Qing looked at them and shook his head. He lifted his right hand. Heaven and earth trembled. The world shook. The five phases formed five heavenly dao fingers up above. And then that hand shot toward the four cultivators.

As their faces fell, their cultivation bases raged as they prepared to fight back. Unfortunately, those five fingers were heavenly daos made from the five elements of this world. They contained the will of the world itself, and since Xu Qing was pulsing with a killing will, it meant this was killing intent from heaven itself.

The storm raged with heaven-rending, earth-crushing power. It didn’t matter how the four cultivators struggled or fought back. It didn’t do any good. An instant later... agonized shrieks rang out.

The four cultivators had been smashed into a bloody pulp that fell down to the ground like red flowers.

“I prefer to trust myself only,” Xu Qing said calmly. Then he looked up at the dome of heaven and clenched his right hand into a fist.

An astonishing sword energy emerged from him, which turned into The Emperor’s Sword. He grasped it, then adjusted the five elements power, sending the might of this world’s heavenly daos into the sword. He slashed it at heaven.

Sword energy raged into the sky. Sword light filled the void. Sword will demolished space. In the blink of an eye, a huge furrow opened up as the dome of heaven was slashed open, revealing the heaven beyond. The beings living on this minor world felt like their minds were being hit by a hundred thousand lightning bolts. All of them just stared up at the sky and the rift there.

Most of them were shaken to the core. There was a heaven beyond heaven.

“Then where are we...?”

As countless people stood there in a daze, Xu Qing headed toward the rift.

The world shook as he reached it. He looked down at the minor world, then stepped out through the rift. He was in a strange place.

A massive dome stretched overhead, almost like a lid. There wasn’t even a scrap of the mutagen of gods. There was only plentiful spirit energy. The sky outside of the minor world was red, and it flowed like a river.

The surrounding lands consisted of a huge swamp. It looked like it had once been a huge body of water that was now almost completely dried up. Bubbles would occasionally surface, and when Xu Qing looked at them, he realized to his astonishment... that they were all minor worlds. And each of those minor worlds contained a suppressed god. This place was some sort of prison for gods!

Xu Qing struggled to control his breathing as he looked around at the countless minor worlds bobbing up and down. And from many of them, something like smoke rose up toward the middle of the sky. There was a vortex there sucking all the smoke away.

This place is a prison for gods... That means that the real world must be outside of this place.

His eyes glittered as he finally came to an understanding of where he was. He looked off into the distance. The moment he did, the aura of an Imperial Sovereign flared off in the distance. He heard a deafening screaming sound. An Imperial Sovereign was on the way.

Then a cold and desolate voice echoed out. “How amusing. I’ve been guarding my clan’s spirit mine for a long time, and at long last there’s been a jailbreak.”

“Spirit mine?” Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. He had considered it likely there would be a guardian. And he had even predicted that it could be an Imperial Sovereign. After all, this was most likely the Fifth Star Ring, and he was dealing with someone who could suppress a Flawless God.

But what did come as a surprise was the term used by the guardian to describe this place. Mines were usually places to gather resources. Based on Xu Qing’s understanding, spirit mines usually contained veins of spirit stone. But in this place... the resources were gods. The life force of gods was being absorbed by the living beings of a minor world, filtered of impurities, and then filtered by powerful cultivators....

The resulting spirit energy would be immeasurably pure. Given that perspective, it did seem proper to call this place a spirit mine.

Those other cultivators mentioned some sort of clan. So did this Imperial Sovereign. This place... must be part of a clan. If this clan has an Imperial Sovereign working as the guardian of a mine, then what kind of cultivation base does the clan patriarch have? And what standing does the clan have in the larger world here?

Xu Qing’s eyes were shining. He was now convinced he had made the right decision, and it seemed more likely than ever that he had reached the Fifth Star Ring.

However, given the fact I got here through the Primeval Sea, why did I end up in that minor world? Was there some circumstance or meddling that sent me there? Maybe I can get some answers from this Imperial Sovereign.

Xu Qing looked up at the figure screaming toward him from the horizon.

Imperial Sovereigns were strong, but Xu Qing had come prepared. He had trump cards that could kill an Imperial Sovereign. But as for this Imperial Sovereign....

I could probably kill him. But he won’t just stand there and let me do it. Therefore... if I need to kill him, I’ll have to get the timing just right. Ideally, though, I’d rather resolve this situation without fighting.

His eyes narrowed as the sound grew deafening, and ripples appeared in the dome covering this place. An instant later, the newcomer arrived with such incredible speed that it looked almost like an eye had opened in midair.

A figure stepped out of it and hovered there. It was a middle-aged cultivator with a wan face, menacing eyes, and a skinny frame that was anything but muscular. He wore a long black robe and was surrounded by swirling red energy that flowed like water and was horrendous in appearance. freewebnovel.com

Most astonishing was his aura. It caused wild colors to flash, and sent crushing pressure down everywhere. Thunderous rumbling filled the area which made him seem even more majestic. At the same time, sludge rose up from the swamp in all directions and floated in the air toward him. The cultivator almost seemed like a black hole that could drag everything in his direction.

Xu Qing even felt like his gaze was being tugged toward the man.

Even as Xu Qing caught sight of him, the man saw Xu Qing. Looking him up and down, he said, “You’re not one of the slaves that inhabits the spirit mine. Nor do you have the life force of a god. And there are no signs that anyone broke in here.”

He looked down at Xu Qing from above for a moment, and something strange occurred to him. Then he looked at the minor world Xu Qing had emerged from, and his eyes narrowed. Suppressing the killing intent in his heart, he growled, “Looks like you accidentally got into our spirit mine and then killed some of the slaves in charge of assimilating the gods. I can accept that. But I need to know who you are and what you’re doing here. And I need to know how you got in here!”

His voice contained a threatening pressure that filled the area.

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. Given the way this person had shown up, he was obviously very perceptive.

It’s clear he’s trying to decide what to do with me. Well... I might as well try to get some information as well. After a moment of thought, Xu Qing clasped hands and bowed.

“I am your humble servant Sir Firedark. And you’re right, it’s only because of a random accident that I ended up in your noble lands—”

“What kind of accident?” the man interrupted, his eyes gleaming.

Xu Qing frowned slightly but stayed calm. “I was exploring a spatial rift.”

The middle-aged cultivator laughed, and his eyes gleamed with strange light. “Exploring? I doubt that. The minor worlds of this spirit mine are separated from the major world outside, in a different spatial dimension. The chances of you accidentally getting inside by means of a spatial rift might as well be zero.

“Now, you have a seventh-level Smoldering God cultivation base, so it makes sense you could kill those slaves before they could power up. But what is less logical... is that you could slash open the sky of that world.... That’s something you don’t see very often. In fact, only a truly spectacular chosen could possibly accomplish it.”

The gleam in the cultivator’s eyes grew more intense. “But a chosen cultivator... couldn’t possibly be ignorant of the rules governing spirit mines. And a chosen would know that spirit mines are very sensitive locations. That’s why my original question involved your background.

“It seems to me that you don’t know what you’re talking about. Add in the fact that the aura of a foreign star ring still lingers on you, and my guess is... that you’re not a local cultivator, are you?”

Xu Qing’s face remained expressionless in the face of the cultivator’s words. Instead of saying anything, he waited to see if this Imperial Sovereign would keep talking.

“According to what I’ve heard...” the Imperial Sovereign went on, “before this place dried up into a swamp, it was called the Primeval Sea. And very occasionally, cultivators from other star rings will try to get here to the Fifth Star Ring by going through the Primeval Sea. That said, in order to do that, you need to have a Lower Immortal cultivation base.... Of course, occasionally you’ll run into chosen cultivators who use other ways to get here. But most chosen like that will come with a dao protector.”

The middle-aged cultivator chuckled and looked at Xu Qing with a flash of greed in his eyes. “And yet there you stand avoiding my questions. That just proves that you’re nervous. You don’t want to reveal who you really are. And that goes to show that you don’t have a dao protector....

“You’re a foreign cultivator from another star ring, aren’t you? You must have a lot of information about that other star ring in your head. Such information would be very valuable to me.”

The cultivator laughed loudly. Eyes shining with even greater intensity, he extended his right hand and pointed at Xu Qing. A huge finger made of natural and magical laws formed in midair. It couldn’t have been clearer to see, and even had fingerprints on it. As the finger grew larger and larger, so did the prints, becoming like huge valleys.

It overtook the dome of heaven, then began to rumble toward Xu Qing like Mount Tai itself. The aura of an Imperial Sovereign erupted everywhere, creating astonishing pressure.

Looking at the finger through narrowed eyes, Xu Qing backed up quickly. The fact that this cultivator had deduced so much from the handful of words Xu Qing had spoken indicated that he was very shrewd. At the same time, Xu Qing had learned a lot based on how the man had reacted.

For one thing, he had indeed reached the Fifth Star Ring. There had been no mistake in his journey. That had been his biggest concern. Everything made sense now that he had learned that the Primeval Sea here had dried up. Now it made sense how he had ended up in this spot.

What was more, the middle-aged cultivator had confirmed something else for him. And that was... there weren’t other powerful experts from this man’s clan in the area. In fact, it seemed possible that this location was a good distance away from the clan itself. That would explain why the man was so interested in whether or not Xu Qing had a dao protector.

If there were other powerful experts around, or if the spirit mine was located inside the clan, then that wouldn’t really matter. After all, given that this Imperial Sovereign was a spirit mine guardian, it indicated that the clan patriarch was much stronger.

Those thoughts flashed through Xu Qing’s mind, and he suddenly felt very confident. As the finger closed in, his eyes shone brightly, and the five elements erupted within him. It formed a resonance with the five elements in this god prison, and then he waved his hand.

The minor world he had slashed open rumbled, and the dao of the five elements from within it emerged through the rift he had slashed open. It combined with the five elements power from outside, and the heavenly dao hand formed again.

Just when the Imperial Sovereign’s finger was about to hit Xu Qing, the heavenly dao hand swept up from below and grabbed it. It jerked it upward. A huge boom rang out.

The Imperial Sovereign’s finger trembled violently when the five elements hand grabbed it. The magical laws within it fought back, and the natural laws resisted. A string of popping sounds rang out in all directions.

The Imperial Sovereign didn’t seem surprised. He had known from the beginning that Xu Qing was extraordinary. So he lifted his right hand, not to unleash another finger attack, but instead to perform an incantation gesture with five fingers. Then he pushed his hand toward Xu Qing. His five fingers transformed into nine worlds, and the nine worlds became nine devils.

The vicious devils all had different appearances. One carried a mountain on its back and had an enormous belly. One had two heads and carried a sea on its back. One shouldered a world and had a body covered with spikes. One was surrounded by a host of living beings, all screaming in anguish. The others were similarly bizarre. The nine devils all howled and rushed toward Xu Qing.

Xu Qing was surprised, and immediately halted his forward momentum and fell back. At the same time, he performed a double-handed incantation gesture, causing Six Thieves Deceive Life to appear, and stirring Five Dogs Cleave Immortals within himself.

He attacked, using something that came from the cultivation system back when Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity was in charge of the Revered Ancient mainland. He used... immortal skills!

Xu Qing had an immortal body and immortal skills. During his nine days of study in the minor world previously, he came to realize that they were now even more gruish and powerful. After all, Grand Emperor Immortal Skill had invented those terrifying abilities specifically for cultivators.

This time, instead of the six desires turning into projected emotions, they turned into a massive sea of six desires! That giant sea spread out, becoming a whirlpool that spun faster and faster. The six desires interacted, building on each other to erupt in full fashion.

If humans have desires, then devils have even more intense desires. In the blink of an eye, the nine huge devils trembled head to toe. As the sea of six desires flowed over them, Xu Qing unleashed Five Dogs Cleave Immortals.

A formless will entered the Imperial Sovereign’s sea of consciousness. It tampered with his memories, hiding inside, eluding his senses. And then a white hair appeared in his sea of consciousness, which turned into a vortex. The gate opened.

The greedy dog cleaves to a place.

All of this caused the Imperial Sovereign’s heart to start beating faster. He frowned. He had never seen any magical technique like this.

“Very interesting. Is this some special daoist magic from your star ring?”

Grand Emperor Immortal Skill had performed a very special service back when Ancient Emperor Dark Serenity conquered Revered Ancient. He created the immortal skills, which boosted the battle prowess of human cultivators and made them far more gruish and deadly.

There were no shortage of such immortal skills that could be considered outright brutal. There had been no other choice but to treat Dark Serenity’s enemies with complete ruthlessness.

However, after the war was over, the fact that immortal skills were harmful to natural harmony resulted in them being sealed away forever and not passed down by legacy. And for unknown reasons, Grand Emperor Immortal Skill disappeared into the sands of history. He became one of the only human Grand Emperors that later generations hardly knew about.

Later on, after the broken face and the gods arrived, many species left Revered Ancient to form the holy lands. Some of them took immortal skills with them and passed them down. The Immortal Skills Halls appeared which were centered on various immortal skills from Revered Ancient.

However, this was the first time the immortal skills had appeared in the Fifth Star Ring. As a result, it was no surprise that this Imperial Sovereign was shocked to the core by what was happening.

The sea of six desires that had swept over his nine devils, plus the vortex in his sea of consciousness, were all of utmost concern to him. Especially noteworthy was the latter, that sensation that there was something hidden in his memories. And then there was the vortex of white hair that turned into a gate, and pulsed with a sinister will. This indecipherable immortal skill was something he had no idea how to defend against.

An intense sensation of danger erupted in him like an unstoppable tide about to overwhelm him. In fact, he also felt like his memories would soon not belong to him. It was almost like his memories had become his own enemy.

As the critical moment approached, the Imperial Sovereign made a quick decision. Without any hesitation, he placed one hand on his forehead and the other at the pit of his stomach. He pushed down at the same time. Rumbling sounds echoed out as he tapped into his incredible cultivation base. The hand over his forehead affected his soul and his memories, causing the gruish transformations there to slow down. The hand over the pit of his stomach sealed his sea of consciousness, suppressing the eruption there.

Having accomplished those things, his eyes glittered with crimson light as he opened his mouth and inhaled. The nine devils that had been surrounded by the sea of six desires all howled as they collapsed, turning into streams of devil energy that flew back into the Imperial Sovereign’s mouth. He swallowed all of them.

Then thunderous booms erupted from inside of him as his previously skinny frame filled in with muscle, his wan face became ruddy, and he grew from ordinary height into a 300-meter-tall giant. His baleful aura raged, and devil flames spread out under his feet. An astonishing and berserk will pulsed out from within him.

By means of the baleful aura and the explosive energy in this body, he managed to viciously rip the invading immortal skills to shreds. This was one of the Imperial Sovereign’s trump cards, Baleful Devil Comes.

As cracking and ripping sounds echoed out, Xu Qing’s face turned grim. He could sense that his immortal skills had been destroyed, as had the memory he had implanted in the Imperial Sovereign.

Meanwhile, the Imperial Sovereign, who was in the form of a baleful devil, looked at Xu Qing with crimson eyes that burned with madness. He lunged forward.

Xu Qing had barely had a chance to feel the raging tempest and towering energy before his entire body was filled with stinging pain.

The Imperial Sovereign was so fast he became a series of afterimages as he launched a palm strike.

Xu Qing reacted with lightning speed. His cultivation base surged as he fell back as fast as he could move. Yet he was still affected by the palm, which caused tremors to pass through him and filled his flesh and bones with the feeling they were being ripped apart. Blood sprayed out of his mouth. freewebnovel.com

The power of an Imperial Sovereign was truly spectacular. In fact, any other Smoldering God wouldn’t just have felt like their bones were being ripped apart. They would have been killed in body and soul. However, he had the body of an extreme immortal, which was extraordinary in unique ways. Though he was injured, he was actually able to borrow some of the power of the palm strike to pick up speed and put some distance between himself and his opponent.

He didn’t flee, though. After gaining the distance, the Imperial Sovereign closed in with another attack. Xu Qing’s eyes glittered coldly. He lifted his right hand in the direction of the Imperial Sovereign, then lowered it.

Metal became a blade. Earth became an altar. Wood became a blade trough. Water became an axle. Fire became the killing force.

Xu Qing was using his own five elements to form a new God Decapitation Altar! And when his right hand dropped, the magnificent five elements God Decapitation Altar appeared in front of him, right in front of the Imperial Sovereign.

It surrounded him!

“Execute!” Xu Qing growled.

The energy fluctuations of the God Decapitation Altar sealed the opponent in all respects. The power of fire erupted and blade light glittered. The sharp blade fell.

A crack rang out!

The blade landed on the devil neck of the Imperial Sovereign. And yet, the God Decapitation Altar, which had never failed to date, simply couldn’t decapitate the Imperial Sovereign. It sliced about halfway through his neck before the power of the blow ran out, and it got stuck. Blood flowed out of the wound as the Imperial Sovereign howled in rage.

Then his body started splitting apart from itself as the nine huge devils came back out. The devils were partially transparent, almost like soul shadows. And they rushed toward the God Decapitation Altar, slammed into it, and exploded. Nine booms rang out. The God Decapitation Altar shook violently and, unable to stand up to the attack, crumbled into pieces.

Xu Qing reeled mentally. Blood sprayed out of his mouth as he backed up again.

Meanwhile, the devilish Imperial Sovereign, having lost his nine devils, now shrank back down into his previously skinny self. There was a gaping wound on his neck that gushed blood, although the wound was already closing up.

“Just what I would expect of a chosen. You have a seven-world Smoldering God cultivation base, but each of your magical techniques is more gruish than the one before it. You’re definitely strong.”

Though the words the man spoke seemed ordinary in nature, they caused Xu Qing’s heart to fill with a sensation of danger. All of a sudden, Xu Qing’s surroundings rippled as a host of spell formations appeared.

It started with 3,300 formations. Then 33,000. And then 330,000!

There were too many to simply count, and as they built up with astonishing speed, obfuscating the sky and enshrouding the land, they exerted crushing pressure onto Xu Qing. This was another of the Imperial Sovereign’s trump cards!

It was called 33 Taboo Formations.

The 33 in the name came from the way the technique worked. As long as 33 words were spoken beforehand, then all it took was a thought to unleash the technique.[1]

It was a devious divine ability that was hard to identify ahead of time unless you were familiar with it. Considering it was Xu Qing’s first time facing it, it would have been difficult to evade it. As the formations surrounded him, and a sense of danger filled him, his right eye glittered as a dao lineament appeared there.

The authority of erasure erupted! And it erased all formations he could see!

Though the formations were being erased in large numbers, they were still working, and Xu Qing was still trapped in place, surrounded by intense rumbling sounds and flashing light.

Seeing what was happening, the Imperial Sovereign coldly said, “So you finally used authority. I was beginning to think you didn’t have any.”

He had not underestimated Xu Qing at all, from the beginning of the fight until now. He knew full well that anyone who could travel alone from a foreign star ring would have trump cards to call on. And from this opponent’s cold manner, it had seemed highly likely that he had a trump card that could harm Imperial Sovereigns.

As the fight had played out, and he saw his opponent’s methods, he had kept his guard up even more. Now, after his opponent used the trump card of that decapitation altar, and he used his 33 Taboo Formations, he still wasn’t going to be careless. In fact, his eyes were glittering.

He wanted to force Xu Qing to use another trump card. As Xu Qing used his authority to get out of the formations, the Imperial Sovereign suddenly lifted his hand. He had produced a treasure.

It was a seed. The moment it appeared, the seed sprouted, and in the blink of an eye, it turned into a sapling, then a full-grown tree, and then a gigantic, hulking tree! It was 147 meters tall![2]

It was sparkling and translucent, like crystal. That was true even of its leaves, and as it glowed with ‘treasure light,’ it looked incomparably beautiful.[3]

Apparently, it had a gravitational force of its own. As that force covered the battlefield, all of Xu Qing’s energy, as well as all traces of his magical techniques, were sucked toward it by some unimaginable power.

Astonishingly, three sealing marks then appeared on the tree. The first was Xu Qing's heavenly dao hand of the five elements. The second was for immortal skills. The third was the God Decapitation Altar.

After the three marks appeared, they fused together to form the projection of a humanoid figure. The outline of that figure... was exactly the same as Xu Qing. Killing intent surged from within the projection, and that killing intent locked onto the real Xu Qing.

Even as Xu Qing used the authority of erasure on the spell formations, his mind and heart reeled.

“This treasure....”

The treasure not only had a gravitational force, it also created a projection that corresponded to him. The figure that looked like Xu Qing was struggling to get out of the tree, which was already starting to split apart to free it. Given the great level of danger, Xu Qing unhesitatingly spoke inwardly.

“Little Shadow.”

Instantly, the shadow beneath his feet surged outward, sending deep darkness out in all directions. Cackling laughter could be heard as a towering black tree rose up. The tree had black leaves and a black trunk, and there was something like a black coffin hanging from it. It also had countless eyes that were now fixed on the crystalline treasure tree.

“Still not using more authority, huh...?” the Imperial Sovereign said. He laughed coldly, and instead of closing in for an attack, he lifted his right hand and then shoved it down.

“Ghost gate: open! Heavenly fury: come!”

The movement of his hand caused heaven and earth to grow dark. A pitch-black door made of bones appeared out of nowhere. It was an ancient door that was obviously produced by means of a magical technique. Along with it came the sound of countless screams and howls from inside. A huge black claw then stretched out from inside. It grabbed the door frame, and an aura of death erupted, along with countless evil ghosts which swept out and swirled around the gate. Whatever terrifying entity that lurked inside was about to crawl out.

He had trapped Xu Qing with his 33 Taboo Formations. And then he was summoning a heavenly fury out of the ghost gate. But things weren’t over yet.

The Imperial Sovereign’s eyes glittered with the same cold light as before as he also took out a violet stick of incense.

“Let the life-locking incense burn, linking to your life. When the incense goes out, your life goes out!”

As the words left his mouth, the incense ignited.

Xu Qing instantly felt like he had been cursed, and that his life force was draining away.

“I forgot to tell you the reason I was selected to guard my clan’s spirit mine,” the Imperial Sovereign said coolly. “It’s not because I have a strong cultivation base. It’s because I live by the motto: never leave loose ends. Therefore, if you don’t have any more trump cards to pull out... then you’ve reached the end of the line!”

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. Even within all the spell formations, a piercing cry could be heard as a flower of black flames appeared. A golden crow flew out of it, rising into the sky, surrounded by an aura of death and the evil ghosts.

Next came three beams of light!

The first beam contained a shield that shot toward the ghost gate, growing larger and larger as it prepared to block the path of whatever was coming out. The second beam of light contained a huge pair of shears that pulsed with the aura of a Grand Emperor. And the shears chopped right toward the burning incense. Karma was severed! The third beam was a beam of sword light.[4]

It wasn’t Grandpa Ninth’s sword, but rather, Xu Qing’s Emperor’s Sword. The Emperor’s Sword could sever heaven and earth. It could smash innumerable formations. And as it gathered the power of the lands, he used the Earth Treasury stance as he shot toward the Imperial Sovereign.

“That sword. You have that sword...?” The Imperial Sovereign’s pupils constricted as he suddenly backed up, his heart racing. “A precious treasure of humankind!”

1. The last thing the Imperial Sovereign said before using the technique was a sentence with 33 words. It was 33 characters in Chinese, and I made sure to make the sentence 33 words long in English as well (remember that two words connected by a hyphen make a single word). ☜

2. I know some will wonder how many ‘zhang’ that is. It’s 49. However, that specific number isn’t relevant in any numerological sense as far as this technique goes, so I’ve just converted it into the real-world measurement. The number 49 actually does come up again shortly, but it’s in a different context, so I think that number was probably just in the author’s mind at the time. ☜

3. The ‘treasure light’ here is made up of two Chinese characters that would normally be rendered as something like ‘unusual brightness.’ But in this context, it’s a magical xianxia word similar to ‘sword light.’ By combining just about anything with the character for ‘light’ you will get a specific light associated with that thing, usually (but not always) something that can move about or has some inherent power of its own. Or at the very least, it’s unique type of light that comes from that specific thing. ☜

4. Chapter title explained: It’s not 100% clear even in Chinese, but the wording in the opening paragraphs of the next chapter make the title of this chapter much clearer. Basically, the first beam of light is the ‘treasure’ light, as the shield is a treasure. It doesn’t actually explain that in this chapter, although it’s sort of clear by context (the author plainly states it in the next chapter). In Chinese, shears (which could also be rendered as scissors), combines two characters. The first is “to cut (as with scissors, shears, or clippers)” and the second is “blade.” So though it doesn’t directly call it “blade light,” it’s obvious in Chinese that the “blade light” is coming from the shears. The third beam is outright called “sword light.” ☜

In a prison of gods in the Fifth Star Ring, divine abilities and magical techniques rumbled loudly.

In the distance, Little Shadow was in the form of a great tree that was currently twisted up around a crystalline treasure tree. The two of them were fighting back and forth, each hoping to suppress the other. Little Shadow had taken shape and was locked in combat with the figure that had come out of the treasure tree. Thunderous booms rang out constantly.

Further away, the authority of erasure eroded the 33 Taboo Formations. And within that area, Xu Qing’s shield, formed from treasure light, flew forth to seal the ghost gate in the dome of heaven. The shield came from Grand Emperor Netherflame. It contained the power of a black lotus, and erupted with netherworld flames that covered an area many times larger than the shield itself. When it hit the ghost gate, both objects shook violently.

Down below, the shears, formed of blade light, pulsed with a Grand Emperor’s aura as well as dazzling light as it viciously cut through the karma of the incense.

Finally... The Emperor’s Sword in Xu Qing’s hand radiated prismatic and dazzling light. Xu Qing himself shot forth with momentum to sever heaven and cleave the earth. It became a towering killing intent that was focused directly on the Imperial Sovereign. At that moment, Grand Emperor Swordsage’s words echoed in Xu Qing’s mind.

“I used Earth Treasury years ago to cut down a vicious killer who was proficient in the dao of earth. The sword move focused on the releasing earth energy to replace the will of the earth with the will of the sword. It takes earth energy and turns it into sword energy. Then it converges to make an earth sword!”

Xu Qing’s powers of understanding had long since struck astonishment into the heart of Master Seventh, as well as the hearts of the Heir Apparent and his siblings. Something similar was happening now. Only a moment before, he had gained enlightenment of Grand Emperor Swordsage’s first sword stance.

Xu Qing knew nothing about the Fifth Star Ring, and he was facing a very competent Imperial Sovereign. Therefore, he didn’t hesitate.

The Emperor’s Sword glittered as the power of Earth Treasury spread out, shaking everything. The surrounding swamp trembled, as did the minor worlds in the bubbles. Streams of energy began to rise up from the ground, and from the minor worlds. It wasn’t the nutrients being generated by the minor worlds. Instead, it was the earth energy being pulled out by Earth Treasury and turned into sword energy. More and more of it.

The swamp vibrated and the minor world bubbles began to tremble with increasing intensity. Countless streams of smoke headed in Xu Qing’s direction.

All of this takes a bit of time to describe but actually happened in the time it takes a spark to fly off of a piece of flint. At that moment, it looked like Xu Qing’s Emperor’s Sword gathered an infinitude of energy streams.

Together, they formed around him in the shape of an astonishingly large sword! He was in the middle of it! It was almost as if Xu Qing himself had become the sword! Sword might raged, shaking the sky, causing the lands to quake, and causing the swamp that was the god prison to seethe like the sea.

Shaken to the core, the Imperial Sovereign fell back at top speed. But then the sword of earth energy shot forward with heaven-shaking, earth-shattering power and indescribable quickness! It shot right toward the Imperial Sovereign! Nothing could stop it!

I want that sword technique! The Imperial Sovereign didn’t give voice to his thoughts. But as they filled his heart, and as his pupils constricted, he unhesitatingly summoned a vortex into his left eye.

A dao lineament appeared, and authority erupted! The first thing to happen was that a flowing river of red mist appeared outside of him. The river of mist was the manifestation of his authority. As the dao lineament stirred, the river swept out into the open.

An instant later...

Xu Qing could sense transformations to his surroundings. The air in front of him seemed to be resisting his movement, forcing him to slow down. Earth Treasury responded with increasing momentum, but... the force of resistance also increased in kind. In fact, it got so powerful that it became like a protective shield for the Imperial Sovereign. Not only did it slow Xu Qing down, but also, it opposed his sword energy.

If that were all there were to it, it might not matter much. But though the energy in the area formed a force of resistance against Xu Qing, it actually did the opposite for the Imperial Sovereign. It reduced the force of resistance against him, and reduced the energy flowing against him. In other words, Xu Qing was moving slower and slower due to this outside force, while the Imperial Sovereign was actually speeding up to an astonishing level.

In fact, he moved so fast that he was easily able to avoid the Earth Treasury sword move. In an instant, he was right next to Xu Qing, his eyes glittering with greed as he reached out to grab The Emperor’s Sword. He moved with outstanding accuracy, and craftily timed his action perfectly. He didn’t give Xu Qing any chance to make a counter move. He grabbed the sword!

Yet before a feeling of exultation could arise in his heart, the sword he had grabbed became illusory. In fact, the Xu Qing in front of him also turned illusory. The Imperial Sovereign’s face fell.

My perceptions have been altered?

Before the Imperial Sovereign had a chance to react, Xu Qing materialized in the distance, and Earth Treasury erupted.

A moment ago, he had used the perception altering abilities of the Heir Apparent. He had three chances to use that ability, and had just used one of them. The Imperial Sovereign’s perceptions might not have been as easily altered had it not been for his greed toward The Emperor’s Sword, and Xu Qing had taken advantage of that. That gave him the opportunity he needed.

Unfortunately, the time in which the perceptions were altered didn’t last long. What was more, this Imperial Sovereign’s authority was very unique. As a result, Xu Qing’s mind didn’t have enough time to rely on Earth Treasury to kill him. Even though he managed to use his trump card, Grandpa Ninth’s sword energy was telling Xu Qing that yet another unexpected twist might be just around the corner.

Unfortunately, he had no idea if his opponent had another trick up his sleeve, or another trump card to unleash. He needed to confirm whether or not he could create an opportunity to get some distance between himself and his opponent.

The reason was that he wanted to get in a fatal blow! He didn’t just want to seriously injure this opponent. Most importantly was that he couldn’t allow this person to escape.

Considering all of those things, he made a snap decision. The Emperor’s Sword erupted, but instead of targeting the Imperial Sovereign, he took advantage of the moment of opportunity he had created to use Earth Treasury to target the land itself! Put more precisely, he was targeting... the minor world bubbles!

He was dealing with a competent opponent, so the first thing he needed to do was distract him. Only if this opponent was distracted would it be possible to identify a way to launch a fatal blow on him. And the best way to distract a guard was to start destroying the thing he was supposed to be guarding.

That was why, though it seemed like this sword move had been targeting the Imperial Sovereign, his actual goal had been to target as many minor world bubbles as he could. Sword energy descended. Lands crumbled. And large numbers of minor world bubbles in the swamp were slashed.

One by one they split apart! The heavens in the minor worlds shattered. The cultivators filtering the energy had no time to wake up, and one after another, they were destroyed in body and soul. Without skies in their worlds, the living beings there awoke as if from dreams. Meanwhile, the gods imprisoned in the worlds were thrown into great chaos.

And of course, the absorption of spirit energy decreased dramatically. The vortex in the sky that was sucking in the spirit energy was instantly affected.

“How dare you!!” shouted the Imperial Sovereign. Face falling, he instinctively looked up at the vortex, his heart filling with trepidation. No matter how much he wanted to, he just wasn’t fast enough to stop Xu Qing. Something that normally wouldn’t have been possible with him here was happening, and all of it was because of that sudden change to his perceptions moments ago.

The spirit mine was collapsing. The vortex was taking in far less spirit energy. And his heart was starting to pound. Seeing what was happening to the mine he was in charge of guarding caused killing intent to explode within him. He howled, and the dao lineament in his eye stirred again.

His dao lineament was unique and terrifyingly powerful. However, it hindered the cultivation, and every time it was used, there was a cost. What was more, if you used it on a large scale... that cost was terrifying. Therefore, it wasn’t something he would even consider outside of extreme circumstances. Right now, he was out of options.

He lifted his right hand and then pushed it down toward the ground. Authority power surged, forming a force of resistance, which became defenses for him as well as a crushing force. It covered the entire crumbling spirit mine, causing the crumbling to slow down significantly. As a result, his skinny frame became even more emaciated, and his eyes shone with cold light.

Unfortunately, he didn’t dare to do much further. His authority couldn’t be used on the spirit mine for much longer. He needed to end the fight quickly and fix the minor worlds. If the vortex above was affected for much longer, he would face severe consequences.

Gritting his teeth, he ignored the cost he would have to pay to use his authority and pointed at Xu Qing. Authority erupted once again.

A tremor passed through Xu Qing, and he suddenly felt like he was being suffocated. The surrounding spirit energy, the air... and all gasses and energies were being extracted and turned into a powerful pressure that crushed down onto him. Shocking and ugly red bumps appeared all over him. He suddenly felt like he was going to be ripped to pieces. Yet he didn’t look flustered.

The opportunity I’ve been waiting for is almost here.

Xu Qing looked at the Imperial Sovereign, then suddenly extended his right hand. Within him, the dao of extreme space stirred.

During his days in that minor world, Xu Qing had contemplated his memories of what happened in the Primeval Sea passageway, including the operations of space. Others who experienced the same thing might not have gained much enlightenment. But to someone who already had the power of space within them, the scenes in that vortex were akin to a wise Master imparting a daoist magic. They told him how space could be manipulated.

An instant later, as Xu Qing’s dao of extreme space was unleashed, the area around him distorted wildly, as if they were being stretched out infinitely.

Next came cutting and isolation!

He cut out space and isolated authority. And as a result, the area for about 30 meters around him became a border. And then an irregular shape appeared in front of Xu Qing, like a section of a grid. That grid piece was unique and independent, and it was under the control of Xu Qing’s dao of extreme space.

More grid pieces appeared, all connected to each other, until there were a hundred of them, all reflecting Xu Qing, who was in the middle. All energy was being absorbed... but each of the hundred grid pieces was essentially an additional world.

Things had turned around. Xu Qing looked up at the Imperial Sovereign.

“Your authority of energy can rip things apart,” he said calmly. “But no amount of ripping can compare to the detonation of space itself.”

A sound like shattering glass rang out in all directions. The one hundred grid pieces shattered, and a spatial tempest picked them up and sent them swirling around Xu Qing. Some of them swept out in all directions, negating the Imperial Sovereign’s attempts to save the spirit mine.

Even as he raged in fury, the rest of the fragments shot toward him. The dao lineament in his eye shone with greater brightness.

“I can’t believe it! That’s the dao of space!”

Shaken, he lifted his right hand and pointed toward the dome of heaven. Suddenly, warmth and coolness appeared at the same time everywhere. The interaction between warmth and coolness then created a huge wind. Thunderous rumbling sounds built on each other, until it was like heavenly might. It slammed into the spatial tempest. A deafening boom swept out in all directions.

Heaven and earth were thrown into chaos. The spatial explosion and the heavenly might created absolute chaos. Everything blurred. Within that blurriness, the wind screamed.

Blood oozed out of the corners of the Imperial Sovereign’s mouth. After unleashing the dao lineament of his authority, the time was approaching in which he would have to pay the cost. However, the killing intent in his eyes had not diminished.

The huge wind was causing trouble for Xu Qing as well. His flesh was being peeled off him, and blood was spraying everywhere. But his gaze was as sharp as ever.

At the critical moment, his dao of extreme time erupted. As the power of time surged, a majestic sundial locked onto the Imperial Sovereign. Time turned, and the moment in which blood began oozing out of his mouth was frozen in place!

Killing intent surged in Xu Qing’s eyes. He had found the moment to launch his fatal blow. He lifted his hand, and the power of Fishing the Moon in the Well rose.

The dome of heaven became the surface of a well. The world became rippling water. The Imperial Sovereign stood on the water, with all of his magical techniques reflected below him.

The sundial locked onto his body. The well locked down his soul. He was thrown into the exact mental chaos that Xu Qing had wanted to create within him....

This was the moment Xu Qing had been waiting for!

A heaven-shaking, earth-shattering sword energy erupted. It was Grandpa Ninth’s sword energy, and it could kill Imperial Sovereigns. A sword appeared that caused the sky to dim and the lands to quake. All of the swords in the various minor worlds of this god prison began to tremble in resonance.

Then they shot out of their respective worlds, swarming forth to merge into Grandpa Ninth’s sword energy, causing its majesty to increase.

Power was building. And the killing force was building too. After only a few breaths of time passed, a killing intent filled the world, something in which the sword was paramount.

It slashed toward the Imperial Sovereign. Heaven fell. The sword fell. Killing intent fell. Something intense and domineering replaced all of the Imperial Sovereign’s senses.

It was inescapable. It was unavoidable. It was unstoppable! Sword energy fell. Body and soul were shattered. He was killed in every respect!

One fatal blow!!

In some unknown location in the Fifth Star Ring, there was a spirit mine where a huge lid covered the sky, cutting the place off from the outside. It also prevented any fluctuations inside from being detected.

The swamp inside was full of craters, which had been created during the battle between Xu Qing and the Imperial Sovereign. In addition, there were innumerable minor world bubbles that had been blasted open.

Xu Qing hovered in midair, his face pale, his body covered in bloody wounds. He wasn’t paying attention to any of that, though. He was looking at the decapitated body of the Imperial Sovereign. He quickly performed a one-handed incantation gesture, all while keeping his guard up in case something else happened. If anything even slightly unusual occurred, he would unleash another sword attack.

He kept watching until the Imperial Sovereign’s energy was gone and his corpse started fading away. Only when it was clear that he had been completely wiped out of existence did Xu Qing start to feel more at ease.

It had not been an easy fight. Perhaps it was because he was in a different star ring where things were different than where he had grown up. Regardless, Xu Qing was fairly certain after what he had experienced in this fight that the Imperial Sovereign he had just killed was stronger than the Imperial Sovereigns from the holy lands.

I can think of three reasons. First, the guy I just fought is special in some way. Two, the Fifth Star Ring is a much more dangerous place than I expected, and thus, all Imperial Sovereigns are more complicated than I’m used to. Three, the Imperial Sovereigns from the holy lands lived comfortable lives and didn’t have a lot of fighting experience.

Xu Qing really had no idea of precisely how different the Fifth Star Ring was, or what unknowns he would be facing. However, his eyes remained calm. And thanks to the fight, the baleful aura on him had grown stronger.

Hovering in midair, he looked around before fixing his gaze on the spot where the Imperial Sovereign’s corpse had disappeared. There was a bag of holding there.

Xu Qing grabbed it, then blurred into motion. When he came to a stop, he was at the spot where the shield had slammed into the ghost gate. It was a divine ability that had summoned the ghost gate, so after the Imperial Sovereign died, it crumbled into nothing. Looking around, he collected back his shield and then stepped over to where the incense stick was. The incense had only burned for a moment before his Grand Emperor’s shears severed its karma and extinguished it.

This thing seems pretty nice.

He waved his hand, and the incense stick flew over to him. He quickly erased any branding marks on it, then marked it for his own. Finally, he looked over at Little Shadow.

Little Shadow’s true form was still fighting it out with the crystalline treasure tree. Little Shadow had started out at a disadvantage. Without its gruish nature and regeneration abilities, it would long since have been killed. But after the Imperial Sovereign died, the crystalline treasure tree trembled and lost its supporting foundation. And that was when Little Shadow had started really fighting back. As rumbling booms echoed out, Xu Qing looked at the copy of himself within the treasure tree.

“You possess a bit of intelligence, don’t you?” he said coolly. “In that case... either you surrender or I wipe you out.”

In response to his words, Little Shadow trembled in excitement and transmitted some emotional fluctuations to lend some weight to Xu Qing’s threat.

The crystalline treasure tree shivered. The figure within it could sense how terrifying Xu Qing was, so after a moment of contemplation, it clasped hands and bowed to him. Then the figure disappeared. The crystalline treasure tree’s true form glittered with bright light a few times, then went dark. It made no further attacks.

Xu Qing reached out and made a grasping gesture. The treasure tree didn’t fight back. It flew toward Xu Qing and let him wipe out the old branding marks and claim it for his own.

Little Shadow returned to him looking extremely tired.

“You did very well,” Xu Qing said.

Little Shadow perked up. Praise from Xu Qing was incomparably meaningful to it, and it looked very happy. “Milord... I’m... useful....”

Xu Qing nodded. Then he looked at the crystalline treasure tree.

The tree was strong, especially when it came to how it could absorb the energy and divine abilities of enemies and use them to create a projection. Combined with the life-burning incense, which would force an opponent to use a similar technique, it could obviously count as a trump card.

I gained quite a bit from this battle. In addition to these two treasures....

He looked at the Imperial Sovereign’s bag of holding. Anticipation suddenly flickered within him.

Before checking the bag of holding, there’s a little matter I need to take care of.

He looked off into the distance and coolly said, “If you haven’t revealed yourself within three breaths of time, I’ll make sure you never do.”

His voice echoed through the spirit mine. After two breaths of time passed, the air above the swamp off in the distance rippled, and a figure emerged, changing from transparent to visible.

It was a young man with a very pale face. He looked terrified. Without any hesitation, he dropped to his knees and kowtowed to Xu Qing. Great beads of perspiration ran down his forehead, until it looked like he was raining sweat. He was the servant of the Imperial Sovereign that Xu Qing had just killed.

He was only in the Spirit Trove level. He had been very content to be the servant of an Imperial Sovereign. And at the beginning of the fight when Xu Qing had been seemingly hemmed in from all sides, he had been feeling quite derisive of him. But then things changed very quickly. The sight of the Imperial Sovereign dying left him stunned and unsure of what to do.

He didn’t dare to make a move, and had been hoping that the invisibility talisman the Imperial Sovereign had given him would keep him safe. He knew it was unlikely to keep him hidden, but had hoped that in the chaos of the moment, Xu Qing wouldn’t notice him. But the words spoken by Xu Qing caused him to tremble uncontrollably as he flopped down and kowtowed.

Xu Qing looked him up and down. He had no intention of killing him. In fact, after the fight that had just played out, Xu Qing got the feeling this person could come in handy. Looking away, he sent his divine will into the bag of holding. After scanning the insides, his eyebrows shot up. There was a lot of good stuff inside. freewebnovel.com

The glimmering spirit stones alone were enough to leave him feeling very pleased. There were enough to form a small mountain. It only took a moment for Xu Qing to realize that these spirit stones were different from the ones in Revered Ancient. Each and every one contained the power of natural laws. He took out one and examined it more closely.

Are these made by assimilating gods? Is that how they get the power of natural laws?

In addition, the bag of holding had something even more valuable than spirit stones. It had pieces of immortal jade. They formed something like a river of immortal energy that flowed within the bag of holding.

The sight of it left Xu Qing feeling stunned.

After examining it for a while, he realized that the immortal jade had even stronger natural laws than the spirit stones. In fact, the sensation he was getting reminded him a lot of the time he had first absorbed essence power. It was just weaker. But even that was shocking.

Given all this, it seems the Fifth Star Ring is definitely more complicated than I thought. And it seems this guy was really rich.

Over the years, Xu Qing had killed a lot of people and taken a lot of loot. This was the first time the contents of a bag of holding had been so shocking. His anticipation grew as his divine will went past the spirit stones and immortal jade and began to scan the other things inside the bag of holding.

Soon he found a huge collection of bottles that were full of medicinal pills. There were different levels of quality. Given the level of his dao of medicine, Xu Qing could assess many of them and tell how to use them. But some were outside of the realm of what he had studied.

Just this short inspection of the bag of holding left Xu Qing’s heart pounding. Next, he sent his divine will in further in the hopes of finding jade slips, ancient records, and magical treasures and items.

Sadly, although there were a few magical treasures, none were very powerful. That was understandable. Given the battle that had just played out, there was no doubt that the Imperial Sovereign would have pulled out any magical treasures that would have been useful. The incense and the crystalline treasure tree were examples.

However, there were still a handful of items that piqued his interest. For instance, he found a beast hide that glowed with black light, as well as a medallion. He pulled both of them out.

The beast hide was about the size of his palm, and with the black light it emitted were many symbols that flitted and flowed about as if they were alive. After examining the hide, he sent divine sense inside to examine the symbols. A moment later, his expression flickered.

“49 Taboo Formations!” he murmured.

There was no information about where the beast hide came from, but it did contain information about a collection of daoist magics called the 49 Taboo Formations!

Xu Qing immediately thought of the 33 Taboo Formations the Imperial Sovereign had used.

The 49 Taboo Formations could gather the power of the magical laws of heaven and earth to unleash a host of taboo formations. Some could unleash killing power, some could seal the enemy. All of them were extraordinary.

The downside was that every time you used it, you had to accumulate all of the formations in advance. The upside... was that to use it, all you had to do was say 49 words, and it would pop out in a way the enemy couldn’t defend against. As you gained enlightenment of the divine ability, and as you furthered your cultivation, the requirement of the number of spoken words reduced.

The dead Imperial Sovereign had cultivated the technique down to the level of 33. Based on the description in the beast hide, if you cultivated it to the highest level, you could unleash the taboo formations with only 2 spoken words. What was more, the speaking requirement wasn’t limited to the person using the technique. It would work even if the enemy spoke the words. The reason the final limit was two words was that the formations were split into yin and yang varieties, and the taboos were split into life and death varieties. They couldn’t be combined.

As Xu Qing held the beast hide, he thought back to how the Imperial Sovereign had used the taboo formations in their fight. All of a sudden, something occurred to him.

This is an interesting divine ability. It’s linked to certain words you speak. So what would happen if I cultivated the ability down to the point of two words? And what if it was my name? Then if someone said my name, and I exercised a thought, the taboo formations would burst out. That would make it... almost impossible to deal with.

After considering the matter, he decided that was within the realm of possibility. If he put the divine ability into his name, then it would really be difficult for anyone to defend against it. For example, if an enemy cursed him by name, then he could use the formations to defend himself. Or if someone who wished him harm asked who he was, he could say his name and instantly unleash the formations.

This would definitely be useful as a trump card!

His eyes shone brightly as he thought about the matter a bit more before putting the beast hide away. He definitely planned to put this technique into his cultivation routine in the future.

Next he looked at the medallion. It was a gruish medallion that pulsed with an intense, baleful aura. As it hovered in the air in front of him, it caused the surrounding temperature to drop. It was as bright red as fresh blood. The background of the medallion depicted an empty field, while in the foreground was an eye.

Looking at it, Xu Qing came to the conclusion that this was the most special item in the Imperial Sovereign’s bag of holding. He didn’t touch it. He just looked at it for a while. Then he suddenly turned to look at the young man prostrating off in the distance.

“Your life depends on how valuable you prove to be. Tell me what this thing is.”

The young man suppressed his dread to look up at the medallion. Voice trembling, he answered, “It’s an Immortal Capital permission medallion.”

Xu Qing’s expression remained unchanged. However, the words ‘Immortal Capital’ definitely attracted his attention. “Tell me more.”

The young man took a deep breath. Considering that this person had just killed his own lord and master, he didn’t dare to hide anything. This person obviously wanted more information about this star ring, and the young man didn’t dare to be too cautious in the moment. Therefore, he gave a very detailed and systematic explanation. In fact, in order to make sure his explanation of the Immortal Capital permission medallion made sense, he went into a history of the Fifth Star Ring itself.

Xu Qing listened carefully. He was glad to have more confirmation he was in the Fifth Star Ring, and that there was a place there called the Immortal Capital.

In the past, the Fifth Star Ring had been full of gods. But when the Immortal Capital rose up, they crushed the gods and wiped out everything related to them. In fact, under the leadership of the Immortal Paragon of the Immortal Capital, the entire starry sky was compacted, and the Immortal Capital came to exist in the very center of the Fifth Star Ring. From then on, the Immortal Capital was considered holy and divine.[1]

What was more, the entire universe surrounding the Immortal Capital was compacted, and it ceased to be something like a starry sky. Instead, it turned into land where cultivators could reside. As time passed, cultivators proliferated until the population reached an astonishing level. It was almost impossible to count how many clans and sects there were.

Because of that, all cultivators had the same dream. They all wanted to ascend to the Immortal Capital! Anyone who did would be like the carp who jumped over the dragon gate. Their identity and status would change forever after that.

The people from the Immortal Capital were the lords of the Fifth Star Ring. And only the Immortal Capital existed high above all else, isolated from the outside world.

“Everyone wants to ascend to the Immortal Capital,” the young man said. “And the only way to get there is by fighting for it!” When he spoke the words ‘Immortal Capital,’ his eyes shone with the light of longing. “There’s a reason I said you have to fight for it. Every so often, the Immortal Capital holds the Trial of the Hunt![2]

“In preparation, the Immortal Capital sends out 10,000 Immortal Capital permission medallions and lets the innumerable cultivators of the Fifth Star Ring fight over them. It’s quite a brutal affair, and the casualties involved are shocking. That’s because the people who hold the permission medallions only qualify to enter the competition. The final number who get to ascend differs each time. Sometimes it ends up being the top 1,000 in the competition, but other times only the first few hundred!

“Senior, what you’re holding right there is an Immortal Capital permission medallion!”

1. The characters I’m rendering as ‘Immortal Paragon’ come up in other Er Gen translations. Different translators have translated the term differently, which in the context seems fine, as they seem to me to mean different things in the different novels. In other words, this term does not seem to be a connection point of terminologies between the novels. If there turns out to be some connection later, I’ll explain with footnotes, but from what I can tell it’s a standalone term. More will come later about what it means. ☜

2. The characters I’m rendering Trial of the Hunt are basically exactly the same as those I rendered “the Great Hunt” back in the Firemoon Darkheaven part of the story. This does not seem to be intentional on the author’s part, and by that I mean, he does not intend for these two different events to be connected. I suppose it’s possible he’s trying to build a theme, but based on how things play out, I’m hesitant to believe that he intends them to be “the same thing.” To keep things clear, I’m giving this version a slightly different name. ☜

“Based on what I’ve heard,” the young man continued cautiously, “Imperial Sovereign Ling Feng got that medallion by offering a bunch of shockingly valuable treasures in compensation. Plus he called in a huge favor. That’s how he got his hands on it.

“My guess is that he planned to give it to someone else as a gift.... That’s why he kept it around but didn’t activate it. Otherwise, the medallion would have displayed his ghost mark on it after he died.”

He had explained everything he knew, and hadn’t left a single thing out. And he had made sure to keep all of his anger and hatred for Xu Qing buried deep where it couldn’t be seen. The young man knew that he was dealing with a person who would be able to detect the slightest bit of animosity or falsehood, and if that happened, the results would be horrible and permanent. As a result, he was exercising utmost caution.

Xu Qing hovered in midair listening to the young man’s explanation, all the while thinking about the ramifications. Finally, he looked at the permission medallion. There was clearly no sort of ‘ghost mark’ on it. He looked expressionlessly back at the young man.

“Continue,” he said calmly.

The young man was trembling in his heart. He wasn’t able to get the tiniest read on Xu Qing, which made him feel more than ever that his life was in danger. After racking his brains, he said, “Senior, to the cultivators of the Fifth Star Ring, that Immortal Capital permission medallion is something incredibly rare. However, while some people think that getting one is a blessing, other people think of them as being inauspicious.

“If you have the appropriate battle prowess, then you could use it to reach the highest heights. But if your battle prowess is lacking, then having that medallion... puts you half a step onto the path of death. For one thing, everyone who wants a medallion will be after you. But worse than that, other people with medallions will also want to take it from you.

“The Immortal Capital only announces the success criteria at the very end. And unless you can get into the top 100... then you are in a very uncertain place. And thus... there’s a lot of killing and robbing. After all, your rank is determined by how many medallions you collect. If you kill someone else with a medallion, then you get their medallion and any others they’ve collected.”

The young man stopped talking at that point, as he had explained everything he knew about the Immortal Capital permission medallions.

“That’s the only way to get into the Immortal Capital?” Xu Qing suddenly asked.

The young man respectfully replied, “There’s another way. That’s to further your cultivation to at least the Grand Emperor level. People outside of the Immortal Capital who are in the Grand Emperor level aren’t allowed to participate in the Trial of the Hunt.”

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. “Are you saying that outside of the Immortal Capital, the strongest cultivators in the Fifth Star Ring are Grand Emperors?”

The young man shook his head. “Not exactly. There are too many sects to count in the Fifth Star Ring. Same with clans. There is no shortage of Lower Immortals. The reason is that not all Lower Immortals who ascend to the Immortal Capital end up settling down there permanently.

“There are a lot of people in the Immortal Capital who end up getting appointed as heavenly inspectors on the outside. Some Lower Immortals like that are lone wolves, but most are the patriarchs of various sects and clans.”[1]

Xu Qing felt like he was finally starting to understand a bit more about how the Fifth Star Ring worked.

He had known from the beginning that the cultivators in the Fifth Star Ring were strong. But hearing the details was more than a bit shocking. After taking a moment to digest the new information, he looked at the young man.

“In other words, when it comes to the fighting and killing over the permission medallions... people like Grand Emperors and Lower Immortals can’t interfere?”

The young man immediately nodded. “The Immortal Capital has set rules prohibiting direct assistance. But as for indirect interference... well I heard that they tend to look the other way. Unfortunately, my level is too low for me to know the details.”

Xu Qing once again looked at the young man.

The young man shivered as a very foreboding sensation filled him, and he was about to start begging for his life.

Before he could, Xu Qing waved his hand, causing the young man to fly over to him. His hand clamped down onto the top of his head as he prepared to do a soulsearch to confirm all the information he had just been told.

The young man was now at the peak of anxiety, and could hardly breathe. He knew full well that he was just on the verge of dying. In the hopes of preventing his soul from being damaged during the soulsearch, though, he suppressed his fear, ceased any struggling, and allowed Xu Qing to search through his memories.

Afterward, Xu Qing looked thoughtful. Because of the great disparity in cultivation bases, the fact that the young man had not struggled ensured that the soulsearch went very smoothly. And the injuries the young man had sustained were not outside of the realm of what he could endure.

Xu Qing thought for a moment. Then, instead of killing him, he sealed his soul, his consciousness, and his perceptions, and put him in his bag of holding. He could think of further uses for the young man, and considering how truthfully he had answered all the questions, he was clearly an intelligent person.

Using divine will, Xu Qing said to the young man, “When I leave the Fifth Star Ring, I’ll free you. In the meantime... you’ll serve as a source of information.”

With that, he focused on the medallion. After some contemplation, he decided not to activate it. Instead, he put it away. He would first do some exploring before deciding whether or not to participate in the fighting leading to the Immortal Capital.

I suppose the time has come to leave.

With that, he scanned the spirit mine, including all of the tattered minor world bubbles. Most of them were about seventy percent destroyed, leaving them hemorrhaging a dense mist of spirit energy that was ultimately sucked up by the vortex overhead. Presumably, the severe damage to the minor worlds meant that something like this would never happen again. It wouldn’t be possible for the minor worlds to put out such an incredible amount of spirit energy permanently.

What was more, because the skies of all the minor worlds had been broken open, and the living beings inside weren’t having their life force absorbed, they were now essentially free. Unfortunately, the people inside were all very confused and in distress. What was more, because of the difference in pressure between their worlds and the outside, they couldn’t just fly out. And they had no idea what was going on outside.

That state of affairs wouldn’t last for long. Eventually, chosen individuals from those minor worlds would start trying to leave and see the real heaven that existed outside of their world.

Xu Qing chose not to interfere. There’s no karmic connection between me and them. It’s their destiny.

At the same time, his divine will scan confirmed what he had theorized about this place being a prison for gods. It was true. Each minor world bubble contained a sealed god. Some were already dead. Some were barely clinging to life. None were conscious. Clearly this god prison, or ‘spirit mine’ as it was called, wasn’t very high-quality. All of the sealed gods here were in the Godfire level. Xu Qing didn’t sense even a single Altar God.

That said, before I leave, it would make more sense for me to take all this spirit energy rather than just let that vortex take it.

Narrowing his eyes, Xu Qing opened his mouth and inhaled deeply. The dense spirit energy roiled in Xu Qing’s direction, entering his mouth and sweeping through him. Not only did it nourish his fleshly body, but it also nourished his seven extreme daos.

However, the huge lid sealing the place still had a vortex in it that was also absorbing the spirit energy. Xu Qing looked up at it, and after some consideration, decided not to destroy it. He clearly remembered how the Imperial Sovereign he had just killed had looked up at that vortex with fear in his eyes.

I’m afraid that the destruction of the spirit mine will affect the vortex. And as for where that vortex leads to....

Eyes narrowing, he sat down cross-legged and circulated the five elements within him. Time and space erupted, creating an even stronger stimulating force. The spirit energy in the place split into two parts. One part went to the vortex, while the rest went to Xu Qing.

In that manner, time passed.

As the spirit energy in the spirit mine grew thinner and thinner, Xu Qing’s cultivation base climbed higher. Meanwhile, the vortex in the lid above was taking in reduced amounts of spirit energy.

***

The events that had just played out were very obvious in another heaven and earth in another part of the Fifth Star Ring. In that heaven and earth, the sky rumbled with thunder, while the lands were bright crimson. Two figures were currently fighting fiercely in midair.

Both were young men. One had red hair, the other white hair, and their killing intent was obvious with each and every blow they launched. Both contained great daos, and both contained authority. Shocking rumbling echoed out.

The red-haired young man was covered with dozens of swirling totem designs. Each one emanated strong spirit power that continuously bolstered his cultivation base.

But then one of the vortex totems went dim, and the spirit energy from there dried up. Normally speaking, he wouldn’t care if one of his clan’s spirit mines suddenly dried up. But this was a life-or-death battle, and his opponent was a top chosen. If he killed this person, then he would be able to add another Immortal Capital permission medallion to his collection.

Failure was not an option. But now something unexpected had happened.

Dammit, what happened at that spirit mine? And why did it have to happen at this critical moment...?

The red-haired young man’s face turned dour.

But he was in the middle of a fight and couldn’t check into the matter right now. Putting it aside for the moment, he went so far as to use some taboo techniques to fight as hard as he possibly could.

***

A very short distance from the spirit mine, a black flying boat zoomed along beneath a gloomy sky. It moved with astonishing speed. There were nine figures aboard, all of them chatting pleasantly. The boat was flying a white flag with a very unique design. The symbol was circular, and imparted a very specific meaning. As the flag flapped, the sound of their chatting and laughter drifted on the wind.

“Just up ahead is the clan spirit mine guarded by Senior Ling Feng. Once we arrive, we can settle down for some very nice cultivation.”

“Our clan mission went very well, and we got some great loot. We got the information we were looking for and delivered it to the clan just as ordered. Now we can just have some fun in the minor worlds in the spirit mine. We’ve been working hard, everyone. We really deserve this break!”

When someone mentioned ‘having some fun,’ it provoked a wave of laughter. Everyone had looks of anticipation on their faces. To elite clan members like this, the minor worlds in spirit mines were places where they could relax and amuse themselves however they wanted.

Just up ahead was an enormous sealing lid that was their destination.

“Finally here.”

The boat accelerated sharply toward the spirit mine.

1. The character for “inspector” makes you think of something akin to a police inspector, i.e. someone who goes on patrol to “inspect” for crimes or something like that. And it’s not like they “inspect heaven.” More like that they are “inspectors from heaven.” Of course, what the heavenly inspectors do has not yet been stated outright. I’m just talking about the initial impression given by the Chinese characters. ☜

The wind carried the sound of chatting and laughter. A black boat was flying at top speed through the air, and it was getting closer and closer to the spirit mine.

From a distance, the spirit mine looked like a huge crater some 500 kilometers from end to end. Covering the crater was an enormous black lid that sealed the entire place. The surrounding area was wilderness without many signs of life.

As the flying boat got closer, the nine figures aboard became clearer. Among them was a handsome young man who had just cleared his throat to get the attention of the others. He was clearly the highest-ranking member of the group, so everyone immediately looked over at him.

“In short order we’ll finally be able to relax,” he said coolly. “The mission we just finished was hard on all of you. Who could have guessed that those fugitives would be hiding amongst mortals? But we still tracked them down and accomplished the mission our clan gave us. Sadly, we had to destroy a few mortal cities to track down our quarry. Well, it is what it is....”

The young man sighed.

Hearing his words, the others on the boat added their opinions.

“You’re so kind, Clan Brother Hai Shan.”[1]

“Clan Brother, in the final analysis, the deaths of those innocent mortals are all the fault of the godly fugitives. It’s not like we set out to kill a bunch of people. The clan will definitely understand.”

“That’s right. The mission to track down those godly fugitives has been an open dharmic decree from the Immortal Capital for a long time now. We can all testify that everything that happened was for the sake of the mission. It wasn’t our fault!”

The young man they had called Hai Shan nodded regretfully for a moment. Then his eyes flitted to the pretty young woman sitting next to him. He smiled.

“Enough talk about that,” he continued. “Of the thirty-five spirit mines controlled by our clan, this is the quietest. That said, I’ve never been here before. Now that I think about it, this place is situated on your clan’s property, isn’t it Junior Sister Ling?”

The others on the boat smiled and nodded as they offered further input.

“That’s right. The guardian of this spirit mine is Senior Ling Feng, who’s a court attendant of our clan, and is also a patriarch in Junior Sister Ling’s family. In a moment, we’ll offer formal greetings to Senior Ling Feng, and hopefully Junior Sister Ling will vouch for us. That way, maybe her patriarch will give us some cultivation tips.”

“Granted, he’s only a court attendant with a foreign surname, but given Senior Ling Feng’s cultivation base, even just a bit of advice from him could be very beneficial to people like us.”

As everyone laughed merrily, the young woman they had called Junior Sister Ling smiled faintly.

“You’re flattering me, Big Bro Hai Shan. I stand in the shadow of my family’s patriarch, that’s all. I couldn’t possibly compare to the rest of you. As a court attendant, the fact that Patriarch Ling Feng was assigned to guard duty here is a magnanimous blessing on the part of your clan.

“But since you mentioned it, Big Bro Hai Shan, when it comes time to meet him, I’ll definitely ask him to give us permission to enter some of the minor worlds to absorb some spirit energy. I just hope it can help all of you Elder Brothers to relax a bit.”

Although the young woman spoke very modestly, the reality was that she was very pleased with the way these clan cultivators were talking about her. It was with such chatting and laughter that the flying boat arrived at the spirit mine.

Everyone flew out, and then Junior Sister Ling bowed to Hai Shan. Taking out a jade slip, she sent a voice message to Patriarch Ling.

Everyone seemed very relaxed. They were all looking forward very much to the rest and relaxation to come, and were simply waiting for the spirit mine’s spell formation to open up. But as time ticked by, the spell formation didn’t open. It didn’t even show signs of opening.

Junior Sister Ling frowned slightly. There had never been a case in the past in which she sent a voice message to Patriarch Ling and he didn’t respond.

Weird... she thought. After a moment of thought, she looked over her shoulder at the others. “The patriarch is probably in the middle of a cultivation session. Big Bro Hai Shan, as a member of the direct bloodline, you should be able to just open the spell formation. Do you want to take the lead here?”

Hai Shan looked at the spell formation. The spell formation blocked sight, making it impossible to see what was going on inside. He considered the situation briefly, then shook his head.

“I do have the authority to do that. But Senior Ling is the guardian here. It would be very rude to just barge in. If Senior Ling is in the middle of cultivation, why don’t we just wait out here for a bit?”
