Everyone agreed. Junior Sister Ling nodded. She sent another voice message via jade slip, and even sent a message to Patriarch Ling’s servant. She got no responses.

It was the first time anything like this had happened, and she was feeling a bit flustered. Could it be possible that there had been some sort of accident? However, given the cultivation base and personality of Patriarch Ling, she decided that the chances of some accident happening were very low.

***

None of the group noticed that a cold gaze from inside the spell formation was sweeping over them. Even as Xu Qing absorbed spirit energy inside the spirit mine, he had opened his eyes and was looking outside. Three in the fourth stage of Void Returning. Four that are two-world Smoldering Gods. One that’s a three-world Smoldering God. And the strongest is a four-world Smoldering God.

Killing these people would be as simple as turning over his hand. However, Xu Qing didn’t want to kill anyone if it wasn’t necessary. Going around slaughtering people would only cause more trouble later.

Of course, if he didn’t kill them, it was possible they might report that something unusual was going on at the spirit mine. Granted, the strange circumstance was nothing more than the spirit mine being locked down. Because the circumstances weren’t clear, the clan would probably send someone to check on the mine. If they did, it would at least take some time for that person to arrive. On the other hand, if he did kill these people, it was likely that there were bloodline magics that would notify their clan, and then they would definitely know something was going on at the spirit mine.

Given all that, Xu Qing decided that since they weren’t doing anything to court death, he wouldn’t take any action. He just continued absorbing the spirit energy. The spirit energy was already starting to get thin. Based on Xu Qing’s estimations, it would only take about two more hours to absorb all of it.

Although absorbing it could help improve his cultivation base a bit, the main reason Xu Qing wanted it was to bolster his seven extreme daos. That’s especially true of the daos of space and time. As far as he was concerned, he had not developed those extremes far enough.

Therefore, as he absorbed the spirit energy, he focused on seeking enlightenment based on his experience in that vortex he had passed through in the Primeval Sea. He had begun doing so in the minor world bubble, and was continuing to do so while absorbing the spirit energy.

As the process went on, he also took some of the holy fardark nectar. That made the enlightenment come even easier.

In that manner, time passed. Occasionally, he would run into side issues, but overall, progress was good.

***

About an hour later, Hai Shan was starting to have some misgivings. “Junior Sister Ling,” he said, looking over at her, “even if Senior Ling is in the middle of cultivation, doesn’t he have a servant? Can’t you get in touch with the servant?”

Junior Sister Ling was feeling more uneasy than ever. She nodded. “I did. But... he didn’t answer.”

Everyone else reacted visibly to this news. One by one, they looked over at Hai Shan.

Hai Shan’s eyes narrowed. “If Senior Ling is so busy with cultivation, we shouldn’t bother him. Let’s just leave.”

With that, he flew back onto the black boat. The others hesitated briefly before following. Junior Sister Ling was feeling extremely worried, and wanted to offer a different suggestion. But considering how serious Hai Shan looked, she didn’t dare.

And thus, the group flew off. After the boat was a certain distance away, it stopped in midair. Hai Shan looked back at the mine, his eyes narrowed.

If Patriarch Ling and his servant aren’t responding to messages, it could mean a number of things. Maybe they really are in the middle of cultivation or some other important thing. It’s even possible they went out to do something. Whatever they’re busy with, maybe they can’t tolerate any distractions, and that’s why they aren’t responding to messages.

Of course, there’s another possibility. What if something bad happened? The spell formation is completely intact, with no damage. That indicates that if something bad happened, it didn’t involve an outside attack.

What’s more, we waited outside for about an hour. Nothing happened to us, and we were able to leave freely. All of this seems to indicate....

After some more thought, Hai Shan turned to Junior Sister Ling. “Does Patriarch Ling have any enemies? When was the last time you were in touch with him?”

“The patriarch never leaves loose ends,” she replied immediately. “He always gets rid of his enemies right away. What’s more, he’s been the guardian here for years, and hasn’t done any traveling in that time. I contacted him only a few days ago. It was after we had finished the mission and were on the way back.”

Hai Shan considered the information. It seemed to him that given only a few days had passed, it wasn’t likely that there had been some dramatic event. Even if there had, it was likely still in the beginning phases. That said, if Senior Ling Feng was so focused that he couldn’t respond to messages, that seemed to indicate that if a dramatic event was underway, it probably involved an Imperial Sovereign. And that meant... that there was a chance to earn some credit here!

If I just report that something suspicious is going on, but it turns out everything is normal, then the clan won’t be happy with me. Therefore....

After more thought, he decided that the best thing would be to try to get more information, but keep his distance. There wouldn’t be any harm in that. Having reached the conclusion that this was definitely the best idea, he took out a jade slip and crushed it. In doing so, he called on his direct bloodline authority to connect to the spirit mine’s formation. His eyes flashed with a blood-colored light. Focusing the clan authority in his eyes, he peered inside the spell formation.[2] freewebnovel.com

When he saw the situation inside, his face fell. The entire area was in ruins! And he saw two eyes as cold as death! A tremor passed through him and blood sprayed out of his mouth. His cultivation base reeled.

“Get out of here!” he shouted. Without any hesitation, he sent the boat speeding off into the distance. At the same time, he took out a clan jade slip to send a call for help. The others had no idea what was going on, but they all looked visibly taken aback.

Unfortunately... before Hai Shan could even finish taking out the jade slip, a cold voice echoed about.

“You shouldn’t have looked.”

A huge hand filled the gazes of Hai Shan and the others. They were suddenly surrounded by a huge spatial grid. Time seemed to slow down. Everything went black.

The hand closed. They were destroyed in body and soul. Even the flying boat was crushed into ashes.

Everything went quiet.

A moment later, the spirit mine’s spell formation rippled, and Xu Qing emerged, having completely absorbed all the spirit energy. He looked around.

“So this is the Fifth Star Ring...” he murmured.

He burst into motion.

1. Hai Shan: Hai is a surname which means “sea, ocean.” It’s not very common as a surname. Shan means “mountain.” So these characters together mean “sea and mountain” and are the same characters from the “Sea and Mountain Incantation” earlier in the novel. If you reverse them, they’re Mountain and Sea, as in “Mountain and Sea Region” from earlier in the novel, or all the Mountain and Sea stuff from ISSTH. This name could well be a Daoist name, but there isn’t any definitive proof either way, and it’s not important, so I’m going to interpret it as an ordinary surname and given name. ☜

2. Just to be clear, his “direct bloodline authority” is not the magical/cultivation/godly authority, but rather, ordinary authority, i.e. permission or the right to do something. ☜

A majestic red aurora swelled like a river through the canopy of heaven. Because it ebbed and flowed, it didn’t cast its light evenly, causing the silty ground to shift back and forth between brightness and gloom.

It wasn’t just the ground in the spirit mine that was covered in sludge. The lands surrounding the mine looked the same. Xu Qing knew the explanation for that thanks to the Imperial Sovereign’s servant. This place was in the south of the Fifth Star Ring, and was considered a very remote area. A long time ago, it had been a huge sea. In fact, it had been the Fifth Star Ring’s Primeval Sea.

Later on, the Immortal Paragon had compacted the starry sky in the Fifth Star Ring, as well as the Primeval Sea, which was a place that countless gods had called home. This place had eventually been occupied by cultivators.

Unfortunately, the lands were poor and infertile. The upside was that there was no mutagen. The gods in the Fifth Star Ring had been conquered, and to some extent, it was correct to say that they had been outlawed.

Considering that the aura of the gods, in other words mutagen, was harmful to cultivators, it was only natural that it would be stamped out. In the end, the cultivators started assimilating the gods, turning them into nutrients, extracting their life force to make spirit energy for cultivators to use.

As Xu Qing traveled, he could feel the effects of that. Every single one of his pores felt extremely comfortable as the spirit energy in heaven and earth automatically poured into him. He felt like parched lands that were benefiting from a spring rainfall. There seemed no end to the spirit energy, and though it wasn’t as strong as it had been in the mine, it was still there.

There’s nowhere in the Revered Ancient mainland that comes close to this.

As he instinctively absorbed the spirit energy, he sent his divine will out to assess his surroundings. He could sense the natural and magical laws in this area; that was an ability unique to Smoldering God cultivators. By means of the local natural and magical laws, it was possible to directly sense the world.

His divine will made it possible to see semitransparent threads all around him, connecting to everything. They were natural and magical laws. Once one’s cultivation base reached a certain level, it would be possible to affect and even control them.

As Xu Qing assessed his surroundings with divine will, he was able to find the sources of those threads.... A thoughtful look appeared on his face, and the vigilance in his heart grew stronger. As he sensed the world around him, he had felt its majesty. What was more, in the sources of the natural and magical laws, he had detected boundless wills.

Many of these natural and magical laws have been laid claim to already.

He retracted his divine will and looked up into the sky. He didn’t make direct contact with any of the wills he had sensed. However, he did check to see what would happen if he tried to use some of those natural and magical laws. It was not a violation to do so.

Although the natural and magical laws here seem to be operating in order, the reality is that they are full of a certain type of chaos....

He looked around. Within the feedback from the natural and magical laws, he could sense blood and slaughter.

So this is also a place where the weak are the prey of the strong. In fact, it’s even more intense than back home.

A day later, he was able to confirm his supposition when he witnessed a bloodbath.

A majestic merchant convoy was flying through the sky. There were several thousand people in it, and as beasts of burden they had a host of gigantic creatures that resembled rhinos. They were transporting some items that Xu Qing didn’t recognize. But obviously, they were things that couldn’t be fit into bags of holding. Based on the auras he could sense, the convoy had powerful experts as guards. It looked like an extraordinary convoy. Considering what Xu Qing could see and sense, he doubted anyone would dare to cause trouble for them.

But then the bloodbath occurred. Rumbling sounds echoed out as a troupe of bandits came out of nowhere. There were thousands of them, maybe even more than ten thousand, and they immediately set upon the merchants.

The fighting was fierce, and there were many deaths. Cultivators screamed. Beasts bellowed. The stench of blood spread everywhere. As the fighting played out, it was even possible to see some enslaved godly entities.

Most shocking of all was that the merchants actually unleashed a god. It was a huge eye that was bound like a slave. At one time, the eye had been covered with tentacles. But most of the tentacles had been severed, and the eye was covered in sealing marks. This god was obviously in the Godfire level. Īt served as some sort of trump card, and as the slaughter played out, it was basically nothing more than a weapon.

Xu Qing wasn’t sure how the battle ended. He watched from a distance for a while, but when he noticed streams of divine will from both sides getting close to him, he left. The incident had nothing to do with him, and there was no need to get involved.

His departure didn’t go completely smoothly. The two incoming streams of divine will were both hostile, and seemed unwilling to let him go free. However, as they got close, his eyes flashed coldly, and he sent his own divine will shooting out aggressively.

Sometimes, avoiding trouble requires more than keeping your head down. It can be better to make it clear you’re not to be trifled with. The principle applied in the Fifth Star Ring just as much as it did in Revered Ancient.

The various streams of divine will clashed. Multicolored lightning flashed in the sky. Natural and magical laws were made manifest, and loud rumblings made it clear that the weather was changing for the worse. A blizzard and heavy rain struck at the same time.

And then... the other two streams of divine will backed away. Clearly they were afraid, and didn’t want to pose an obstacle.

Xu Qing went on his way, his face completely expressionless.

Similar incidents occured on three additional occasions over the next few days.

And seeing bloodbath after bloodbath gave Xu Qing a clear picture of how brutal and blood-stained this world was.

Like venomous bugs in a jar. It’s almost like the entire Fifth Star Ring is full of powerful experts who climbed mountains of corpses and swam through seas of blood to get to where they are.

Xu Qing looked down beneath his feet. There was a valley below, and inside, another bloodbath had just played out. Corpses lay everywhere, an incredibly strong aura of death had overtaken the spirit energy.

Next to a large pile of blood-soaked corpses was a young man in a black robe, seated cross-legged. His expression was cold as he performed breathing exercises using the death energy. An instant later, he opened his eyes and looked up at Xu Qing.

“This is my spirit lode,” he said.

After stating his claim to the location, the young man’s eyes flitted to another spot outside the valley. There, ripples were spreading out as a person was forced out of the concealment of invisibility.

It was a pretty young woman. She opened her mouth to speak, but didn’t have time.

A flying sword shot out of the young man’s head, glittering with cold aggression. Moving with blinding speed, it stabbed right into the young woman’s forehead. As her corpse toppled to the ground, the flying sword returned to the young man. Then it shifted to point at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing looked down with narrowed eyes. He had noticed the invisible young woman, of course. Now, sensing the hostility from the young man in black, he chose to continue on his way without saying a word.

After Xu Qing was gone, the young man continued to look up at the sky vigilantly. After confirming that the powerful expert had indeed left, the young man breathed a sigh of relief.

That guy... really felt dangerous.

***

Some distance away, Xu Qing thought back to the young man with the sword.

He’s not an Imperial Sovereign. He’s only a Smoldering God. But he has some sort of authority related to death. What’s more, he doesn’t actually seem alive.

That said, they had no beef with each other. After some thought, Xu Qing realized it just went to show how he should view the cultivators from the Fifth Star Ring.

This place doesn’t have a lot of weaklings. Although the Imperial Sovereign’s servant made it seem like this place is very orderly, after everything I’ve seen, I can tell that the only rules that really count are those put in place by the Immortal Capital.

As long as you don’t break their rules, then you can do whatever you want. And that means this place is dangerous and chaotic.

Considering the level of the servant’s cultivation base, he only knows some of the basics. When it comes to all the finer details, for instance the geographic layout or the specific organizations here, I can’t rely fully on the information I got from his memories.

Being as cautious as he was, Xu Qing wasn’t even going to fully trust the information from the soulsearch. If he did that, but then it turned out the person he had soulsearched was misinformed, then he could pay a price for that incorrect information.

I need to stick to my original plan. I need to find a city where I get some accurate information.

After some thought, he picked a place he had learned about from the servant’s memories, and headed in that direction.

***

In the central part of the southern region was a place the Fifth Star Ring cultivators called the Grand Immortal Mountain.

It was called a mountain, but the reality was that it was an endless mountain range filled with many rising and falling mountains that numbered in the hundreds of thousands at the very least.

The place was filled year-round with white mist, within which moved drifting forms that seemed to be immortal beings. Sometimes the wind would blow, thinning the mist and revealing spectacularly beautiful palaces and temples crafted from the finest jade. It really did seem like an immortal paradise.

The immortal spirit energy here surpassed any other area in the south, as this place was the capital.

In a location in the very middle of Grand Immortal Mountain, in a place surrounded by a ring of mountain peaks... there was an astonishing silver-colored temple. The temple had staircases of more than ten thousand steps leading up to it from all sides. The towering temple itself looked almost like an altar.

The temple was glorious to behold. It was constructed primarily from 16,000 planks of immortal green cedar, had golden-colored roof tiles made from glazed spirit ceramics, featured two golden osmanthus trees shaped like coiling dragons, and was decorated with delicate sculptures carved from immortal jade. It went without saying that every surface was richly ornamented. Below the temple was a plaza crafted from immortal jade slabs, within which were 160 glowing statues organized into two rows.

Within the main hall of this extravagantly amazing temple was a holy throne, atop which sat an old man clad in a silver robe. He almost looked like a mortal, except that his eyes would occasionally flash with something brilliant that made it seem like he was gazing down on the entire world.

There was currently a performance going on including singing and dancing. Sleeves rippled in the wind, bells chimed, and voices undulated melodiously. Some sandalwood incense was burning, the smoke curling through the hall and making everything seem hazy and mysterious.

A middle-aged man entered the hall, clad in a long robe decorated with clouds. When he walked, the clouds looked like they were moving, lending him a very extraordinary aura. Walking through the dancers and the haze of the incense, he reached the seat of honor. Clasping hands, he gave a deep bow of respect.

“Greetings, Immortal. The opening ceremony of the Trial of the Hunt will begin soon in the Immortal Capital. How many disciples of our Grand Immortal Mountain will be joining the hunt this time?”

A moment passed after his voice echoed out. Then the old man on the throne, who was hardly visible through the haze, nodded slightly.

“Thirty percent. I hope one of them turns out to have potential. By the way, Lan Yun, I hope all of you remember to follow the rules, unlike last time. Grand Emperors are not to interfere. That’s the rule. The Immortal Capital wants to find chosen who have risen fairly through the carnage. They don’t want greenhouse flowers.” His voice was calm, but it contained a bit of a threat.

“Yes, sir,” Lan Yun replied respectfully.[1]

The old man on the throne regarded Lan Yun for a moment, then coolly continued, “There’s no need for such formality between us, Lan Yun.”

Lan Yun considered his words and then nodded. “You occupy the highest of positions, Immortal. Etiquette must be maintained.”

With that, Lan Yun turned and left.

The old man said nothing further.

The singing and dancing resumed. The smoke from the sandalwood incense continued to burn, swirling about in the hall, slowly obscuring the delicate, beautiful, and lifelike images in the artwork. The octagonal palace lanterns hung about cast their light into the haze... causing the entire hall to become increasingly mysterious.

1. Lan Yun. Lan is not very commonly used as a surname, but it is listed as a surname. It means “mist, mountain forest vapor.” Yun means “cloud.” When I asked Madam Deathblade for her reaction, she actually thought it was a woman’s name, which led to some confusion. It’s conceivable this could be intended to be a daoist name, but there’s not enough evidence to prove it, so I’m treating it like an ordinary surname and given name. ☜

In the Fifth Star Ring, the passage of time was calculated by means of the little vortexes that would appear in the red aurora in the sky. When 1,000 vortexes appeared, it counted as one year. After that, the aurora vortexes would disappear, and a new year would begin.

At the moment, there were 753 vortexes in the red aurora.

Xu Qing was currently looking up at the vortexes. This was the thirtieth vortex-day in which he had been traveling. If he traveled at this speed in Revered Ancient, he would have been able to go from the imperial capital of humankind all the way to Sea-Sealing County. But here, he was still on the border of the south of the Fifth Star Ring.

The lands were still swampy. The Fifth Star Ring was massive.

At least I’ve finally reached my destination.

He looked up ahead in the swamp to a majestic city.

The city was the color black, and beneath the light of the aurora, it looked like a sleeping beast. In the gloom, it was hard to see the entirety of the city with the naked eye. In fact, it was so large that, from what Xu Qing could tell, it was like one of the prefectures back home.

In the memories of the Imperial Sovereign’s servant, this city... was actually considered rather small in the south of the Fifth Star Ring. There were a lot of cities like this in the south, but there were also many that were larger.

Most cities controlled by the servant’s clan were like this one. As for the larger cities, given his status and cultivation base, he had never seen any of them. For his entire life, he had lived in the remote parts of the south.

As for the clan his lord and master had belonged to, Xu Qing had learned something about it during the soulsearch. Although that clan had some sizable territory in the periphery of the south, its patriarch was only a Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperor. In other words, they didn’t really count as a domineering organization. There were other such forces in the south.

It seems to me my previous understanding was a bit flawed, Xu Qing thought as he looked at the city. Given what had played out at the spirit mine, he had assumed that since the guardian was an Imperial Sovereign, the strongest member of the clan would probably be one of the legendary Summer Immortals. As a result, he had really put his guard up.

But clearly, Summer Immortal was a level of personhood considered uncommon no matter where you went. freewebnovel.com

I still need to be careful. There are as many powerful experts in the Fifth Star Ring as there are clouds in the sky.

Taking a deep breath, Xu Qing headed straight toward the city.

Given the current level of Xu Qing’s cultivation base, it was an easy thing to alter his physical appearance and aura, plus hide his cultivation base level, so that he looked like the Imperial Sovereign’s servant. Considering he also had the servant’s identity medallion, it was easy to get into the city. He didn’t run into any obstacles.

Before long, he was through the city gate. There were people everywhere, most of them being cultivators. Mortals were in the minority.

There were lots of shops, and a buzz filled the air.

Given Xu Qing’s past experiences, going into this city and seeing so many cultivators left him feeling a bit dazed. He had never seen anything like this, not even back in the imperial capital of humankind back in Revered Ancient. There were just so many people.

Without even realizing it, Xu Qing started feeling like a stranger in a strange land. That was just human nature. Sometimes wide-open spaces will feel unfamiliar to people, but the reverse can also be true. Crowds of people can leave one feeling like a stranger.

But Xu Qing had grown up traveling to all sorts of places, so despite that feeling, he managed to stay calm and just blend into the crowd.

He spent some time analyzing the people around him. He tried to identify ways that he was different, then make adjustments so that he would fit in. For about half of a vortex-day, he spent time studying the accents, mannerisms, and other nuanced differences between himself and the local cultivators.

From the conversations he overheard, he was also able to get a sense of what things were like in the Fifth Star Ring and in this specific city. Although the information came in bits and pieces, he managed to get more than enough as he searched for a specific type of shop.

At the moment, he was standing just outside the type of shop he had been looking for. It had three floors and a very luxurious facade on the outside. A lot of cultivators were coming in and out. Inside, he could see rows of shelves filled with all sorts of magical treasures. All of them were sealed so that they couldn’t be taken away, but at the same time, had accompanying jade slips with descriptions of the items used. This place was obviously a shop that sold magical treasures.

Xu Qing walked into the store and looked around the first floor at the various items for sale. After a moment, he sighed inwardly. Back in Revered Ancient, magical treasures were rare, and most of them would be precious treasures that could form the backbone of an entire sect. For example, Seven Blood Eyes had those blood-colored eye treasures. To find random treasures unaccounted for was even rarer, and most of them were just fragments. Most of the time, what you found unaccounted for were really just magical devices. But this shop had all sorts of magical treasures.

Xu Qing thought back to Revered Ancient.

Most of the magical treasure fragments back in Revered Ancient actually come from the gods. Perhaps if Eminent Desolation never came to Revered Ancient, it would have ended up similar to this place. But as it stands, there’s a huge difference between the two.

What’s more, there’s another reason Revered Ancient never became like this. And that’s because the Summer Immortals reached a dead end in Revered Ancient. But here in the Fifth Star Ring, it’s been a long time since they found the path leading beyond Summer Immortal. That’s why this is such a flourishing place.

Xu Qing didn’t spend too much time browsing the magical treasures. Though they were nice, given his current level, he didn’t need any of the things on the first floor.

Soon he proceeded to the second floor of the shop. That was where he found what he was looking for. It was a map of the Fifth Star Ring.

One of the salesgirls on the second floor noticed Xu Qing looking at a jade slip that was a Fifth Star Ring map. Walking over, she smiled and said, “Maps like that are very expensive. And that’s truer the more detailed they are. Senior, that particular one is a very detailed map of the south. However, I have to warn you ahead of time that it’s a copy. What’s more, it has a warding spell on it that prevents it from being copied again.”

Xu Qing looked away from the jade slip. “I need more than just the south,” he said coolly.

The salesgirl’s eyes lit up and she flashed another pretty smile. “We do indeed have higher-level maps like that here at the Immortal Treasure Palace. We have branch locations throughout the Fifth Star Ring, so it’s only natural that we have maps of all sorts. Senior, exactly what type of map are you looking for?”

Xu Qing thought for a moment then looked at her. “I want the entire Fifth Star Ring, including information about all the organizations and all the chosen. I want something very comprehensive.”

The woman smiled until her eyes were slits. Inside, she was speculating that Xu Qing was probably involved in the Trial of the Hunt. Those were the only type of people who would want a map like that. After all, he was essentially asking for a map that would have information about all of the enemies he would be up against from throughout the star ring.

And of course, the people who were part of the Trial of the Hunt were all killers to the core. With that thought in mind, the woman became a bit more respectful.

“We do have maps like that here in the Immortal Treasure Palace. But if you calculate the cost in immortal jade, it’s quite high....”

Xu Qing flashed his hand to reveal a huge pile of immortal jade pieces. Then he put them away and looked calmly at the salesgirl.

“Please, follow me to the third floor, Senior,” she said quickly.

He nodded and followed her up. The third floor was less crowded. It was full of partitioned areas where business could be conducted safely and privately.

The salesgirl led him into one such partitioned area, then bowed and left. Some time passed, whereupon she returned with a silver tray. Atop the silver tray was a white jade slip.

Xu Qing waved his hand, causing the jade slip to fly over to him. He quickly scanned it with divine will. A huge map appeared in his mind’s eye. It showed the east, west, south and north, and included information about all the sects and clans. It also had details about local conditions and customs. It also listed information about local chosen.

It was very detailed. That said, most of the information was blurred out by a warding spell so that you couldn’t read it until you bought it.

Xu Qing was pleased. Retracting his divine will, he wasted no time in handing over a large amount of immortal jade to buy the map. The salesgirl respectfully escorted him out, and soon he disappeared into the crowd.

Once safely away in the crowd, Xu Qing changed his appearance and aura a few times. After he was sure that no trouble had arisen because of his purchase, he settled on the appearance of an ordinary cultivator and just let the crowd carry him along. At the same time, he started taking in the basic information from the map.

The Immortal Capital is in the very middle. It’s a holy place that you can’t get information about.

There are four regions on either side of it, to the east, south, west, and north.

Although they’re often called regions, they’re actually entire planetary systems. And each of them is further divided into east, west, south, and north. However, because this entire place is the Fifth Star Ring, people tend to name things based on the perspective of the star ring as a whole.

Each of the four great planetary systems is home to many sects and clans.

The most orthodox of the organizations are as follows: the Grand Immortal Mountain in the southern planetary system; the Sword Immortal School in the northern planetary system; the Star Ring Pagoda in the eastern planetary system; and the Dao Immortal Sect in the western planetary system. The reason those four groups are considered the most orthodox is that they are led by Lower Immortal patriarchs who have been appointed by the Immortal Capital as heavenly inspectors.

Outside of the Immortal Capital in the Fifth Star Ring, there are a total of sixteen Lower Immortals serving as heavenly inspectors! Four of them are leaders of those major sects. But the other twelve are incarnated as heavenly bodies that serve as inspectors in the aurora in various assigned locations.

Thanks to the information from the map, Xu Qing was finally starting to get a fair picture of what the Fifth Star Ring was like. He was also able to determine where exactly he was.

I'm on the outer edge of the southern planetary system, close to the western planetary system. In fact, I’m very close to the border, which is formed by the God Blood River.... According to the description, it’s supposedly a river made from the blood of gods. There are some dangerous and gruish entities in that river, such that only someone with a Grand Emperor cultivation base can cross it.

The God Blood River forms the border between the west and the south, and ordinarily speaking, you can’t get across it. Cultivators who want to get to the other side have to take ferries....

Because of that, there’s a unique profession on the river. They’re called the ferry pilots.... Only a ferry pilot can get you safely across the God Blood River. And that’s because the ferry pilots all come from the Immortal Capital. Apparently, they’re convicts who committed crimes there, and as part of their sentence, they have to serve as ferry pilots.

The cost of passage across the river isn’t spirit stones or immortal jade. It’s longevity.

The first time you cross the river, you have to give the ferry pilot six days of longevity. That’s because the journey takes six days.

The second time you cross the river, the cost increases. It becomes a sixty-year-cycle.

You can’t go a third time. And that’s because the cost of a third trip is all of your longevity.

Upon seeing that information, Xu Qing’s heart pounded.

I can’t believe that’s how you pay to cross the river.... Considering how ridiculous the price is, there seems little point in crossing the river. And I bet there must be more to the story.

As Xu Qing continued to peruse the information in the map, he was able to confirm his previous supposition.

The God Blood River doesn’t just separate the west and south. It forms the borders between the other regions as well. And the process of crossing the river is guaranteed to be safe!

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed.

Once you step foot on the ferry pilot’s boat, they take responsibility for your safety for the duration of the six-day journey. They won’t allow anything to interfere with the voyage. No one seems to know exactly how strong the ferry pilots are. But they do come from the Immortal Capital, and they’re not just ordinary people from there, they’re convicted felons.

It didn’t take long for Xu Qing to come up with a theoretical possibility.

Based on what I know of the Immortal Capital’s Trial of the Hunt, the people with the permission medallions are like venomous bugs in a jar. Their main goal is to rob and kill each other. And that means that these so-called ferry pilots... can provide a safe haven to the participants in the Trial of the Hunt. Twice!

It doesn’t matter what danger they’re in. As long as they can get to a ferry pilot’s boat, they’ll have six days to rest and recuperate. When powerful experts fight, a six-day break to recover and prepare can completely change the outcome.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered brightly. Looking at it from that perspective, crossing the river could be considered a very valuable asset.

The key is the timing. And if I can understand this, so can other cultivators in the Fifth Star Ring. In fact, probably everyone realizes it. This Trial of the Hunt thing is getting more and more interesting the more I learn about it.

Xu Qing carefully analyzed all the different bits of information to make sure he wasn’t making an error in logic. As he continued on his way through the bustling city, he went on to look at the information about the various chosen. The records contained a lot of details about them.

The planetary systems to the east, south, west, and north each had more than a hundred. Some came from specific sects and clans. Some came from rogue organizations. Others were lone wolves.

All had their extraordinary assets. And considering all of them were listed in the map from the Immortal Treasure Palace, it was a given that they were incredibly famous. From what Xu Qing could tell, this map with details of all the Fifth Star Ring chosen was essentially a ranking list.

And there were eight people on the list whose information was highlighted in a different color. Of all the hundreds of chosen in the Fifth Star Ring, they were like shining stars that everyone else looked up to. Because of that, they were collectively referred to as the Shining Stars.

Xu Qing was interested mainly in the southern planetary system, and of the Shining Stars, two were in the south.

The first came from the orthodox sect in the south, which was the Grand Immortal Mountain. He was the apprentice of someone named Lan Yun, who was a Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperor. This Quasi-Immortal Lan Yun had a very venerable position. He was apparently the Junior Brother of the Grand Immortal Mountain’s heavenly inspector. It was said that, years ago, he had been just on the verge of opening the door of immortality. However, some accident occurred that delayed him, and now he was still half a step away from opening the door. Naturally speaking, a sect disciple like that could only be described as extraordinary.[1]

He had an apprentice named Jiang Fan who had not yet been practicing cultivation for 500 years and was an early Imperial Sovereign. He had command of seven types of authority, and had engaged in a spectacular battle in which he ended up killing a peak Imperial Sovereign, although he ended up severely injured in the process.[2]

That battle took place a full sixty-year-cycle in the past, and it shook the entire southern planetary system. In fact, even chosen cultivators from other planetary systems heard about it through their various information networks. Because of that incident, Jiang Fan was considered this generation’s number one chosen in the south.

Another of the eight Shining Stars from the southern planetary system didn’t come from a sect. Rather, this person was a cultivator from the Yuanshan Clan, which was one of the top three clans in the south. She was a female cultivator named Yuanshan Su, and because she was fond of wearing an upper garment of green silk, she was often called by the nickname Green Silk Immortal Fairy.[3]

Her cultivation base was a bit higher than Jiang Fan’s, as she was in the mid Imperial Sovereign level. However, in terms of authority, she wasn’t on Jiang Fan’s level, as she only had four. In addition, she had also fought a peak Imperial Sovereign, only she had lost and barely escaped with her life.

As Xu Qing looked over this information about the southern chosen, his eyes glinted with an aggressive light.

One in the early level, one in the middle.... The former has seven types of authority and killed a peak Imperial Sovereign. The latter has four types of authority but failed to kill an Imperial Sovereign. Either way, both of them are definitely exceptional.

Mind and heart spinning, Xu Qing went on to look at the information from the other three planetary systems.

In the northern planetary system, both of the Shining Stars are from the orthodox Sword Immortal School! They’re twin brothers, and people say that due to supernatural phenomena which appeared at their birth, both of them were born with swords in their hands. They have preheaven sword bodies, and both of them were taken as apprentices of the Sword Immortal School’s heavenly inspector. Their names are Hordeslayer and the Rampart.[4]

During the entire time they’ve practiced cultivation, they’ve crushed everyone else in their generation, gaining immense prestige and becoming celebrities in the north. Both of them are early Imperial Sovereigns, and they each have four types of authority. On their own, they’re both capable of fighting late Imperial Sovereigns, and if they join forces, they can fight a Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperor! Because of their stellar fighting record, they’re considered to be in second place among the eight Shining Stars of the Fifth Star Ring.

Xu Qing was already looking forward to encountering these people. Next, he looked over the information about the eastern planetary system. When he saw the details about the chosen from there, his pupils constricted.

The east was considered the most prominent of the four planetary systems in the Fifth Star Ring. For one thing, three of the eight Shining Stars came from there. But also, there were more chosen there than any of the other regions. Of the three Shining Stars from there, one came from an organization of rogue cultivators, one came from a clan, and one came from the orthodox sect known as the Star Ring Pagoda.

The rogue chosen was known as Sir Vilespirit. He had risen to prominence by fighting many deadly battles and was known for his devouring magic. He was a born killer who cultivated a dao of vile devils.

Back when he was a mortal, he joined a sect but eventually betrayed it. They chased him for a full sixty-year-cycle without ever catching him. Eventually he disappeared. Some years later he resurfaced and joined another sect. Yet again, he betrayed them, and yet again, they chased him but never caught him. Over the years, the same thing happened seven times. He joined seven sects. He betrayed seven sects. Despite being constantly on the run, he managed to become an Imperial Sovereign, whereupon he went back and exterminated all of the sects he had betrayed.

He had climbed mountains of corpses and swam through seas of blood, and that was how he achieved his dao of slaughter. Eventually, he fought a battle with one of the other Shining Stars from the east, the one who came from one of the top clans, but neither could gain the upper hand in the fight. That was how he ended up being listed as one of the Shining Stars.

As for that sect chosen, he was also an extraordinary individual. He had a mid Imperial Sovereign cultivation base, five types of authority, and had defeated a late Imperial Sovereign in battle. His name was Zhou Zhengli, and he came from the number one clan in the east. His name matched his reputation. He was chivalrous, kind, charitable, and was respected by countless cultivators in the east. He and Sir Vilespirit were like polar opposites who both wanted to put an end to each other. [5]

The third Shining Star from that planetary system was actually the number one chosen in the east. He had been bestowed with a name based on the star ring itself, and as such, was this generation’s Sir Star Ring. He had a late Imperial Sovereign cultivation base, nine types of authority, and because he rarely fought in public, few people knew how strong he actually was. In the one public battle he had fought, he had challenged a Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperor. He had won. His name was known far and wide.

Any one of those seven individuals could be called incredibly exceptional.

The final Shining Star came from the western planetary system. That planetary system was known as the weakest in the Fifth Star Ring. Not only did they only have one Shining Star among the eight, but also, their orthodox group, the Dao Immortal Sect, was known to be in dire straits.

For one thing, the western region’s heavenly inspector didn’t care much about the affairs of the world, much less the situation with his sect. Because of that, membership was down, and most of the people who were left didn’t seem to care much about the sect either. Another reason for the situation was that there were actually more clans and organizations in the west than the other regions. Because the Dao Immortal Sect was on the decline, everyone else was fighting each other in the hopes of gaining supremacy.

The Shining Star from the west came from one of the clans. Unfortunately, after working hard and taking advantage of his clan’s reserve powers, he ended up joining the Dao Immortal Sect, where he became the apprentice of the heavenly inspector.

His name was Li Mengtu. One of the unique features of his clan was that all direct bloodline clan members had the character “tu” at the end of their name.[6]

His cultivation base was in the early Imperial Sovereign level, and he had four types of authority. However, because of his clan’s gruish magical technique, as well as the training he had received from his Master, he was able to kill a mid Imperial Sovereign. As a result, he ended up being listed among the Shining Stars.

Other than him, the west didn’t have anyone worthy to be in that list. After all, the general standard to be among the Shining Stars was to have practiced cultivation for less than 1,000 years.

After looking at all the information, Xu Qing felt that he knew a lot more about the flourishing Fifth Star Ring, as well as the eight Shining Stars. More than ever, he felt the desire to do battle.

I have to work hard to get a lot stronger!

Taking a deep breath, he went to find more places to shop. There was more he wanted to accomplish than just buy a map. He wanted to get some medicinal pills and magical treasures. Just to be safe, he wasn’t going to buy everything at one shop. Instead, he would shop around at different shops to get everything he needed. Around the time another vortex was about to appear in the aurora above, he prepared to leave the city.

I’m going to go out in the mountains and go into seclusion for a while. I really need to seek enlightenment of some magics related to time and space. And I need to gain enlightenment of the eighth extreme... That way I can break through to the level of an eight-world Smoldering God.

The information from the map had just reinforced to Xu Qing the danger he was in, and how important it was that he get stronger.

In that manner, time passed.

As he was getting ready to leave the city, a little vortex appeared in the aurora in the dome of heaven. That indicated that a new day was starting.

When the vortex appeared, something unexpected happened. The blood-red aurora surged, spreading out to cover the entire sky in the southern region. Stars appeared in the aurora! There were about two thousand of them, filling the sky. Some seemed near, some seemed far. Some glittered brightly, others seemed dim.

The moment they appeared, countless cultivators in the south instinctively looked up.

Xu Qing frowned. He had just noticed that the Immortal Capital permission medallion in his bag of holding was vibrating. And it was emitting a force that his bag of holding couldn’t contain, a force that seemed to connect to one of the stars up above.

That star was very dim. Right next to his star was another star that was shining brightly.

An instant later, the image in the sky vanished. An uproar ensued.

“The Trial of the Hunt is advancing to the second round!”

“All of the permission medallions are becoming visible.... Now they’ll all be able to sense each other.”

“I don’t know about the other planetary systems, but here in the south... it’s about to start raining blood.”

As Xu Qing heard the buzz of conversation, he thought back to the image of that other star next to his.

The reason I didn’t activate the medallion is that I’m not interested in that whole thing. I guess it doesn’t matter that I didn’t activate it. Now that the second round is beginning, the medallions that weren’t activated have been revealed. The only question is whether or not the other participants will be able to sense the medallions that haven’t been activated.

He kept his facial expression neutral so as not to attract attention in the crowd. And instead of rushing toward the city gates, he just kept moving along at the same speed.

***

At the spirit mine where Xu Qing had arrived some thirty vortex-days earlier, a young man with red hair and a body covered with dozens of vortex tattoos stood looking up into the sky.

Sometime later, he looked away from the sky to the broken minor world bubbles. He could sense how thin the spirit energy was. His expression was very grim.

Ling Feng told me a while back that he was going to give me an Immortal Capital permission medallion as a gift. And now... he’s dead, and the medallion is gone??

Not only that, but the destruction of this spirit mine affected that fight earlier.... Is someone looking to die?!

1. I doubt I need to explain this, but for anyone who wasn’t paying close attention, we saw Lan Yun and (presumably) the heavenly inspector just two chapters ago in 1100. ☜

2. Jiang Fan: Jiang is listed #54 on the top 100 surnames. It also means “ginger.” Fan is a common character that can mean many things, among them “mortal, ordinary, common.” When I asked Madam Deathblade for her reaction, she said he sounds like “a cool dude.” I thanked her for her very deep insights and decided not to ask for further clarification. ☜

3. Yuanshan Su: Yuanshan is a compound surname invented by the author. The two characters are actually a common term that means “distant mountain.” This combination of characters is often used in adjectives. Su can mean a number of things including “raw silk, white, plain, vegetarian.” In this case, as is made obvious by the text, the meaning of the character as used in her name is silk. Madam Deathblade says she sounds like “a pretentious conservative lady.” The kind of upper garment mentioned here is usually some sort of sleeveless garment or jacket. Like all my other footnotes about clothing, I have to say that fashion changed through the ages, plus this is a fantasy novel, so as for what the author actually envisions, it’s hard to say. Here are a couple images I pulled up if you search for this specific type of garment. ☜

4. Hordeslayer and the Rampart: These guys both have names that Madam Deathblade said “are not real names for real people, but are good names for weird fantasy people.” The first name takes two characters out of a common idiom that is used to either describe a magnificent army, or used metaphorically to describe someone extremely strong. The second is a word that’s also part of a saying/idiom that refers to someone or something so scary they make others back away in fear. They’re supposed to be names, not nicknames, but as you can see from Madam Deathblade’s reaction, they’re not “real” names. One look at them gives you an instant sense of the over-the-top fantasy feeling, so I decided to go with a translation in the hopes of conveying that same sensation. ☜

5. Zhou Zhengli: Zhou is listed #10 in the top 100 surnames. Zheng means “straight, upright, proper” and Li means “to stand, to set up, to establish.” Even I was able to guess the feeling of this name when looking at it, and that feeling is confirmed in the explanation provided in the text. Madam Deathblade had the same reaction. ☜

6. Li Mengtu: Li is the #2 most common name on the list of 100 surnames. Meng means “dream” and Tu means “earth, soil, home, homeland.” There is no explanation yet as to any significance to the “tu” character. It’s the same character as “earth” from the five elements, but there’s no reason yet to believe that has anything to do with the name. With the facts we have at hand, the explanation about that aspect of the name seems more like an interesting trivia point the author decided to throw in. Madam Deathblade says it sounds somewhat romantic, as in her mind it sounds like someone who is homesick and loves their home. ☜

In the same city as Xu Qing, and not too far away from him, was the two-story city magistrate’s office. The magistrate himself was a middle-aged man wearing a white robe, who was currently standing at the balcony, his hands clasped behind his back. Looking away from the sky, he glanced at the crowd below, then looked off into the distance.

Killing intent flickered in his eyes. He was looking in the direction of Xu Qing.

The man was of medium height and was slightly pudgy. But he clearly had a bit of muscle on him. His hair was a bit white with age, but was neatly combed. He had faint crows feet at his eyes and wrinkles on his face. That, coupled with his sunken eyes, bore testament to the hardships he had faced in life.

It wasn’t possible to assess his cultivation base, but given that he was surrounded by natural and magical laws, and had dao lineaments in his eyes, meant that he obviously had the strength of an Imperial Sovereign.

I couldn’t possibly have predicted that a second Immortal Capital permission medallion would show up in my city. However, it’s dark, which means it hasn’t been activated.... The person who bears it is either a coward, or they’re planning to give it as a gift to someone else. If it’s the former, I might as well just kill them. But if it’s the latter....

The city magistrate wasn’t sure what to do. In the second round of the Trial of the Hunt, it was possible to detect other medallions. But it worked both ways. Anyone who had fused with their medallion would be able to sense other medallions, even if the other medallion wasn’t activated.

In contrast, someone who hadn’t activated their medallion wouldn’t be able to sense other medallions. That was why carrying around an unactivated medallion during the second round could be dangerous. In fact, few people ever did that.

All of those factors gave this magistrate a lot to think about. After all, he was an Imperial Sovereign, but he was only an early Imperial Sovereign. In this remote little city, that was fine. But it didn’t mean much when dealing with big sects and clans, which was why he had always kept his head down over the years. If he ended up offending the wrong people by going after a permission medallion, he could end up bringing disaster on himself.

But when I got that medallion early on, I activated it. And that means I’ve thrown caution to the wind! Life has become tedious. Why live in a rut, boxed in from all sides, just waiting to die...? Why not put everything on the line?? Besides, my cultivation base has been shackled for long enough. If things keep going on like they have been, I’ll never make any more progress.

With such thoughts on his mind, the city magistrate’s eyes flashed with cold light. “Come with me to crush an enemy.”

“Yes, sir,” voices chorused in response, and a host of figures became visible around him.

The city magistrate strode off of the balcony, flanked by several dozen attendants. Locking onto the position of the other medallion, he started moving.

***

Xu Qing was moving quickly toward the city gate.

When he saw the stars appear in the sky earlier, he had been struck with a sense of deep foreboding. And considering how one of those stars had been so close to him, he knew that danger was just around the corner. It got worse as he neared the city gates, only to notice that there were a lot more guards present than normal. What was more, the gates were currently closing.

Thanks to the spell formations and warding spells in the city, flight was prohibited. If he wanted to avoid being trapped in the city, he would either need to negate the formations and spells, or get through the gate. He felt like he was being hemmed in from all sides. It took only an instant for him to realize what was going on.

Someone ordered the gates closed. And the person who gave the order is probably connected to that other star that was close to me. It’s someone with a permission medallion. Either that, or someone close to that person.

Regardless, it indicates that the person has a high standing and status in this city.

Furthermore, I can’t sense this person, but they can sense me. Or rather, they can sense the medallion. It doesn’t matter that I haven’t activated the medallion, now that the second round has started. In that case, holding back from activating the medallion is putting me at a big disadvantage.

These thoughts ran through Xu Qing’s mind in a flash. It was without any further hesitation that he quickly pulled out the Immortal Capital permission medallion and pushed down on it. The moment he did, the medallion vibrated, then turned into a liquid that fused into the palm of his hand and entered his body.

An instant later, Xu Qing saw an image of a red aurora in his mind’s eye. Within the aurora, he could see the very same image of stars that he had seen earlier in the sky!

That said, there were some differences. Earlier, there were very few instances in which the stars in the southern planetary region were overlapping. But now, quite a few of them were....

And many of them were moving. It was no stretch of the imagination to say that the ones that had overlapped represented different people trying to rob and kill each other.

What was more, Xu Qing could now see his own ranking. He was #1733. That wasn’t his ranking in the Fifth Star Ring as a whole, but rather, his ranking in the southern region.

An instant later, the image vanished. Apparently, the only time you could see a full image of the entire region and all the stars was when you activated the permission medallion.

However, even after the image was gone, Xu Qing could tell that he had the ability to sense any other medallions within 50,000 kilometers of himself. It was a function of the medallions, not anything to do with cultivation base or divine will. The permission medallions were from the Immortal Capital, and they were extremely unique. Without absorbing one, you couldn’t unlock any of its functions.

As of right now, Xu Qing could actually sense two different medallions! One of them was a good distance away, right at the edge of the 50,000-kilometer area. In fact, it seemed to be moving away from him, and disappeared only a moment later.

The other one was very close and getting closer. It was flying right toward him.

Instantly, his cultivation base erupted. The power of the five elements spread out in all directions, and he bolstered his speed, shooting toward the closing gate like an arrow released from a bow. His opponent was approaching aggressively and clearly wanted to fight. There would be no avoiding it.

Xu Qing didn’t know what level of cultivation base he was dealing with, so he could only plan based on the worst-case scenario.

If he had to fight, then the choice of battlefield was going to be very important. If they fought inside the city, the formations and spells would be a detriment to Xu Qing. He would be trapped, and whether he focused on breaking free or fighting back, he would be in a passive position. But if he could break free of the city, then he would have a chance to seize the initiative.

He moved with astonishing speed thanks to how hard he had worked at coming to understand the dao of space, and the methods he had come up with to use it.

The space ahead of him shrank. The space behind him stretched out. Thanks to that effect, in the blink of an eye, he was outside the city gate. The guards couldn’t react in time to block him. They felt a gust of wind, and he was past them.

Then he coldly stretched his hand behind him and pinched his fingers together.

The city magistrate and his attendants had just arrived on the scene. But thanks to the hindrance of Xu Qing’s spatial manipulation magic, they were now much further behind. They had missed their best chance to intercept him.

When Xu Qing pinched his fingers together, the space around him rippled and then collapsed. A deafening boom shook everything. The space outside the city gate completely shattered in all directions, giving rise to a gale force wind. Everything was thrown into chaos.

Within that chaos, a cold snort echoed out. Next, a thunderous rumbling filled the sky, and black clouds appeared. Rain started to fall, turning into heavy sheets that soaked everything inside and outside the city gate.

Xu Qing was included. The moment he sensed the rain, his gaze hardened.

This rain is the manifestation of the dao lineaments of authority! My opponent’s authority... is rain....

Even as Xu Qing sensed that, the surrounding rain transformed, becoming sharp blades that whistled toward him.

At the same time, the shattered space inside the city gate wasn’t blocked by the rain. However, the city magistrate’s attendants took advantage of the rain itself to disappear from sight. When they reappeared, they had passed through all the shattered space and had surrounded Xu Qing. Unleashing Smoldering God might, they coordinated with the rain attack to unleash fatal blows on Xu Qing.

Puppets? Are they unliving dirt? Or are they made primarily from rainwater?

Eyes flashing coldly, Xu Qing shot backward. At the same time, his gaze passed through the sheets of rain to lock onto the white-garbed figure inside the city. He wasn’t launching any attacks, but rather, was just standing there looking coldly at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing considered the situation. He’s obviously a cautious person. He doesn’t know how strong I really am, so even though he can tell I’m not an Imperial Sovereign, he still doesn’t want to face me in person. He’d rather fight from a distance using his authority and his puppets. However, caution can be a strength and a weakness. If you’re cautious at the wrong time, you can lose the initiative.

Eyes narrowing, Xu Qing shot backward again, this time focusing, not on the puppets, but on the blades formed from rain. All of a sudden, an idea popped into his head.

I have cultivator authority. And I have godly authority. Cultivator authority comes from natural and magical laws. Godly authority comes from something else. The two types of authority have similarities and differences. They’re similar in that they both have an origin. They’re different because they’re used in different ways.

Natural and magical laws come when cultivators create heavenly daos. The heavenly daos produce the natural and magical laws. When cultivators gain enlightenment, they have authority. It’s a cycle. The origin of godly authority is even more ancient, and not even I know the details.

Erasure. Immortal skills. Rain. Energy.... All of those things can become authorities. In that case, what about my extreme five elements? Are they... all types of authority? They do not originate with heavenly daos, though. Their origin is me.

Xu Qing had been considering this question during the entire thirty vortex-days in which he traveled to this city.

Then he saw this rain turn into blades, and decided to forget about all of his other magical techniques. Instead, he unleashed his dao of extreme water.

Something unimaginable happened. The water blades shooting toward him suddenly stopped in midair. In fact, all of the falling rain around him suddenly came to a complete and utter halt. The puppets also ceased moving.

Then Xu Qing lifted his hand... and the blades turned around. The puppets spun in place. All of the rain water vibrated... and turned into blades that pointed back toward the city at the shocked city magistrate.

The city magistrate had been watching as the young man he was targeting was surrounded by the water of his authority. But now he was the one who was shocked.

Clearly, this person was a true lord of the rain.

Xu Qing and the city magistrate faced off, one of them inside the city, the other outside of it. The rainwater floated in midair, pulsing with aggressive killing intent.

The two figures standing in that rain formed a very strong contrast. One of them was extremely good-looking. Floating in the rain, his hair drifted around him, and his eyes shone with a strange light. One of them had gray hair and had dignified facial features, though they were marred by a grimace. The city gate was in between them.

The raindrops had become sharp blades, and with the flick of his wrist, Xu Qing had turned them all to point at the city magistrate on the other side of the city gate.

As of this moment, both of them were pulsing with killing intent. However, neither of them chose to launch an attack.

Xu Qing was merely observing the situation. This was his first time trying to control an opponent’s dao lineaments of authority. He needed to see things play out more in order to confirm his theories.

The city magistrate was also observing the situation. He was observing Xu Qing, and he was observing the rain. The authority of rain was a manifestation of his dao lineaments. As a native of the Fifth Star Ring, it was a given that he had been a brave warrior long before becoming an Imperial Sovereign.

He had fought many duels and had killed many opponents. It had been very difficult to break through into the Imperial Sovereign level. And before he could stabilize himself, he ended up facing a powerful enemy. During that fight, he was seriously injured and had to flee for his life. Because of that injury, he had been unable to make any further cultivation progress.

Feeling completely disheartened, he had ended up settling down in this remote location. It had taken a long time for him to make the decision to go all out.

Unfortunately, how could he ever have guessed that his first fight... would involve something like this?

After becoming an Imperial Sovereign, he hadn’t been involved in many fights. Therefore, it was little surprise that he had never been in such a situation, in which he lost control of his own authority. That said, he had at least heard of things like this. Normally speaking, if someone lost control of their authority in a fight, it was because they were dealing with someone who had the same type of authority. If the opponent had a deeper understanding of the authority, they might be able to take control of it.

Authority comes from the immortal dao that accompanies an immortal embryo.

Immortal daos are similar to heavenly daos. But they aren’t corporeal. They’re illusory and imperceptible. And they’re the manifestation of the star ring power that normally belongs to the gods, but that cultivators can seize.

In any given star ring, there are special lineaments that belong to the gods. Those lineaments are what the gods can sense. They’re godly authority. Cultivators have no way to control them. But in the process of forming an immortal embryo, they can naturally absorb them and make them part of one’s essence. That’s why it’s not very likely that two people will have the same authority.

As the city magistrate considered these things, he kept calm, and his eyes shone with a fierce light.

Although I don’t have experience dealing with this kind of thing... it doesn’t mean I can’t come out on top! After all, this guy is a mere Smoldering God, not an Imperial Sovereign! He might be a chosen, but even he has limits!

After a long moment in which the two of them just looked at each other, the city magistrate was the first to make a move.

He lifted his right hand and hit himself hard on the chest. A thunderous thump rang out, and a tremor passed through him. Then blood exploded out of all the pores on his body. The blood immediately merged into the rain, causing the sheets of rain to turn into a rain of blood.

At the same time, his will became part of the blood rain, which bolstered his dao lineaments. That allowed him to seize control of the rain and try to drive out Xu Qing. Unfortunately, there was no way this would succeed.

Xu Qing’s water of the five elements was far more special. It didn’t matter that the city magistrate was bolstering the water with his own will. That was only enough to take back a bit of control over the authority.

An instant later, the city gate became the delineation between the rain controlled by Xu Qing and that controlled by the other cultivator. Inside the city gate, the blood rain spread, bringing with it the odor of gore. Outside the city gate, the rain was sparkling and translucent; it was incomparably pure.

The two types of rain then exploded, each of them becoming sharp blades, rain puppets, and magical techniques. From a distance, it was like two magnificent armies full of thousands of men and horses, slamming into each other. Rumbling booms shook heaven and earth. Wild colors flashed in the dome of heaven. The lands shook. In the city, countless cultivators reeled. As for the city gate, the two astonishing forces slamming together there caused the gate to explode into ashes.

Xu Qing and his opponent were both struck by massive force. They both staggered backward.

However, the two of them had very different facial expressions. The city magistrate was scowling. Xu Qing, in contrast, seemed to be in good spirits.

The reason Xu Qing had not been the first to launch an attack was that he needed to get more information to confirm his theories. Just now, he had picked up on some important clues. He could now sense that his seven extreme daos did seem like they could lead to authority. That was what it seemed like from his perspective. Furthermore, during the clash of rain just now, he had sensed that his five elements water had emanated an instinctive longing.

I can devour this guy’s authority of rain to make my five elements water stronger!

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered brightly. He was also able to ascertain that this city magistrate was a lot weaker than the Imperial Sovereign he had fought in the spirit mine.

The spirit mine guardian he had fought had been very close to the mid Imperial Sovereign level. You could say he was a peak early Imperial Sovereign. As for this current opponent, he had an old injury that resulted in his battle prowess being sub-par.

Either this guy just stepped into the Imperial Sovereign level not long ago, or this is the result of that old injury. In other words... I can kill him without using Grandpa Ninth’s sword energy!

Having reached this point in his train of thought, Xu Qing’s killing intent surged, and he burst into motion toward the city magistrate.

Within him, his dao of the five elements erupted. Astonishingly, a host of supernatural phenomena appeared around him.

The ground churned as the power of earth went wild. It was almost as if some being were waking up under the surface of the ground, causing even mountains to shake as a result. Plants and trees everywhere swayed wildly, looking like demonic monsters. All vegetation was stimulated wildly as the power of wood surged. The city rumbled as the power of metal was influenced. Magical devices, magical treasures, and all other metal objects vibrated and shot up into the air.

From a distance, the scene that was playing out was unsurpassably shocking. The sky rippled as majestic heavenly fire appeared. Everything turned crimson as the aurora was obscured, and a seething sea of flames overtook everything.

Meanwhile, the air rippled and distorted as all cultivators, and all other living things for that matter... found the water emerging from their bodies, as if a huge ocean were being summoned into the world.

This was all very different from Xu Qing’s fight with Ling Feng, in which he had used heavenly daos to do everything. This time, Xu Qing’s thoughts and his dao lineaments of authority were being unleashed.

The city magistrate was struck with even more astonishment than when he had lost control of his authority earlier.

“Five types of authority?? That’s impossible!” The city magistrate’s mind was being battered by waves of shock, and he felt like he was being struck by millions upon millions of bolts of lightning. Based on what he knew, the only people who had five types of authority were those listed among the eight Shining Stars. Of even greater significance was the fact that he had never heard of any Smoldering God who had five types of authority. “Just who exactly are you?!”

Even as the words left the mouth of the city magistrate, Xu Qing closed in on him. Next, the sound of a massive explosion filled the area where the city gate had once stood.

Within the resulting chaos, it was hard to see anything clearly. Anyone without a sufficient cultivation base would lose their mind. And even those who could see what was happening, unless they surpassed a certain level, would only perceive an abstract picture. It was because they couldn’t comprehend what was happening.

When one’s perceptions couldn’t comprehend something, the mind would be thrown into chaos, and it wouldn’t be possible to form an actual image of what was happening. Because they couldn’t see what was happening, the blurry distortions would form something abstract. After all, in addition to the five elements, there were also transformations to space, as well as time being manipulated.

It lasted for a very long moment. Then a beam of sword light flickered, and the shimmering abstract image returned to normal.

The city magistrate was there, blood oozing out of his mouth, his hair disheveled. A sword had been stabbed into the top of his head, and had pierced through his entire body. Blood dripped onto the ground.

Xu Qing hovered in midair looking at his opponent.

The city magistrate managed to look back up at him. From the look of it, he wanted to say something. But when he opened his mouth, it filled with blood, making it impossible for him to speak.

Xu Qing didn’t really care what he wanted to say anyway. With the wave of his hand, he pulled out The Emperor’s Sword.

A tremor passed through the city magistrate. The light in his eyes went out; his soul had been wiped out.

Then Xu Qing made a grasping gesture, causing his opponent’s authority of rain to transform into crystalline water droplets that flew out and became part of Xu Qing’s five elements. His five elements water swelled.

Xu Qing’s aura now surpassed what it had been before the fight. Beyond all of that, he also acquired the city magistrate’s ring of holding. In addition, Xu Qing realized that the range in which he could sense other permission medallions had increased by tenfold!

At the same time, a new ranking number appeared in his head. He was now #1145 in the southern region!

Silence reigned.

Xu Qing looked at the corpse below. He waved his hand, and the corpse crumbled into nothing. He also removed any signs that a battle had taken place.

If I’d come up with this idea earlier, I might not have needed to use one of Grandpa Ninth’s streams of sword energy to defeat that spirit mine guardian.

After some thought, he decided that even with this enlightenment, he still might have been forced to use some of the sword energy. When fighting in unfamiliar territory and circumstances, if you had the chance to launch a fatal blow, you should always take it. Having decided that that was the best way to look at it, Xu Qing looked off into the distance.

There’s no point in sticking around here.

He blurred into motion and disappeared.

***

Up in the dome of heaven, the crimson aurora flowed.

Xu Qing was a streak of prismatic light that shot through the sky at top speed. He made sure to keep a close eye on his surroundings as he mentally reviewed how the fight had played out.

When all was said and done, the most important thing he had learned was that his five elements as authority could take control of the authority of his opponents. That was going to be a big help going forward. It not only confirmed his previous theorizing, but also gave him food for thought about the Imperial Sovereign level.

Previously, Xu Qing had been aware that in the cultivator system, the Void Returning level involved the process of gaining enlightenment of the natural and magical laws of heaven and earth.

The four sub-levels were all like that. It was in that manner that Void Returning cultivators could use the heavenly daos of the world they lived in to create and control the natural laws of their own major worlds. Xu Qing now understood that such control didn’t provide an origin. It was only the ability to use authority.

Perhaps it was correct to say that by gaining enlightenment from the larger world, a cultivator could then create their own major world. Overall, it was like the process of working with a thread and needle.

The fact that Xu Qing had stepped from Void Returning right into Smoldering God put him in that category. One reason was that he had built up a sufficient stockpile beforehand. Another was that the essence of Netherflame’s fleshly body was incomparably pure.

In combination with his success at gaining enlightenment of Deep Earth’s Ten Extreme Daos, Xu Qing’s stockpile and his original essence allowed him to break through into Smoldering God. That was how he had formed his seven worlds.

The term ‘Smoldering God’ was coined in Revered Ancient. In other locations, that level was actually called ‘Smoldering Immortal.’ The name was different, but the significance was the same. The ‘god’ referred to in ‘Smoldering God’ wasn’t an actual god. Rather, it was a nascent divinity.[1]

Before leaving Revered Ancient, Xu Qing had already begun to explore the substructure of the Smoldering God level. He knew that the level was fundamentally about gaining sufficient enlightenment of natural and magical laws, then use that to form one’s own major world.

Ultimately, one would form nine major worlds. Those nine worlds might be consistent with each other, or they might not. It depended on the cultivator’s way of thinking, background, and decisions. Regardless, those worlds ultimately became nutrients that one could use to propel themselves into the Imperial Sovereign level.

Unfortunately, the path of the Imperial Sovereign had been severed on the Revered Ancient mainland. Only people with very special bloodlines could force their way through. Most of the time... it wasn’t possible. One reason for the situation was that something had gone wrong with the heavenly daos created by the Summer Immortals years in the past. But in the final analysis, the biggest problem was the influence of the broken face of Eminent Desolation. The godly aura was too strong, making it very difficult for immortals to rise up.

After all... the Imperial Sovereign level was very special. It involved fusing one’s nine major worlds to make an immortal embryo. Transforming from a cultivator into an immortal was a major watershed point. Once you formed an immortal embryo, you were a Quasi-Immortal, in other words, a Grand Emperor.

For example, Empress Summer Departure had the help of Swordsage, the bloodline of Dark War, and the blessing of humankind’s destiny aura. Despite that, she could go no further than the Imperial Sovereign level. She had no way to become a Grand Emperor.

That was also why no Grand Emperors ever appeared in Revered Ancient after the broken face came.

As a result of that situation, the empress had been forced to switch her cultivation to the path of the gods. By means of a special ceremony, she ignited godfire, using the immortal embryo she had never fully formed as the fuel. Then, as the fire raged hotter and hotter, shē eventually reached the Altar God level. After that, shē could never become an immortal.

Before leaving Revered Ancient, Xu Qing went to the Summer Immortal Palace, where he had learned these things about Imperial Sovereigns, and the way of Quasi-Immortal Grand Emperors.

According to the records of the Summer Immortal Palace, authority had never appeared in Deep Earth before. It was only after cultivators went to Revered Ancient that it was seen.

The Summer Immortal Palace originally assumed it was the same as essence. But in reality, essence had appeared within Deep Earth cultivators long before that.
