There were differences between the two, the most obvious being dao lineaments. What was more, the manner in which it first appeared was in the process of an Imperial Sovereign forming an immortal embryo by means of their immortal dao.

The so-called immortal dao existed in the void, above the level of the heavenly daos. It appeared as authority, and as dao lineaments.

The Summer Immortal Palace actually didn’t understand why it appeared. That said, normally speaking, dao lineaments of authority only showed up in the Imperial Sovereign level. There were exceptions. For example, there were some chosen who could produce it in the Smoldering God level. That became the standard to define chosen cultivators before the arrival of the broken face.

As for Summer Immortals, in other words, the Lower Immortals... they were cultivators who formed an immortal embryo, nurtured it to the proper level, then broke through, causing the embryo to transform, and giving birth to a full-fledged immortal.

According to the records of the Summer Immortal Palace, the level of Summer Immortal was the limit for the Deep Earth star ring. In Deep Earth, that was known as the ninth step.

That said, there was a difference between Summer Immortal battle prowess in Deep Earth compared to Revered Ancient. In the Deep Earth star ring, Summer Immortals could encompass the entire star ring with a thought. Other than actually destroying the star ring, they could do anything they wished.

That wasn’t the case in Revered Ancient. After a certain level of analysis, the Summer Immortal Palace came to understand why that was. They understood that Revered Ancient was located in the Ninth Star Ring. And they eventually realized that the Ninth Star Ring was part of a larger heavenly system that had a total of thirty-six star rings.

The Ninth Star Ring, which was also known as the Brilliant Heaven star ring, was only one of them. Based on what the Summer Immortal Palace understood, those thirty-six star rings existed on a high level. To some extent, they could be considered higher worlds.

As for Deep Earth, it was a lower-level star ring. In other words, it was a lower world. According to the Summer Immortal Palace, it wasn’t possible that Deep Earth was the only lower world. Most likely there was a correspondence. In other words, there were also thirty-six lower star rings. In fact, maybe there were more. One thing was certain: above Deep Earth was Brilliant Heaven.

This was just a theory of the Summer Immortal Palace, and there was no way to confirm if it was true or not. That said, though it was just a theory, it did explain the situation with Summer Immortal battle prowess.

There would be a pressure difference between lower and higher worlds, which was why there would be a difference in battle prowess. It was like the difference between a major world and a minor world.

In minor worlds without much pressure, it would be easy for someone to call the wind and summon the rain. But they might not be able to do the same thing in a major world.

Fundamentally speaking, the Summer Immortal Palace’s research indicated that the thirty-six higher star rings were the lands of the gods. The source of godly authority, the mysterious lineaments, created a massive pressure that weighed down on all of the thirty-six higher star rings.

It was the same for gods and cultivators alike.

That point didn’t mean very much to Xu Qing. After all, he had never been to Deep Earth. Therefore, he had no idea what terrifying level his cultivation base would be like there. His entire life had been lived in a higher star ring.

My five elements turned into authority, their uniqueness....

His eyes narrowed as he rubbed his chest. At the moment, a violet crystal was there, glittering.

What exactly is it...? Back when I gained enlightenment of the Ten Extreme Daos, I saw a design that included a crystal, broken into ten parts. But my crystal isn’t broken at all. It’s whole.

For instance, it’s the character from divine will, divine sense, nascent divinity, etc. I’ve been trying to render it ‘god’ when related to the god ‘species’ but in other ways depending on the context when it relates to non-god stuff. In the south, my rank is #1145....

Xu Qing was currently speeding through the sky underneath the aurora. His expression was one of pure vigilance. In no way had he relaxed after killing that city magistrate. In contrast, his guard was up more than ever.

Now that he had activated the permission medallion, which involved absorbing it into himself, he was officially part of the Immortal Capital’s Trial of the Hunt.

He could already feel danger looming. And that was because the range at which he could sense other medallions had increased. One unique function of the Immortal Capital permission medallions was that they couldn’t sense other medallions unless you activated them first. You could be literally standing right next to someone else with a medallion and your divine will wouldn’t be able to detect their medallion.

The only way to sense other medallions was to activate and absorb your medallion. The medallions qualified you to join the competition, but at the same time, served a specific function.

Xu Qing had absorbed his medallion before killing the city magistrate, and at that time, the range of his own medallion was 50,000 kilometers. That meant that he would instantly sense any other medallions that were within that range.

He had previously assumed everyone else could do the exact same thing. However... after killing that city magistrate, who had also possessed a medallion, Xu Qing realized that, not only had his ranking climbed, but also, his medallion had changed. It was as if the medallion had upgraded from a basic state to a second, more advanced state.

The most obvious change was that the range in which he could sense other medallions had increased by tenfold. He could now sense anything within 500,000 kilometers.

That was the reason for his grave attitude.

I only got one additional medallion, but my range increased by a huge amount. Logically speaking, I can expect the range to increase even more as I get more medallions. In that case, everyone else....

Xu Qing’s pupils constricted. This was not a good situation for him. The more people you killed, and the more medallions you accumulated, the greater the range of your own senses.

And of course, that meant that there were going to be people with clear advantages and clear disadvantages. The strong people would have the advantage. The weak people would have a disadvantage.

It was easy to imagine a scenario in which there were enemies who could sense him, but were too far away for he himself to sense. A situation like that could prove fatal in a hunting event like this.

The more medallions you got, the higher your rank would be, and the bigger advantage you would have. As time passed, and more people got an advantage, the range in which they could sense other medallions would become completely terrifying. It would eventually be impossible to flee from such people.

No wonder my rank jumped up so much by just killing one other competitor. Now that the second round has begun, I bet similar things are happening throughout the south. So, this is the second round. No wonder this thing is called the Trial of the Hunt.

By merely having the range of his permission medallion increased, Xu Qing was able to deduce how deadly and brutal this event was. And it just went to confirm further that the Immortal Capital was trying to raise venomous bugs in a jar. The Immortal Capital recruited people for the event because they weren’t interested in greenhouse flowers. They wanted apex predators. They wanted true chosen who had climbed mountains of corpses and swam through seas of blood.

The details of how the medallion range worked might be somewhat unfair. But if you looked at it from a different angle, it was very fair. Everyone started out exactly the same. How far you proceeded would depend on your own skill and ability. Either you lived or you died.

Xu Qing licked his lips, and a cold light flickered in his eyes. Now that he thought about it, this system actually made things interesting. At the very least, it made him feel a lot of pressure.

This was not the Revered Ancient mainland. His Master was not here to save him. He couldn’t get help from Empress Summer Departure. His Eldest Brother wasn’t here to provide backup. Though he had the clay fox around, the Fifth Star Ring repelled gods, so the fox was dormant.

I have to rely on myself and myself alone. I will have to face all the consequences of my decisions.

His vigilance had reached the highest level possible. Narrowing his eyes, he cleared his thoughts and proceeded forward at top speed.

At the same time, he took some time to assess and organize everything he had acquired thanks to the fight from earlier.

For instance, there was the authority that came from the extreme five elements.

In reality, my authority isn’t limited to the five elements. I also have space and time. However, I need more insight and practice with the latter two. Then there’s my authority of erasure, plus the dao lineament from Six Thieves Deceive Life.

If you tally everything precisely, I actually have nine types of authority. Going forward, I need to focus my cultivation on the five elements authority, while also contemplating space and time. Plus I need to work on producing my eighth extreme.

In terms of other ways he had benefited from the fight, the augmentation to his medallion counted as the second.

As for the third... it was the ring of holding. Now that the primary owner was dead, the branding mark on the ring was gone. As Xu Qing scanned the ring with divine will, he was able to see the contents very clearly. It went without saying that anyone who could become an Imperial Sovereign in the Fifth Star Ring would have ample resources.

The spirit mine guardian he had killed had been stationed at that mine for a long time, and thus kept his possessions with him. As for this second individual Xu Qing had killed....

Anyone who had intentionally activated and absorbed a permission medallion would be fully aware of the bloodshed they were in for. Such people would either be extremely confident, or they were the type who had no choice other than to throw caution to the wind. As for the former, it would be difficult to predict what they would carry around with them. But the latter would definitely keep all their most valuable things with them at all times.

That was exactly the case with this ring of holding.

It contained masses of spirit stones and immortal jade. However, there was only one treasure inside. It was a geomantic compass that was in really bad shape. It had clearly been severely damaged and not yet repaired.

There were some medicinal pills, though. Obviously this city magistrate had focused a lot on stockpiling pills. There were many, many types.

When Xu Qing attacked he had used his authority to lock down space. Plus, the fight had been very fast-paced. Because of that, though the man had managed to take out a few pills and use them, none of them had played a significant role in the battle.

Xu Qing scanned the pills to identify them, then put the ring away and shot through the sky as fast as possible.

In that manner, time passed. Five vortex-days went by.

Perhaps because he was in such a remote place in the south, or perhaps because of the speed he maintained, he didn’t run into any dangerous situations. In fact, he didn’t encounter any people at all. The sense of impending danger he had felt earlier had eased a bit.

Eventually, as night was about to fall, and a new vortex was about to form in the aurora, he stopped on a remote mountain to quickly hew out a cave. Once inside, he settled down cross-legged.

Darkness fell outside, and it was pitch black inside the cave. There he sat in the darkness, surrounded by silence.

As he became part of the gloom, he hid his aura and worked on cultivation. He was seeking enlightenment of his dao, and probing his path forward.

Darkness came and went outside. Vortexes appeared one after another in the aurora. Seven vortex-days passed.

Xu Qing opened his eyes within the gloom of the cave. It was as quiet as ever. The darkness was like an old friend.

It’s like... back when I was a kid. [1]

Xu Qing looked around and sighed softly. Truth be told, Xu Qing knew exactly what it was like to be completely alone and surrounded by danger. Back when he was young, he had lived every day with that feeling.

From the time he left Peerless City until he became an apprentice of Master Seventh, he had licked blood from his blade like an assassin, and had always preferred to stay out of sight. Back then, he would always walk in the shadows when possible. The shadows offered protection. When he was part of them, he became darkness and gloom, and he could stay hidden. It was the same now.[2]

Eventually, Sergeant Thunder became part of his life, giving him the familial love he had missed for so long. His Eldest Brother had brought brightness to his life. Master Seventh took him as an apprentice and protected him, helping him to understand what it meant to have an elder watching out for you. Ling’er had helped him to feel relaxed inside. With Plumdark around, he had been stricken with feelings he couldn’t identify, perhaps nervousness, perhaps something else.

In Sea-Sealing County, Palace Lord Kong taught him what it meant to be a swordsage. The empress showed him that even gods could have human nature. And Grand Emperor Swordsage showed him that it was possible for a person to live a life that would always be remembered.

That had all been part of the process of growing up for him. He had experienced many things and had truly lived life to the full. Those things were part of him. They couldn’t be taken away. They had made him who he was now. After all those experiences, now here he was, in the unfamiliar Fifth Star Ring, all alone, surrounded by danger.

This is just another of my experiences.

He found himself subconsciously patting his clothing to try to find his iron skewer. It wasn’t there.

Little Shadow seemed to sense his emotions, and sent out some fluctuations to remind him it was there. The god vine sent a little branch snaking out to caress his face. The trip through the Primeval Sea had severely damaged the pagoda, and the god vine as well. It hadn’t fully recovered yet. The actions of the shadow and the vine brought a smile to Xu Qing’s face. And with that, he closed his eyes and prepared to continue working on his cultivation.

But then his eyes snapped open, and he turned to look toward the south. His expression was one of complete vigilance. He had just sensed another medallion within the range of his senses, located roughly in the same direction he was looking.

At first, it had seemed that the person was just passing by. But then he sensed them change direction and start moving toward him.

This person has the same range as me!

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered with cold light. Many thoughts were running through his head.

I can’t run. If I do, they’ll realize I noticed them and have the same range. If I did that, I would be making a gamble. I’d be gambling on whether or not they chased me. And if they did chase me, it would mean that we would have to fight eventually.

Doing that... would be too passive! Instead, I’ll pretend that I don’t notice them. In the time it takes them to get here, I’ll make preparations. That way, I can create the most ideal field of battle for myself. That’s definitely the best option!

Heart filling with determination, Xu Qing waved his hand to produce 49 Taboo Formations, which he had acquired from Ling Feng, the spirit mine guardian. He had already studied them a bit and knew how to use them.

In addition, he had Little Shadow spread out into the area and go into hiding.

Next, he made certain other preparations. He enhanced the power of the land, and made sure there was plenty of vegetation in the area. He also took out a stick of incense, put it in front of him, and lit it.

Finally, after making all of his preparations, he put the crystalline treasure tree in front of him and activated it so that its aura began to spread out. Before long, an exact copy of Xu Qing appeared in the crystalline treasure tree. Even its aura was exactly like his own.

“Sit down cross-legged,” Xu Qing said calmly. The figure nodded and sat down cross-legged.

Then Xu Qing sank down into the ground, making sure to stay fairly close to the figure in the tree. That way, anyone following the location of his medallion would come right to this spot, and his real aura would overlap with that of the figure in the tree. Having accomplished all those things, Xu Qing sat waiting, killing intent building in his eyes.

About 450,000 kilometers away from Xu Qing in his cave, a young man in a bright yellow robe was flying through the sky underneath the crimson aurora. He was moving with such incredible speed that it wasn’t possible to track him with the naked eye. He was clearly heading right toward Xu Qing.

His cultivation base was very close to the mid Imperial Sovereign level, but he contained all of his power so that it didn’t go farther than 300 meters away from him. And as he sped along, his power built up to greater heights within that area. He had plain facial features, as well as a faint birthmark on the right side of his face, which gave him a bizarre and gruish appearance.

The crafty look in his eyes made it clear that he wasn’t a simpleton.

Not moving at all? How interesting... It’s possible this guy didn’t notice me. Maybe he just activated his permission medallion. Either that, or he’s trying to be clever and has set up some kind of trap! Of course, the third possibility is that he’s just really confident....

As the young man considered the possibilities, he sped onward, not slowing down a bit.

It doesn’t matter. I’m not afraid of traps! And if it’s the third possibility, well, I still have options to work with.

The young man lifted his hand to produce a special dimensional ring of holding that he himself had crafted. It was one of a pair. He threw it down. Beneath him was a swamp. The ring fell down and immediately sank into the swamp.

His action seemed casual and even random. And he didn’t waste any time doing it. An instant later, and he had sped past, leaving that location behind.

Normally speaking, a ring of holding would have a dimensional holding space inside, with the body of the ring serving as the gateway leading inside. And most of the time, there was only one gateway leading into a holding dimension.

But this young man had created two. That second gate was a secret that no one else knew about. In fact, anyone who had learned the secret had ended up being killed by him. freewebnovel.com

As the young man sped along, his killing intent grew stronger. Time itself seemed to sense the killing intent and the anxiety, and flew past. He got closer and closer to Xu Qing.

350,000 kilometers. 250,000. 150,000....

Soon he was 50,000 kilometers away!

At that point, the young man, who had already been going incredibly fast, suddenly accelerated. He had decided that, regardless of which possibility in his analysis was correct, he would proceed according to plan.

And that plan had been to get within 50,000 kilometers, which was the range of a newly-activated permission medallion. And at that point, he would move with such incredible speed that his opponent wouldn’t have any chance to react.

***

The sky above Xu Qing’s cave trembled. Rumbling sounds echoed out, and blue light suddenly filled the area. It was so bright that it supplanted the light of the red aurora. And then a gigantic stone hammer appeared out of nowhere.

It was simple and unadorned, and pulsed with a great ancientness, as if it had been around for an extremely long time. The moment it appeared, there was no delay at all. It instantly smashed down onto the mountain. Heaven and earth shook violently as a blue shockwave rolled out in all directions, smashing everything it hit.

The hammer was not corporeal. When it smashed down, it actually passed through the mountain itself and into the cave, right toward the head of Xu Qing, who sat there looking up. It moved with shocking speed and came with devastating momentum.

In the time it takes a spark to fly off a piece of flint, and without giving Xu Qing the slightest chance to react, it smashed down.

And then, even as the hammer fell, the young man with the birthmark followed with terrifying speed. His killing intent roiled out with shocking ferocity.

At that moment of danger, Xu Qing’s expression flickered, and he quickly performed a double-handed incantation gesture. Instantly, the surrounding spell formations activated.

Forty-nine taboo formations flared to life, as well as hundreds of thousands of other formations, creating innumerable threads of light that became a closed fist. It shot upward to meet the hammer. The impact shook everything in the area.

The mountain was incinerated into ash. The surrounding lands were instantly turned into rubble. Even the air rippled and distorted as spatial rifts were ripped open. The fist of hundreds of thousands of formations ultimately proved too weak, and it shattered.

However, thanks to the power of the taboo formations, and of the explosion itself, the hammer was blocked, and it even moved backward a bit.

Unfortunately, the force of the blow was still difficult for Xu Qing to deal with. His face was pale, and he was shaking from head to toe. Clearly, he was unable to deal with this level of attack, as he took advantage of the moment to flee.

Before he could, the young man behind the hammer looked over, and a dao lineament stirred in his eye as he waved a hand. In the blink of an eye, a massive wind kicked up! His authority was that of wind. A heavenly gale descended, becoming a huge tempest that whipped about everywhere, locking down the entire area.

Xu Qing’s path of escape was blocked.

Within the tempest could be heard countless howling sounds, as if a magnificent army with thousands of men and horses were in it, charging right toward Xu Qing.

Up above, the young man with the birthmark seethed with killing intent as he shot in Xu Qing’s direction.

Madness burned in Xu Qing’s eyes now that he couldn’t flee. Throwing caution to the wind, he waved his hand. The authority of erasure erupted, clashing with the authority of wind. Next, Xu Qing rose up into the air, performing incantation gestures one after another to release magical techniques and divine abilities. He and the young man instantly started fighting.

Booms rang out constantly.

Xu Qing seemed to be going completely mad. He appeared to be desperate, and was putting everything on the line, hardly even paying attention to his own safety as he tried to push his opponent backward. It took only a short moment for deafening booms to fill the air.

Unfortunately, there was a clear disparity. After only about ten breaths of time, Xu Qing shivered as the young man’s palm clamped down onto the top of his head. Without giving Xu Qing any chance to do anything, and without even saying a word, the young man viciously clamped his hand down.

A pop rang out as Xu Qing’s head exploded. The moment it happened, Xu Qing unhesitatingly self-detonated, blocking his opponent and sending his soul fleeing off into the distance.

Rumbling booms again echoed out. The power of the self-detonation created a terrifying vortex, and yet, the young man with the birthmark just laughed coldly. Astonishingly, the aura of another dao lineament surged within him, creating a sea of flames.

He had two types of authority. One was wind, the other was fire.

This young man fought in a completely different way than the spirit mine guardian or the man from the city earlier. He led with his authority and his trump cards. The sea of flames raged, completely devouring the vortex created by the self-detonation. It seemed it was only going to take a moment to resolve the entire situation. The fire merged with the wind, then swelled outward to block the path of Xu Qing’s fleeing soul, then destroy it.

But then...!

Down underground, the real Xu Qing opened his eyes.

The figure from the crystalline treasure tree looked exactly like him, even down to the aura. It could even produce a soul. Although it was fake, it would be hard for anyone to notice the difference, especially in a short time. After getting his opponent to use his authority of fire, he created a big opening.

Xu Qing’s eyes flashed with cold light. The authority of the five elements erupted. The lands that had been reduced to ashes churned, and the power of the lands converged. Land-shaking, mountain-rocking force surged. The soil became like a sea, whipped up by the wind to crush the young man’s fire authority.

And then, Xu Qing’s five elements flame appeared in the sky, spreading out like heavenly fire. Countless streams of water vapor formed, and within each one was an image of Xu Qing. The power of wood swirled as innumerable wooden sword sheaths filled the area. Inside of each sheath was the power of metal. Five elements authorities were on full display, deadly and terrifying.

But Xu Qing still wasn’t content. Without any hesitation, he burned the life essence incense. Incense smoke swirled up, filling with the power to burn life.

As the five elements authority raged, Xu Qing decisively emerged from the ground. Moving with stone-shattering momentum, he hefted The Emperor’s Sword and shot toward the young man with the birthmark. All of this takes some time to describe, but happened in the twinkling of an eye.

Xu Qing sent out a thought to Little Shadow, who sent pure darkness spreading out, all while taking control of all the shadows cast by the aurora. This was the deadly trap Xu Qing had laid.

The young man with the birthmark reacted with visible shock. Falling back, he sent his authorities of wind and fire out, all while calling on some of his magical treasures. He also used some divine abilities to try to escape.

Clearly, he was too slow. Though he had deduced that this whole thing could be a trap, he didn’t realize that the projection from the crystalline treasure tree was fake. And that had determined how everything turned out.

The five elements were raging; the land bolstered the body, the sea of flames eradicated magic, the shine of metal hastened the soul; the power of wood ended life; water vapor was deadly! The shadow entrapped. One sword destroyed.

A boom rang out far and wide. The young man exploded, becoming a cloud of gore plus a ring of holding.

The fight was over.

Little Shadow seemed extremely excited and sent out a lot of emotional fluctuations. It then rushed over to grab up the chunks of flesh and the ring and bring them to Xu Qing.

Except... Xu Qing’s face had turned grim. With the wave of his hand, he stopped Little Shadow from reaching the chunks of flesh and the ring.

Little Shadow was stunned.

Xu Qing’s eyes were glittering coldly, the reason being that he had not sensed his opponent’s authority rushing toward him, nor had he detected any change to his permission medallion. His opponent wasn’t actually dead!

His senses were telling him that the other medallion was so close it was almost overlapping with him. Because of that, he wasn’t able to assess his opponent very accurately. To do so, he would have to go some distance away.

As that thought ran through his head, he suddenly waved his hand. All of a sudden, ripples flowed as the surroundings became a surface of water.

Heaven and earth became a well. It was none other than Fishing the Moon in the Well.

Xu Qing had acted with incredible decisiveness to use Fishing the Moon in the Well on the surroundings. His decisive reaction brought results.

The instant he used the technique, reflections appeared! On the surface of the water it was now possible to see the magical techniques and authorities that Xu Qing had used moments ago.

They were the reflections Xu Qing had selected. In addition, in the location where the ring of holding and the chunks of flesh were, it was possible to see the reflections of the various magical techniques, as well as the authorities of wind and fire. It was even possible to see the items in the ring of holding’s dimension.

That was when Xu Qing saw something very unusual! The ring of holding had two gateways!

What was more, he was astonished to find that there was a shadowy figure stuck up against the wall of the ring of holding’s dimensional space. Or had it been stuck there by someone...?

As Xu Qing studied it, he realized there was only one word that could properly describe it. It was glued to the wall!

The shadowy figure looked like it was glued on the wall of the dimensional space, in a clever way that would make it almost impossible to ever see. Moments before, it had been moving.

Because Fishing the Moon in the Well caused all things to go still, it was being affected. However, because it had the power of an Imperial Sovereign, it wasn’t rendered completely motionless, and was still moving very slowly.

The scene caused Xu Qing’s gaze to harden. It only took a moment to deduce that he was looking at his opponent’s true form! What he had killed was only a clone! His opponent had not noticed that the projection from the crystalline treasure tree was fake. But Xu Qing had also failed to realize that he wasn’t fighting his opponent’s true form. Both of them had used similar methods to try to deceive the other.

As for the enemy’s true form, it was very close by, and was thus able to use the overlapping effects of the permission medallions to hide. Beyond that, he had glued himself to the wall of the ring of holding’s dimensional space, making it even more difficult to detect him. Because of that method, he was almost part of the wall within the ring. To some extent, he was in between the illusory and the corporeal. An outside force would have a hard time affecting him.

Xu Qing had no idea how he was able to do this. But right now wasn’t the time to sit around contemplating it. Without any hesitation, he once again unleashed the previous magical techniques within the confines of Fishing the Moon in the Well.

“I don’t care if you are hiding. I can still hurt you in your hiding place!”

Fishing the Moon in the Well was fundamentally a spatial manipulation magic. Maybe he was glued to the wall. Maybe he was really part of it. But the power of Fishing the Moon in the Well could still affect him!

Xu Qing’s magical techniques and authorities erupted within Fishing the Moon in the Well. This time, his target was that shadowy figure! In the blink of an eye, everything exploded.

***

Over 450,000 kilometers away in the swamp, the other ring of holding the young man had thrown down suddenly flashed. A figure appeared within it. It was the same young man with the birthmark. This time, his face was very pale. After emerging, he coughed up a massive mouthful of blood, then looked back in Xu Qing’s direction. His expression was very serious.

He had the authorities of wind and fire. Two authorities made him chosen, but he wasn’t satisfied with that. Unfortunately, his aptitude made it impossible for him to form a third type of authority.

Therefore, he had found a new way. Using a unique item with a rare spatial function, plus the power of his flame authority to temper it, he added some immortal serum. The serum would remain inside until he needed it. Then he could use his wind authority to scatter the immortal serum.

As a result, the serum would harden a bit and turn into something like a glue.

After developing this technique, he would use it in dangerous fights. He could take his true form and glue it onto the wall of the dimensional space in his ring of holding. As a result, he actually became part of the dimension. It was a great concealment method. And oftentimes, an opponent would think they had killed him, then pick up his ring of holding afterward, only for him to jump out and surprise them. It had always worked.

Unfortunately, in the Immortal Capital’s Trial of the Hunt, anyone who died would have their permission medallion absorbed by the person who killed them. That created a bit of a flaw in his technique.

The damned rules of the Trial of the Hunt messed everything up. However, it’s surprising that this guy figured out everything so fast, and thus prevented me from launching my sneak attack. He’s no one to take lightly. And he even figured out a way to injure my true form. And then there’s his authority....

The young man’s eyes narrowed.

The fact that he laid such a careful trap shows that he’s clever. And his authority makes it clear he has aptitude. He acts decisively as well. All of that indicates... that this guy is an uncharacteristically extraordinary chosen! I bet he was hiding his true cultivation base level.

Heart pounding with lingering fear, he decided to just leave. It wasn’t worth it to get involved in a life-or-death struggle with a person like this in the second round. Besides, having been injured, he wasn’t in top shape now. He needed to find a place to treat his injuries.

I need to make sure he’s not following me....

The young man sighed and turned to leave. However, that was when his expression flickered and he took out a messaging device. After looking at it, his eyes flashed.

After some thought, he sent a response. “I just ran into a guy that matches that description. He could be the one you want.”

Meanwhile, back where the battle had been fought, the lands were devastated. The mountain had been destroyed, and everything else in the area had been flattened. The fluctuations of lingering magical techniques rolled out everywhere.

Xu Qing hovered in midair, his expression fierce as he looked off into the distance.

Wind and fire. This guy’s authorities are....

This is my first time in the Fifth Star Ring encountering someone with two authorities. This guy is obviously a chosen cultivator. That’s especially true considering his crafty techniques. He’s obviously a clever, formidable opponent!

When Xu Qing thought about how his opponent had hidden himself by pasting his true form to the wall of his dimensional space, Xu Qing had to admit that it was impressive.

I wonder how exactly he pulled that off. Maybe he was using a treasure with spatial abilities.... If it weren’t for the functionality of the permission medallion, I might not have realized what was going on, at least not at first.

Xu Qing’s guard went up further. He had believed himself to be acting very cautiously, only to realize that he had been careless.

Next time I kill an enemy and take their holding item, I need to pay closer attention.

Mind racing, he collected the incense and the tree. The incense had gone out when the clone died, but there was still more left that could be used. As for the tree, it had sustained some damage when self-detonating, and Xu Qing wasn’t sure how to fix it.

I can probably get it to self-detonate one more time.

After collecting the 49 Taboo Formations beast hide and the other items, he prepared to leave.

It didn’t seem likely that the person he had just fought would flee only to return shortly after. This fellow was obviously smart. Considering the second round of the Trial of the Hunt had just begun, it didn’t seem like a good move to target an opponent who you knew wasn’t weak. Now was the time to conserve strength and avoid getting badly hurt. The only exceptions would be a situation in which fleeing wasn’t possible, or you had a grudge to settle.

Xu Qing was thinking that if he were in this person’s shoes, he definitely wouldn’t try to keep on fighting. However, just as he was about to burst into motion, he stopped in place. A look of surprise appeared on his face.

“He’s coming back?”

He had just noticed the blip of a star appear within the range of his permission medallion, about 500,000 kilometers away. Contrary to what Xu Qing had assumed, this person wasn’t leaving. Instead, he was moving at top speed toward Xu Qing.

Xu Qing frowned slightly. Something about the situation seemed unusual. Only a moment later, though, his eyes flashed with cold light, and killing intent rose in his heart.

Since he’s coming back, then this fight... should be fought to the end!

Xu Qing burst into motion, not toward his incoming opponent, but rather, in the opposite direction. The formations he had set up in the area had all been used. This was not the ideal location for a fight.

Therefore, Xu Qing shot through the air toward a towering peak covered in vegetation. It was so high, its summit was surrounded by clouds.

Xu Qing landed on the top of the mountain and stood there waiting. It seemed strange for his opponent to do this, and therefore, Xu Qing wasn’t going to do anything impulsive. He also didn’t want to fall into any traps.

And the best way to avoid fighting on his opponent’s terms was to pick a location that he knew his opponent hadn’t been to. This mountain provided a clear view of the surroundings, and the misty surroundings would make a great place to fight.

Xu Qing didn’t waste any time. He waved his hand to send out his five elements authorities. Fire went into the sky. Water went into the clouds. Earth went into the mountain itself. Metal went into his own body. Wood filled the surrounding vegetation.

This time, Xu Qing didn’t have to wait for long.

The young man with the birthmark could tell what Xu Qing was doing, and he took advantage of even teleportations to approach as quickly as possible. With terrifying speed, he crossed over 500,000 kilometers, and since Xu Qing wasn’t moving, it took only a moment... for him to appear on the horizon.

As the aurora sent crimson light shining down, the sound of a thunderstorm rumbled.

Next, Xu Qing saw that, in addition to the red from the aurora, there were five other colors!

Black. Green. Yellow. Blue. Violet! The five colors came from five enormous flags, each of them several hundred meters long. They spread through the sky, and as they passed along, they gathered all other colors and cut them off. Those five colors became everything.

A majestic might erupted from within them, which focused primarily on the power of the five elements!

After the fight earlier, Xu Qing had learned a lot about his opponent. But the opposite was true. His opponent had learned about him. Therefore, the first thing he was trying to do was lock down Xu Qing’s five elements.

The moment Xu Qing spotted the five-colored flags, a five-colored light swept out, and the flags were right at the top of the mountain. Five colors erupted, scattering the five elements power and covering the summit of the mountain. From a distance, it looked like a five-colored tempest. Deafening booms rumbled out everywhere.

Meanwhile, Xu Qing’s eyes flashed with killing intent as he waved his hand, unleashing the five elements preparations he had made. Water flowed from the clouds. Wood erupted from the vegetation. Fire fell from the sky. Earth exploded from the mountain. As Xu Qing’s killing will spread, the five elements reacted accordingly.

These five-colored flags were extraordinary, and the five-colored tempest could disrupt the five elements power in the area. However... they couldn’t touch the five elements that belonged to Xu Qing. That was because Xu Qing’s five elements came from his five yin organs, and did not come from the natural and magical laws of the surrounding world.

An instant later, the rumbling sounds grew even louder. Xu Qing’s five elements authorities fought against the five-colored tempest, and they clearly had the upper hand. The five colors began to fade; clearly, it wouldn’t take very long for Xu Qing to crush them.

But this time, Xu Qing was up against an extraordinary opponent.

After summoning the five-colored tempest, the young man didn’t close in and start fighting close-quarters. He stayed on the edge of the battlefield, a cold smile on his face. He waved his finger, all while reciting a dao chant under his breath.

“Heaven serves as the world. Air serves as the backdrop. Five colors add embellishment. All magics in one image!”

As he waved his finger, the five flags that were struggling against Xu Qing’s five elements authorities suddenly shivered. And then, all of them... exploded.

A five-colored self-detonation ripped out in all directions. As a result, the five colors mixed with each other! From a distance, it looked like the five-colored light became a physical substance, as if it was paint that mixed together and then scattered in the air.

It turned into... a five-colored canvas! And Xu Qing was right in the middle of the canvas.

As for the painter, it was the wind! The wind was also performing a sealing!

That sealing had been concealed within the five colors, and as soon as it erupted, it locked down the five elements.

“I’ll help you to understand that although the five elements are formidable, the wind is stronger! When the great wind strikes up, it scatters earth, dissipates water, withers wood, grinds metal, and puts out fire! Seal, seal, seal, seal, seal!”

The young man’s hands flashed in five double-handed incantation gestures, after each of which he waved his finger. The five-colored paint became more chaotic, and as the colors mixed, with Xu Qing in the middle, they formed a sealing mark. It was a sealing mark, not just focused on withering and grinding away, but on isolation.

It isolated Xu Qing’s five yin organs, and thus isolated Xu Qing’s five elements. For the first time in the fight, Xu Qing looked surprised.

This guy’s authority... has been developed to a very high level. Except, I used the dao of space earlier. There’s no way he doesn’t realize that what he’s doing is basically pointless, right?

Xu Qing waved his hand thoughtfully.

Yet again, Fishing the Moon in the Well appeared. Everything was reflected within the water. But this time, what Xu Qing planned to fish out of the water wasn’t his opponent, but himself.

As the magic of Fishing the Moon in the Well erupted, Xu Qing fished out the five-colored sealing mark. Now he was outside of the canvas, outside of the five colors, and outside of the mountain! The moment he appeared, the canopy of heaven rumbled. Blue light spread out as a massive hammer appeared and viciously swung down toward Xu Qing.

The Emperor’s Sword appeared in his hand. The lands quaked. The mountain shattered. Earth power surged.

The first sword move was Earth Treasury. It slashed the hammer. Heaven and earth distorted. The air blurred. A deafening sound rang out.

The earth-powered sword shot up, and the hammer vibrated. Cracks spread out all over it, and then it was sent spinning off to the side. At the same time, the backlash caused Earth Treasury to dissipate, turning once more into earth energy that dissipated.

Xu Qing burst into motion toward the young man with the birthmark.

When the young man saw that both of his tactics had been vanquished by Xu Qing, his pupils constricted. Now more than ever he was convinced that his previous supposition had been correct.

Shooting backward with eyes narrowed, he waved a hand to throw something out in front of him. It looked like a ball of clay, and it seemed to contain some sort of spatial power. As it flew through the air, it left behind ripples in its wake.

Then, the young man exercised a thought, and authority erupted in the space between himself and Xu Qing.

It started with the authority of fire, which landed on the item streaking through the air. That item was obviously sensitive to fire, as it immediately started to melt, all while emanating an explosive power.

A boom rang out, and then something like rainwater started falling from the sky. However, this rain was sticky.

As it fell, the young man’s second type of authority was unleashed.

A great wind blew. As the wind blew on the sticky rain, it started to dry and solidify, turning into... glue! In all directions, everything that the rain touched began to harden. It was another type of sealing. Using the glue he had created, he was sealing heaven and earth.

All of a sudden, Xu Qing understood how his opponent had pasted himself onto the wall of his spatial dimension. Just as he had guessed, his opponent was using a special item.

However, there was something else that he hadn’t thought of. And that was how his opponent was using the item.

He’s combining two types of authority with that object to create the effect of a third type of authority! This guy is really a genius!

Xu Qing took a deep breath as this thought occurred to him. This fight... was proving to be deeply meaningful to him. It was giving him a lot of inspiration.

If I added that to my five elements, there would be even more variations possible!

That said, now wasn’t the time to think deeply about the subject. What was more, everything that had happened in this fight up to this point had revealed a very important thing.

He doesn’t want to fight me directly! And he doesn’t want to get hurt. He’s hoping to hem me in and seal me! Everything he’s been doing falls in line with that strategy. And to achieve that end, he’s even gone so far as to reveal some of his secrets....

This points to one thing. He’s trying to buy time!

This realization caused a sensation of intense danger to rise up in Xu Qing.

He has someone helping him, and they’re on the way. And they’re much stronger than him!

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered with cold light.

If things keep going as they are, it’s going to be hard to end this fight. In that case... I can’t hold back my sword energy. I need to end this fight right away!

***

Meanwhile, a good distance away from the battlefield, someone was shooting through the sky at top speed, even using teleportation magics in the process. This person had a terrifying aura. He was the very same red-haired young man who had appeared not too long ago at the spirit mine. He had the cultivation base fluctuations of a late Imperial Sovereign.

You destroyed my clan’s spirit mine and killed the guardian. Your actions made me lose that fight. And you even stole the Immortal Capital permission medallion that Ling Feng had prepared as a gift for me! I’m very curious to see how you got the outrageous gall to do things like that!
